       ♦ _*EIFA' E AHD O PAIMAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (622) 📜

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَوْفُوا بِالْعُقُودِ ۚ أُحِلَّتْ لَكُمْ بَهِيمَةُ الْأَنْعَامِ إِلَّا مَا يُتْلَىٰ عَلَيْكُمْ غَيْرَ مُحِلِّي الصَّيْدِ وَأَنْتُمْ حُرُمٌ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَحْكُمُ مَا يُرِيدُ*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Hudood o quyood aur Mu'ahedon (Rules & Limitations & Covenant) ki pabandi karo. ....... Beshak Allah jo chahta hai Woh Faisla karta hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 1)

📚📖 📜
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj se ham Sura Ma'idah ki Tafseer shuru karte hain. Ye Madni Sura hai aur kul 120 Aayaat hain.
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Sura Maeda Rehlate Paighambar (saww) se do ya teen mahine pahle nazil hui."_
(Tafseer e Burhan, Vol 1, P-430)
Ek rivayat ke mutabiq Hajjatul Wuda mein Mekka aur Medina ke darmiyan nazil hui.
(Al Munar, Vol 6, P-116)
Is Surah ka naam مائده Ma'idah isliye rakha kiyonki​ is Surah mein Hazrat Esa (as) ke Ansar ke liye jo Ma'idah (Khana rakhne ka bartan) ke nazool ka waqea Ayat 114 mein darj hai.
Is Ayat ka pahla hissa Eifae Ahd (Fulfilment of Covenant) ke bare mein hai.
Ahd kai tarah ke hote hain. Do admi ke darmiyan Agreement, partnership, qarardad etc. Ye Duniya ke hain.
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Duniya bhar ke logon mein tamam tar ikhtelafat ke bawajood Eifae Ahd ki tarah kisi aur amr par ittefaq nahi hai. Isliye to Zamana e Jahiliyyat ke But Parast bhi Ahd o Paiman ka ehtram karte the. Kiyonki woh Ahd Shikni ke dardnaak​ anjam jaan chuke the."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Letter No. 53)

Aap ne dekha hoga sare do no. ke kaam isi Ahdo Paiman par chalte hain, aur Ahd Shikni karne wale ko uda diya jata hai. (misal)

Lekin ye yaad rakhna chahiye ke hamne bhi Allah aur Uske Rasool se Ahd o Paiman kiya hua hai. Isliye agar ham Allah ke Ahd Shikni karen to kiya hashr hoga.
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
                 *لا دين لمن لا عهد له.*
_"Jo shakhs apne Ahd o Paiman ka wafadar nahi uska koi Deen nahi."_
(Bihar, Vol 16, P-144)

Yaha tak ke Irshad e Amirul Momenin Ali (as):
_"Agar koi ishare se bhi koi Ahd apne zimme le le to use poora karna chahiye."_
(Mustadrakul Wasail, Vol 2, P-25)

Imam Ali Naqi (as):
_"Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne das martaba logon se Hazrat Ali (as) ki Khilafat ka Ahd liya tha isi liye ye Ayat jahan baqi Ahd o Mu'ahedon ki pabandi ka hukm deti hai wahan ye Ayat Musalmano ko ye hukm bhi deti hai ke woh Khilafat ke Ahd par bhi qaem rahen."_
(Noorus Saqlain, Vol 2)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Agar hamare Shia, Allah unko Uski ita'at ki tafeeq de, *ek dil hokar unke Ahdo  Paiman ko poora karte to hamari mulaqat mein takheer nahi hoti, aur jald hi hamari ziyarat se sharaf yab hote,* Haq ki Ma'arefat ke sath aur hamari huqooq ki tasdeeq karte hue."_
(Al Ehtejaaj, Vol 2, P-602)
📂📜
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Teen cheezen aisi hain jin ki mukhalifat ki Khuda ne kisi ko ijazat nahi di._
_(1) Amanat ki adaygi._
_(2) Ifae Ahd (Fulfilment of Covenant)_
_(3) Maa Baap se husne Sulook_
_chahe woh achchhe hon ya bure."_
(Usool e Kaafi, Vol2, P-162)

        ♦ _*CHAUPAYE (CATTLES)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (623) 🐄🐪🐐

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَوْفُوا بِالْعُقُودِ ۚ أُحِلَّتْ لَكُمْ بَهِيمَةُ الْأَنْعَامِ إِلَّا مَا يُتْلَىٰ عَلَيْكُمْ غَيْرَ مُحِلِّي الصَّيْدِ وَأَنْتُمْ حُرُمٌ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَحْكُمُ مَا يُرِيدُ*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Hudood o quyood aur Mu'ahedon (Rules & Limitations & Covenant) ki pabandi karo. *Tum par maveshi (Cattles) ki qism ke sab janwar halal kiye gaye siwai unke jinka tazkara aage kiya jayega lekin Ehram ki haalat mein shikar ko apne liye Halal na karo.* Beshak Allah jo chahta hai Woh Faisla karta hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 1)

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Jo Shakhs har Jumerat ke Din Surah Ma'idah padhe to woh apne Imaan ko Zulm se makhloot nahi karega aur woh kabhi shirk mein mubtila na hoga."_
(Kitab Sawabul Aamaal)

📚📖 🐄🐪🐐
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
'Baheema' بهيمة means sakht Patthar (hard rock), aur har cheez jiska samajhna mushkil ho use 'Ibham' إبهام kahte hain. Chunki tamam janwar jo bol chal nahi sakte aur ham unki awaz nahi samjh sakte isliye inhe 'Baheema' kaha gaya. 'Ana'am انعام means Cattles, Chaupaye jo rahme madar se paida hote hain. Ab is ayat mein ek general rule bata diya gaya. Ab kiya Halal aur kiya Haram in particular baad ki Ayaton mein unka zikr hoga. Lekin kuchh Cattles pahle se Halal qarar de diye gaye hain jaise Oont (Camel), Gaye (Cow), Gosphand (Goat or Sheep) etc. Ek rule yaha bataya gaya ke Hajj ke mauqe par haalat e Ehram mein Shikar haram hai.
🐃🐂
Imam Baqir & Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jis Jinin جنين (Embroy​) ke jism par bal (hair) aur oon (wool) paida ho chuki ho to uski maa ka zabiha uska zabiha hai aur is Ayat se yehi mafhoom murad hai."_
(Al Kaafi)
🐘 🐻 🐒
Hazrat Ali (as) se Haathi (Elephant), Reechh (Bear) aur Bandar (Monkey) ke gosht ki Halal o Haram ke bare mein poochha gaya to Aap (as) ne farmaya: _"Inka talluq khane jane wale maveshiyon se nahi hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)

Kuchh aur Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🐃🐂🐄🐐🐑🐪🐫
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Gosht (ka khana) Gosht ko ugaata hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v17, p43)
🐃🐂🐄🐐🐑🐪🐫
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Mujhe Paaye khaane ki daawat di jaati hai to qubool kar leta hoo'n aur agar koi mujhe Paaye hadiya karta hai to usay qubool kar leta hoo'n."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p186)
🐃🐂🐄🐐🐑🐪🐫
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs 40 din tak Gosht na khaa sakey usko chaahiye ke qarz le kar Gosht khaaye jiski adaaygi Allah ki taraf se hogi. Aur agar 40 din tak Gosht na khaaye to pehle daahine kaan (Right Ear) mein Azaan kahi jaaye phir Gosht khaaye."_
(Roohul Hayaat)
📚📖📚📖📚📖📚📖
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*إجعلوا قصدكم إلينا بالمودة على السنة الواضحة، نصحت لكم، و الله شاهد على و عليكم.*
_"Ham (Ahle Bait e Ismat o Taharat) se apni Muhabbat o dosti ka maqsad Ahkam e Ilahi ka nifaz aur Sunnat par Amal ki buniyad qarar do, beshak ham ne zaroori shifarishon aur lazim Mau'ezon (Nasihaten) ko anjaam diya hai, Khud wand Alam ham aur tum sab par Gawah hai."_
(Al Ghaiba Toosi, P-286, H-245, Ehtejaaj, Vol 2, P-279, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-179, H-9)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*EHTERAM-E-SHA'AR E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (624) 🕋

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُحِلُّوا شَعَائِرَ اللَّهِ وَلَا الشَّهْرَ الْحَرَامَ وَلَا الْهَدْيَ وَلَا الْقَلَائِدَ وَلَا آمِّينَ الْبَيْتَ الْحَرَامَ يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلًا مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ وَرِضْوَانًا ۚ وَإِذَا حَلَلْتُمْ فَاصْطَادُوا ۚ وَلَا يَجْرِمَنَّكُمْ شَنَآنُ قَوْمٍ أَنْ صَدُّوكُمْ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ أَنْ تَعْتَدُوا ۘ وَتَعَاوَنُوا عَلَى الْبِرِّ وَالتَّقْوَىٰ ۖ وَلَا تَعَاوَنُوا عَلَى الْإِثْمِ وَالْعُدْوَانِ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۖ إِنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ*

_*"Aye Imaan walo! Sha'are Ilahi ki be hurmati na karo aur Haram Mahinon mein se kisi ko Halal na karo. Qurbani ke janwaron par dastdarazi na karo aur un janwaron par dastdarazi na karo jin ki gardano mein Nazre Khuda wandi ki Alamat ke patte pade hue hon aur un logon ko na chhedo jo apne Rab ke Fazal aur Khushnoodi ki talash mein Mohtaram Ghar (Ka'aba) ki taraf ja rahe hon.* Haan jab ehraam ki haalat khatm ho jaye to tum shikar kar sakte ho aur dekho ek giroh jisne tumhare liye Masjid e Haram ka raasta band kiya hai to un par tumhara ghussa tumhe itna mushta'il na kar de ke tum unke muqabile mein na rawa zyadtiyam karne lag jao. Neki aur Taqwa ke kaamon mein ek doosre se ta'awun karo aur gunah aur zyadti ke kaamon mein ta'awun na karo aur Allah se darte raho. Beshak Allah sakht Azaab Dene Wala hai."_
(Surat Ma'idah: 2)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat Sulah Hudaibiyah ke agle saal nazil hui aur waqae Ghadeer ke pahle nazil hui.
Is Ek Ayat mein 8 Ahkam bayan kiye gaye hain. Is mein se kuchh aaj bayan karenge:
(1) Sha'ayerallah شعائر الله ka ehtram karo. Sura Baqarah: Ayat 158 ke mutabiq Sha'are Khuda se murad Manasike Hajj hain. Is Saal Rasool e Khuda (saww) ka Akheri Hajj tha. Is Ayat ke mutabiq jahan jahan aur jis cheez mein bhi Allah ki nishani payi jaati hai uska ehtram karna chahiye. Jis cheez ki nisbat Allah aur uske Rasool aur Janasheen e Rasool (as) se hai woh Sha'are Khuda hai. Isliye ye bidat nahi ho sakta. Nisbaton ka Ehtram ek fitri amal hai.

(2) Haram Mahinon mein Jang karna Haram hai, iska lihaz Kafir bhi rakhte the. Ye Mahine hain Rajab, Zilqad, ZilHajj, Muharram.

Dhyan rahe ke Karbala ki Jang Muharram mein hui jis mein dono fareeq Muslim the, Munafiqon ne is qanoon bhi lehaz na rakha.
Karbala ke waqea ke baad Ka'aba par hamla hua, usko jalaya gaya, ghode bandhe gaye, phir aaj log unko Ashaabe Rasool bata kar unka ehteram karte hain na ke in waqeat ki mazammat ho. Isliye is Ayat ki roshni mein Karbala ne haqeeqi Islam ko naqli Islam se alag  kar diya. Warna Ka'aba ka wujood khatm tha.

(3) Jo Janwar Hajj ke waqt laye jate the ya to nishani ke bagair hote the (هدى), ya unke gale mein Nishani padi hoti thi (قلائد), Hajiyon ke Qurbani ke Janwaron par dastdarazi ki gayi.

(4) Ye Aman ki jagah hai, jo bhi yahan Hajj karne aye Azadi se Ahkam baja laye chahe woh koi bhi ho, usse koi mazahemat nahi honi chahiye. Chahe Dushman hi kiyon na ho. Imam Husain (as) ne isi liye apne Hajj ko Umrah mein tabdeel kiya jab pata chala Dushman Hajiyon ke bhes mein Mecca pahunch gaye hain. Imam (as) ne Ka'aba ki hurmat ko baqi rakha. Aur is Ka'aba ki Hurmat ko bachane wala is jagah se Aaj hi ke din Zuhoor karega. Aur aaj Khud sakhta khadim Harimain un se Muqabila karna chahte hain. Rasoole Khuda ka Zahoor bhi Kafiron ke darmiyan se hua, unke Akhiri Janashin ka bhi Zahoor Munafiqon ke darmiyan Ka'aba se hoga.

(To be Cont'd ....Jari)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕋
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aakhri zamane ki nishaniyo'n mein ek ye bhi hai ke jo musalmano'n mein se bad-tareen honge wo Hajj karenge. Ameer log saer (picnic) karne Hajj ke liye jayenge, middle-class (madhyam-varg) tijaarat ki garaz se jayenge aur gareeb log mazhabi hone ka dikhawa karne aur muttaqi hone ki shohrat haasil karne jayenge."_
(Holy Quran Commentary - Agha Pooya)

          ♦ _*HAJJ SE ROKNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (625) 🕋

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُحِلُّوا شَعَائِرَ اللَّهِ وَلَا الشَّهْرَ الْحَرَامَ وَلَا الْهَدْيَ وَلَا الْقَلَائِدَ وَلَا آمِّينَ الْبَيْتَ الْحَرَامَ يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلًا مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ وَرِضْوَانًا ۚ وَإِذَا حَلَلْتُمْ فَاصْطَادُوا ۚ وَلَا يَجْرِمَنَّكُمْ شَنَآنُ قَوْمٍ أَنْ صَدُّوكُمْ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ أَنْ تَعْتَدُوا ۘ وَتَعَاوَنُوا عَلَى الْبِرِّ وَالتَّقْوَىٰ ۖ وَلَا تَعَاوَنُوا عَلَى الْإِثْمِ وَالْعُدْوَانِ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۖ إِنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ*

_"Aye Imaan walo! Sha'are Ilahi ki be hurmati na karo aur Haram Mahinon mein se kisi ko Halal na karo. Qurbani ke janwaron par dastdarazi na karo aur un janwaron par dastdarazi na karo jin ki gardano mein Nazre Khuda wandi ki Alamat ke patte pade hue hon aur un logon ko na chhedo jo apne Rab ke Fazal aur Khushnoodi ki talash mein Mohtaram Ghar (Ka'aba) ki taraf ja rahe hon. *Haan jab ehraam ki haalat khatm ho jaye to tum shikar kar sakte ho aur dekho ek giroh jisne tumhare liye Masjid e Haram ka raasta band kiya hai to un par tumhara ghussa tumhe itna mushta'il na kar de ke tum unke muqabile mein na rawa zyadtiyam karne lag jao.* Neki aur Taqwa ke kaamon mein ek doosre se ta'awun karo aur gunah aur zyadti ke kaamon mein ta'awun na karo aur Allah se darte raho. Beshak Allah sakht Azaab Dene Wala hai."_
(Surat Ma'idah: 2)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein 8 Ahkam bayan kiye gaye hain. 4 hamne kal bayan kiye. Baqi aur hazire khidmat hain:
(5) Ehram ke nikalne ke baad Shikar jaez hai.

(6) Hudaibiya mein Rasool (saww) aur Musalmano ko Ka'aba ki Ziyarat ke ijazat nahi di sab ko wapaz lautna pada, lekin Fateh Mecca ke baad jab sab ne Islam qubool kar liya to ye munasib nahi ke pichhle karnaamo ka unse badla liya jaye ya tane mezi baten ki jayen. Ye zaroori nahi ke ab woh Musalman ab unko Hajj se roken. Lekin Tarikh mein bhi milta hai aur aaj bhi Hajj ke liye Hakim e Waqt Hajj par pabandiyan laga dete hain.

(7) Nek mein madad karo na ke gunah mein sath do.

(8) Parhez o Taqwa ikhtiyar karo, nafarmani se bacho.

(To be Cont'd .......)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ki qasam, Allah ne aise kisi kaam mein faayda nahi rakha jo Hajj ke liye rukawatt bane. Har shakhs apne gunaho'n ki wajah se Hajj se mehroom rehta hai."_
(Greater Sins III)
📁📂
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*والعاقبة بجميل صنع الله سبحانه تكون حميدة لهم ما اجتنبوا المنهى عنه من الذنوب*
_"Jab tak hamare Shia Gunahon se door rahen us waqt tak Khuda Wande Alam ke Lutf o Karam se sar anjam bakhair hoga."_
(Ehtejaj, Vol 2, P-325, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-177, H-8)
🕋
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Jab Imam Mahdi (atfs) zahoor farmayenge, to wo Khana e Kaaba ki deewar se apni peethh tek kar khade honge aur unke 313 ashaab unke ird-gird khade honge. Aur jo pehla lafz wo kahenge wo Quran ki ye Ayat hogi:_
*بَقِيَّتُ اللَّهِ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ وَمَا أَنَا عَلَيْكُمْ بِحَفِيظٍ*
_[Surat Hud 86]_
_*BAQIYATALLAHI KHAIRUL LAKUM IN KUNTUM MOMENEEN*  Iske baad wo kahenge, 'Main Baqiyatallah hoo'n, Allah ka Wali aur Khalifa aur tumpar Uski Hujjat hoo'n". Aur iske baad jo koi unhe Salaam karega, wo in jumlo mein Salaam karega, As Salaamu alaika ya Baqiyatallahi Fi Arzehi._
*السلام عليك يا بقية الله فى أرضه.*
(Noor ul Absaar - Syed Momin Shablanji (Shafa'ee Aalim, The Promised One in Quran, p13)

  ♦ _*TA'AWUN (CO-OPERATION)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (626) 🤝

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُحِلُّوا شَعَائِرَ اللَّهِ وَلَا الشَّهْرَ الْحَرَامَ وَلَا الْهَدْيَ وَلَا الْقَلَائِدَ وَلَا آمِّينَ الْبَيْتَ الْحَرَامَ يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلًا مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ وَرِضْوَانًا ۚ وَإِذَا حَلَلْتُمْ فَاصْطَادُوا ۚ وَلَا يَجْرِمَنَّكُمْ شَنَآنُ قَوْمٍ أَنْ صَدُّوكُمْ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ أَنْ تَعْتَدُوا ۘ *وَتَعَاوَنُوا عَلَى الْبِرِّ وَالتَّقْوَىٰ ۖ وَلَا تَعَاوَنُوا عَلَى الْإِثْمِ وَالْعُدْوَانِ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۖ إِنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ*

_"Aye Imaan walo! Sha'are Ilahi ki be hurmati na karo aur Haram Mahinon mein se kisi ko Halal na karo. Qurbani ke janwaron par dastdarazi na karo aur un janwaron par dastdarazi na karo jin ki gardano mein Nazre Khuda wandi ki Alamat ke patte pade hue hon aur un logon ko na chhedo jo apne Rab ke Fazal aur Khushnoodi ki talash mein Mohtaram Ghar (Ka'aba) ki taraf ja rahe hon. Haan jab ehraam ki haalat khatm ho jaye to tum shikar kar sakte ho aur dekho ek giroh jisne tumhare liye Masjid e Haram ka raasta band kiya hai to un par tumhara ghussa tumhe itna mushta'il na kar de ke tum unke muqabile mein na rawa zyadtiyam karne lag jao. *Neki aur Taqwa ke kaamon mein ek doosre se ta'awun karo aur gunah aur zyadti ke kaamon mein ta'awun na karo aur Allah se darte raho. Beshak Allah sakht Azaab Dene Wala hai."*_
(Surat Ma'idah: 2)

📚📖 🤝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein 8 Ahkam bayan kiye gaye hain. Guzishta post mein sab  hamne bayan kiye. Is Ayat ki Akhiri hissa aaj hazire khidmat hai:

(7) Neki mein madad karo na ke gunah mein sath do.

(8) Parhez o Taqwa ikhtiyar karo, nafarmani se bacho.

Is Ayat ke mutabiq Musalmano ko Neki mein ek doosre ki madad karni chahiye. Jaise Ghuraba, Miskeen ki madad karna. Islahi kaam mein madad karna. Deeni idaron, Taleemo idaron mein imdad karna Nekiyon mein shumaar hota hai.
Lekin jo gunah wa badi ke kamon mein imdad karega woh unhi gunehgaron​ mein shamil hoga.
Yahan Khums ki adaygi ki taraf bhi ishaara hai. Khums mein do ke huqooq ada hote hain. Ek Imam ka Haq hai aur doosra Ghareeb Sadaat ka Haq. Agar koi Khums nahi nikalta woh do ka Haq ghazb kar raha hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤝 💰
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*أنه من التقى ربه من اخوانك فى الدين و أخرج مما عليه إلى مستحقه، كان آمنا من الفتنة المبطلة، و محنها المظلمة المظلة و من بخل منهم بما أعاره الله من نعمة على من أمره بصلته، فإنه يكون خاسرا بذالك لاولاه و آخرته.*

_"Beshak ke jo shakhs apne Deeni bhai ke huqooq ke silsile mein Hukm e Ilahi ka ehteram kare aur apne zimme Maali huqooq ko iske mustaheq tak pahunchaye to aisa shakhs Batil raah ki taraf le jaane wale fitno se aur khatarnak balaon se mehfooz rahta hai, aur jo shakhs bukhl (kanjoosi) se kaam le aur Khuda Wande Alam ne jin Ne'maton ko uske pas Amanat rakha hai un mein se Mustaheq ko na de, to aisa shakhs Duniya mein ghata uthane wala hoga."_
(Ehtejaaj, Vol 3, P-325, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-177, H-8)
🤝
Imam Ali (as):
_"Neki ka hukm do aur khud bhi uspar amal karo. Buraai se roko aur khud bhi oos se ruko. Kyun ki humein buraai se rukne ke baad rokne ka hukm diya gaya hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v11, p323)
🤝
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Kisi ke saath ki gayi Neki ka Ajr aur nekiyo'n se pehle milta hai aur kisi pe kiye Zulm ki Sazaa aur gunaho'n se pehle milti hai."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*HARAM CHEEZEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (627) 🐷💉⚰

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*حُرِّمَتْ عَلَيْكُمُ الْمَيْتَةُ وَالدَّمُ وَلَحْمُ الْخِنْزِيرِ وَمَا أُهِلَّ لِغَيْرِ اللَّهِ بِهِ وَالْمُنْخَنِقَةُ وَالْمَوْقُوذَةُ وَالْمُتَرَدِّيَةُ وَالنَّطِيحَةُ وَمَا أَكَلَ السَّبُعُ إِلَّا مَا ذَكَّيْتُمْ وَمَا ذُبِحَ عَلَى النُّصُبِ وَأَنْ تَسْتَقْسِمُوا بِالْأَزْلَامِ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ فِسْقٌ ۗ* الْيَوْمَ يَئِسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ دِينِكُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِ ۚ الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الْإِسْلَامَ دِينًا ۚ *فَمَنِ اضْطُرَّ فِي مَخْمَصَةٍ غَيْرَ مُتَجَانِفٍ لِإِثْمٍ ۙ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_*"Tum par Haram kiya gaya hai Murdaar (Dead), Khoon (Blood), Suar ka gosht (Pork), aur woh Janwar jo Khuda ke siwa kisi aur ke naam par zabah kiya gaya ho, jo gala ghot kar ya chot kha kar ya bulandi se gir kar, ya takkar kha kar maraa ho, ya jise darindon ne phada ho siwai usi ke jise tumne zinda pa kar zabah kar liya ho aur wo jo kisi but kadah ke aastane (Mandir) par zabah kiya gaya ho aur jue ke teeron se taqseem (divide) karo ye bhi Haram hai. Ye sab af'al (action) fisq hain (abomination).*_
_Aaj ke Din Kafir tumhare Deen se mayus ho gaye hain lehaza tum unse na daro balke Mujhse Daro. Aaj ke Din Meine tumhare liye tumhara Din Mukammal kar diya hai hai aur Meine tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kar di aur tumhare liye Islam ko tumhare Deen ki haisiyat se qabool kar liya hai, (lehaza apni hudood o quyood ki pabandi karo aur Mu'ahedon par qaem raho)_
_*Albatta jo shakhs bhook se majboor ho kar un mein se koi cheez khaa le albatta uska gunah ki taraf mailan (inclination) na ho to beshak Allah Ma'af Karnewala aur Rahem Farmane Wala hai."*_
(Surah Ma'idah 3)

📚📖 🐷🐪🐃🐂🐐
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein 11 cheezon ko Haram qarar diya gaya hai:

(1) Murdaar (Dead)
(2) Khoon (Blood)
(3) Suar (Pork
(4) Woh Qurbani jis mein Allah ka zikr na ho.
Majoosi is tareeqo ko apnate the:
(5) l المنخنقة = Woh Janwar jo gala ghot ke mara ho.
(6) l الموقوذة = Woh jo bimari ki wajah se mara.
(7) l المتردية = Woh Janwar jo upar se gir kar mara.
(8) l النطيحة = Do Janwar ko jab ek doosre se ladaya ho, aur seengo se takra kar mare hon.
(9) Woh Jo Darindon ke hamle ki wajah se mar jaye.
(10) Mandir par bali dene wale.
(Khulasa Hadis Imam Baqir (as), Uyoonul Akhbar)
(11) Arab mein dastoor tha ke panse ke teeron ki madad se gosht taqseem karte the, jisko Allah ne Haram qadar diya. Unke yahan ye rasm raej thi ke Oont (Camel) naher karte the aur uske gosht ke 10 hisse banate the. Phir das admi us mein shamil hote aur inke pas 10 panse ke teer maujood hote the. 7 teer thode mude hote, 3 seedhe. Phir teeron ke zariye lottery hoti. Jin ke muqaddar mein seedhe teer aate unhe Oont ki qeemat ada karni padti aur gosht mein unka koi hissa nahi hota tha, baqi 7 logon mein gosht bat jata. Allah ne ise Haram qarar diya kiyonki ye ek tarah ka Juwa (Game of Chance) aur Lottery ki qism thi.
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
🐮
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Har woh Janwar jise kisi But (Idol), Murti ya kisi darakht ke liye zabah kiya jaye (Bali di jaye). Chunanche aisa Janwar Murdaar, Khoon aur Suar ke gosht ki tarah Garam hai aur Ayat (ka akhiri hissa) yani aisa shakhs zindagi bachane ki had tak Murdaar khaa sakta hai."_
Is ke jawab mein ke aadmi kab majboor hota hai, Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Jab tumhe Subah ki Roti na mile aur Shaam ki Roti na mile aur Zameen par khane ke qabool koi ghaas na mile to tum Murdaar kha sakte ho."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih)
🐮
Hazrat Ali (as), Imam Mohd Baqir (as), Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khoon aur Suar ke alawa sab Janwar pak hain, agar Janwar ke Kaan ya uski dum ya uski Aakhen harkat kar rahi hon to use zabah karke khana jaez hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🐮
Hazrat Ali (as), Imam Mohd Baqir (as), Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khoon aur Suar ke alawa sab Janwar pak hain, agar Janwar ke Kaan ya uski dum ya uski Aakhen harkat kar rahi hon to use zabah karke khana jaez hai."_
_"Halal Janwar jo upar se gira ya takraya ho, ya gala ghonta ho, agar woh abhi zinda ho, Ankhen jhabak raha ho aur paon mar raha ho ya dum hila raha ho to use zabah karke khao "_
(Noorus Saqlain, Majmaul Bayan, Tehzeebul Ahkam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍗🍤
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo koi ek lukma Haraam khayega uski 40 raato'n tak Namaz qubool nahi hogi aur 40 subah tak Dua mustajaab nahi hogi._"
(Noori - Dar as Salaam, p213)(The Prayer)

  ♦ _*KUFR KE MAYUSI KA DIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (628) 😫

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

حُرِّمَتْ عَلَيْكُمُ الْمَيْتَةُ وَالدَّمُ وَلَحْمُ الْخِنْزِيرِ وَمَا أُهِلَّ لِغَيْرِ اللَّهِ بِهِ وَالْمُنْخَنِقَةُ وَالْمَوْقُوذَةُ وَالْمُتَرَدِّيَةُ وَالنَّطِيحَةُ وَمَا أَكَلَ السَّبُعُ إِلَّا مَا ذَكَّيْتُمْ وَمَا ذُبِحَ عَلَى النُّصُبِ وَأَنْ تَسْتَقْسِمُوا بِالْأَزْلَامِ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ فِسْقٌ ۗ *الْيَوْمَ يَئِسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ دِينِكُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِ ۚ الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الْإِسْلَامَ دِينًا ۚ* فَمَنِ اضْطُرَّ فِي مَخْمَصَةٍ غَيْرَ مُتَجَانِفٍ لِإِثْمٍ ۙ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ.

_"Tum par Haram kiya gaya hai Murdaar (Dead), Khoon (Blood), Suar ka gosht (Pork), aur woh Janwar jo Khuda ke siwa kisi aur ke naam par zabah kiya gaya ho, jo gala ghot kar ya chot kha kar ya bulandi se gir kar, ya takkar kha kar maraa ho, ya jise darindon ne phada ho siwai usi ke jise tumne zinda pa kar zabah kar liya ho aur wo jo kisi but kadah ke aastane (Mandir) par zabah kiya gaya ho aur jue ke teeron se taqseem (divide) karo ye bhi Haram hai. Ye sab af'al (action) fisq hain (abomination)._
_*Aaj ke Din Kafir tumhare Deen se mayus ho gaye hain lehaza tum unse na daro balke Mujhse Daro. Aaj ke Din Meine tumhare liye tumhara Din Mukammal kar diya hai hai aur Meine tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kar di aur tumhare liye Islam ko tumhare Deen ki haisiyat se qabool kar liya hai, (lehaza apni hudood o quyood ki pabandi karo aur Mu'ahedon par qaem raho)*_
_Albatta jo shakhs bhook se majboor ho kar un mein se koi cheez khaa le albatta uska gunah ki taraf mailan (inclination) na ho to beshak Allah Ma'af Karnewala aur Rahem Farmane Wala hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 3)

📚📖 😫
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jahan is Ayat mein Halal o Haram ke Ahkam bayan kiye wahin is Ayat mein Janashin e Paighambar (saww) ka Ailan hua, taake ainda ke liye in Ahkam ka muhafiz is Duniya mein baqi rahe warna koi aur agar apni khud sakhta Janashini ka Ailan kare to woh Halale Muhammadi ko Haram aur Haram e Muhammadi ko Halal kar dega. Aur waqai mein baad e Shahadat e Rasool (saww) aisa hi hua, jab logon ne Rasoole Khuda ke muntakhab shuda Janashin se doori ikhtiyar ki ye batate hue ke Rasool (saww) to kisi ko bana kar gaye hi nahi.
Is Ayat mein 3 baton ka zikr hai:
(1) Kuffar is Roz Mayus ho gaye.
(2) Din Mukammal hua.
(3) Ne'mat e Ilahi tamam ho gayi.
(4) Khuda Wande Alam ne Deen e Islam ko Akheri Deen ke taur par qubool kiya.
Musalmano ki aksariyat ne aur Paid Tarikh dano ne is Ayat ke shane nuzool se chashm poshi ki. Isliye Mufasserin mein ikhtelaf paya jata hai.
Is Din ki ahmiyat itni hai ke kuchh Yahoodi aur Eisaiyon ne jab is Ayat ko suna to ye kaha ke agar hamari aasmani Kitabon mein aisi Ayat hoti to ham is Din ko Eid ka Din qarar dete.
(Tafsir Al Munar, Vol 6, P-155)
Ab sawal uthta hai woh kaunsa Din tha jis Din Deen Mukammal hua aur Kafir Mayus ho gaya.
Ye Options tarikh mein milte hain:
(1) Hujjat UL Wuda ka Arfe ka Din?
(2) Fateh Mecca ka Din?
(3) Surah Bara'at ki Ayat nuzool ka Din?
(4) Rasool (saww) ke Besat ka Din?
Ye 4 option sahi nahi hain Kiyonki inki tarikhen alag hain. Jabke Mufassir Ahle Sunnat Tafseer Fakhruddin Raazi, Tafseer Roohul Ma'ani aur Tafseer Al Munar  mein manqool ha: _"Ye Ayat ke nuzool ke baad Paighambar (saww) 81 Din se zyada din zinda nahi rahe."_ Is ke mutabiq ye Din 18 ZilHajj ka hota hai.
Is Din ki mazeed guftgu ainda post mein jari rahegi.

(To be Cont'd.....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😫
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_*"Jab Qaem Ale Muhammad (atfs) (Imam Mahdi) ka Zahoor hoga to Bani Umayya ki mayusi Inteha ko pahunch jayegi aur ye log Ale Muhammad (as) se mukammal taur par mayus ho jayenge."*_
(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

              ♦ _*GHADEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (629) 🕌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*....الْيَوْمَ يَئِسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ دِينِكُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِ ۚ الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الْإِسْلَامَ دِينًا ۚ....*

_*...Aaj ke Din Kafir tumhare Deen se mayus ho gaye hain lehaza tum unse na daro balke Mujhse Daro. Aaj ke Din Meine tumhare liye tumhara Din Mukammal kar diya hai hai aur Meine tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kar di aur tumhare liye Islam ko tumhare Deen ki haisiyat se qabool kar liya hai, (lehaza apni hudood o quyood ki pabandi karo aur Mu'ahedon par qaem raho)"...*_
(Surah Ma'idah: 3)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta post mein bataya tha ke Hazrat Ali (as) ki Vilayat ke Ailan se Kafiron ko mayusi hui. (Tafsir Ali Ibne Ibrahim)
Iski wajah ye hai ke unhe pata tha ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke koi Narina (gent) Aulad nahi hai. Jab ye wafat payenge to unki wafat ke sath Islam ka bhi khatma ho jayega. Lekin jab Ghadeer mein Hazrat Ali (as) ki Vilayat ka Ailan hua to unke mansoobon par pani phir gaya. Ab Kuffar ka daur khatm hua aur Munafiqat ke daur ki shuruaat hui.

Ye Ayat Rasoole Khuda ke Hujjatul Wuda ke baad Ghadeer e Khum mein nazil hui.
Ahle Sunnat ke bahut si kitabon mein waqea darj hai. Jaise:
(1) Kitabe Vilayat - Ibne Jurair Tabari.
(2) Kitab 'Ma Nazala minal Quran fi Ali (as)' Hafiz  Abu Naeem.
(3) Tarikh e Baghdadi mein Abu Huraira se Rivayat hai.
(4) Kitabul Haq, Vol 2, P-353.
References ki lambi list hai. Zyada detail ke liye Kitab Al Ghadeer - Allama Amini refer karen.
Yahan sirf khulasa bayan kar rahe hain.
Ye waqae ke mukammal hone ke baad ye Ayat nazil hui.
Ye waqea Allah ke is hukm ke baad amal mein aya jab isi Surah ki Ayat:67 (يا ايها الرسول بلغ ما أنزل اليك) nazil hui.

Imam Baqir (as):
_"Islam mein ek farz ke baad doosra farz nazil hota raha aur tamam faraez ke Akhir mein Vilayat ka Fareeza nazil hua. Phir ye Ayat nazil hui. Is ka maqsad ye hai ke iske baad Mein koi Faraez nazil nahi karoonga. Ab Maine tumhare liye Tamam Faraez mukammal kar diye. Aur Deen ki Takmeel Ali Ibne Abi Talib (as) ki Vilayat se hui."_
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚩
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*قلوبنا أوعية لمشية الله فإذا شاء الله شئنا، والله يقول: "و ما تشاؤون الا أن يشاء الله."*

_"Hamare dil Mashiyat e Ilahi ke liye zarf hain, agar Khuda Wande Alam kisi cheez ka irada kare aur usko chahe to ham bhi usi cheez ka irada karte hain aur usi ko chahte hain. Kiyonki Khuda Wande Alam ka irshad hai: "Tum nahi chahte magar wohi cheez jiska Khuda irada kare."_
(Sura Rajveer:29, AL Ghaiba Toosi, P-247, Biharul Anwaar Vol 25, P-337, H-16)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             *28th Shabaan 1438*
       *25th May 2017, Thursday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
              ♦ _*GHADEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (630) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الْيَوْمَ يَئِسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ دِينِكُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِ ۚ الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الْإِسْلَامَ دِينًا ۚ*

_*...Aaj ke Din Kafir tumhare Deen se mayus ho gaye hain lehaza tum unse na daro balke Mujhse Daro. Aaj ke Din Meine tumhare liye tumhara Din Mukammal kar diya hai hai aur Meine tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kar di aur tumhare liye Islam ko tumhare Deen ki haisiyat se qabool kar liya hai, (lehaza apni hudood o quyood ki pabandi karo aur Mu'ahedon par qaem raho)"...*_
(Surah Ma'idah: 3)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Musalmano mein 2 waqae aise guzre hain jis mein se ek waqea sab ko yad raha aur doosra bhula diya gaya. Ek hai Ghadeer, doosra hai Saqeefa. Ghadeer mein Quran ki ye Ayat nazil hui. Saqeefa ka waqea Rasoole Islam (saww) ki Shahadat par pesh aya. Jo log Saqeefa mein sharik the woh Rasool (saww) ke janaze mein sharik nahi the. Jabke Ghadeer mein sab sharik the. Dono ka maqsad ek hi tha 'Janashin e Rasool.'

Tarikh batati hai Ghadeer mein sawa lakh ka majma tha jis mein Ashaab aur Haji the. Rasool e Akram (saww) Akheri Hajj ke bad Ghadeer e Khum ke maqam par ruke. Beech jangle mein, tez garmi ki tapti sehra mein sab ko baithaya. Oont ke Kajawon (Saddle) ka Mimbar banaya. Us par Rasoole Akram (saww) ne tawil Khutba diya aur phir logon se sawal kiya:
الست اولى منكم...
Kiya mein tum sab se Awla (Master) nahi hun? Sab ne kaha بلى يا رسول الله 'Kiyon nahi'. Phir Aap (saww) ne Ali (as) ke bazoo ko pakad kar itna buland kiya ke Aapki (saww) baghle ki safedi namudar ho gayi aur buland awaz mein farmaya:
*من كنت مولاه فهذا على مولاه، اللهم وال من والاه و عاد من عادته.*
_"Jiska mein Maula hun uske ye Ali (as) Maula hai. Khudaya! Jo isse dosti rakhe Tu usse Dosti rakh, aur jo usse Dushmani rakhe Tu usse Dushmani rakh."_
(Rozatul Kafi, Khutba e Raseela)
Is tarah Aap (saww) ne apne Janashin ka Ailaan kiya. Phir sab ko hukm diya ke sab Ali (as) ko mubarakbad den.
Tarikh e Baghdadi (Sunni) mein Abu Huraira se naql karte hain ke waqae Ghadeer, Vilayat e Ali (as) ke Ahd o Paiman aur Umar ke *"بخ بخ يابن أبى طالب أصبحت مولاة و مولا كل مسلم."* ( _"Kiya kahne, Aye farzand e Abu Talib! Aap mere aur har Musalman ke Maula ho gaye"_) kahne ke baad ye Ayat اليوم اكملت nazil hui.
(Kitabul Haq, Vol 6, P-353, Abu Huraira se Rivayat)
Is ke baad Dua ke sath ye program jo ke 5 ghante ka tha khatm hua aur sab Haji lag bhag 3 din late apne ghar pahunche.

(To be Cont'd ......)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇🤚🏻🖐🏻
*Dua-e-Alawi Misri.*

*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*رب من ذا الذي دعاك فلم تجبه، و من ذا الذي سألك فلم تعطه، و من ذا الذي ناجاك فخيبته، أو تقرب إليك فأبعدته.*

_"Parwardigaar! Kaun hai aisa shakhs jisne Tujhse duayen mangi hon aur Tu ne uski Hajat rawai na ki ho, aur kaun hai aisa shakhs jisne Tujh se darkhwast ki ho lekin Tu ne usko Ataa' na kiya ho, aur kaun hai aisa shakhs jisne Tujh se Munajat ki ho aur Tu ne usko na Ummid kiya ho, ya khud ko Tujh se nazdeek karne ki koshish ki ho aur Tu ne usko door kar diya ho.?!"_
(Muhajjud Dawat, P281, Al Baladul Ameen, P-393, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 92, P-267, H-34)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (631) 🕌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الْيَوْمَ يَئِسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ دِينِكُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِ ۚ الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الْإِسْلَامَ دِينًا ۚ*

_*...Aaj ke Din Kafir tumhare Deen se mayus ho gaye hain lehaza tum unse na daro balke Mujhse Daro. Aaj ke Din Meine tumhare liye tumhara Din Mukammal kar diya hai hai aur Meine tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kar di aur tumhare liye Islam ko tumhare Deen ki haisiyat se qabool kar liya hai, (lehaza apni hudood o quyood ki pabandi karo aur Mu'ahedon par qaem raho)"...*_
(Surah Ma'idah: 3)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne is Ghadeer ke Program ke Khatm par Dua ki:
*اللهم وال من والاه و عاد من عاده و انصر من نصره و اخذل من خذله.*
_"Khudaya jo inse Dosti rakhe Tu bhi usse Dosti rakh aur jo unse Dushmani rakhe Tu in se bhi Dushmani rakh aur jo unki madad kare Tu bhi uski Madad kar aur jo unhe be yawaro madadgar​ chhod de Tu bhi use be yawaro madadgar chhod de."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Eid e Ghadeer ke Din ki Dua:
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Parwardigaar! Tere alawa koi Ma'bood nahi', aur Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) Tere And aur Tere Rasool hain aur Hazrat Ali (as) Momineen ke Ameer hain aur unki Vilayat ka Iqrar Teri Tauheed ka Itmam aur Teri Wahdaniyat ka Ikhlaas aur Tere Deen ki Takmeel aur Teri tamam Makhlooq par Teri Ne'mat o Fazl ki Takmeel ka Mazhar hai. Kiyonki Tu ne khud farmaya hai aur Tera Farman Haq hai: " Aaj Meine tumhare liye tumhare Deen Ko Kamil kiya aur tum par Apni Ne'mat tamam ki aur tumhare liye Islam ko bataur Deen pasand kiya." Parwardigaar! Tere liye Hamd hai ke Tu ne hamen apni Wahdaniyat ka Ikhlaas bakhsha kiyonki Tu ne hamen Wali ki dosti ki Hidayat ki hai jo Tere Nabi e Munzar ke baad Haadi hai aur Tu ne unki dosti ki wajah se Islam ko bataur e Deen pasand kiya."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam)

Inshallah baqi aur Tazkara Ayat 67 ke zel mein hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p160)
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):

(40 Hadith – Ghadeer)

             *18th ZilHajj 1438*
     *10th September 2017, Sunday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
                  ♦ _*GHADEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

*الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰہِ الَّذِی جَعَلَنا مِنَ الْمُتَمَسِّکینَ بِوِلایَۃِ صدیق الاکبر و فاروق الاعظم مولای و مولانا ٲَمِیرِ الْمُؤْمِنِین علی ابن ابی طالبَ وَالْاََئِمَّۃ المعصومین عَلَیْھِمُ اَلسَّلَامُ*

Start your Day by reading Quran: (730) (Cont'd ......)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الْيَوْمَ يَئِسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ دِينِكُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِ ۚ*
*الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الْإِسْلَامَ دِينًا ۚ*

_*Aaj ke Din Kuffaron ko tumhare Deen ki taraf poori Mayus ho chuki hai, lehaza tum unse na daro balke Mujhse Daro."*_
_*"Aaj Maine tumhare Deen ko tumhare liye Mukammal kar diya, aur apni Ne'mat tum par tamam kar di aur tumhare liye Islam ko tumhare Deen ki hasiyat se qubool kar liya....*"_
(Surah Maeda: 3)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Wo Ailan wa announcement ke Allah ne jo itni badi tambi ki thi ke agar ye na kiya to Risaalat ka koi kam anjaam nahi diya, aaj woh anjam pa gaya.
Ameerul Mo'meneen Hazrat Ali (as) ko logon ka Maula hone ka Ailan kiya. (Maula Means Master, Mutawalli, Trustee etc.) Rasoole Akram (saww) ne apne baad Islam ki bagdor Hazrat Ali (as) ko di. Ye kaam sawa lakh ke Hajiyon/Ashaab ke saamne kiya, yani itne log is baat ke gawah hain.
Ye waqea itna Aashkaar hai ke Munafeqeen ko iska chhupana mushkil ho gaya. Jab waqae ki haqiqat sabit hai to Maula ke maani ki taujeeh shuru kardi. Yani Rasool (saww) ne Ali (as) se dosti ki hidayat di. Agar aisa hota to ye Ailan is tarah se na hota balke Mecca mein ek hadis bayan kar di jaati, lekin kis situation mein ye ailan hua ye ham bata chuke hain.
Ailan ke baad Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Dua ki jo bayan kar chuke hain.
Phir ye Ayat nazil hui: (5:3)
*Aaj ke Din* (18th ZilHajj, 10 AH, Thursday, Asr ke waqt, 1,20,000 ke majme mein) Ailane Vilayat e Ali (as) hua.  Ayat mein hai: ye dekh Kafir mayus ho gaya, qare'een bata sakte hain us majme koi Kafir tha? Ye Ayat Rasool ki us hadis ko confirm kar rahi hai ke jis ne Ali (as) ki Vilayat ka inkar kiya woh Kafir hai. Isliye Ali (as) ka Munkir sirf Kafir hi ho sakta hai.
*Aaj* Deen Mukammal hua, yani Vilayat e Ali (as) ke baghair Deen Mukammal nahi hua tha.
*Aaj* Ne'maten Tamam hui, yani Vilayat e Ali (as) Ne'mat hai. Isliye ham Al Hamd mein kahte hain Bare Ilaha hame us raaste par chala jis par Tu ne Apni Ne'maten nazil ki.
*Aaj* Allah is Deen e Islam se Raazi hua. Kiya isse pahle jo Deen tha woh Islam nahi tha? Lekin aaj Khuda is Islam se Raazi hua jise ham Ghadeeri Islam kah sakte hain. Yani woh Islam jis mein Vilayat e Ali (as) ho. Yehi Asl Deen hai.
*Aaj* ke Din Shaitan ka khwab chakna choor ho gaya. Iska tazkara baad mein karenge. Pas Ghadeer mein ye Ayat nazil hui jis par tamam Ummat e Muslema ka ittefaq hai.
Sawal yehi uthta hai ke jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Ali (as) ko apna Janashin bana diya to phir kaise kah diya ke Rasool (saww) ne kisi ko apna Janashin nahi banaya (Sahih Muslim, Kitabul Amarah)
Sirf itna hi nahi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne ek aur hukm diya. Ek Tent banaya gaya, 3 din qayam raha, sab ne ek ek karke Ali (as) ke haath par bayat ki, Mubarakbad di. Hazrat Abu Bakar, Hazrat Umar ne Aap se haath milaya aur farmaya:
*بخ بخ لك يابن أبي طالب ، أصبحت مولاي ومولى كل مسلم*
_"Mubarak ho, aye Ibne Abi Talib aap tamam Mo'meneen wa Momenat ke Maula ho gaye."_
(Tarikh Ibne Asakir)
Is Mubarak mauqe par baqaeda Qaseeda Khwani hui, Mashoor Shayer Hasaan bin Sabit ne is munasibat se bahut umda Qaseeda padha.
*فقال له قم يا عليُّ فإنَّني*
*رضيتك من بعدي إماماً و هادياً*
Unhone apne Ashaar mein Ali (as) ko apna Hadi wa Imam se mukhatib kiya. Agar unke Ashaar ghalat hote to Rasool (saww) zaroor tokte. Rasool (saww) ka unke Ashaar ko dad o tehseen se nawazna Ali (as) ki Imamat ki tasdeeq ke liye kafi hai.
(Ye sab Kutub e Ahle Sunnat mein maujood hain, ek lambi list hai jiski yaha gunjaish nahi.)
(To be Cont'd ........)

🌻 *EID-E-GHADEER MUBARAK* 🌻
***********************************
⚜⚜⚜

*الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰہِ الَّذِی جَعَلَنا مِنَ الْمُتَمَسِّکینَ بِوِلایَۃِ مولانا ٲَمِیرِ الْمُؤْمِنِین علی ابن ابی طالبَ وَالْاََئِمَّۃ المعصومین عَلَیْھِمُ اَلسَّلَامُ*

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ إِخْوَةٌ فَأَصْلِحُوا بَيْنَ أَخَوَيْكُمْ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُرْحَمُونَ*

_*"Momin to ek doosre ke bhai hain, lehaza apne bhaiyon ke darmiyan talluqaat ko durust karo aur Allah se Daro, ummid hai ke tum par Rahem kiya jaye."*_
(Surah Hujurat: 10)

📚📖 🤝
Aaj Yaum-e-Ghadeer Ahdo Paiman ka Din hai. Ghadeer ke maidan mein bhi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne logon se Ali (as) ki Vilayat par Ahdo Paiman liya. Sab Musalmanon ko ek doosre ka bhai bataya.
Jaisa ke Rivayaat mein hai jisne Vilayat-e-Ali (as) ka iqraar kiya woh Momin hai. Aur aaj ke Din ye zaroori hai ke har brother e Momin doosre brother e Momin ka haath mein haath de kar ye Ahd kare ke woh bradari ke Haq par qaem rahega. Isliye aaj ke Din Seegha-e-Ukhuwat padhne ki zyada takeed ki hai.
Har Momin ek doosre ka haath pakde aur ye Seegha padhe:

*وَاخَيْتُكَ فِي اللّٰهِ وَ صَافَيْتُكَ فِي اللّٰهِ وَ صَافَحْتُكَ فِي اللّٰهِ وَ عَاهَدْتُ اللّٰهَ وَ مَلَاۤئِكَتَهُ وَ كُتُبَهُ وَ رُسُلَهُ وَ اَنْبِيَاۤءَهُ وَ الْاَئِمَّةَ الْمَعْصُوْمِيْنَ عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ عَلٰىۤ اَنِّيْۤ اِنْ كُنْتُ مِنْ اَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ وَ الشَّفَاعَةِ وَ اُذِنَ لِيْ بِاَنْ اَدْخُلَ الْجَنَّةَ لَاۤ اَدْخُلُهَاۤ اِلَّا وَ اَنْتَ مَعِيْ۔*
_"Main Allah ki khatir tumse bhaichargi ka ailan karta hun, Mein Allah ki khatir tumse dostana Ma'melaat rakhta hun, Mein Allah ki khatir tumse Musafeha (shake Hand) karta hun, Mein Allah, Malaika, Uski Kitab, Uske Rasool o Anbiya aur Aimma (as) se Ahd karta hun ke agar mein Ahle Jannat mein shumar hua aur mujhe doosron ki Shafa'at karne ki ijazat mili, Jannat mein dakhil hone ki ijazat mili to mein tab tak dakhli na hunga jab tak tum mere saath shamil hun."_
(Aamaal-e-Ghadeer)

Isse aapko andaza ho gaya hoga ke ek Momin doosre Momin kis tarah se bhai hota hai. Isliye zaroori hai ke jab ham ye Seegha padh kar iqraar kar rahe hain to is Aqd par kam se kam ek saal tak baqi rahen aur apni doosre bhai ko aziyyat na pahunchayen aur ek doosre ki hurmat ka khayal rakhen.

Bare Ilaha hame Vilayat e Ali Ibne Talib (as) par qaem o daem rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (662) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَسْأَلُونَكَ مَاذَا أُحِلَّ لَهُمْ ۖ قُلْ أُحِلَّ لَكُمُ الطَّيِّبَاتُ ۙ وَمَا عَلَّمْتُمْ مِنَ الْجَوَارِحِ مُكَلِّبِينَ تُعَلِّمُونَهُنَّ مِمَّا عَلَّمَكُمُ اللَّهُ ۖ فَكُلُوا مِمَّا أَمْسَكْنَ عَلَيْكُمْ وَاذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ ۖ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ*
(Surah Maeda: 4)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Abhi tak Ramzanul Mubarak mein hamne Ramazan, Roza, Qur'an ke mutalliq 30 Ayaten pesh ki.
Ramazan ke pahle hamara Silsila bayan Surah Maeda ke mutalliq tha jo ke Ghadeer ke topic par khatm hua tha. Surah Maeda ki Ayaten Shikar karne, Halal wa Haram khane ke mutalliq thi. Konsa Janwar ham kha sakte hain.
Inshallah Kal se ham usi bayan ko jari rakhenge.

Apse darkhwast hai ke tawajjo se hamare bayan padhte rahen.

           ♦ _*HALAL GOSHT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (662)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَسْأَلُونَكَ مَاذَا أُحِلَّ لَهُمْ ۖ قُلْ أُحِلَّ لَكُمُ الطَّيِّبَاتُ ۙ وَمَا عَلَّمْتُمْ مِنَ الْجَوَارِحِ مُكَلِّبِينَ تُعَلِّمُونَهُنَّ مِمَّا عَلَّمَكُمُ اللَّهُ ۖ فَكُلُوا مِمَّا أَمْسَكْنَ عَلَيْكُمْ وَاذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ ۖ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ*

_"Woh Aap (saww) se sawal karte hain ke unke liye kiya Halal kiya gaya hai? Aap kah den ke tumhare liye tamam Pakeeza Cheezen Halal ki gayi hai aur Shikari Janwar jo tumne shikar ke liye sadha rakhe hain (trained to hunt) aur jo Tareeqe Khuda ne tumhe bataye hain un mein se kuchh tumne un Janwaron ko bhi sikhaya ho to ye Shikari Janwar jis Shikar ko tumhare liye pakad rakhen usko khao aur Janwar ko shikar par chhodte waqt Allah ka Naam le liya karo aur Khuda se darte raho. Beshak Allah bahut jald hisab lene wala hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 4)

📚📖 🐺
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Surah Maida ki guzishta Ayat no.3 mein Haram Janwar ka zikr hua tha. Is Ayat mein un janwar ka zikr hai jo Halal tareeqe se zibah hone par hamare liye unka khana jaez hai.
Ye fiqhi Masael hain isliye is silsile ke kuchh rivayat aur Ay. Sistani DZ ke Ahkam ham pesh karte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

Imam Sadiq (as) se Jameel bin Daraj ne poochha:
_"Ek Shakhs apna Kutta shikar par chhodta hai. Kutta shikar ko pakad lata hai. Admi ke pas chhuri nahi hai ke use zibah kare to agar wo shikar ko us waqt tak Kutte ke qabze mein rahne de ke woh us shikar ko maar daale to kiya aise Shikar ka gosht Halal hai?"_
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_*Koi harj nahi. Allah farmata hai (5:4) "Jo woh tumhare liye pakad layen use khao." Albatta jise Cheetah maar daale to uska khana Sahih nahi hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🐺
Imam Sadiq (as) se Shikari Kutte ke bare mein poochha to Imam ne farmaya ke unka pakda hua Shikar khao.
Jab raavi ne poochha ke agar usne us mein se kuchh khaa liya ho to?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Usne (Kutte) wo shikar tumhare liye pakda hi nahi apne liye pakda hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

---------------------------------------------------------
*TOPIC: HUNTING - SHIKAAR*
*************************************
_*Shikari Kutte ka Shikar karna*_

2618. Agar Shikari Kutta kisi Halaal gosht wale jangali janawar ka shikar kare to us haiwan ka paak hone aur Halal hone ke liye chhe (6) sharten hain:

1. Kutta aise sadha hua ho ki jab bhi use shikar pakadne ke liye bheja jae chala jae aur jab use jaane se roka jae to ruk jae. Lekin agar shikar paas hone aur shikar ko dekhne ke baad use jaane se roka jae aur na ruke to koi harj nahin hai aur lazim nahin hai ki uski aadat aisi ho ki jab tak maalik na pahunche shikaar ko na khae balki agar iski aadat yeh ho ki apane maalik ke aane se pahale shikaar se kuchh kha le to bhi harj nahin hai aur isi tarah agar yah shikaar ka khoon peene ki aadat ho to ishnal nahin.

2. Uska maalik use shikaar ke lie bheje, aur agar woh apane aap hi shikaar ke peechhe jae aur kisi Jaanaear ka shikaar kar le to us hauwan ka khaana haraam hai. balki agar kutta apane shikaar ke peechhe lag jai aur baad mein uska maalik baang lagae taake woh jaldi shikaar tak pahunche to haalanki woh maalik kee awaz ke vajah se tej bhaage phir bhi ehatiyaat ke aadhaar par is shikaar ko khaane se bachna chaahie hai.

3. Jo shakhs Kutta shikaar ke peechhe lagae zaroori hai ke Musalamaan ho is tafseel ke mutabiq jo hathiyaar se shikaar karne ke sharayet mein bayaan ho chuki hai.

4. Kutta shikar ke peechhe bhejate waqt shikaari Allah Ta'ala ka Naam le aur agar jaan boojh kar Allah Ta'ala ka Naam na le to wo shikaar haraam lekin agar bhool jae to harj nahin.

5. Shikaar Kutte ke kaatne se jo zakhm aae woh isse mare. isliye​ agar Kutta shikaar gala ghont de ya shikaar daudne ya dar jaane ki wajah se mar jae to Halal nahin hai.

6. Jis shakhs ne Kutte ko shikaar ke peechhe bheja ho agar woh (shikaar kiye gae haiwan ke paas) tab pahunche jab woh mar gaya ho ya agar zinda ho to use zibah karne ke lie waqt nahin ho. Lekin shikari ke paas pahunchana ghair mamooli takheer ki wajah se na ho. Aur agar aise waqt pahunche jab use zibah karane ke liye waqt ho lekin woh Jaanavar ko zibah na kare yahaan tak ki woh mar jai to woh jaanavar Halaal nahin hai.

      ♦ _*AHLE KITAB KA KHANA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (663) 🍵🍪

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الْيَوْمَ أُحِلَّ لَكُمُ الطَّيِّبَاتُ ۖ وَطَعَامُ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ حِلٌّ لَكُمْ وَطَعَامُكُمْ حِلٌّ لَهُمْ* ۖ وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ إِذَا آتَيْتُمُوهُنَّ أُجُورَهُنَّ مُحْصِنِينَ غَيْرَ مُسَافِحِينَ وَلَا مُتَّخِذِي أَخْدَانٍ ۗ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِالْإِيمَانِ فَقَدْ حَبِطَ عَمَلُهُ وَهُوَ فِي الْآخِرَةِ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ.

_*"Aaj tumhare liye Halal kar di gayi hain aur Ahle Kitab ka khana tumhare liye Halal hai aur tumhara khana unke liye Halal hai* aur Paak Daaman Aurten tumhare liye Halal hain khwah unka talluq Ahle Imaan ke giroh se ho ya un qaumon se ho jinhen tum se qabl Kitab di gayi hai. Bashart ye ke tum unke Mehr ada karke Nikah mein unke muhafiz bano na ye ke Azad Shahwat Rani karne lago (Romance Freely) ya chori chhupe Ashnaiyan (Secret Love affair) karo aur jo bhi Imaan ka inkaar kare to uska saara  nek amal akarat ho jayega aur woh Akherat mein ghate mein rahega."_
(Surah Maeda: 5)

📚📖 🍵🍪
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
'Aaj ke Din' se murad kuchh Mufasserin Arfah ya Fateh Khaibar ka Din kahte hain lekin haqiqat mein ye Din Yaum e Ghadeer ka Din hai.
Ahle Kitab (Jews & Christians) ke khane ke bare mein zyada tar Ahle Sunnat maante hain ke har tarah ka khana jaez hai. Lekin Shia Aqeeda jo Aimma Tahereen (as) ke mutabiq hai maante hain ke gosht ko chhod kar.
Rivayaton se pata chalta hai ke ye sookha (dry) khana se murad hai. Is lihaz se Ahkam mein hame kuchh chhot di gayi hai.
Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen.
Ahkam doosre post mein pesh honge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*TOPIC:  KHANE KE AHKAM*
*************************************
_*Questions & Answers*_

_1. Sawal: Christians ke desh mein gosht aur doosre khane ki cheezen khaane ka kya hukm hai?_

Jawab: Gosht tazkaya shuda ho maloom hona chaahiye.
-------

_Sawal: Kafiron ke saath khaana khaane ka kya hukm hai?_

Jawab: Agar Kafir gair Kitaabi ho aur usake haath ya shareer ko nami khane ko chhoo jae to woh khaana Najis ho jaega aur khaana khaana haraam ho jaega, isake alaawa Najis nahin hai aur agar nami chhoo jaane ke baad paak hone mein shak karen ya Kafir Ahle Kitab ho to Ghiza taahir hai.
--------

_Question: Can I eat Christians' foods that contain meat?_

Answer: All kinds of food with the exception of meat, fat, and their extracts are permissible for a Muslim, even if he doubts that it might contain something which is forbidden for him to eat or doubts that its cook may have been a non-kitabi (non-Christian) individual.
--------

_Question: Can I eat at the house of Ahle Kitab even though their books aren't the true Bible and Torah?_

Answer: If their food is made from the meat of an animal which has not been slaughtered according to Islamic rules, it is not permissible; otherwise, there is no problem.

--------
_*Condition of Slaughter:*_
Answer: There are certain conditions for the slaughtering of an animal. They are as follows:-
1. A person, a man or a woman, who slaughters an animal must be a Muslim. An animal can also be slaughtered by a Muslim child who is mature enough to distinguish between good and bad, but not by non-Muslims other than Ahle Kitab, _*or a person belonging to those sects who are classified as Kafir, like, Nawasib - the enemies of Ahlul Bait (as).*_ In fact, even if Ahle Kitab non-Muslim slaughters an animal, as per precaution, it will not be halal, even if he utters 'Bismillah'.

      ♦ _*AHLE KITAB SE NIKAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (664) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

الْيَوْمَ أُحِلَّ لَكُمُ الطَّيِّبَاتُ ۖ وَطَعَامُ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ حِلٌّ لَكُمْ وَطَعَامُكُمْ حِلٌّ لَهُمْ ۖ *وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ إِذَا آتَيْتُمُوهُنَّ أُجُورَهُنَّ مُحْصِنِينَ غَيْرَ مُسَافِحِينَ وَلَا مُتَّخِذِي أَخْدَانٍ ۗ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِالْإِيمَانِ فَقَدْ حَبِطَ عَمَلُهُ وَهُوَ فِي الْآخِرَةِ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ.*

_"Aaj tumhare liye tamam Pakeeza Cheezen Halal kar di gayi hain aur Ahle Kitab ka khana tumhare liye Halal hai aur tumhara khana unke liye Halal hai *aur Paak Daaman Aurten tumhare liye Halal hain khwah unka talluq Ahle Imaan ke giroh se ho ya un qaumon se ho jinhen tum se qabl Kitab di gayi hai. Bashart ye ke tum unke Mehr ada karke Nikah mein unke muhafiz bano na ye ke Azad Shahwat Rani karne lago (Romance Freely) ya chori chhupe Ashnaiyan (Secret Love affair) karo aur jo bhi Imaan ka inkaar kare to uska saara  nek amal akarat ho jayega aur woh Akherat mein ghate mein rahega."*_
(Surah Maeda: 5)

📚📖 👰🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat ke pahle hisse mein Ahle Kitab ke khane ka bayan hua. Isi Ayat ke doosre hisse mein Shaadi ka tazkara hai. Shaadi us Aurat se ki jae jo Paak Daaman ho.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Word محصنات lafzi means Shauhardar Auraten aur isse murad Pakdaman Auraten mani jati hain. "_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih)

Allah ne is Ayat mein ye ishaara kiya ki jis Aurat ko bhi tum chahte ho usse baqaeda Nikah karo shart ye hai ke woh Mominah Paak Daaman ho chahe Ahle Kitab mein se ho. (Agar woh hamare Aqeede par aa jaye). Ye nahi ke kisi bhi Aurat ke saath affair chalao, ghalat kaam karo. Aaj ki Duniya mein jabke Sex bahut aam hai. Aise log apne entertainment ke khatir Aurat ka beja istemal karte hai, ek chhodi-doosri pakdi, ye kaam chalta rahta hai. Islam ne Aurat ko Izzat bakhshi hai na ke uske saath khela jae. Islam aise Western Culture ki mazammat karta hai.

Is Ayat se ye nahi samjh lena chahiye ke ham Ahle Kitab se Shaadi kar sakte hain. Ye Ayat ko doosri Ayat ne mansookh kar diya hai.
Rivayat mulaheza ho:

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"l *وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ*
ye Ayat masnookh hai.
*وَلَا تُمْسِكُوا بِعِصَمِ الْكَوَافِرِ*
[Surah Mumtahana 10]
Ye Ayat Nasikh hai jo pahli Ayat ko cancel kar rahi hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)

Is silsile mein Fiqhi Masael bhi hain jo ke Ahkam ke next post mein mulaheza farmayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

Imam Sadiq (as) se Raavi ne sawal kiya ke ek Momin Jew ya Christian se Nikah karna chahe to kiya hukm hai?

Raavi ne kaha: "Use usse Mohabbat (Love) ho gayi hai."

_"Agar woh aisa karta hai to use Sharaab noshi aur Suar ka gosht khane se rok de. Aise Shakhs ke Deen mein kamzori payi jati hai."_
(Means agar woh itna chahta hai to usko apni Deen par kiyon nahi laya.)
(Noorus Saqlain)

*AHKAM TODAY*
(Ref: Tauzeehul Masael By Ayatullah Al Sistani DZ)
(http://www.al-sistani.org/urdu/book/61/3637/)
---------------------------------------------------------
*TOPIC:  NIKAH KE AHKAM*
*************************************
_*Questions & Answers*_

_Sawal: Main kaam ke silasile se teen maheene Japan mein akele rahane par majboor hun, jabki apane nazar mein Ahle Kitab ke alaawa doosre mazhab ki Aurat se Mut'ah jayz nahin hai aur Ahle Kitab se Mut'ah ke liye Biwi ki ijazat hona zaroori hai to kya majboori ki haalat mein Biwi ki ijazat ke bina kisi Kafir Aurat se Mut'ah kiya ja sakata hai?_

Jawab: Ayatullaah Sistani Daam Zillahu, Biwi ki ijazat ke saath Ahle Kitab se Mut'ah mai, Ehtiyaat ke qael hain, Aap is Masleh mein kisi aur Aalam ki Taqleed kar sakate hain.

_Sawal: Bairooni Mumalik (Foreign Countries) ke pesh aane wale safaron mein gunah se bachane ke liye, kya main Biwi ki ijazat ke bagair Ahl Kitab Aurat se Mut'ah kar sakta hun?_

Jawab: Jaez nahin hai magar yeh ki woh Musalamaan ho jae.

_Sawal: Kiya Ahle Kitab se Mut'ah ke waqt Seegha padhna zaroori hai jabki woh is hukm ko nahin jaante? Aur kiya Badkaar Aurat se Mut'ah kiya ja sakta hai agar dukhool na kiya jae to kya hukm hai?_

Jawab: (A) Seegha padhna zaroori hai agarche woh Arabi ke alaawa kisi aur zaban mein hi kiyon na ho aur use Mut'ah ka mafhoom samajhna zaroori hai.
(B) Agar woh Badkar Aurat Zinaah mein mashhoor ho (yani is kaam se aba na rakhti har kisi ke saath tayyar ho) to Ehatiyaat e Wajib ki bina par uske Tauba kar lene se pahle usse Shaadi nahin karna chaahiye agarche dukhool na karna ho to tab bhi.

_Question: A Muslim man who is married to a Muslim woman migrated from his country. After a lengthy stay in the West country, he wants to embark on temporary marriage with a woman from Ahlul Kitab just a few days after divorcing his Muslim wife. Is this permissible for him, espeually when his Muslim wife is still in her waiting period (al-‘idda)?_

Answer: The temporary marriage mentioned​ in the question is considered invalid because the wife who is in the waiting period of a revocable divorce is still considered as a wife. It has just been mentioned that to temporary marry an Ahlul Kitab woman while one has a Muslim wife is not permissible [as a matter of compulsory precaution].

_Question: A Muslim couple got separated for a long time. Is it permissible for him to marry, temporarily or permanently, a woman from Ahlul Kitab without the knowledge of his Muslim wife? Is it permissible for him to marry, with the permission of his Muslim wife?_

Answer: For a Muslim man to marry a woman from Ahlul Kitab permanently is against the compulsory precaution in any circumstance. And his temporary marriage to a Jewish or a Christian woman is allowed, only if he is not already married to a Muslim wife. If he has a Muslim wife, temporary marriage with an Ahlul Kitab woman is not permissible without her consent; nay, even with her consent, it is not permissible, based on compulsory precaution.

_Question: Is it permissible for a Muslim man to consummate temporary marriage contract with a Christian or Jewish woman?_

Answer: Yes, it is permissible.

                    ♦ _*WUZU*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (665) 💦

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا قُمْتُمْ إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ فَاغْسِلُوا وُجُوهَكُمْ وَأَيْدِيَكُمْ إِلَى الْمَرَافِقِ وَامْسَحُوا بِرُءُوسِكُمْ وَأَرْجُلَكُمْ إِلَى الْكَعْبَيْنِ ۚ*وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ جُنُبًا فَاطَّهَّرُوا ۚ وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ أَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مِنَ الْغَائِطِ أَوْ لَامَسْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَلَمْ تَجِدُوا مَاءً فَتَيَمَّمُوا صَعِيدًا طَيِّبًا فَامْسَحُوا بِوُجُوهِكُمْ وَأَيْدِيكُمْ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ لِيَجْعَلَ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنْ حَرَجٍ وَلَٰكِنْ يُرِيدُ لِيُطَهِّرَكُمْ وَلِيُتِمَّ نِعْمَتَهُ عَلَيْكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ)

_*"Aye Imaanwalo! Jab tum Namaz ke liye utho to apne moo aur haath kohniyon tak dho lo aur apne saron aur takhno tak paon ka Masah kiya karo.* Agar Halat e Janabat mein ho to Taharat (Ghusl) kar lo. Aur agar tum beemar ya safar mein ho ya tum mein se koi rafa hajat (relieve from toilet/urine) karke aye ya Auraton se hambistari (Sexual Intercourse) ki ho aur tumko Paani na mil sake to Paak Khaak se Tayammum kar lo aur Tayammum mein apne moo aur haathon ka Masah kar lo. Allah tum par kisi tarah ki tangi musallat karna nahi chahta. Woh ye chahta hai ke tumhe Paak o Pakeezah kar de aur tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kare taake tum shukr guzar ban jao."_
(Surah Maeda: 6)

📚📖 💦
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
_*Wuzu ka Tareeka:*_

Imam Baqir (as) se poochha ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) kaise Wuzu karte the?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Aap (saww) ne pani ke bartan se dayan haath dal kar chullu Paani bhara aur Chehra dhoya._
_Phir Aap (saww) ne bayan haath Paani mein dala aur ek chullu Paani bhar kar apne dahne bazoo (haath) par dala aur kohniyon se dhona shuru kiya aur hatheli par dhona khatm kiya._
_Aap (saww) ne Hatheliyon se dhone ki ibteda karke kohniyon par ikhtetam nahi kiya._
_Phir Aap (saww) ne Dahne haath ki hatheli mein Paani ka chullu liya aur isse bayen haath ko Kohniyon se dhona shuru kiya aur ise hatheliyon tak dhoya._
_Iske baad Aap (saww) ne haathon ki usi tari se Sar aur Paon ka Masah kiya._
_Naya Paani istemal na kiya._
_Phir Aap (saww) ne farmaya: Apni Ungliyan​ joote ke tasme ke andar dakhil na kare._
_Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai (5:6)."_
Raavi ne poochha Takhne kiya hain?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Isse Paon ka buland hissa murad liya gaya hai."_
Phir sawal kiya ek ek Paani chullu kafi hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Agar chullu achhi tarah bhar lo to ek hi kafi hai jabke do chullu se iski takmeel ho jati hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain, Raavi Amr bin Azeena)

Is silsile ke Fiqhi Masael Ahkam ke Section mein mulaheza farmayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💦
Imam Reza (as):
_"Wuzu ka hukm isliye diya gaya hai aur Ibaadat ki ibteda isse isliye ki gayi hai taake Bande jab Bargarh e Ilahi mein khada ho aur Munajat kare to Paak o Pakeezah hon, iske Ahkam par karband hain aur aaloodgiyon (Dirt) aur Nijasaton se door hain. Iske alawa Wuzu ke sabab se Neend aur Susti ke asaraat Insaan se door ho jate hain nez ye isliye hai taake Dil Dargah e Khuda wandi mein khade hone ke liye Roshni aur Pakeezgi hasil kar le."_
(Wasaelus Shia, Vol 1, P-257)

                 ♦ _*GHUSL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (665) 💦

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا قُمْتُمْ إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ فَاغْسِلُوا وُجُوهَكُمْ وَأَيْدِيَكُمْ إِلَى الْمَرَافِقِ وَامْسَحُوا بِرُءُوسِكُمْ وَأَرْجُلَكُمْ إِلَى الْكَعْبَيْنِ ۚ *وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ جُنُبًا فَاطَّهَّرُوا ۚ* وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ أَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مِنَ الْغَائِطِ أَوْ لَامَسْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَلَمْ تَجِدُوا مَاءً فَتَيَمَّمُوا صَعِيدًا طَيِّبًا فَامْسَحُوا بِوُجُوهِكُمْ وَأَيْدِيكُمْ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ لِيَجْعَلَ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنْ حَرَجٍ وَلَٰكِنْ يُرِيدُ لِيُطَهِّرَكُمْ وَلِيُتِمَّ نِعْمَتَهُ عَلَيْكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ.

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Jab tum Namaz ke liye utho to apne moo aur haath kohniyon tak dho lo aur apne saron aur takhno tak paon ka Masah kiya karo. *Agar Halat e Janabat mein ho to Taharat (Ghusl) kar lo.* Aur agar tum beemar ya safar mein ho ya tum mein se koi rafa hajat (relieve from toilet/urine) karke aye ya Auraton se hambistari (Sexual Intercourse) ki ho aur tumko Paani na mil sake to Paak Khaak se Tayammum kar lo aur Tayammum mein apne moo aur haathon ka Masah kar lo. Allah tum par kisi tarah ki tangi musallat karna nahi chahta. Woh ye chahta hai ke tumhe Paak o Pakeezah kar de aur tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kare taake tum shukr guzar ban jao."_
(Surah Maeda: 6)

📚📖 💦
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Namaz ke pahle Wuzu ya Ghusl karna zaroori hai. Jo ham pahle zikr kar chuke hain.
Sawal hota hai ke Paishab (Urine) ke baad Ghusl nahi hai jabke Mani (Semen) kharij hone par hai.
Science aur Doctors ke mutabiq jism ke jism mein do Nervous System hain Sympathetic aur Para-sympathetic. Pahla tezi paida karta, active banata hai, jabke doosra raftar ko sust (lazy) banata hai. Ek accelerate karta hai to doosra break lagata hai. Isliye jinsi urooj (sexual climax) par aisa active haalat paida hoti hai jo poore badan ke nizam ko asar andaaz karti hai. Is haalat ko normal karne ke liye poore badan par paani dalna zaroori hai.
Yehi baat rivayat mein bhi hai:
Imam Reza (as):
*إن الجنابة خارجة من كل جسده فلذلك وجب عليه تطهير جسده كله.*
_"Janabat sare badan se kharij hoti hai lehaza poore badan ko dhoya jaye."_
(Wasailus Shia, Vol 1, P-466)

Is silsile ke Fiqhi Masael Ahkam ke Section mein mulaheza farmayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💦
Rasoole Akram (saww):
_"Jab Adam (as) ne darakht ka phal khaya to uske asaraat unki ragon, baalon aur skin tak pahunche the. Jab koi shakhs apni Biwi se jinsi khwahish (sex) ki takmeel karta hai to uske rag o baal se madda manoya (semen) nikalta hai isliye Allah ne zuriyyat e Adam (generation) par roze Qayamat tak Ghusl-e-Janabat farz kiya. Jahan tak Paishab (Urine) ka talluq hai to wo Admi ke piye hue Paani ki hi badli hui shakl hoti hai aur Paikhana (Stool) insaan ki ghaza ka fuzla (excreta) hota hai, isi liye Paishab aur Paikhana par Allah ne Wuzu wajib kiya hai."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

              ♦ _*TAYAMMUM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (667) 💦

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا قُمْتُمْ إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ فَاغْسِلُوا وُجُوهَكُمْ وَأَيْدِيَكُمْ إِلَى الْمَرَافِقِ وَامْسَحُوا بِرُءُوسِكُمْ وَأَرْجُلَكُمْ إِلَى الْكَعْبَيْنِ ۚ وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ جُنُبًا فَاطَّهَّرُوا ۚ *وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ أَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مِنَ الْغَائِطِ أَوْ لَامَسْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَلَمْ تَجِدُوا مَاءً فَتَيَمَّمُوا صَعِيدًا طَيِّبًا فَامْسَحُوا بِوُجُوهِكُمْ وَأَيْدِيكُمْ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ لِيَجْعَلَ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنْ حَرَجٍ وَلَٰكِنْ يُرِيدُ لِيُطَهِّرَكُمْ وَلِيُتِمَّ نِعْمَتَهُ عَلَيْكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ.*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Jab tum Namaz ke liye utho to apne moo aur haath kohniyon tak dho lo aur apne saron aur takhno tak paon ka Masah kiya karo. Agar Halat e Janabat mein ho to Taharat (Ghusl) kar lo. *Aur agar tum beemar ya safar mein ho ya tum mein se koi rafa hajat (relieve from toilet/urine) karke aye ya Auraton se hambistari (Sexual Intercourse) ki ho aur tumko Paani na mil sake to Paak Khaak se Tayammum kar lo aur Tayammum mein apne moo aur haathon ka Masah kar lo. Allah tum par kisi tarah ki tangi musallat karna nahi chahta. Woh ye chahta hai ke tumhe Paak o Pakeezah kar de aur tum par Apni Ne'mat poori kare taake tum shukr guzar ban jao."*_
(Surah Maeda: 6)

📚📖 💦
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Same Topic jo hamne 6 January 2017 ko post ki thi dubara repeat kar rahe hain:

*Tayammum:*
Jab Bimari ya Safar mein Ghusl ya Wuzu mein paani istemal na kar sake ya na mile tab Tayammum karna chahiye.
*Method:*
Niyat, Apne dono hatheliyon ko Matti par mare, poori peshani par dono hatheliyon ko phere bal ki jagah se naak ke sire tak, phir Matti par hath mare, left hatheli ko dayen hath (right hand) ke tamam pusht (back) par, phir dayen hatheli ko bayen hath ke tamam pusht par phere (masah) kare. Ise is Tarteeb se kiya jaye.

*Q:* Sawal hota hai ke Tayammum se kiya fayda, jabke isse gandgi to saf nahi hoti.

*Wujuhat (Reasons):*

*A. Akhlaqi Fayda:*
Tayammum ek Ibaadat hai. Jab insaan apne hath mitti par marta hai. Isse Khuda ki bargah mein aajezi o inkisari (humbleness) paida hoti hai, jisse woh doosri Ibaadaton ki taraf amada hota hai.

*B. Hifzane Sehet (Health):*
Aaj ki Duniya mein ye sabit ho chuka hai ke Mitti (Mud) apne bahut se germs (Bacterias) ki wajah se gandgiyon ko door kar sakti hai. Ye germs jo kisi bhi cheez ko analyse karke tarah tarah ki badboo door karte hain, zamin ki satah (surface) par hi rahte hain jinhe sunlight milti rahti hai. Isiliye jab murde aur doosri ghalazaten zamin mein dafan ho jati hain, unko ye germs decompose kar ke sari badboo nikal dete hain. Hence Mitti (Mud, clay) Antibiotics ka kam karti hai. Isliye Matti wohi paani ka kaam karti hai. Paani (Water) Hallal (حللال) hai, means woh nuqsandeh germs ko apne aap mein dissolve kar ke baha le jata hai, jabke Mitti usko nist o nabood (destroy) kar deti hai, Maut ke ghat utar deti hai.
Lekin zaroori hai Tayammum ki Mitti Paak (Pure طيب) ho. Surface (satah) se li hoi ho jis par light padti hai.

Allah ke bataye hue sabhi Ahkam be Ma'ani nahi hoti, har fe'l mein kuchh na kuchh maslehat hoti hai, ye alag baat hai ke ham isse waqif nahi hote.

Iska Surah Nisa:43 ke zel mein ham tazkara kar chuke hain.

Tayammum ke detail Fiqhi Ahkam Tauzeehul Masael Ay. Sistani Maslah no. 655 - 691 refer karen.
Ham is group mein pahle English aur Urdu mein pesh kar chuke hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💦
Imam Sadiq (as) se Tayammum ke bare mein sawal kiya to ye Ayat padhi:
*وَالسَّارِقُ وَالسَّارِقَةُ فَاقْطَعُوا أَيْدِيَهُمَا*
(Surah Ma'idah 38)
Phir Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tayammum mein haath ke us hisse par Tayammum karo jise Chori ki saza mein kata jata hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
💦
Imam Reza (as):
_"Wuzu mein haatho'n ke dhone ko is liye waajib qaraar diya gaya hai ke insaan inhi haatho'n ko Takbeer ke saath buland karta hai aur inhe Dua ke liye uthhata hai."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p194)
💦
Imam Reza (as)
se sawaal hua ke Wuzu mein sirf chehra, haath, sar aur paon ki kyun shamil hain?
Imam (as) ne jawab diya: _"Namaz mein yehi aaza (bodyparts) hi zyada numaya hote hain. Insaan chehre ke saath Sajda karta hai aur khuzoo (humbleness) ka izhaar karta hai aur haathon se sawaal karta hai aur unhe Dua ke liye buland karta hai aur Ruku aur Sajde mein apne sar ko kaam mein laata hai aur apne qadmon ke zariye se uthta aur baithta hai."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p223)

       *5th July 2017, Wednesday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
      ♦ _*AHD O PAIMAN (COVENANT)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (668) 🤝

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَمِيثَاقَهُ الَّذِي وَاثَقَكُمْ بِهِ إِذْ قُلْتُمْ سَمِعْنَا وَأَطَعْنَا ۖ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلِيمٌ بِذَاتِ الصُّدُورِ*

_"Khuda ne tum par jo Ne'mat ki hai use yaad karo aur us Ahd o Paiman (Covenant) ko yaad karo jo tum se liya hai jab tumne ye kaha tha ke hamne suna aur ita'at qubool ki, aur Khuda se darte raho. Beshak Allah seenon mein chhipe hue razon ko jaanta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 6)

📚📖 🤝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Meesaq (ميثاق) means Kisi cheez se bandhna. Ahd o Paiman chunke ek girah ki manind hai jo do afraad ya do giroh ke darmiyan bandha jata hai aur unke itminaan ke baes banta hai.

Is Ayat mein ye bataya ja raha hai ke ham ne Allah se Ahd o Paiman kiya hai. Ye Ahd kab liya gaya iski Musalmano mein alag alag Tafseer hai.
Lekin Quran ke mutabiq ye Ahd sab se Pahle Alam e Zar mein liya gaya, jab ham Duniya mein nahi aye the. (Tafseel Sura Araaf mein ayegi). Duniya mein aate hi ye Ahd bhool gaye. Isliye Hazrat Ali (as) ne Anbiya ke bhejne ka maqsad batate hue farmaya:
*ليستادوهم ميثاق فطرته.*
( _"Anbiya isliye bheje gaye ke woh logon ko Paiman e Fitrat pura karne ki dawat de."_)
(Nahjul Balagha)

Yehi Ahd ki Tajdeed (renewal) Hujjatul Wuda mein hui jab Ali (as) ki Vilayat ka iqrar liya gaya.

Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim mein hai ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Iqraar e Vilayat liya tha aur uske jawab mein logon ne kaha tha ke hamne sun liya aur ita'at ki lekin Habib e Khuda (saww) ke baad logon ne is Ahd ko tod diya. Imam Baqir (as) ke mutabiq 2 Ahd liye gaye ek ye ke Haraam cheezon se parhez karen aur Taharat ke tareeqo par karband rahen aur doosre Vilayat.

Bare Ilaha hame apne Ahd o Paiman ko poora karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤝
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Roze Ghadeer shukrane ki Namaz padho aur ek doosre se milo to ye kah kar Allah ka shukr ada karo:_
*الحمد لله الذى أكرمنا بهذا اليوم و جعلنا من الموفين بعهده إلينا و ميثاقه الذي واثقنا به ولاية أمره والقوام بقسطه.*
_"Tamam ta'reefen Us Khuda ke liye hain jisne is Din ke zariye se hamen Mukarram banaya aur hamen Wada Wafai ki Taufeeq di aur hamen is Meesaq (Covenant) ki pabandi ki Taufeeq di jo Usne apne Waliyan e Amr aur Apni Adaalat qaem karne walon ke mutalliq hamse liya tha."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

(Isse pata chalta hai ke Meesaq e Ilahi mein Ailan e Ghadeer bhi shamil hai.)

                ♦ _*ADAALAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (669) ⚖

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُونُوا قَوَّامِينَ لِلَّهِ شُهَدَاءَ بِالْقِسْطِ ۖ وَلَا يَجْرِمَنَّكُمْ شَنَآنُ قَوْمٍ عَلَىٰ أَلَّا تَعْدِلُوا ۚ اعْدِلُوا هُوَ أَقْرَبُ لِلتَّقْوَىٰ ۖ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَبِيرٌ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ * وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ ۙ لَهُمْ مَغْفِرَةٌ وَأَجْرٌ عَظِيمٌ * وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَكَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا أُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ الْجَحِيمِ*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Allah ke liye Haq par qaem rahne wale aur Insaaf ki gawahi dene wale bano, aur kisi qaum ki dushmani tumhe itna mushta'il na karne paye ke Insaaf se phir jao. Adl karo. Ye Khuda Tarsi (Taqwa) se zyada munasibat rakhta hai aur Allah se darte raho (Taqwa ikhtiyar karo). Yaqeenan Allah tumhare tamam Aamaal ki khabar  rakhta hai."_
_"Allah Imaan walon aur Nek Aamaal baja laane walon se bakhshish aur Ajre Azeem ka Wada kiya hai."_
_"Aur jin logon ne Kufr kiya aur Hamari Ayaat ko jhutlaya woh dozakhi hain."_

(Surah Maeda: 8 - 10)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Same isi tarah ki Ayat Surah Nisa: 135 mein guzar chuki. Ayat ka repeatation aur ek hi Ayat mein isko dohrane se Adalat ki ahmiyat ka pata chalta hai. Ham pahle is topic par zikr kar chuke hain. Kuchh aur Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
🌿
Paighambar e Islam (saww):
_"Zulm se bacho kiyonki har amal Roze Qayamat apni munasib shakl mein mujassam hoga aur Zulm zulmat o taareeki ki surat mein mujassam hoga aur taareeki ka pardah zalimo ko ghere hue hoga."_
(Safinatul Bihar-Zulm)
🍀
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Aasman aur Zameen Adl ki buniyad par qaem hain."_
(Tafseer Saafi Sura Rahman:8 ke zel mein)
🍁
Ek aur Rivayaat mein hai:
_"Hukoomaten Kufr se to mumkin hai baqi rah jayen, lekin zalim hon to unhe dawam (continuity) hasil nahi ho sakta."_
🍃
Ye Ayat se hamen sabaq milta hai ke ham zara zara si baat par mushta'il ho jate hain aur apni opposite par zulm karne lagte hain. Zalim Dushman se Jihad karna hai na ke hamen zulm karna. Hazrat Ali (as) ne jab apni Dushman ko maut ke ghat utara to ye dekh kar ke uski nasl mein koi Momin nahi hai. Agar hai to chhod dete the.

Bare Ilaha hame logon ke saath Adl se pesh aane ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Qayamat ke Din Teen qism ke afraad tamam Makhlooq mein se Khuda se zyada qareeb honge yahan tak ke Allah hisaab se farigh ho jaye:_
_Woh Shakhs hai,_
_(1) Jo Qudrat rakhte hue bhi apne se Kamzor Aadmi par zulm na kare._
_(2) Jo do afraad ke darmiyan chale magar woh kisi ek taraf ju barabar bhi mael na ho._
_(3) Jo har haal mein Haq baat kahe khwah usse uska fayda hota ho ya nuqsan."_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

                 ♦ _*SAFETY*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (670)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ إِذْ هَمَّ قَوْمٌ أَنْ يَبْسُطُوا إِلَيْكُمْ أَيْدِيَهُمْ فَكَفَّ أَيْدِيَهُمْ عَنْكُمْ ۖ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ وَ عَلَى اللَّهِ فَلْيَتَوَكَّلِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Allah ki Ne'mat ko yaad karo jo Usne tum par ki hai. Jabke ek Qaum ne tum par dastdarazi ka irada kiya tha magar Khuda ne unke haath tum par uthne se rok diye aur Khuda se darte raho (Taqwa ikhtiyar karo) aur Ahle Imaan ko Khuda par hi bharosa rakhna chahiye."_
(Surah Maeda: 11)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah us Ne'mat ko yaad kara raha hai jahan Allah ne hame Dushmano ke sharr se mehfooz rakha hai.

Aur Surah Hamd ke mutabiq Ye Ne'maten Allah ke woh Masoom Rehbar hain jinke Seedhe Raaste par ham gamzan hain.

Hamara Dushman bahut Taqatwar hai aur hamare naboodi ke liye koshan rahta hai. Agar Khuda ki madad shamil e haal na hoti to ham kab ka halaak ho gaye hote.

Bare Ilaha ham sabko Dushman ke sharr se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👨🏻‍🎨
Imam Mahdi (as):
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*إنى لأمان لأهل الأرض كما أن النجوم أمان لأهل الأرض السماء.*
_"Beshak mein Ahl Zameen ke liye Amn o Salamti hun, jaisa ke sitare Aasmaan walon ke liye Amaan ka baes hain."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-485)

*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*أنا خاتم الأوصياء، و بى يدفع الله عز وجل البلاء عن أهلى و شيعتى.*
_"Mein Khatemul Ausiya hun, aur Khuda Wande Alam mere sabab aur waseele se mere Ahl aur mere Shiyon se balaon ko door karta hai"_
👨🏻‍🎨
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*إنا غير مهملين لمراعاتكم، ولا ناسين لذكركم، و لو لا ذلك لنزل بكم اللأواء و اصطلمكم الأعداء.*
_"Ham tumhari sarparasti aur dekh bhal mein kotahi (delay) nahi karte, aur tumhari yaad ko kabhi nahi bhulate, agar ham aisa na karte to tum par balayen aur musibaten nazil ho jaati aur Dushman tum ko bilkul neest o nabood kar dete."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-441, H-12, Al Ghaiba Tusi, P-246, H-215, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 52, P-30, H-25, Vol 53, P-175, H-7, Ehtejaaj, Vol 2, P-323, Al Kharaej wal Haraej, Vol 2, P-903)

               ♦ _*12 KHALIFA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (671) 1⃣2⃣

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

وَلَقَدْ أَخَذَ اللَّهُ مِيثَاقَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ *وَبَعَثْنَا مِنْهُمُ اثْنَيْ عَشَرَ نَقِيبًا ۖ* وَقَالَ اللَّهُ إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ ۖ لَئِنْ أَقَمْتُمُ الصَّلَاةَ وَآتَيْتُمُ الزَّكَاةَ وَآمَنْتُمْ بِرُسُلِي وَعَزَّرْتُمُوهُمْ وَأَقْرَضْتُمُ اللَّهَ قَرْضًا حَسَنًا لَأُكَفِّرَنَّ عَنْكُمْ سَيِّئَاتِكُمْ وَلَأُدْخِلَنَّكُمْ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ ۚ فَمَنْ كَفَرَ بَعْدَ ذَٰلِكَ مِنْكُمْ فَقَدْ ضَلَّ سَوَاءَ السَّبِيلِ)

_"Allah ne Bani Israel se pukhta Ahd o Paiman (Covenant) liya tha aur *Hamne un mein 12 Naqeeb muqarrar kiye* aur Allah ne unse kaha tha ke Mein tumhare sath hun, agar tumne Namaz qaem ki aur Zakat ada ki aur Mere Rasoolon ko maana aur unki madad ki aur tumne Khuda ko Qarza-e-Hasana (paying loan and waiving) diya, to yaqeen rakho ke Mein tumhari buraiyan tum se zael (erase) kar donga aur tumko aise baghat mein dakhil karonga jinke neeche Nehren baih rahi hongi aur uske baad jisne tum mein se Kufr ka ravayya apnaya to woh rahe raast se bhatak gaya."_
(Surah Maeda: 12)

📚📖 1⃣2⃣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein phir se Bani Israel ke Ahd ka zikr karke wohi Ahd o Paiman ki yaad dilayi hai jo Ghadeer mein liya gaya.
🌿
"Naqeeb" *نقيب* means ek underground hole ya surang . Terminologically, istelahan Naqeeb us leader kahte hain jo apne followers ke asraar, secrets​ jaanta ho. Aur ko bhi kha jata jo kisi giroh ka role model ho. Isi word se bana hai "Manaqib" (Manqabat - منقبت) yani Fazail,  jahan kisi shakhs ki Ma'arefat justujo wa tehqeeq karke hasil ki jati hai.
Pas Naqeeb apne giroh ke leader ko kahte hain. Uske hi Fazail wa Manaqib padhe jate hain.
Allah ne Bani Israel ke liye 12 leader muntakhab kiya. (Pas Imam Allah ki taraf se muntakhab hota hai na ke log chune.)
🍃🌱
Rasoole Khuda (saww) apne Naqeeb bhi Bani Israel ke Naqeeb ke barabar yani unki ta'adad 12 batayi.
(Tafseer Roohul Ma'ani, Vol 6, P-78)
🍂🍃🌱
Samura bin Jabir se Rivayat hai:
_"Meine Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko kahte suna, "12 Khalifa honge" phir maine nahi suna, phir farmaya, "sabke sab Quraish mein se honge."_
(Sahih al-Bukhari (English), Hadith: Volume 9 Book 89 Hadith 329, Kitabul Ahkam; Sahih al-Bukhari, (Arabic), 4:165, Kitabul Ahkam)
🍁🌾
Maine Abdullah bin Masood se poochha to jawab mein farmaya:
_"Hamne Paighambar e Khuda (saww) se yahi poochha tha to unhone jawab mein farmaya ke 12 afraad Nuqubaye Bani Israel ki ta'daad ke mutabiq."_
(Musnad Imam Ahmed bin Hambal, Vol 1,, P-298, Tareekh Ibne Akasar, Faizul Taqdeer Sharh Jameus Saghir, Vol 2, P-459)
✨🎍
_"Nuqubaye Bani Israel ki ta'daad ke barabar 12 Khulufa is ummat par hukumat karenge."_
(Muntakhab Kanzul Ummal hashiya Musnad e Ahmed, Vol 5, P-312)

*Other References on 12 Caliphs:*
Tarikh ibn Kathir, 6:248; Kanz al-Ummal, 13:27; Al-Haskani, Shawahid al-Tanzil, 1:455, Tradition No. 626.
Musnad Ahmad ibn Hanbal v1 p398 and p406; Mustadrak al-Hakim, 4:501; Al-Dhahabi, Talkhis al-Mustadrak 4:501. I; Ibn Hajar Asqalani, Fath al-Bari 16:339; #Ali ibn Abu Bakr al-Haythami, Majma al-Zawa'id 5:190; Ibn Hajar Al-Haythami, Al-Sawa'iq al-Muhriqa, vol 12; Suyuti, Tarikh al-Khulafa, Vol 10; Jami' al-Saghir 1:75; Kanz al-Ummal, 13:27.

Rasool (saww) ne kaha kuchh Musalmano ke amal kiya aur kuchh.

Bare Ilaha hame 12 (Isna Ashari) ke raaste par chalne ki hidayat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌿🍃
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Mere baad 12 Aimma (as) honge jinme ka pehla fard Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) hain aur aakhri Qaim (atfs) hain. Ye hi mere Khulafa, mere Awsiya, mere Awliya hain, meri Ummat par mere baad Allah ki Hujjat hain. Unka iqraar karne wala Momin aur unka inkaar karne wala kafir hai._"
(Kamaluddin, v1, p279)
🍁🌾
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Zameen par Imam ka hona zaruri hai jo Halaal o Haraam aur oon tamaam umoor (affairs) ka aalim ho jinke log mohtaj hai."_
(Kamaluddin, v1, p248)
