 ♦ _*AHD-E-VILAYAT SE DAGHA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (672)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبِمَا نَقْضِهِمْ مِيثَاقَهُمْ لَعَنَّاهُمْ وَجَعَلْنَا قُلُوبَهُمْ قَاسِيَةً ۖ يُحَرِّفُونَ الْكَلِمَ عَنْ مَوَاضِعِهِ ۙ وَنَسُوا حَظًّا مِمَّا ذُكِّرُوا بِهِ ۚ وَلَا تَزَالُ تَطَّلِعُ عَلَىٰ خَائِنَةٍ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا مِنْهُمْ ۖ فَاعْفُ عَنْهُمْ وَاصْفَحْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ الْمُحْسِنِينَ*

_"Iske baad *Hamne unki Ahd  Shikni ki wajah se un par Laanat ki* aur unke dilon ko sakht bana diya. Ab unka ye haal hai ke woh alfaz ka ulat pher karke baat ko kahin se kahin le jaate hain aur unhe jin baaton ki nasihat ki gayi thi uska bada hissa faramosh kar baithe hain aur aye din tumhe unki Khayanat ka pata chalta rahta hai, un mein se bahut kam afraad Khayanat se bache hue hain. Tum unko ma'af kar do aur darguzar karo. Yaqeenan Allah Ehsaan ki ravish apnane walon ko pasand karta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 13)

📚📖 💔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat *(5: 12)* 12 Khulufa ke bare mein thi. Rasoole Khuda (as) ki Ahadees jo ke Ahle Sunnat ki bhi Kitabon mein darj hai ke Rasool ke apne Khulufa ki ta'daad Nuqubaye Bani Israel ki ta'daad ke barabar batayi. Isse ye sabit hua ke Rasool ke Janashin, Wasi sirf 12 hain. Wohi 12 Imam hain jo ke Rasool ke Khandan se hain jinko Quran ne Ahle Bait (as) se khitab kiya hai.
Hujjatul Wuda yani Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Akhri Hajj ke mauqe par Ghadeer ke maidan mein sawa lakh Musalman wa Ashaab ke majme mein yehi to Ahd liya tha ke Ali (as) Rasool ke baad Khalifa, Wasi, Maula hain. Jaise Allah ne Bani Israel se uske Nuquba ke liye Ahd liya tha. Ye Ahd e Vilayat tha.

Iske baad wali Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala un par Laanat kar raha hai jinhone is Ahd ko toda. Aur unka haal bhi hamare saamne pesh kar raha hai jo ke haqeeqat mein aaj bhi aisa hi ho raha hai. Jab bhi khud sakta Rehbaron ki kartoot ke bare bataya jata hain ye kah kar apna daman jhad liya jata hai aap apne amal ko dekhe na ke doosron ke amal, Allah aap ke amaal bare mein sawal karega na ke doosron ke bare mein (mulaheza ho Ayat: Alfaz ka ulat pher...)

Is Ayat se pata chalta hai jisne bhi Vilayat se moo phera usne Khayanat ki. Itna waazeh taur par Allah Ta'ala ne Rasool ke wasi ke bare zikr kar diya iske baad to shak ki koi gunjaish hi nahi rahti.
Hamne is Ayaat par zyada​ tawajjo dene ki takeed ki. Ahadees kal bayan kar chuke hain.

Bare Ilaha hame un Khayanat karon se door rakh jin par Tu ne Laanat bheji hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍁
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa le'n, yaani sargardaa'n (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumraah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar usay zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayaanat ki._"
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
🍁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs hum logo'n ki mohabbat ki thandak apne dil mein mehsoos kare use chahiye ke wo apni Maa ko bahut bahut Duaein de is liye ke usne uske Baap ki Amaanat mein khayanat nahi ki."_
(Elal ush Sharaaye, p108)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*AHDO PAIMAN CHRISTIANS SE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (673)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمِنَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّا نَصَارَىٰ أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَهُمْ فَنَسُوا حَظًّا مِمَّا ذُكِّرُوا بِهِ فَأَغْرَيْنَا بَيْنَهُمُ الْعَدَاوَةَ وَالْبَغْضَاءَ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ ۚ وَسَوْفَ يُنَبِّئُهُمُ اللَّهُ بِمَا كَانُوا يَصْنَعُونَ*

_"Usi tarah se Hamne un se bhi pukhta Ahd liya jo apne aap ko Nasara (Christians) kahlwate hain magar unki bhi ye haalat hai ke unhe jo kuchh yaad karaya gaya tha woh uska bada hissa faramosh kar chuke hain. Hamne Qayamat tak ke liye un mein bughz o adawat ko dal diya aur anqareeb Khuda unhe unke Aamaal o Afa'al ki khabar dega."_
(Surah Maeda: 14)

📚📖 📝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne kin kin se Ahd liye is ka bayan jari hai. Jaisa ke hamne pahle bataya Allah ne sab se is Duniya mein aane pahle Aalam Zar mein Ahd liya gaya tha lekin is Duniya mein aane ke baad woh bhool gaye jaise ek aadmi khwab dekhta hai lekin suna nahi pata hai ke kiya dekha, woh bhool jata hai. Hazrat Ali (as) ke mutabiq Anbiya is Ahd ki tajdeed karne aye, soyi hui fitrat ko jaga saken.
Guzishta Ayat mein Bani Israel ko is Ahd o Paiman yaad dilayi usi tarah is Ayat mein is baat ki taraf ishara hai ke Nasara (Christians) se bhi Ahd liya. Ghadeer mein bhi aisa hi Ahd liye kiyonki jitne bhi rahbar aye sab ka maqsad yehi tha. Lekin is Ayat ke mutabiq asl baat yehi hai ke in Ahd o Paiman ko faramosh kar diya. Allah ne unko saza ye mili ke unke darmyan adawat dal di. Allah ne yaha ye ishaara kiya ke anqareeb unko unke Afa'al ki khabar de di jayegi.
Ab jaise ke hame Rivayaat se pata chalta hai ke jab Imam Mahdi (atfs) ka Zahoor hoga to poori Duniya mein Islam ka bol bala hoga. Jab Hazrat Esa (as) bhi is Duniya mein ayenge aur Imam Mahdi (as) ke pichhe Namaz padhenge to sab Christians bhi asl Ilahi Deen par palat ayenge. Us din Allah unko sachchai dikha dega.
Poori Duniya par Imam Mahdi (as) ki hukumat hogi aur poori Duniya unke taabe hogi.

Bare Ilaha hame bhi Hazrat Mahdi (atfs) ke awan o ansaar mein shamil farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📝
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar Duniya ki umr se ek din bhi baaqi reh jayega to Allah us din ko tulaani kar dega ke mere Ahlebait (as) mein se ek aise shakhs (Imam Mahdi (atfs)) ko mab'oos karega jo zameen ko Adl o Insaaf se aisa bhar dega jis tarah wo zulm o jaur se bhari hogi."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p20)

  ♦ _*NOOR WA KITAB E MUBIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (674)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ قَدْ جَاءَكُمْ رَسُولُنَا يُبَيِّنُ لَكُمْ كَثِيرًا مِمَّا كُنْتُمْ تُخْفُونَ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَيَعْفُو عَنْ كَثِيرٍ ۚ قَدْ جَاءَكُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ نُورٌ وَكِتَابٌ مُبِينٌ*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab! Hamara Rasool tumhare paas aa gaya hai jo Kitab-e-Khuda ki bahut se un batoon ko tumhare liye khol raha hai jinhen tum chhupaya karte the aur bahut si baton se darguzar (overlook) karta hai. Khuda ki taraf se tumhare pas chamakta hua Noor aur saaf saaf bayan karne wali Kitab aa chuki hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 15)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Christians se jo Ahd liya tha uski yaad dahani ki gayi. Is ayat mein usi baat ko jari rakhte hue Allah Ahle Kitab se mukhatib ho kar agah kar raha hai ke Hamara Rasool to unke paas aa gaya. Lekin sab kuchh jante hue bhi Ahle Kitab Haq ko chhupate hain.
Phir Allah Ta'ala farmata hai chamakta hua Noor aur Waazeh karne wali Kitab aa gayi. Yahan Noor se murad khud Rasool aur unke Ahle Bait (as) hain jiski wazahat guzishta ayaton mein kar chuke hain.
Jaisa ke Rasoole Akram (saww) ki maroof rivayat hai:
_"Mein do wazni cheezen chhod kar ja raha hun ek Khuda ki Kitab aur meri itrat Ahle Bait (as)"_
(al-Imam al-Hafiz Abu ‘Abd Allah al-­Hakim al-­Naysaburi, al-­Mustadrak ‘ala al-Sahihayn [Dar al-Ma’rifah li al-­Tiba’ah wa al-­Nashr: Beirut), vol. iii, pp. 109-110).

Yehi sahi raasta hai. Allah Ahle Kitab ko is raaste par aane ki dawat di.

Bare Ilaha hame Kitabe Ilahi wa Noor e Ilahi ki roshni mein hidayat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Islam ke 5 buniyaadi sutoon (foundation pillars) hai:
_(1) Namaz padhna,_
_(2) Zakaat adaa karna,_
_(3) Hajj adaa karna,_
_(4) Maah e Ramzaan mein Roze rakhna,_
_(5) Hum Ahle Bait (as) se mohabbat rakhna._

_4 cheezon mein kami hai magar Ahle Bait (as) ki mohabbat mein kami nahi hai._
_Jiske paas maal nahi hai uspar Zakaat nahi._
_Jiske paas maal na ho Hajj nahi._
_Jo bimaar ho wo baith kar Namaz padhh sakta hai aur Maah e Ramzaan ke Roze ko iftaar kar sakta hai_ (bimari mein Roza nahi).
_Magar hum Ahle Bait (as) ki mohabbat rakhna har haal mein laazim hai."_
(Khisaal, p145)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*SEERAT E MUSTAQEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (675)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَهْدِي بِهِ اللَّهُ مَنِ اتَّبَعَ رِضْوَانَهُ سُبُلَ السَّلَامِ وَيُخْرِجُهُمْ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ بِإِذْنِهِ وَيَهْدِيهِمْ إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ*

_"Jiske zariye se Allah un logon ko jo uski Raza ke talib hain Salamti ke Raaste dikhata aur Apne Hukm se unhe andheron se nikal kar ujale ki taraf lata hai aur Seedhi Raah ki taraf unki Rahnumai karta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 16)

📚📖 🛤
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya ke Noor aur Kitab e Mubeen aa gayi.  Noor e Mubeen se murad pahle bhi bata chuke hain ke ye Rasoole Akram (saww) aur Janabe Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) aur Aimma (as) hain
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai ke inhi ke zariye Allah woh Sirate Mustaqeem ki taraf Hidayat karta hai jo Allah ki Raza aur Salamti ka raasta hai. Sura Al Hamd mein bhi ham yehi Dua maangte hain ke Parwardigaar hame Seedhi Raah ki taraf Hidayat farma, unka Raasta jin Par Allah ki Ne'maten nazil hoti hain. Allah ki Ne'maten kisi khatakaar, Zalim, gunehgar par nazil nahi hoti. Isliye Allah ne apni Hidayat ki shart ye laga di ke jo Allah ki Raza ka talib hai unhi ko Hidayat hasil hogi. Sura Al Hamd ne saaf taur par do raaste bata diye ek Seerat e Mustaqeem aur doosra Zalleen ka Raasta. Chunki abhi taak Haqeeqi Rahbar ko koi pahchan nahi paya isliye Sura Al Hamd mein is Dua ko Qayamat tak ke liye raej kar diya. Jisne Haqeeqi Rahbar ko paa liya samajhye ke uski Dua qubool ho gayi.

*اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ * صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛤 ✨
Imam Sadiq (as):
_" 'Siraat e Mustaqeem' Hazrat Ali (as) aur unki Imamat ka eteqaad karna hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p46)
🌟✨
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hazrat Esa (as) ne Sham'oon bin Hamlon As Safa ko apna Wasi banaya. Sham'oon ne Yahya bin Zakariya ko apna Wasi banaya. Yahya bin Zakariya ne Munzir ko apna Wasi banaya. Munzir ne Sulaima ko apna Wasi banaya. Sulaima ne Burdah ko apna Wasi muqarrar kiya._
_Phir Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:_
_"Burdah ne mujhe Wasi banaya aur Aye Ali! Mein tujhe apna Wasi bana raha hun."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       *13th July 2017, Thursday*

            ♦ _*JESUS CHRIST*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (676)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ كَفَرَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْمَسِيحُ ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ ۚ قُلْ فَمَنْ يَمْلِكُ مِنَ اللَّهِ شَيْئًا إِنْ أَرَادَ أَنْ يُهْلِكَ الْمَسِيحَ ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ وَأُمَّهُ وَمَنْ فِي الْأَرْضِ جَمِيعًا ۗ وَلِلَّهِ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا ۚ يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*

_"Yaqeenan un logon ne Kufr kiya jinhone kaha ke Allah Maseeh bin Maryam hai. Aap kah den ke agar Khuda Maseeh bin Maryam aur unki Maa aur tamam zameen walon ko halaak karna chahe to kis ki majal hai ke Usko is irade se baaz rakh sake. Aasmano, Zameen aur jo kuchh unke darmiyan hai wo sab ke sab Khuda ki Milkiyat o Saltanat hai. Woh jo Chahta hai paida karta hai aur Khuda har cheez par Qudrat rakha hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 17)

📚📖 ⛪
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Christianity ke Trinity ke Batil Aqeede ke bare Surah Nisa:170 ke zel mein wazahat kar chuke hain. Christian 3 Khuda ka Aqeeda rakhte hai: The God, The Holy Spirit, Jesus Christ.
Allah ne is Ayat mein daleel pesh ki hai poori Kainaat ka Khuda Allah hai, Woh chahe to Jesus & Mary ko bhi halaak kar sakta hai aisi misal di hai. Ayat 116 mein mazeed wazahat ki jayegi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⛪🕍
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Ya Ali! Tumhari misaal Isa bin Maryam (as) ki tarah hai, jis se Isaiyon ne hadd se zyada pyaar kiya to Kafir ho gaye aur Yahudiyon ne bughz kiya to Kafir ho gaye._"
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p129)
🌍☁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ke 12000 Aalam hai jinme se har ek Sutoon Aasman aur Zameen se bada hai aur inme se har ek ke rehne wale doosre Aalam ke rehne wale se anjaan hai."_
(Sharh Dua e Kumail)
🙏🏻🌍🙌🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Aye Sahib e Karam! Aye Mere Parwardigaar! Tu meri kamzori ko jaanta hai ke Duniya ki zara zara aazmaish aur uski mamooli takleefen aur jo na-pasand cheezen Ahl e Duniya par guzarti rehti hain (unhe main bardaasht nahi kar sakta), bawajood iske ke wo aazmaish aur wo takleefen daymi nahi hoti, uski muddat thodi aur uski baqaa' chand-roza hoti hai. To bhala phir mujh se Aakherat ki Balaa aur usme musibaton ke wurood ki bardaasht kyun-kar ho sakegi? Halaanki wahan ki muddat lambi hogi aur baaqi rehna uska daymi (permanent) hoga aur jo usme phans jayega unke azaab ko halka na kiya ja sakega, is liye ke wo Azaab Tere gazab, Tere Inteqam aur Tere Gusse ke sabab se hoga aur Tere gusse ko na aasmaan bardaasht kar sakte hain, na zameen. Aye mere Sardaar! To bhala meri kya haalat hogi? Halaanki main Tera ek kamzor, zaleel, haqeer, miskeen aur aajiz banda hun."_
(Dua e Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*JANNATI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (677)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ وَالنَّصَارَىٰ نَحْنُ أَبْنَاءُ اللَّهِ وَأَحِبَّاؤُهُ ۚ قُلْ فَلِمَ يُعَذِّبُكُمْ بِذُنُوبِكُمْ ۖ بَلْ أَنْتُمْ بَشَرٌ مِمَّنْ خَلَقَ ۚ يَغْفِرُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَلِلَّهِ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا ۖ وَإِلَيْهِ الْمَصِيرُ*

_"Yahood o Nasaara (Jews & Christians) ye kahte hain ke ham Khuda ke Farzand aur Uske chaheete hain. Tum kah do agar aisa hai to Woh tumhe tumhare gunahon par saza kiyon deta hai? Tum bhi doosre insaano ki tarah se Khuda ki Makhlooq ho. Woh jise chahe Bakhsh de aur jise chahe saza de. Zameen, Aasmaan aur unke darmiyan jo kuchh bhi hai sab Khuda ki Milkiyat hai aur sabko Usi ki taraf laut kar jana hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 18)

📚📖 🍁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke bayan ko jari rakhte hue Allah ne phir Ahle Kitab ko tanbeeh ki. Jaise aajkal har koi kahta hai 73 firqo mein se jo ek Jannat mein jaega woh mein hun. Har shakhs apne aap ko Jannati kahta hai, is baat ki koi tehqeeq nahi karta kya woh Siraate Mustaqeem par hai? Allah ne ye sawal kiya agar Allah ke bete bante ho to gunah kiyon karte ho. Kuchh ka sawal hai ke ho sakta hai Allah ka beta hona majazi (Metaphorical) ho. To aise nahi hai Christians haqeeqat mein Allah ka beta maante hain.

Tafseer Majmaul Bayan mein zere behes Rivayat hai :
_"Paighambar e Khuda (saww) ne Khuda Azaab se daraya to ek giroh kahne laga ke hame dhamkao mat aur na darao kiyonki ham to Khuda ke bete aur uske dost hain agar Woh ham par naraaz bhi ho to Uski Naraazgi aisi hai jaise koi insaan apne bete par naraaz hota hai."_ (yani bahut jald uska ye ghussa thanda ho jata hai.)
Jabke Khuda ne is Ayat mein isi baat ka jawab diya hai.

Bare Ilaha ham sabke dilon Teri taraf mael kar.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ☘
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Meri Ummat ke oon logon ke liye sakht azaab hai jo ye kehte hain ke fulaan shakhs Jannati hai aur fulaan Jahannumi hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p811)
🍀
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jannat Amal se haasil hoti hai Ummeed se Nahi haasil hoti."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         ♦ _*AYYAM-E-FATRAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (678)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ قَدْ جَاءَكُمْ رَسُولُنَا يُبَيِّنُ لَكُمْ عَلَىٰ فَتْرَةٍ مِنَ الرُّسُلِ أَنْ تَقُولُوا مَا جَاءَنَا مِنْ بَشِيرٍ وَلَا نَذِيرٍ ۖ فَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بَشِيرٌ وَنَذِيرٌ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab! Hamara Rasool aise waqt tumhare pas aaya hai aur tumhe Deen ki waazeh (clear) Taa'leem de raha hai, jabke Rasoolon ki aamad ka silsilah ek muddat se band tha (Ayyame Fatrah) taake tum Khuda ki Bargah mein ye na kah sako ke hamare pas koi Basharat denewala (Basheer) aur Daranewala (Nazeer) nahi aaya."_
(Surah Maeda: 19)

📚📖 🔘
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
"Fatrah" *فترة* means Sukoon o Itminaan hai. Do harkaat, koshish, Inquilabat ke darmiyani fasle ko bhi Fatrah kahte hai.
Hazrat Esa (as) aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke darmiyan ke arse mein koi Rasool na the, isliye is darmiyani fasle ko jo ke qareeb 600 saal ka hai, isko Ayyam e Fatrah kahte hain. (English Calendar ke mutabiq 570 years ho sakta hai.)
Sawal ye uthta hai Quran o Rivayaat ke mutabiq Zameen Hujjat-e-Khuda se khali nahi rah sakti. To kiya is darmiyan zameen Hujjat-e-Khuda se khali thi? Nahi. Yahan is Ayat mein lafz Rasool aya hai. Hujjat-e-Khuda maujood thi, Ausiya the.
Rasool ka kaam hota hai Khuda ke taraf se Nai Shariyat lana, Ausiya is Shariyat ka ijra (execute) karte hain, usi Shariyat ko jari rakhte hain. Hazrat Ismail bin Ibrahim (as) ki nasl se Rasoole Khuda (saww) tak ek paak o muhazzab chain hai jinhone ye faraez anjaam diye. Khuchh Rivayaat mein hai ke is darmiyan 3 Nabi bhi the. (Zyada Tafseel ki yaha gunjaish nahi hai, Kaafi rivayaat hain, is topic par Kitaben refer karen.)

Bare Ilaha hamare saron par har waqt Teri Hujjat (atfs) ka saya rahe.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔘
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Haan rooye Zameen aise shakhs ke wujood se hargiz khaali nahi hoti jo Hujjat-e-Khuda ke sath qayam kare, woh aashkaar aur mashoor ho ya makhfi (open or hidden) aur na pahchana ho taake Khudai Ahkam, Dalail aur Nishaniyan khatm na ho jayen. (Aur woh unhe tehreef aur dastbard (theft) se mehfooz rakhen). Khuda unke zariye apne Dalail aur Nishaniyon ki hifazat karta hai taake woh unhe apne jaise afraad tak pahuncha den, ahista ahista khorafaat, Shaitani waswason, tehreefaat aur Taa'leem e Ilahi se be khabari phailti rahegi aise mein mumkin hai kuchh log apne zimmedariyon se faraar ke liye aisi surat ko bahana banayen to is surat mein Khuda Aasmaani jawan mardon ke zariye is bahane ko munqata kar deta hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Kalamat e qisar No. 147)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹
*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
             *21st Shawwal 1438*
       *16th July 2017, Sunday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
♦ _*ANBIYA: ALLAH KI NE'MAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (679)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ قَالَ مُوسَىٰ لِقَوْمِهِ يَا قَوْمِ اذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ إِذْ جَعَلَ فِيكُمْ أَنْبِيَاءَ وَجَعَلَكُمْ مُلُوكًا وَآتَاكُمْ مَا لَمْ يُؤْتِ أَحَدًا مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Aur yaad karo jab Moosa (as) ne apni qaum se kaha tha ke Aye meri qaum Khuda ki un Ne'maton ko yaad karo jo Usne tum par nazil ki hain. Usne tum mein  Nabi paida kiye, tumko farma rawa banaya aur tumko Khuda ne wo kuchh diya jo Usne Duniya mein kisi ko nahi diya."_
(Surah Maeda: 20)

📚📖 🛣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ab tak Ahle Kitab se mutalliq zikr ho raha tha. Ab aaj se Hazrat Moosa (as) aur unki qaum Bani Israel ka zikr hoga. Full story ki to yahan gunjaish nahi qaereen is se mutalliq Kitaben refer kar sakte hain.

Is Ayat mein Allah ne Bani Israel par kuchh Ne'maton ka zikr kiya hai. Is mein jo khaas Allah ki Ne'mat hai woh Anbiya wa Rahbaron ka nuzool hai. Jaisa ke ham kai bar bata chuke hai Sura Al Hamd ke zel mein ke Ne'mat se murad woh Allah ke muntakhab shuda Rehbaran hain jinhone hame Seedha Raasta dikhaya.
Is Ayat se ye Sabit hai ke Hamara Deeni Peshwa Allah muntakhab karta hai, ham ya tum nahi. Kiyonki sab insaan khaati hai woh sahi ghalat ka imtiyaz nahi kar sakta.
Rivayaat mein hai ke Hazrat Moosa (as) ke zamane mein 70 se zyada Anbiya the.
Bani Israel ko ek ye Ne'mat di ke Usne Firaon ke zulm se nijaat di Anbiya ko bhej kar, aur Bani Israel ko Sahebe Ikhtiyar banaya.
Baqi sab maaddi Ne'maten jaise Manna aur Salwa ka nazil karna, darya shaq hona bhi unke liye ata hui. Phir bhi woh apne raaste se bhatak gaye.

Bare Ilaha hame Anbiya (as) ke raaste par chalne Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛣
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ek zamana meri Ummat par aisa aane waala hai ke log Ulema se is tarah bhaagenge jis tarah bakri bhediye se bhaagti hai. Khuda unko 3 balaao’n mein mubtela karega:_
_(1) Unke maal se barkat uthha lega,_
_(2) Unpar Zaalim Sultaan (badshah) ko musallat karega,_
_(3) Unko duniya se bina Imaan uthayega."_
(Jaame ul Akhbar, p227)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*BAITUL MUQADDAS*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (680)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا قَوْمِ ادْخُلُوا الْأَرْضَ الْمُقَدَّسَةَ الَّتِي كَتَبَ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ وَلَا تَرْتَدُّوا عَلَىٰ أَدْبَارِكُمْ فَتَنْقَلِبُوا خَاسِرِينَ*

_"Aye meri qaum! (Shaam ki) is Muqaddas sarzameen mein dakhil ho jao jo Allah ne tumhare Haq mein likh di hai. Peechhe na hato warna na kaam wa na murad paltoge."_

(Surah Maeda: 21)

📚📖 🕍
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Hazrat Moosa (as) ke waqeat ka zikr jari hai. Moosa (as) ne apni qaum se Muqaddas Sarzameen mein dakhil hone ki request ki. Ye Muqaddas Zameen Bani Israel ke liye likh di gayi. Tafseeron is sarzameen ke bare mein ikhtelaf hai. Lekin zyada motabar Shaam (Syria) ke area ke bare mein bataya jata hai. (Noorus Saqlain ke mutabiq).
Shaam jisko aaj ham Syria kahte hain iski boundaries change hoti rahi hain. Us zamane ke lehaz se ye Lebanon, Israel, Jordon, Syria ye poora area ko Shaam kaha jata tha. Aur ye area Anbiya-e-Ilahi ka gahwara raha hai. Azeem Adyaan isi zameen se nikle. Baitul Muqaddas (Jerusalem) bhi wahin hai. Ho sakta hai is ka zikr ho.
Aaj jo Israel hukumat us par qabiz hai wo Zionism hai. Ye woh sachche Bani Israel nahi hai jin par Ne'maten nazil hui. Aaj bhi Sachche Yahoodi is Zionist hukumat ke khilaf hain. Yahoodi maante hain ke jab tak Messiah nahi ayega Jewish State qaem nahi ho sakta. Un mein do sect (firqe) hain:
(1) Haredim (2) Ashkenazi.
Ashkenazi Zionist hai, jo raaj kar rahe hain. Ye tehreef shuda Kitab Talmood par amal karte hain.
Hardedim (Ultra Orthodox) Hazrat Moosa (as) ke Sachche pairokar hain. Ye log bar khilaf Talmood, Torah par amal karte hain.
Isliye Quran mein jo hai ke ye zameen unke liye likh di, to ye un Sachche Moosa (as) ke pairokaron ke liye thi, na ke aaj ke Zionist ke liye.
Bahut pahle ham Sachche Yahoodi mazhab ke kuchh qanoon ko Islam se compare kar chuke hain jin mein kuchh similarity payi jati hai. Zionist aaj Israel mein bahut zulm kar rahe hain Baitul Muqaddas par qabiz hain, aur bahut si pabandiyan laga rakhi hain aur wahan Ibadat ki poori azaadi nahi hai. Chunki sab Anbiya is sarzameen e Baitul Muqaddas ke area mein aye isliye ye sab Ahle Kitab wa Musalamaano ke liye ye jagah Muqaddas hai.

Bare Ilaha jald az jald Baitul Muqaddas ko zalimo ke chungul se azaad kar de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💒
Imam Husain (as):
_"Hazrat Isa (as) ko sirf Bani Israel ka Nabi bana kar bheja gaya tha aur unki Nabuwwat Baitul Muqaddas tak mehdood (limited) thi."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p86)

   ♦ _*BANI ISRAEL KI BUZDILI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (681)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالُوا يَا مُوسَىٰ إِنَّ فِيهَا قَوْمًا جَبَّارِينَ وَإِنَّا لَنْ نَدْخُلَهَا حَتَّىٰ يَخْرُجُوا مِنْهَا فَإِنْ يَخْرُجُوا مِنْهَا فَإِنَّا دَاخِلُونَ*

_"Unhone kaha: Aye Moosa (as) wahan to bade zabardast log rahte hain aur jab tak woh wahan se chale na jayen us waqt tak ham wahan hargiz dakhil na honge. Haan agar woh nikal gaye to ham dakhil hone ke liye tayyar hain."_

(Surah Maeda: 22)

📚📖 🕍
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Poore waqea ki yahan gunjaish nahi hai, in short mulaheza farmayen:
Hazrat Moosa (as) ne jab Bani Israel ko Firon ke Zulm o sitam se nijaat dilayi aur unko Misr se bahar nikaala to farmaya:
_"Allah Ta'ala ne tumhare liye Muqaddas Zameen ka wada kiya hai lehaza tum Sarzameen e Muqaddas Palestine o Shaam ke fateh ke liye tayyar ho jao."_
Hazrat Moosa (as) ne 12 afraad ko unke wahan bheja aur jaankari hasil ki to pata chala ke wahan ki qaum Amaleqa bahut mazboot, Taqatwar aur sarkash hai. Unhone ne kaha ke ham agar unse muqabila karenge karenge to Shikast (defeat) se do char honge. Aur ye sun kar Israeliyon ne himmat haar di. Isse qaum ki buzdili saabit hui. Aur Dushman ka saamna karne ke liye koi tayyar na hua.
(Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕍
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki wafat ke baad jab logon ne apni hukumat qaem kar li to Hazrat Ali (as) Masjid gaye aur farmaya:
_"Khuda tum par Rahem kare. Tum wapas chale jao. Aaj meri haalat Janabe Moosa (as) jaisi ho chuki hai jinki sada e Labaik kahne ko koi tayyar na tha aur log unki madad ki bajae unka mazaq uda kar kahte the ke "Tum apne Rab ko apne saath le kar Jang karo, ham yahan baithe hue hain."_
_"Aaj ke baad mein is Masjid mein Ziyarat e Rasool (saww) ke liye aaonga ya phir logon ke faisle karne ke liye aaonga. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne mujhe Hujjat banaya tha aur Hujjat e Khuda logon ko hairat o pareshaani mein mubtila hota hua nahi dekh sakta."_
(Ehtejaaj e Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             ♦ _*BANI ISRAEL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (682)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ رَجُلَانِ مِنَ الَّذِينَ يَخَافُونَ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمَا ادْخُلُوا عَلَيْهِمُ الْبَابَ فَإِذَا دَخَلْتُمُوهُ فَإِنَّكُمْ غَالِبُونَ ۚ وَعَلَى اللَّهِ فَتَوَكَّلُوا إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Do afraad jo Khuda ka khauf rakhte hain aur jin par Khuda ne apna Fazl o Karam kiya tha unhone kaha un Jabbaron ke Muqabile mein darwaze ke andar ghus jao aur jab andar pahunch jaoge to tum hi ghalib rahoge aur agar tum Sachche Imaandar ho to Khuda par hi bharosa rakho."_
(Surah Maeda: 23)

📚📖 🕍
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein bataya ke Hazrat Moosa (as) ne apne qaum Bani Israel se kaha ke woh Sarzameen e Muqaddas mein dakhil ho jayen aur wahan ki qaum Amaleqa se Muqabila karen lekin ye log unki taqat ko dekh kar dar gay aur aage badhne par raazi nahi hue. Sirf do admi jo Mutaqqi wa parhezgar the is kaam ke liye badhe. Un par Allah ka Karam hua kiyonki woh Allah par Tawakkal (bharosa) rakhte the, Sachche aur Imaandar the. Ye do afraad aksar Tafseer ke mutabiq Yusha bin Noon aur Kalib bin Yufana bataya jata hai jo Bani Israel ke Naqeebon mein se the. Wo ye jaante the ke agar Dushman ke ghar mein ghus kar lada jae to fatah hona tay hai.
Hazrat Ali (as) farmate hain:
_"Bakhuda jis qaum par bhi uske ghar mein hamla kiya gaya, woh zaleel hui."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Khutba 27)

Ye waqea Maujooda Torah mein bhi hai: *سفر تثنيه باب اول*
(Shemot/Exodus:) End mein refer karen.

(To be Cont'd .....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔐
*وَعَلَى اللَّهِ فَتَوَكَّلُوا إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Tawakkal (Bharosa) Imaan ki chaabi 🗝 hai aur_
_Imaan Tawakkal ka taala 🔒 hai._
_Tawakkal ki haqeeqat Eesaar ايثار hai aur_
_Eesaar ki buniyad Haq ke tahet kisi cheez ko pesh karna hai aur_
_Tawakkal karne wala do mein se ek tarah ke Eesaar ka zaroor saboot deta hai._
_Agar woh Tawakkal ke Ma'lool معلول (effect) yani Kainaat ke liye Eesaar kare to woh Uske Hijaab mein aa jata hai aur agar woh Illat علت (Cause) ke liye Eesaar ka muzahera kare aur Illat e Eesaar Bari e Ta'ala hai to use Khuda ke saath Baqa (Everlasting) hasil ho jati hai."_
(Misbah ul Shariyah, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

_*TORAH (Old Testaments) of Jews:*_
(Shemot/Exodus:
_Exodus begins the story of God's revelation to his people of Israel through Moses, who leads them out of Egypt (Exodus 1–18) to Mount Sinai. There the people accept the covenant with God, agreeing to be his people and abide by his holy Law, in return for his agreeing to be their God, and protect and defend them from their enemies, and provide for and prosper them_)

_*Some related verses:*_
_"4: And also, I established My covenant with them to give them the land of Canaan, the land of their sojournings in which they sojourned."_

_"5: And also, I heard the moans of the children of Israel, whom the Egyptians are holding in bondage, and I remembered My covenant."_

_"6: Therefore, say to the children of Israel, 'I am the Lord, and I will take you out from under the burdens of the Egyptians, and I will save you from their labor, and I will redeem you with an outstretched arm and with great judgments."_

_"7: And I will take you to Me as a people, and I will be a God to you, and you will know that I am the Lord your God, Who has brought you out from under the burdens of the Egyptians."_

_"8. will bring you to the land, concerning which I raised My hand to give to Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob, and I will give it to you as a heritage; I am the Lord.'"_

_"9: Moses spoke thus to the children of Israel, but they did not hearken to Moses because of [their] shortness of breath and because of [their] hard labor."_

(Directly pasted from Torah, Shemot/Exodus online)

   ♦ _*BANI ISRAEL PAR AZAAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (683)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالُوا يَا مُوسَىٰ إِنَّا لَنْ نَدْخُلَهَا أَبَدًا مَا دَامُوا فِيهَا ۖ فَاذْهَبْ أَنْتَ وَرَبُّكَ فَقَاتِلَا إِنَّا هَاهُنَا قَاعِدُونَ * قَالَ رَبِّ إِنِّي لَا أَمْلِكُ إِلَّا نَفْسِي وَأَخِي ۖ فَافْرُقْ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ الْقَوْمِ الْفَاسِقِينَ * قَالَ فَإِنَّهَا مُحَرَّمَةٌ عَلَيْهِمْ ۛ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً ۛ يَتِيهُونَ فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ فَلَا تَأْسَ عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الْفَاسِقِينَ*

_"Qaum e Moosa (as) ne kaha: ke jab tak woh Jabbar  afraad wahan maujood hain us waqt tak ham hargiz wahan dakhil na honge. Bas  tum aur tumhara Rab dono jao aur lado. Ham yahan baithe hue hain."_
_"Is par Moosa (as) ne kaha ke Khudaya mera apni zaat aur apne bhai ke siwa kisi par qaboo nahi hai. Ab hamare aur un nafarman logon ke darmiyan judai dal de."_
_*"Allah ne jawab diya ke woh Mulk un par 40 Saal tak haram hai. Ye log is muddat mein zameen mein maare maare phirenge. Un nafarmanon ki haalat par hargiz taras Na khana."*_
(Surah Maeda: 24 - 26)

📚📖 🕍
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is waqae ka khulasa yun hai ke Moosa (as) ki qaum ne unki baat manne se inkar kiya to Hazrat Moosa (as) mayoos hue aur unhone Allah se apni bebasi ka izhar kiya. Allah ne in nafarmanon ko faasiq qarar diya aur unko badi kadi saza di, wo ye ke unke darmiyan judai payi jaegi aur 40 saal tak Sinai (Egypt) ke sehra mein bhatakte rahegi. Udhar Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki wafat ke baad Ali (as), Hasan (as), Husain (as), Salman e Farsi, Miqdaad Khuda ke Ahd par qaem rahe aur 40 saal baras tak Ummat e Islami ki sargardani (roaming) qaem rahi. Phir Hazrat Ali (as) bar sare iqtedar aye aur Aap (as) ne mukhalefin se jang ki. (Noorus Saqlain)
Bani Israel 40 Saal bhatakne ke baad hi Arze Muqaddas Shaam mein dakhil hui (unke pote dakhil hue).
Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya gaya kiya Arze Muqaddas Israeliyon ke liye likh di gayi thi?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Ji haan, Allah ne likh di thi, phir Khuda ne apna irada badal diya aur faisla kiya ke woh us mein dakhil na honge aur Khuda apne faisle badalne mein Azaad hai. Yehi wajah hai ke jab Namaz shuru hui thi to 2 Rakat thi magar Allah ne muqeem ke liye baad mein 2 Rakat aur add kar di aur musafir ke liye 2 Rakaten baqi rahin."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Misr ki mitti se apna sar na dhowo aur Misr ki mitti se bane hue bartano mein khana na khao, un mein khana zulmat ka moojib hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
Isiliye Allah ka Hazrat Moosa (as) ko hukm hua ke Yusuf (as) ki haddiyan wahan se nikal lo.

Bare Ilaha hame aisi nafarmani se bacha jiski wajah se Bani Israel ko is Azaab mein mubtila kiya.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕍
Amirul Momenin Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Aye logo! Agar tum Haq ki Nusrat o Imdad se pahlu na bachate aur Batil ko kamzor karne se kamzori na dikhate to jo tumhara ham paya na tha woh tum par daant na rakhta aur jisne tum par qaboo paa liya woh tum par qaboo na pata. Lekin tum to Bani Israel ki tarah Sahraye tayyah (desert) mein bhatak gaye. Mujhe apni Jaan ki Qasam mere baad tumhari sargardani (roaming) o pareshani kai gunah badh jayegi kiyonki tumne Haq ko pase pusht (pichhe) dal diya hai aur Qareebon se qata talluq kar liya hai aur door walon se rishta jod liya hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*ZAMEEN PAR PAHLA QATL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (684)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ ابْنَيْ آدَمَ بِالْحَقِّ إِذْ قَرَّبَا قُرْبَانًا فَتُقُبِّلَ مِنْ أَحَدِهِمَا وَلَمْ يُتَقَبَّلْ مِنَ الْآخَرِ قَالَ لَأَقْتُلَنَّكَ ۖ قَالَ إِنَّمَا يَتَقَبَّلُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْمُتَّقِينَ*

_"Aur unhe Adam (as) ke do beton ka qissa kisi kam o kast ke baghair (khara khara) sunayen. Jab unhone Qurbani ki to un mein ek ki Qurbani qubool hui aur doosre ki qubool na hui. Usne kaha ke mein zaroor tujhe qatl karonga. Usne jawab diya Allah to sirf Muttaqeen ki Nazaren hi qubool karta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 27)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jab Hazrat Moosa (as) Allah se baaten kar rahe the to Allah ne farmaya ke inko Hazrat Adam (as) ka qissa sunayen.
Rooye Zameen par ye pahla qatl waqe hua. Qatl ki wajah Nazr thi.
Aksar Tafseer mein zaeef rivayaten darj hain aur mashoor bhi hain. Woh ye ke Hazrat Adam (as) ke Judwa bachche paida hue ek ladka aur ek ladki. Aur Habeel ki Shaadi Qabeel ki bahen se aur Qabeel ki Habeel ki bahen se jo bad surat thi. isliye Qabeel razi nahi hua aur dono bhaiyon mein Dushmani ki wajah bani. (Majmaul Bayan).
Lekin Rivayat zaeef hai, kiyonki ye Haram kaam Janabe Adam (as) se kaise sarzad ho sakta hai. Imam (as) ne farmaya ye Hazrat Adam (as) par ghalat tohmat hai.
Shia Nazarya ye hai:
Imam Sadiq (as) se ye sawal kiya gaya ke Habeel aur Qabeel mein kis baat ka jhagda tha? Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_*"Maslah e Wasiyat ki wajah se usne bhai ko qatl kiya.* Allah Ta'ala ne Adam (as) ko Waḥy ki ke woh Wasiyat aur Isme Aazam e Ilahi Habeel ke supurd karen jabke Qabeel umr mein Habeel se bada tha. Jab Qabeel ne suna to use ghussa aya. Usne kaha ke is Wasiyat ka mein zyada Haqdar hun. Allah ne Waḥy ki dono apni Qurbaniyan (Nazr) pesh karen. Jab unhone Qurbaniyan pesh ki to Habeel ki qurbani manzoor hui aur Qabeel ki namanzoor hui. Isse Qabeel ko Hasad paida hua aur usne bhai ko qatl kar diya."_
(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
Hazrat Adam (as) Baitul Shareef ki Ziyarat ko Mecca gaye the. Tab Qabeel ne Patthar se Hazrat Habeel ka sar kuchal diya.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Qabeel ne apne bhai Habeel ko qatl kiya aur usne unke lashe ko zameen par dal diya. Use ye ilm nahi tha ke ab kiya kare. Darinde uski laash khane ko aage badhe. Qabeel uski laash ko bori mein dal kar apni pusht par dal kar chalne laga._
_Allah ne do Kawwe (Crow) bheje jo apas mein ladne lage. Ek ne doosre ko qatl kiya. Phir usne apni chonch aur qadmon se ek gadha (pit) khoda usne murde ko gadha mein dala aur mitti se uski laash chhupa di. Jab Qabeel ne ye manzar dekha to usne bhi waise hi kiya."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
Ye pahla dafn tha.

Bare Ilaha hame in Gunahe Kabirah jaise Hasad o Qatl se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚔
Imam Baqar (as):
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Qayamat ke Din sab se pahle Allah Ta'ala Khoon ka Faisla karega. Sab se pahle Hazrat Adam (as) ke do farzandon ko laya jayega, unke darmiyan Faisla kiya jayega. Phir tarteeb war tamam maqtooleen ke Faisle honge. Us Din Maqtool (Killed one) apne Qatil (Killer) ka gareban pakad kar Khuda ki Adalat mein pesh hoga aur Maqtool ke chehre se Khoon tapak raha hoga. Us waqt koi Qatil Khuda se kuchh bhi chhupa nahi sakega."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*DUNIYA KA PAHLA NAUHA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (685)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَئِنْ بَسَطْتَ إِلَيَّ يَدَكَ لِتَقْتُلَنِي مَا أَنَا بِبَاسِطٍ يَدِيَ إِلَيْكَ لِأَقْتُلَكَ ۖ إِنِّي أَخَافُ اللَّهَ رَبَّ الْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Aur agar tu mujhe qatl karne haath uthayega to mein tujhe qatl karne ke liye apna haath nahi uthaonga. Mein Allah Rabbul Aalameen se darta hun."_
(Surah Maeda: 28)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Qissa e Adam (as) ke zel mein is Ayat mein ye Habeel ka qaul hai.
Jaisa ke ham ne bataya ke Habeel Shaheed hue, ye Duniya ka pahla qatl tha.
Isliye ek Shaheed par pahli baar Nauha bhi padha gaya. Hazrat Adam (as) bahut ghamzada hue aur ye Ashaar padhe.
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) se Rivayat hai:
Hazrat Adam (as):
*تغيرات البلاء و من عليها*
*فوجه الارض مغبر قبيح*
*تغير كل ذى لون و طعم*
*و قل بشاشة الوجه المليح.*
_"Ilaqe aur unke rahne wale sab badal gaye. Zameen ka chehra ghubar aalood aur qabeeh dikhai dene laga hai. Rang o zaiyqa rakhne wali har cheez badal gayi aur khoobsurat chehre ki bashashat kam ho gayi."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)

*قتل قابيل هابيل اخاه*
*فوا أسفا على الوجه المليح.*
_"Qabeel ne apne bhai Habeel ko qatl kar diya hai._
_Hai afsos is Khoobsurat chehre par."_
(Kitabul Khisaal)
♨
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
Jaisa ke Ayat mein hai: "Jis Qurbani (Nazr) par Aasmani aag girti to wo Nazr qubool ho jati."
Isliye Qabeel ne Aag ki pooja karne ke liye Aatish kada (Agni Mandir) taamir kiya. Ye Duniya ka sab se pahla Mandir tha. Lekin Qabeel ki Nazr (Prasad) qubool nahi hui aur is Hasad mein Habeel ka qatl kar diya. Jab Hazrat Adam (as) ne Habeel ko Maqtool paya to Nauha kuna hue:
Zameen ko mukhatib hokar kaha:
_"Tujh par Laanat ho, tu ne Habeel ka Khoon choos liye."_
Hazrat Adam (as) chalis raatein Habeel par girya karte rahe, rote rahe.
🚩
Ab jo Azadari e Imam Husain (as) par eitraz karte hain dekh len ke Nauha wa girya ye sab Sunnat e Adam (as) hai, jo ke ek Nabi the. Apne Mehboob ki judai par ghamzada hona ye insaani fitrat hai. Ise koi rok nahi sakta.

Bare Ilaha hame bhi unke Azadaron mein mahshoor farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ♨
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Dozakh ke nichle tabqe mein Sandooq hoga aur us mein 12 afraad qaed honge aur unhe Dozakh ka sakht tareen Azaab diya jayega. Un mein 6 afraad ka talluq Awwaleen aur 6 ka talluq Akherin se hoga. Aur un mein Adam (as) ke farzand jisne apne bhai ko qatl kiya tha aur Firaon wa Hamaam sare fehrist honge."_
_"Jis Kawwe ne zameen khodi thi uska na to koi Baap tha na hi koi Maa."_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
             *28th Shawwal 1438*
       *23rd July 2017, Sunday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
         ♦ _*QATL KA GUNAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (686)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنِّي أُرِيدُ أَنْ تَبُوءَ بِإِثْمِي وَإِثْمِكَ فَتَكُونَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ النَّارِ ۚ وَذَٰلِكَ جَزَاءُ الظَّالِمِينَ*

_"(Habeel:) Main chahta hun ke tu mera aur apna gunah samet le aur Dozakhi ban jaye aur Zulm karne walon ke liye yahi Saza hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 29)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Tazkara e Habeel aur Qabeel Jaari hai:

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
"Jab Adam (as) ke dono farzandon ko Qurbani ka hukm mila to ek ne apne revad (sheep herd) ka mota taza Dumba (Sheep) Qurbani ke liye pesh kiya aur doosre ne kuchh bekar khoshe pesh kiye. Dumbe ke malik Habeel ki Qurbani qubool hui aur jis ne bekar khoshe rakhe the uski Qurbani na manzoor hui.
Qabeel ko Gussa aya. Usne Habeel se kaha mein tujhe qatl kar dunga...Ayat..phir Habeel ne kaha: Mein Chahta hun ke tu mera gunah samet le...(Aaj ki Ayat)"
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim)

Qur'an Majeed mein Hazrat Adam (as) ke beton ka naam nahi diye gaye hain. Bible Old Testaments ki Torah mein Cain aur Abel naam ayen hain. Aur Rivayaat mein bhi inke naam yehi bataye gaye hain.

Torah ka is waqea ka ek part peshe khidmat hai:

_"Now, it came to pass at the end of days that Cain brought of the fruit of the soil an offering to the Lord. And Abel, he too brought of the firstborn of his flocks and of their fattest, and the Lord turned to Abel and to his offering. But to Cain and to his offering, He did not turn, and it annoyed Cain exceedingly, and his countenance fell. And the Lord said to Cain, "Why are you annoyed, and why has your countenance fallen? Is it not so that if you improve, it will be forgiven you? If you do not improve, however, at the entrance, sin is lying, and to you is its longing, but you can rule over it." And Cain spoke to Abel his brother, and it came to pass when they were in the field that Cain rose up against Abel his brother and slew him."_
(Genesis 4: 3-8)

Bare Ilaha hame Tere muhibbon ke Ehya (enlivement) karne walon mein shumar kar, aisa na ho ke anjane me hamse kisi ka qatl ho jaye.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📆
Hazrat Ali (as) se sawal kiya gaya ke hame Budh ka Din (Wednesday) bhari bhari kiyon lagta hai, aur ham ise unlucky maante hain?
Imam (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Woh Mahine ka Akhiri Budh hota hai aur isi Din Qabeel ne Habeel ko qatl kiya tha aur Raaton mein chaand thodi der ke liye namudar hota hai."_

🍽 🍪🍵🥛
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek Momin ko khaana khilana mere nazdeek 10 Ghulam azaad karne aur 10 bar Hajj karne se behtar hai._
_Agar tum Momin ko khaana nahi khilaoge to woh mar jayega ya phir majboor ho kar kisi Nasibi ke darwaze par Roti ka sawal karega. Jabke Nasibi ke saamne sawal karne se uske liye Maut kahin behtar hai._
_Jo shakhs kisi ek Momin ko zindagi bakhshe to goya usne tamam insaano ko zindagi bakhshi hai. Agar tumne use khana na khilaya to goya tumne use maar diya hai aur agar tumne use khaana khilaya to goya tumne use zindagi di hai."_
(Usool e Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

( *Nasibi* means Ahle Bait (as) ka Dushman)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
       ♦ _*HAZRAT ABU TALIB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (687)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَطَوَّعَتْ لَهُ نَفْسُهُ قَتْلَ أَخِيهِ فَقَتَلَهُ فَأَصْبَحَ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ*

_"Akhirkar uske Nafs ne uske bhai ka qatl uske liye aasaan bana diya aur usne use qatl kar diya aur yun woh khasara (Loss) uthane walon mein se ban gaya."_
(Surah Maeda: 30)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Habeel ke qatl ka tazkara is Ayat mein bhi jaari hai jiski wazahat ho chuki hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*EVENT OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📖
🌷 *IMAAN E ABU TALIB (as)* 🌷
Hazrat Abu Talib (as) us shakhsiyat ka naam hai jab Islam ubhar raha tha, usko sahara diya. Kiya Islam Kufr ki goud mein pala. Islam to 40 Saal ke baad logon ke darmiyan aya, kiya 40 Saal ye ek Kafir ki goud mein pal raha tha. Rasool e Islam Abu Talib ke qile mein pale. Kiya ye Kufr ka qila tha. Duniya ne ye ajab Islam ka mazaaq udaya: 'Islam ko pala posa Kufr ne.' phir sawal Rasool e Akram (saww) ke Nikah par bhi uthta hai ke ek Kafir ne Rasool (saww) ka Nikah kaise padh diya. Hamare Nabi ko Kuffar se bachane ke liye unhe Shebe Abi Talib (as) mein rakha, yani Islam ki hifazat hui Shebe Abu Talib mein.
Kaun kahta ke Islam ki shuru'at Be'sat e Rasool e Akram (saww) se hui. Kiya pahle Islam ka wujood nahi tha. Qur'an mein Allah ne declare kiya Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka Deen Islam tha. Woh bhi Deen-e-Hanif. Hazrat Esa (as) se Rasool e Akram (saww) ke darmiyani waqfe ko Ayyam e Fatrah kahte hain jiski wazahat ham kar chuke hain. Tarikh mein hain ke in Ayyam mein agar Nabi na the lekin Ausiya the. Duniya ek Din bhi Hujjat e Khuda se khali nahi rah sakti. Tarikh mein hai Hazrat Ismail bin Ibrahim (as) ki nasl Arab mein Ka'abe ke muhafiz rahi aur baqi Deeni faraez anjam diye. Jo Ka'abe ki sarparasti karta wohi sab ka Rahnuma hota. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne jab Ailane Risalat kiya to sab se pahle Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ko hi mukhalifat karni chahiye thi, ke jabke mein yahan ka sarparast hun, aap kaise ye dawa kar rahe hain. Tarikh mein Abu Jahl ka naam hai, Abu Talib (as) ka naam mukhalifat mein nahi. Abu Talib (as) par Kufr ke fatwe dene wale ye Tarikh mein dekha den ke kab unhone but parasti ki. Ye baat sirf Hazrat Abu Talib (as) tak nahi rah sakti balke Rasool (saww) ke poore khandan par lagu hoti hai. Kiya Hazrat Abdullah, Hazrat Abdul Muttalib ..... ne Kalma padha. Kalma woh padhta hai jo pahle Kafir ho. Aaj bhi ek Kafir jab Kalma padh leta hai to kiya woh Musalman ho jata hai? Lekin kiya sirf zaban se Kalma padh lena Musalman hone ki daleel hai. Hamne to aaj ek pandit ko stage par Arabic mein Kalma sunate hue suna balke uska tarjuma wa wazahat karte hue suna. To kiya woh Musalman ho gaya? nahi. Woh to wapas Mandir mein pooja kar raha hai. Isliye sirf zaban se kalam kafi nahi, amal bhi dekha jata hai.
Hamne Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ko Mohsin e Islam paya. Unke Islam par bahut ehsanaat hain. Karbala mein Imran ke pote Imam Husain (as) ne Islam ko bachaya to Imran (Abu Talib as) ne Baani e Islam Rasoole Akram (saww) ko Kuffar ke sharr se bachaya, warna Rasoole (saww) ki zindagi to bahut khatre mein thi. Isliye agar aaj Islam ke wujood agar hai to Hazrat Abu (as) ki wajah se.
Ikhtesar se kaam lete hue ham is baat ka tazkara ke is Kufr ke fatwe ki kab aur kaise shuru'at hui aur iske pichhe kiya asbaab the, isko chhote hue sirf itna bata sakte hain jinhone is haqeeqat ko jaan liya woh raahe raast par aa rahe hain.
Ahle Sunnat ke Azeem Rahnuma Aala Hazrat ne bhi ye iqraar kiya ke Hazrat Abu Talib (as) is Duniya se Musalman ki hasiyat se gaye. Unhone sirf kaha hi nahi balke ek poori Kitab likhi hai jiska naam hai:
_"Sharhul Matalib fi Mabhas e Abi Talib"_ (1316 AH)
(Ye kitab ham ne khud dekhi bhi hai. Urdu mein hai.)

Bare Ilaha hame Imaan e Abu Talib (as) ke sath mehsoor karna, unke naqshe qadam par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
*Faqat Wiladat Mubarak.*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

       *25th July 2017, Tuesday,*

       ♦ _*QAATIL KA ANJAAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (688)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ غُرَابًا يَبْحَثُ فِي الْأَرْضِ لِيُرِيَهُ كَيْفَ يُوَارِي سَوْءَةَ أَخِيهِ ۚ قَالَ يَا وَيْلَتَا أَعَجَزْتُ أَنْ أَكُونَ مِثْلَ هَٰذَا الْغُرَابِ فَأُوَارِيَ سَوْءَةَ أَخِي ۖ فَأَصْبَحَ مِنَ النَّادِمِينَ*

_"Phir Allah ne ek Kawwa (Crow) bheja jo zameen khodne laga taake use batayen ke apne bhai ki laash kaise chhupaye. Ye dekh kar usne kaha: Mujh par afsos mein to is Kawwe jaisa bhi na ho saka ke apne bhai ki laash ko chhupa sakta aur woh pashemani uthane walon mein se ban gaya."_
(Surah Maeda: 31)

📚📖 ⚰
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj ki Ayat ke mauzoo ki rivayaten ham pahle bayan kar chuke hain. Mazeed kuchh Rivayaat peshe khidmat hain:

Mohd bin Muslim ne 2 sawal kiye:
_"(1) Duniya ki 1/4th (ek chauthai) abadi kab khatm hui?_
_(2) Qatil Qabeel ka anjaam kiya hua?"_
🍁
Imam Mohd Baqir (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Jis waqt Qabeel ne Habeel ko qatl kiya us waqt insaano ki abadi kul 4 afraad par mushtamil thi: Adam, Hawwa, Habeel aur Qabeel. Chunanche jab Qabeel ne Habeel ko qatl kiya to insaani abadi ka ek chauthai hissa khatm ho gaya."_
_"Adam (as) ka beta Qabeel balon ke saath chashma e Aftab ke sath muallaq (hanged) hai. Woh Qayamat tak sardi garmi ka Azaab jhelta rahega. Jab Qayamat ka Din hoga to use Dozakh mein dal diya jayega."_

Insaan jab pasti (lowly) ki taraf jata hai to janwar se bhi badtar ho jata hai jiska iqraar Qabeel ne kiya. Qatil apne junoon mein apne hosh kho baithta hai aur ye zalil harkat karne par amada ho jata hai phir naadim hota hai.

Bare Ilaha hame aise marahil se bachane ke ham apne hosh na kho baithe jiske natije mein hame pachhtana pade.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡 *Ajr-e-Jaariyah*
Hazrat Ali (as):
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs koi achchi ravish jaari karega to use uska Ajr diya jayega aur Qayamat ke Din tak jo bhi uski qaem kardah ravish par amal karega, amal karne wale ke sath sath us ravish ko jaari karne wale ko bhi uska Ajr milta rahega._
_Aur jo koi buri ravish jaari karega uska bojh uski gardan par hoga aur uske baad jo bhi us par amal karega uske gunah sath sath buri ravish ke baani ko bhi gunah milta rahega."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🗡
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jis kisi insaan ka bhi khoon bahaya jata hai uski jawab dehi ka ek hissa Qabeel ke zimme hota hai ke jis ne Insaan kashi ki is buri sunnat ki Duniya mein buniyad rakhi."_
(Tafseer fi Zilal, Vol 2, P-703)

            ♦ _*AHYA-E-INSAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (689)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مِنْ أَجْلِ ذَٰلِكَ كَتَبْنَا عَلَىٰ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ أَنَّهُ مَنْ قَتَلَ نَفْسًا بِغَيْرِ نَفْسٍ أَوْ فَسَادٍ فِي الْأَرْضِ فَكَأَنَّمَا قَتَلَ النَّاسَ جَمِيعًا وَمَنْ أَحْيَاهَا فَكَأَنَّمَا أَحْيَا النَّاسَ جَمِيعًا ۚ وَلَقَدْ جَاءَتْهُمْ رُسُلُنَا بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ ثُمَّ إِنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ بَعْدَ ذَٰلِكَ فِي الْأَرْضِ لَمُسْرِفُونَ*

_"Isi wajah se Hamne Bani Israel par ye hukm likh diya ke jisne kisi Insaan ko Khoon ke badle ya Zameen mein fasaad phailane ke siwa kisi aur wajah se qatl kiya to usne goya tamam Insaano ko qatl kar diya aur jisne kisi ko zindagi bakhshi usne goya tamam insaano ko zindagi bakhshi magar unka haal ye hai ke hamare Rasool pai dar pai unke paas khuli khuli hidayat lekar aye phir bhi aksar afraad ziyadti karne wale."_
(Surah Maeda: 32)

📚📖 🥛
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaton mein tazkara Qaatil Qabeel ka chal raha tha. Aaj ki ayat ki Tafseer guzishta post mein kar chuke hain.  Rivayaaton se ye bhi pata chala 1 Habeel ke qatl se Insaanon ki 1/4th abadi kam ho gayi. Usi tarah kisi Insaan ko zindagi bakshna jiski Rivayaat ham pesh kar chuke hain. Ek aur Rivayat pesh e khidmat hai:
🌿☘
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke jo koi kisi ko jalne ya doobne se bachaye to usne goya tamam Insaano ko zindagi ata ki hai."_
Iske baad Aap (as) khamosh ho gaye aur phir farmaya:
_*"Iski Azeem Taweel ye hai ke agar koi kisi ke Haq mein Dua kare aur wo Dua qubool ho jaye to usne bhi goya tamam Insaano ko zindagi ata ki."*_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame aisi taufeeq ata farma ke ham insaano ke liye zindagi ka sabab bane na ke unki halakat ka sabab.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌹🌷
Qazi Nurullah Shushtari (d. 1109 A.H) rivayat karte hain:
🕌🌻
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):

*تُقبَض فيها امْراةٌ منْ وُلْدى، اِسْمُها فاطِمَةُ بِنْتُ مُوسى، وتَدْخُلُ بِشَفاعَتِها شيعَتى الجنّة بَاجْمَعِهِمْ*

_"Meri aulad mein se Ek Khatoon jiska naam Fatema binte Musa hai, unki wafat Qum mein hogi. Qayamat ke Din woh hamare sabhi Shiyon ki Jannat mein dakhil hone ke liye Shafa'at karengi."_
(Bihār al-Anwār, vol. 60, p. 228; Majālis al-Mu’minīn, vol. 1, p. 83.)
🕌🌻
Allama Majlisi rivayat karte hain:  
Imam Sadiq (as):
*وَسَتُدْفَنُ فيها امْرَأةٌ مِنْ اَوْلادى تُسَمّى فاطِمَةَ، فَمَنْ زارَها وَجَبَتْ لَهُ الجنّة*

_"Meri aulad mein se Ek Khatoon jiska naam Fatema binte Musa hai, woh Qum mein dafn hongi. Jo bhi unki (Qabre Mathar) Ziyarat ko jayega woh yaqeenan Jannat mein dakhil hoga."_
(Bihār al-Anwār, vol. 48, p. 317 & vol. 60, p. 216 & vol. 102, p. 266)

     ♦ _*MUHAREBIN KI SAZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (690)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا جَزَاءُ الَّذِينَ يُحَارِبُونَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَيَسْعَوْنَ فِي الْأَرْضِ فَسَادًا أَنْ يُقَتَّلُوا أَوْ يُصَلَّبُوا أَوْ تُقَطَّعَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَأَرْجُلُهُمْ مِنْ خِلَافٍ أَوْ يُنْفَوْا مِنَ الْأَرْضِ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ لَهُمْ خِزْيٌ فِي الدُّنْيَا ۖ وَلَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ * إِلَّا الَّذِينَ تَابُوا مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَقْدِرُوا عَلَيْهِمْ ۖ فَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Jo log Allah aur Uske Rasool se ladte hain aur zameen mein fasaad barpa karne ke liye koshish karte hain to unki saza ye hai ke qatl kiye jayen ya Sooli (hanged) par chadhaye jayen ya unke haath aur paon mukhalif simton se kaat dale jayen ya woh jila watan (exiled) kar diye jayen. Ye to Duniya mein unki zillat o ruswai hai aur Akherat mein unke liye bahut bada Azaab hai."_
_"Albatta woh afraad isse mustashna hain (chhoot hai) jo tumhare qaboo paane se pahle Tauba kar len. Jaan lo ke Allah Ma'af Karnewala aur Rahem Farmanewala hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 33 - 34)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jo Allah wa Rasool se lade unke liye 4 Saza batayi gayi hain:
(1) Rasool e Jang aur fasaad :> Qatl
(2) Qatl aur Loot: > Sooli aur Qatl
(3) Sirf Loot: > Haath paon kaatna.
(4) Jang kare lekin na qatl kare na loote: > Jila Watan.
(Rivayat Imam Reza (as)- Noorus Saqlain)

Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Zamana e Jang ke do hukm hain. Jab jang chal rahi ho aur Kuffar ki poori tarah se sarkoobi na hoi ho (suppressed) to is haalat mein jo bhi Janjoo giraftar ho to Imam (as) (ya Naeb e Imam, hakim e sharah) ko ikhtiyar hai chaahe to uski gardan qalam kar de aur agar chaahe to uske haath paon mukhalif simt se qata karaye aur use zakhmi haalat mein chhod de yahan tak ke woh tadap tadap kar mar jaye. Allah farmata hai (Ayat: 5:33). Imam ko Kufr ki buniyad par mukhtalif sazayen dene ka ikhtiyar hai"_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Ye sazae unke liye bhi hain jinhone ne Rahbarane Deen, Allah ke numaindon, Janashine Rasool se jang ki. Dushmanane Ahle Bait (as) ke liye bhi yehi sazayen hain. Woh to Hazrat Ali (as) ne Jang e Jamal mein us zan par rahem kiya aur sirf uski oontni ke pair kaat diye warna ye hadd iske liye bhi jaari kar sakte the.

Bare Ilaha hame Imam ke nasir o madadgaron mein shamil rakh na ke unke Dushmanon mein.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚔
Jab sawal kiya gaya ke kiya koi bhi saza di ja sakti hai:
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
_"Aisa nahi hai, tamam sazaon ki koi na koi hadd na hai. Agar koi qatl kare aur maal bhi loot le to use qatl kiya jayega aur Saleeb par chadhaya jayega aur agar koi qatl kare aur maal na loote to use qatl kiya jayega aur agar koi maal loot le aur qatl na kare to uske haath paon kaat diye jayenge aur agar woh bhag jaye aur haath na aye. Phir kuchh arse baad pakda jaye to uske haath paon kaat diye jayenge. Haan agar koi giraftari se qabl Tauba kar le to uske haath paon nahi katenge."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚔
Surah bin Kalbi ka bayan hai ke ek shakhs ghar se Masjid ki taraf ravana hota hai ya apne kisi kaam ke liye kahin jata hai. Raaste mein ek shakhs milta hai aur usse mara mari karta hai aur uske kapde utar leta hai. To Sharayi hukm kiya hai? Fuquha se poochha to bataya ke ye loot mar ka waqea hai to uska jurm "Muharib" (yaani ladne wala) mein nahi hai."
⚔
Imam Sadiq (as) ne usse sawal kiya:
_"Achha batao Darul Islam ki hurmat zyada hai ya Darush Shirk ki?"_
Raavi ne jawab diya Darul Islam.
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Is mujrim ka talluq "Muharebin" mein se hai aur is Ayat (5:33) mein shamil hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*WASEELAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (691)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَابْتَغُوا إِلَيْهِ الْوَسِيلَةَ وَجَاهِدُوا فِي سَبِيلِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Allah se darte raho aur *Uski Bargah mein baryabi ka (qurbat ke liye) WASEELA talash karo* aur Uski Raah mein Jihad karo taake kamyab ho jao."_
(Surah Maeda: 35)

📚📖 💹 ⛓
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein 3 Ahkam bayan kiye gaye hain:
(1) Taqwa-e-Ilahi
(2) Khuda se Qurbat ke liya Waseela ki talash.
(3) Jihad fi Sableelillah.

Waseela us cheez ko kahte hain jo mukhtalif cheezon ko ek doosre se milati hai. Jaise seedi (ladder) Chhat chadhne ke liye waseela hai. Same usi tarah se Ahle Imaan ke liye wohi waseela hoga jiska ek rukh Makhlooq aur doosra rukh Khaliq ki taraf hoga, aur woh Khuda se lega aur insaano tak iska faiz pahunchayega. Allah ne ye nahi kaha ke Waseela banao balke ye kaha talaash karo, banana Allah ka kaam hai. Aur talaash karna Ahle Imaan ka kaam hai. Anbiya o Mursalin aur Aimma e Huda ko Allah ne Waseela banaya.
Ek nuqte ki taraf ishara karna hai woh ye ke saare Musalman Salwaat/Darood Sharif padhte hain.
*اَللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلى مُحَمَّدٍ وَّآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ*
_"Aye Allah! Muhammad aur unke Ahle Bait (as) par Rahmat nazil kar."_
Kiya unko is Dua ki zaroorat hai? Kiya un par Rahmat nazil nahi ho rahi? Nahi. Ye Dua mangna khud iska saboot hai ke hamne inko hamara Waseela qarar diya. Ham apni upar Rahmat nazil hone ki Dua nahi kar rahe. Yaani jitni bhi Rahmat ham par nazil hongi Muhammad wa Ale Muhammad (as) ke waseele se nazil hongi.
Means har cheez hame Waseele se milti hai. Rizq, barish, aur baqi Ne'maten Allah se direct nahi milti, balke farishton ke zariye Ahle Bait (as) ke waseele se ham tak pahunchti hain.
Zyada tafseel ki gunjaish nahi.
Imam Reza (as):
_"Aimma Aulade Husain (as) se honge jisne unki ita'at ki to usne Allah ki ita'at ki aur jisne unki nafarmani ki to usne Allah ki nafarmani ki. Woh Mazboot Rassi hain aur Khuda ki Bargah tak pahunchne ka Waseela hain."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)

Bare Ilaha ba Waseela Chahardah Masoomeen (as) ke hame aur tamam Mo'meneen ko behtareen Ne'maton se nawaz.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇📚 💹⛓
*"Khutba-e-Waseela"*
Ke kuchh important point:

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"logo! Allah Ta'ala ne apne Nabi (saww) se "Waseele" ka waada kiya hai aur Allah hargiz Waada khilafi nahi karta. Agah raho! "Waseela" Jannat ka buland tareen darjah hai aur Maqame Taqarrub ka Akhiri Nuqta hai aur Aarzo'on ki Akhri hadd hai. ......_
_Maqame Waseela yaani Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke dayen taraf hadde nigah baadal dikhai dega aur jisse ye nida ayegi: Ahle moqif! Khush khabri hai uske liye jo Nabi (saww) par imaan laya aur uske Wasi se Muhabbat ki ho aur jisne inkaar kiya uska thikana Dozakh hai. ...."_
(Poora Khutba Nahjul Balagha mein refer karen.)
🌿☘
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Jannat mein Batin Arsh tak do tarah ke Moti honge. Ek safed aur doosra zard (yellow) rang ka hoga aur phir har ek mein 70 Hazaar bala khane honge jinke darwaze aur peyalon ka madda ek hi hoga. Safed Rang ke mahallaat ka naam "Maqame Waseela" hai woh Muhammad (saww) hain aur unke Ahle Bait (as) ke liye hoga aur yellow Ibrahim (as) aur unke Ahle Bait ke liye honge."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ _*TAWASSUL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (692)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَابْتَغُوا إِلَيْهِ الْوَسِيلَةَ وَجَاهِدُوا فِي سَبِيلِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Allah se darte raho aur *Uski Bargah mein baryabi ka (qurbat ke liye) WASEELA talash karo* aur Uski Raah mein Jihad karo taake kamyab ho jao."_
(Surah Maeda: 35)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
(Cont'd ........)
Jaisa ke Qur'an mein zikr hota hai ke Waseela talaash karo. Iske zel mein hamne kuchh Rivayaat pesh ki.
Anbiya wa Aimma (as) se Tawassul bhi ek Allah se Qurbat ka ek Waseela hai. Is topic par ham pahle Sura Nisa:64 ke zel mein tazkara kar chuke hain, is Ayat mein hai ke Allah ne Rasool (saww) ko hukm diye ke agar woh Gunehgaro ke liye Maghfirat talab karenge to Allah qubool karega.
Nez Sura Yusuf:97 mein braderaan e Yusuf (as) ne apne baap se Bargahe Khuda wandi mein Istighfar ki request ki aur Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne unki request ko qubool ki.
Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne apne baap ke liye Maghfirat talab ki. (Tauba:114)
(Jo Qur'an mein Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Baap ka zikr hai, asl mein woh unke chacha the, jo baap ki manzil par the.)

Maroof Ahle Sunnat Alim Samhoodi apni book "Wafa ul Wafa mein bayan karte hain:
_"Bargahe Khuda mein Rasulullah (saww) aur unke maqam o martaba ke Waseele se Aap ki Wiladat se pahle, Aapki Wiladat ke baad, Aap ki rehlat ke baad, Aalam e Barzakh ke dauran mein aur Qayamat ke Din, Shafa'at talab karna jaez hai."_
(I وفاء الوفا,Vol: 3, P-1371)

1. Tawassul ka ye matlab ye nahi ke unse Hajat talab ki ja rahi hai, balke unki Manzelat ko samne rakh kar Allah ki hi taraf tawajjo karna hai.

2. Anbiya wa Aimma (as) ki Hayaat wa Wafaat mein farq nahi hai. Dono mein woh Shafee hain. Kiyonki Shaheed zinda hote hain (Ale Imran: 169)

3. Ahle Sunnat ke kuchh hazrat aur aksar Wahabi nazrayat rakhne wale Wasilah wa Shafa'at ko nahi maante jabke is par kaseer ta'daad mein Rivayaat maujood hain, woh unko jhutlate hain aur zaeef qaraar dete hain. Jabke ye Ayat (5:35) to bilkul clear hai. Ye unki hatdharmi ke siwa kuchh nahi.

Bare Ilaha hame ba Tawassul e Ahle Bait (as) hamare gunahon ki maghfirat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Reza (as)
se sawaal huwa ke Namaz e Janaza ka hukm kyun diya gaya hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Taaki log uski Khuda ke huzoor shafaa'at karein aur uski maghferat ki Dua maangein aur koi bhi shakhs us ghadi se zyada Shafa'at aur Astagfaar ka mohtaaj nahi hota jitna ke marne wala mohtaaj hota hai"._
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p241)

                 ♦ _*KAFIR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (693)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَوْ أَنَّ لَهُمْ مَا فِي الْأَرْضِ جَمِيعًا وَمِثْلَهُ مَعَهُ لِيَفْتَدُوا بِهِ مِنْ عَذَابِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ مَا تُقُبِّلَ مِنْهُمْ ۖ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ*

_"Yaqeenan jin logon ne Kufr kiya agar unke qabze mein rooye Zameen ki sari Daulat ho aur itni mazeed Daulat bhi unke paas ho aur woh chahen ke woh ise fidya de kar Qayamat ke Din ke Azaab se bach jayen tab bhi unse wo Daulat qubool na ki jayegi aur unke liye dardnaak Azaab hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 36)

📚📖 ♨
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Waseela wa Tawassul ka zikr hua. Ab jo log iska inkar karte hain, yani Khuda ke hukm ko nahi maante, Kufr karte hain. Shaitan ne chahe kitni Ibaadaten ki lekin Hazrat Adam (as) ko Sajdah nahi kiya. Uski daleel thi ke Allah ke siwa kisi ko bhi mein Sajda nahi kar sakta. Usne Qayas kiya. Wo ye nahi samjha ke woh Khuda ke hukm ko nahi maan raha hai. Isliye mardood ho gaya aur aaj insaano mein bhi kuchh isi tarah ki taujeeh par amal kar rahe hain.
Kafir ke liye Qayamat ke Din koi rishwat kaam nahi ayegi. Duniya koi Daulat kaam nahi ayegi sirf kaam ayegi to wo hai Muhabbate Ahle Bait (as). Allah ne kaha Ahle Bait (as) ke naqshe qadam par chalo, ab jo is par amal na kare yaani Kufr kar raha hai.
Imam Baqir wa Sadiq (as) se Rivayaat hain ke Kafiron ki tarah Hazrat Ali (as) ke Dushmanon ke liye bhi Abadi Azaab hai unhe kisi qimat par Dozakh se rihai naseeb na hogi.
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha ham un Kafiron se panah mangte hain jo Tere Hadi o Wali ka inkaar karte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo banda Ali (as) par doosre ashaab ko fazilat o fauqiyat (preference / praadhanya) de, wo yaqeenan Kaafir hai."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p623)

Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jisko Allah aur uske Rasul (saww) mein shak ho wo Kaafir hai."_
(Al Kaafi, v4, p357)

             *7th Zilqad 1438*

              ♦ _*DOZAKH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (694)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَخْرُجُوا مِنَ النَّارِ وَمَا هُمْ بِخَارِجِينَ مِنْهَا ۖ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ مُقِيمٌ*

_"Wo chahenge ke Dozakh ki aag se nikal jayen magar woh wahan se nikal nahi sakenge aur unke liye daymi Azaab hoga."_
(Surah Maeda: 37)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇📚📖 ♨
Imam Ali (as):
_"…Ahle Dozakh ki kaal-kothdi mein kabhi thandi hawa ka guzar nahi hoga. Unki zindagi khatm na hogi aur unhe nit-naye tariqe se azaab diya jaayega. Na to Dozakh ki aag khatm hogi aur na hi Ahl e Dozakh ki zindagi tamaam hogi."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p559)
♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Meri aur mere Ahlebait (as) ki Wilayat Dozakh se amaan deti hai."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p444)
♨
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"H. Fatima Zahra (sa) ki azmat ke sabab Allah Ta'ala ne unki zurriyat par aatish e Dozakh ko haraam kar diya hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p113)
✍🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hargiz kisi Aalim ko mat jhutlao aur na uske qaul (baat) ki tardeed (mukhaalifat) karo aur na us se bugz rakkho…Jis kisi ne Aalim ki tauheen ki usne meri tauheen ki aur jis ne meri tauheen ki usne Khuda ki tauheen ki aur jis ne Khuda ki tauheen ki wo Dozakh mein gaya….Aagah ho jao ke Khuda Aalim ki tauheen se aisa hi gazab-naak hota hai jaise koi Ameer ba-ikhtiyaar (Powerful king) apne na-farmaan gulaam par."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p52)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                  ♦ _*CHORI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (695)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَالسَّارِقُ وَالسَّارِقَةُ فَاقْطَعُوا أَيْدِيَهُمَا جَزَاءً بِمَا كَسَبَا نَكَالًا مِنَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ*

_"Chor khwah Mard ho ya Aurat dono ke haath kaat dalo. Ye unki kamai ka badla hai. Ye unke liye Allah ki taraf se ibratnak saza hai. Allah Ghalib aur Saheb e Hikmat hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 38)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Chori Haram qarar di hai kiyonki Chori Amwal ke ziya (wastage of wealth) aur nufus ke qatl ka mojib banti hai aur is se Ma'ashere (society) mein kharabiyan janam leti hain. Chori ka ek nuqsan ye hai ke Chori karne wala na to tijarat karta hai aur na hi husool e rizq ke liye koi Halal tareeqa apnata hai aur Chor ke dayen (right) haath kaatne ka hukm isliye diya gaya hai ke Chor apne dayen haath se hi Chori shuda ashya (things) pakadta hai aur dayan haath hi uska afzal aur mufeed tareen azoo (part) hota hai aur is mufeed azoo ko kaat kar use baqi logon ke liye Namoona e Ibrat banaya jata hai taake log doosre ke Maal par na Haq qabza na karen."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
🤚🏻
Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha gaya ke Tayammum kaha tak karna chahiye?
Imam (as) ne ye Ayat padhi (5:6) aur farmaya:
_"Tayammum mein usi jagah Masah karo jahan se haath kata jata hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🤚🏻
Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya gaya ke Chor ka haath kahan se kaatna Wajib hai?
Imam (as) ne apni ungliyan phailayi aur farmaya:
_"Yahan se yaani hathaili ke jod se."_
🤚🏻
Imam Mohd Taqi (as) se ungliyan kaatna aur haath chhodne ki wajah poochhi gayi to Aap (as) ne farmaya:
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Azaa (parts) e Sajda 7 hain: (1) Chehra (2)(3) dono haath (4)(5) dono ghutne (knee) (6)(7) dono paon._
_Aur jab kisi ka haath hathaili se ya kohni se kaat diya jaye to uska Sajda sahi nahi rahega jabke Allah Ta'ala ka farman hai:_
*و إن المساجد لله*
( _Sajdah ke muqamat Allah ki Milkiyat hain._)
_Yahan maqamat e Sajdah se 7 parts murad hain aur jo cheez Khuda ki Milkiyat ho use jaata nahi ja sakta."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                   ♦ _*TAUBA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (696)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَنْ تَابَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ظُلْمِهِ وَأَصْلَحَ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَتُوبُ عَلَيْهِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Haan jo apne zalimana raviyya ke baad Tauba kar le aur apni islah kar le to yaqeenan Khuda uski Tauba qubool karega. Beshak Allah Bakhshne wala, Meherban hai.'_
(Surah Maeda: 39)

📚📖 ⛓🗡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Chor ka tazkara ho raha tha. Aaj ki ayat ye hai ke agar mujrim Tauba kar le to us chhod diya jaye.
Chori saza ke liye kuchh sharayet hain, jab ye Conditions pure honge tabhi saza di ja sakti hai:
(1) Chori kiya hua Maal kam az kam 1/4th Dinar ki value ka hona chahiye.
(2) Maal mehfooz jagah (Ghar ya dukan ya jeb) se chori kiya ho.
(3) Chori qahat saali (femine) mein na ho.
(4) Baligh ho.
(5) Baap ka bete ki maal ki chori, ek partner ki doosre partner ki chori is hukm mein nahi aati.
(6) Baagh ke darakhton se phal ki chori is hukm nahi hai.
(7) Har woh mauqa jahan ghalti se kisi ne apna maal samajh kar le liya ho.
(Tafseer Namoona)

Bare Ilaha hamari jo bhi jane anjane mein ghalti hui hon unse darguzar farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Jo aatish e Jahannum se darega wo Allah se apne gunaho'n ke baare mein jaldi Tauba karega aur Haraam kaam karne se bachega."_
(Tuhfal Uqool p281, Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tum mein behtareen wo log hain jo khata ke baad Tauba karein."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p41)
🙏🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Gunaho'n ka tark (avoid) karna Tauba karne se zyada behtar hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p807)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦ _*KAINAT KA MALIK ALLAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (697)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَمْ تَعْلَمْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ يُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَغْفِرُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*

_"Kiya tumhe nahi maloom ke Aasmaano aur Zameen mein Khuda ki hukumat hai. Wo jise chahe Azaab de aur jise chahe Ma'af kar de, Allah har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 40)

📚📖 👑
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Agar insaan ye ehsaas kar le ki poori Kainat mein Sirf Allah ki hukumat hai to woh koi Gunah na kare. Khauf e Khuda uske dil mein paida hoga. Muttaqi o Parhezgaar ban jayega. Kisi se nahi darenge siwai Allah ke. Aur uska hadaf sirf aur sirf Ibaadat o Qurbe Ilahi hoga, na jaa o mansab na iqtedar. Sirf apne Hakim Allah ke saamne apna sar kham kiye hoga.

Bare Ilaha hame jaante hain Sirf Tu hi Bakhshne wala hai, isliye hamari maghfirat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"…Aye meri ghulami ke Maalik! Aye Wo ke jiske haath mein meri taqdeer hai. Aye mere nuqsaan aur meri miskeeni ki haalat Jaannewaale! Aye mere Rab! Aye mere Rab! Aye mere Rab! Main Tujh se Tere Haq ka waasta aur Teri Pakeezgi ka aur Tere bahut Shaandaar Sifaat aur Naamo'n ka waasta dekar sawaal karta hun ke mere raat aur din ke waqto'n ko Apni yaad se bharpoor kar de, aur Apni khidmat mein lage rehne ki dhun lagaa de aur mere Aamal ko Apni huzoor mein maqbool farma taake mere kul Aamaal aur mere kul Awraad ki ek hi lai ho jaaye, aur mera haal ye ho ke hamesha Teri hi khidmat kiya karun. Aye mere Sardaar! Aye Wo ke jis par mera bharosa hai. Aye Wo ki jiski bargaah mein main apni har haalat ki shikaayat karta hoo'n."_
(Dua e Kumail)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tu Khaaliq hai aur main makhlooq hun. Tu Maalik hai aur main mamlook hun. Tu Parwardigaar hai aur main Tera banda hun. Tu Raaziq hai aur main Rizq paane wala hun. Tu Ataa karne wala hai aur main maangne wala hun. Tu Sakhawat karne wala aur main kanjoos hun. Tu Quwwat wala aur main kamzor hun…
(Dua e Yastasheer)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*SAAZISH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (698)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الرَّسُولُ لَا يَحْزُنْكَ الَّذِينَ يُسَارِعُونَ فِي الْكُفْرِ مِنَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا آمَنَّا بِأَفْوَاهِهِمْ وَلَمْ تُؤْمِنْ قُلُوبُهُمْ ۛ وَمِنَ الَّذِينَ هَادُوا ۛ سَمَّاعُونَ لِلْكَذِبِ سَمَّاعُونَ لِقَوْمٍ آخَرِينَ لَمْ يَأْتُوكَ ۖ يُحَرِّفُونَ الْكَلِمَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَوَاضِعِهِ ۖ يَقُولُونَ إِنْ أُوتِيتُمْ هَٰذَا فَخُذُوهُ وَإِنْ لَمْ تُؤْتَوْهُ فَاحْذَرُوا ۚ وَمَنْ يُرِدِ اللَّهُ فِتْنَتَهُ فَلَنْ تَمْلِكَ لَهُ مِنَ اللَّهِ شَيْئًا ۚ أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يُرِدِ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُطَهِّرَ قُلُوبَهُمْ ۚ لَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا خِزْيٌ ۖ وَلَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ*

_"Aye Rasool (saww)! Wo log aap ke liye baes e ranj na hon jo Kufr mein tezi kar rahe hain khwah unka talluq us Jamat se ho jo moo se kahti hai ke ham Imaan laye hain haalanki unke dil be-Imaan hain (Munafeqeen) ya inka talluq Yahoodiyon se ho jo ke jhooti batein sunne ke liye kaan lagaye rahte hain aur un logon ke jasoos hain jo tumhare paas kabhi nahi aaye aur woh Kalemat ke asli mauqe chhod kar unhe mutaghayyar (doctored, changed) kar diya karte hain aur logon se kahte hain ke agar tumhe ye hukm diya jaye to manoge nahi, to na mano, aur usse alag hi raho. Jise Khuda ne Fitne mein dalne ka irada kar liya ho us Allah ki giraft se bachane ke liye tum kuchh nahi kar sakte. Ye woh log hain jinke dilon ki Pakeezgi ka Khuda ne iraada hi nahi kiya, unke liye Duniya mein ruswai hai aur Akhirat mein unke liye sakht saza hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 41)

📚📖 😏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah is Ayat mein Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko dilasa de raha ke Aap Kafiron aur Munafiqon ki kartooton par ranjeeda na hon, unko Yahoodiyon ka misl qarar diya hai. Jo jasoosi karne mein busy rahte hain aur kuchh unhe mil jata hai to use logon ke samne tod madod ke pesh karte hain taake log gumrah hon. Ye log Fitne par utar aate hain aur Akhir mein unhe ruswai ka moo dekhna padhta hai.
Jo log nek kaam mein gamzan hain Allah ka ye paigham unke liye bhi hai ke ranjeeda na ho, Allah unki rukawaton ko door karega aur unke mukhalefin ko ruswa karega.

Bare Ilaha aaj ke is Mubarak Din par hame hamari kohtayyon ko door farma aur apne nek maqsad mein kamyabi ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸
_*EVENT OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⛓
_*HADIS SILSALATUZ ZAHAB (Golden Chain)*_
(Daurane Safar Nishapur mein)
Imam Raza (as):
_"Mere Walid Musa Kazim, unke Walid Imam Jafar Sadiq (as), unke walid Mohd Baqir (as), unke walid Imam Zainul Abidin (as), unke walid Shaheed e Karbala (Imam Hussain) (as), unke Walid  Ali ibn Abu Talib (as), Rasoole Khuda  (saw), Jibrail (as) se marvi hai ke Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:_

_"Kalima e 'La ilaha illallah' Mera Qila hai, jo bhi is ko dohraiga Mere Qile mein dakhil hoga, aur jo Mere Qile mein dakhil hoga Mere Azaab se bach jayega."_

Phir Imam Reza (as) ne farmaya:
_"Kuchh sharait ke sath."_

_*"Aur mein un sharton mein se ek hun."*_
(Ahsan al-Maqaal by Syed Safdar Hussain Najafi quoted from The official website of grand ayatollah Saafi Gulpaygani, Ibn Sabbagh al-Maleki. Al-Fusool al-Mohimmah. pp. 243–244.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                   ♦ _*FAISLA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (699)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*سَمَّاعُونَ لِلْكَذِبِ أَكَّالُونَ لِلسُّحْتِ ۚ فَإِنْ جَاءُوكَ فَاحْكُمْ بَيْنَهُمْ أَوْ أَعْرِضْ عَنْهُمْ ۖ وَإِنْ تُعْرِضْ عَنْهُمْ فَلَنْ يَضُرُّوكَ شَيْئًا ۖ وَإِنْ حَكَمْتَ فَاحْكُمْ بَيْنَهُمْ بِالْقِسْطِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ الْمُقْسِطِينَ*

_"Ye jhoot sunne wale aur Haram khane wale log hain. Agar woh (apne muqadmat ke liye) Aap (saww) ke paas ayen to tumhe ye ikhtiyar diya jata hai chaho to unka faisla karo warna inkar karo. Aur agar tumne inkaar kar diya to ye tumhara kuchh bigad nahi sakenge. Aur agar aap faisla karen to phir Adl o Insaaf se unke darmiyan faisla karen be shak Allah Insaaf karne walon ko pasand karta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 42)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ke shaane nuzool mein kafi Rivayaat hain, sirf ek likhte hain:
Medina mein Aulade Haroon mein se do Qabeele the Bani Qareeza (ta'daad 700) aur Bani Nazir (ta'daad 1000) (Yahoodi). Dono mein ye agreement tha ke agar Bani Nazir ka koi shakhs qatl hua to Bani Qareeza ke kisi fard ko oont par ulte moo baitha kar uske moo par keechad mal di jayegi aur aadhi deyet ada karega. Kiyonki Bani Qareeza kamzor the. Hijrat tak ye muayeda jaari raha. Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Medina aye to ek shakhs ke qatl hone par ye log faisle ke liye aye. Chunke Muaeda tha chahe woh ghalat tha. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne faisle se inkaar kiya, kiyonki woh unki baat ko maante nahi.
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
Is Ayat mein Allah ne faisla ka ikhtiyar Rasoole Khuda (saww) par chhod diya. Us waqt bhi aur aaj bhi jo power mein hota hai, zabar hota hai uski chalti hai, wohi hakim aur judge ban jate hain. Jabke Haq ki himayat mein Insaaf hona chahiye. Majboor ko uska Haq diya jana chahiye. Yahan phir Allah Rasoole Akram (saww) ki himmat afzai kar raha hai, darne ke koi baat nahi Dushman unka koi kuchh nahi bigad sakta.
Yehi hukm e aam hai jo log hidayat ki raah mein gamzan hain woh apna kam karte rahe kise se koi darne ki zaroorat nahi kiyon Allah Saleheen ke sath hai aur Insaaf pasand logon ko Allah pasand karta hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq ata farma ke ham logon ke darmiyan sahi faisla kar saken. Mazloom ka sath den aur zabar ko maat den.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Insaan ke har azoo (part) ke liye Imaan ka alaidah aur alaihda taqaza hai._
_Allah ne Dil par iqraar, Ma'arefat, Tasleem o Reza ko wajib kiya._
_Aur Dil ka farz hai ke woh is baat ko tasleem kare ke Allah Wahdao Lasharik hai, Uski koi biwi nahi hai aur Uske haan koi beta nahi hai aur Dil ye tasleem kare ke Muhammad (saww) Allah ke Abd aur Rasool hain aur Khuda ki taraf se jitne bhi Rasool aur Kitaben aayen hain woh sab ki sab bar Haq hain."_
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

                  ♦ _*TORAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (700)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَيْفَ يُحَكِّمُونَكَ وَعِنْدَهُمُ التَّوْرَاةُ فِيهَا حُكْمُ اللَّهِ ثُمَّ يَتَوَلَّوْنَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ذَٰلِكَ ۚ وَمَا أُولَٰئِكَ بِالْمُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Ye tumhe kaise hakam (Judge) banate hain jabke unke paas Torah maujood hai jis mein Allah ka hukm likha hua hai. Phir ye us hukm se moo mod rahe hain. Asl baat ye hai ke ye log Imaandar hi nahi hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 43)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein zikr hua tha ke kuchh Yahoodi Hazrat Rasoole Akram (saww) ke pas aate the apne faisle ke liye. Yahan Allah unse sawal kar raha hai ke woh apni Torah ke mutabiq bhi faisla kar sakte hain. Lekin Haq baat ko woh chhupate hain. Jabke woh usko apni aasmani Kitab maante the, jabke woh tahreef shuda thi, lekin phir us mein kuchh haqaiq baqi the. Allah ne unko Be Imaano se khitab kiya. Torah mein 'Safar tasniyah, fadl 22 mein ye hukm maujood hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Agar main Momin ki naak bhi talwaar se kaat doo'n ke mujhse adaawat kare to nahi karega aur agar Munafiq par saari duniya undeyl dun ke mujhse mohabbat kar le to nahi karega, is liye ke ye faisla Rasule Akram (saww) ki zabaan se ho chuka hai ke *"Aye Ali (as), Momin tumse dushmani nahi kar sakta aur Munafiq tumse mohabbat nahi kar sakta"*._
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p190)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
