⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
                   ♦ _*TORAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (701)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّا أَنْزَلْنَا التَّوْرَاةَ فِيهَا هُدًى وَنُورٌ ۚ يَحْكُمُ بِهَا النَّبِيُّونَ الَّذِينَ أَسْلَمُوا لِلَّذِينَ هَادُوا وَالرَّبَّانِيُّونَ وَالْأَحْبَارُ بِمَا اسْتُحْفِظُوا مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ وَكَانُوا عَلَيْهِ شُهَدَاءَ ۚ فَلَا تَخْشَوُا النَّاسَ وَاخْشَوْنِ وَلَا تَشْتَرُوا بِآيَاتِي ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا ۚ وَمَنْ لَمْ يَحْكُمْ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْكَافِرُونَ*

_"Hamne Taurait utaari jis mein Hidayat aur Roshni thi. Saare Nabi jo Muslim the usi ke mutabiq un Yahoodiyon ke Maamelat ke faisle karte the aur usi tarah se "Rabbani" aur "Ahbaar" bhi usi ke mutabiq faisle karte the kiyonki inhe Kitabul Allah ki hifazat sonpi gayi thi aur woh us par gawah the. Lehaza (aye Yahoodi Group) tum logon se na daro balke Mujh se Daro aur meri Ayaat ko mamooli qeemat par mat becho. Jo log Allah ke nazil kardah Qanoon ke mutabiq Faisla Na karen wohi Kafir hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 44)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat se sabit hota hai jitne bhi Anbiya (as) ayae sab ke sab Muslim the. Jinhone ne haqiqat mein in Anbiya ki pairavi ki chahe Yahoodi hon ya Christians sab Muslim the, yani Kitab e Khuda aur Sunnat par amal karte the. Baad mein sab unke qawaneen bhool gaye aur apni man mani karne lage. Isliye woh apne banaye hue qanoon ke mutabiq ghalat faisle lene lage. Allah unko usi ki yaad dila raha hai.

Imam Reza (as) ne ek nashisht mein Raasul Jaloot (Ahle Kitab) se poochha ke Zaboor mein Dawood (as) ki ek  Dua hai jise tum padhte ho: "Parwardigaar! Inqetae Rusul (Ayyame Fatrah) ke baad Sunnat qaim karnewale Ko mab'oos farma." Batao zamana e Fatrah ke baad Hazrat Muhammad (saww) ke alawa koi aur Nabi aya?
Usne kaha ji haan Dua padhte hain lekin isse murad Hazrat Esa (as) hain.
Imam ne farmaya: tu ne jihalat ka saboot diya. Hazrat Esa (as) to Sunnat ke mukhalif the he nahi." (Yani isse murad Rasoole Khuda (saww) hain. Aur sab Anbiya Allah ki sunnat par amal karte the.)

Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
"Imamat ke liye gunahon se Paak hona zaroori hai. Imam ke paas makhfi Ilm (Hidden Knowledge) hona chahiye. Use Kitab ke khas o Aam, mohkam o Mutashabehaat, gharaib taaveel, nasikh o mansookh ka Ilm hona chahiye."
"Allah ne jineh faisla karne ka Haq tafveez kiya hai aur unke ausaaf Quran mein bayan kiya hain (5:44). "Rabbani" se murad hain Anbiya jo ke Ilm ke waris hote hain aur "Ahbaar" woh Ulema hain jinka area "Rabbani" se kam ho."
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
Qur'an Majeed ki Ayat aur Aimma huda ki Rivayaat se ye baat sabit hoti hai ke Aimma wa hukkam ko Ahle Kitab ke muqadmat ki samat aur usse inkar ka ikhtiyar hasil hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda se darte rahna behtareen ibadat hai. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:_
*إِنَّمَا يَخْشَى اللَّهَ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ الْعُلَمَاءُ ۗ*(35:28)
_*"Ulema hi Allah se darte hain."*_ (35:28)
_Allah Ta'ala ne mazeed farmaya:_
*فَلَا تَخْشَوُا النَّاسَ وَاخْشَوْنِ*
( _"Logon se mat daro Mujh se darte raho."_(5:44)"
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*QISAAS (BADLA)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (702)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

وَكَتَبْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ فِيهَا أَنَّ النَّفْسَ بِالنَّفْسِ وَالْعَيْنَ بِالْعَيْنِ وَالْأَنْفَ بِالْأَنْفِ وَالْأُذُنَ بِالْأُذُنِ وَالسِّنَّ بِالسِّنِّ وَالْجُرُوحَ قِصَاصٌ ۚ فَمَنْ تَصَدَّقَ بِهِ فَهُوَ كَفَّارَةٌ لَهُ ۚ وَمَنْ لَمْ يَحْكُمْ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الظَّالِمُونَ

_"Aur Hamne us mein Yahoodiyon ke liye ye hukm likh diya tha ke Jaan ke badle Jaan aur Aankh ke badle Aankh aur Naak ke badle Naak aur Kaan ke badle Kaan aur Daant ke badle Daant aur Zakhm ke badle mein waisa hi barabar ka Zakhm. Phir jo shakhs usko Ma'af kar de to wo uske liye Kaffara hai, aur jo log Allah ke nazil kardah qanoon ke mutabiq faisla na karen wohi zalim hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 45)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
📚📖 👉 _*Tafseer:*_  
Is Ayat ke zere nazar kuchh Rivayaat pesh e khidmat hain:
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal hua ke agar koi kaana kisi ki ek Aankh nikal de to us se Qisaas (badla) ki kiya surat hogi?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Kaane ki Sahetmand Aankh nikal li jaye"_
Raavi: _"Isse to woh bilkul andha ho jayega."_
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Use Haq ne andha kiya hai."_
⚖
Imam Sadeqain (as) se sawal hua:
Agar koi shakhs kisi bachche ko thappad mare jis se uska daant toot jaye phir wohi daant ug aye to kiya thappad marne wale ka daant nikala jayega?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Usse Qisas nahi liya jayega usse Jurmana (Fine) wusool kiya jayega."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)
⚖
Ek muhibbe Ahle Bait (as) ne Imam Sadiq (as) se Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki janghon ke mutalliq sawal kiya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Allah ne Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ko paanch talwaren de kar mab'oos kiya jin mein 3 talwaren khuli hui hain aur woh us waqt tak niyaam mein na jayengi jab tak Duniya mein Jang ka khatma na ho jaye aur Jang ka khatma us waqt tak nahi hoga jab tak Suraj Maghrib se tuloo na kare aur jab Suraj Maghrib se Tuloo karega to us waqt sab log Imaan le ayenge lekin us Din ka Imaan is liye faydemand hoga jo pahle se Imaan la chuke hoga aur neki kar chuka hoga aur ek talwar lipti hui hai aur ek talwar ghilaf mein hai._
_In mein se pahli teen talwaren Kuffar o Mushrekin ke liye hain aur jo talwar lifafe mein covered hai wo baghiyon ke khilaf buland hone wali talwar hai. Aur woh talwar jo ghilaf mein hai woh Qisaas (badla) ki talwar hai.  Allah ne ye talwar maqtool ke warison ke haath mein di hai aur faisla karne ka Haq hamen ata kiya hai."_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)
⚖
Aimma Sadeqain (as):
_"Allah ne Khums mein Ale Muhammad (as) ka ek hissa muqarrar kiya hai. Lekin ek shakhs ne hasad o adawat ki wajah se unhe unke Haq se mehroom rakha jabke Allah Ta'ala ka farman hai ke jo Khuda ke nazil kardah qanoon ke mutabiq faisla na kare to woh fasiq hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
Chunanche is shakhs ne sab se pahle Ale Muhammad (as) ka Haq roka aur un par zulm kiya aur logon ne unki gardano par sawar kiya. Iske baad uska Janashin Hukumat ke mansab par faiz hua to usne bhi apne pesh ro ki ravish jaari rakhi aur Ale Muhammad (as) ko unke Huqooq se mehroom rakha.

Akhbari hazrat jinhone Khums ko band kar rakha hai is Rivayat par tawajjo den.

Bare Ilaha jis kisi ne Aimma Massomeen (as) par zulm kiya Khuda usse badla le.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

                 *16th Zilqad 1438*
       *9th August 2017, Wednesday,*

                   ♦ _*INJEEL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (703)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَفَّيْنَا عَلَىٰ آثَارِهِمْ بِعِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ مِنَ التَّوْرَاةِ ۖ وَآتَيْنَاهُ الْإِنْجِيلَ فِيهِ هُدًى وَنُورٌ وَمُصَدِّقًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ مِنَ التَّوْرَاةِ وَهُدًى وَمَوْعِظَةً لِلْمُتَّقِينَ*

_"Phir Hamne un Paighambaron ke baad Maryam ke Farzand Esa (as) ko ravana kiya aur woh us Kitab Taurait ki tasdeeq karte the jo unke saamne thi aur Hamne unhe Injeel ata ki jis mein Hidayat aur Noor tha aur woh apne se pahli Kitab Taurait ki musaddiq (tasdeeq karnewali) thi aur Hidayat aur Parhezgaron ke liye Nasihat thi."_
(Surah Maeda: 46)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayatoon mein ham Rivayaat ke zariye zikr kar chuke hai ke Qur'an Noor hai. Isliye sab Ayaat ka khulasa ye hai ke Allah ki sab Aasmani kitaben Hidayat wa Noor hain. Sab Aasmani Kitaben Khuda ki taraf se nazil hui aur har agli Kitab pichhli Kitab ko verify karti thi. Lekin Qur'an chhod kar Saheb e Kitab yani Paighambar ke is Duniya se jaane ke baad in Kitabon mein tehreef hui, us mein changes aa gaye. Isliye unki authenticity khatm ho gayi aur asl Kitab ko sab bhool gaye. Isliye Khuda har in Ayaton mein bar bar yad dahani kara raha hai ke ye sab qawaneen, rules un Kitabon mein maujood the jo nai Kitabon mein se ghayeb ho gaye. Aaj ki Bible jo old and New Testament ka majmua hai ye woh asl Kitab nahi hai. Injeel Ibrani zaban mein nazil hui jis zaban ka wujood hi khatm ho gaya. Ye Ibrani se Latin aur Greek languages mein translate hui aur baad mein English mein. Aaj jo sab ke pas maujood hai wo sirf translation hai. Aur translation ki haqiqat sab ko maloom hai. Qur'an ke hi alag alag translation ko samne rakhe sab mukhtalif nazar ayenge. Yehi wajah hai Qur'an ko Arabic mein baqi rakha aur usi zaban mein padha wa likha jata hai.
Zayada tafseel ke liye refer karen:
الهدى الى دين المصطفى، انيس الإعلام.
Ek aur baat ki taraf ishara hai ke ye Muttaqeen ke liye Hidayat hai, yani jo log Haq ke talash mein rahte hain aur is mein zyada interest rakhte hain. Jo log Deen e Islam mein interested nahi hain Allah unse koi wasta nahi rakhta. Unko Hidayat ki bhi jaye to koi asar hone wala nahi.

Bare Ilaha hame Qur'an e Karem par amal karne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Aye Bakhshne waale! Tere hi Noor se humein hidayat mili. Tere fazl se hum malamaal huwe. Aur Teri Rehmat ke saath hum subh o shaam karte hain. Hamare gunah Tere saamne hain. Aye Allah! Hum Tujh se unki bakshish chaahte hain aur Tere huzoor Tauba karte hain."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)

_*"Aur Salaam ho mujh par jis Din MEIN PAIDA HUA aur jis Din mein marunga, jis Din mein uthaya jaonga."*_
(Surah Maryam: 33)

                     ♦ _*INJEEL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (704)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلْيَحْكُمْ أَهْلُ الْإِنْجِيلِ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِيهِ ۚ وَمَنْ لَمْ يَحْكُمْ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْفَاسِقُونَ*

_"Ahle Injeel ko us hukm ke mutabiq faisla karna chahiye jo Allah ne u his mein nazil kiya hai aur jo log Allah ke nazil kardah qanoon ke mutabiq Faisla na karen to wohi Fasiq hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 47)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke guzishta Ayaat ke zel mein bhi tazkara ho chuka hai ke jis Injeel ki is Ayat mein baat ho rahi hai woh wohi Asl Injeel hai jo Khuda ki taraf se nazil hui. Woh bhi Allah ka Kalam tha. Isliye Allah hukm de raha hai ke Christians ne kiyon us Asl Anjeel par amal nahi kiya, uske mutabiq kiyon faisle nahi kiye. Is ki asl wajah yeh hai ke unhone ne Injeel mein tehreef karke apni mansha mutabiq bana diya. Isi liye to baad mein Qur'an nazil hua taake un pichhli Aasmani Kitabon ke qanoon ki tasdeeq kare. Yani Islam koi naya ijad kardah Deen nahi tha balke sabhi Anbiya ka ek hi Deen aur ek hi Usool tha. Isliye Allah ne kaha ke jisne Allah ke qawaneen ka inkar kiya ya uske mutabiq faisla nahi kiya woh Kafir hai, Zalim hai, Fasiq hai.

Bare Ilaha hame mein panah mangta hun aise fasiqon se jo Allah ke qanoon chhod apna qanoon chala kar logon par zulm karte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jisne Khuda ke nazil karda qanoon se hat kar do dirahamo ka faisla kiya to usne Kufr kiya."_
(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

      ♦ _*MINHAJ WA SHARIYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (705)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَنْزَلْنَا إِلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ بِالْحَقِّ مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَمُهَيْمِنًا عَلَيْهِ ۖ فَاحْكُمْ بَيْنَهُمْ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ۖ وَلَا تَتَّبِعْ أَهْوَاءَهُمْ عَمَّا جَاءَكَ مِنَ الْحَقِّ ۚ لِكُلٍّ جَعَلْنَا مِنْكُمْ شِرْعَةً وَمِنْهَاجًا ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَجَعَلَكُمْ أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً وَلَٰكِنْ لِيَبْلُوَكُمْ فِي مَا آتَاكُمْ ۖ فَاسْتَبِقُوا الْخَيْرَاتِ ۚ إِلَى اللَّهِ مَرْجِعُكُمْ جَمِيعًا فَيُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ تَخْتَلِفُونَ*

_"Phir aye Nabi! Hamne tumhari taraf ye Kitab bheji jo Haq le kar aayi hai aur apne se pahle wali Kitabon ki tasdeeq (verify) karti hai aur uski Muhafiz aur Nigran hai. Tum Khuda ke nazil kardah qanoon ke mutabiq logon ke darmiyan faisla karo aur jo kuchh tumhare pas aa chuka hai usse moo na mod kar unki khwaheshat ki pairavi na karna. Hamne tum mein se har ek ke liye ek Shariyat aur Rahe Amal muqarrar ki hai. Agar Khuda chahta to tum sab ko ek Ummat bhi bana sakta tha lekin Us ne ye isliye kiya hai ke jo kuchh Us ne tum logon ko diya hai us mein tumhari azmaish (test) kar le, lehaza bhalaiyon mein ek doosre se aage padhne ki koshish karo. Akhir kar tum sab ko Khuda ke Huzoor mein jana hai. Woh tumhe asl haqiqat bata dega jis mein tum ikhtelaf kar rahe ho."_
(Surah Maeda: 48)

📚📖 🛤
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat bilkul wazeh hai. Guzishta Anbiya aur unki Kitab ke bayan ke baad ab Qur'an ka tazkara hai. Yahan is baat ko wazeh kiya hai ke Anbiya ke Deen wa Kitab asl mein wohi Deen e Islam tha. Wohi Qurani Ahkam the.
Shariyat شریعة us raaste ko kahte hain jo Paani ki taraf jata ho aur wahan ja kar khatm hota ho aur Deen e Shariyat is liye kahte hain ke woh Haqaeq aur aisi taalimat tak pahunchata hai jo Paakeezgi, Taharat aur Insaani zindagi ka sarmaya hain.
Nahj ya Minhaaj منهاج us wazeh raaste ko kahte hain.
Isliye "شرعة" aur "منهاج" mein farq yeh hai ke "Shara' " use kahte hain jo Qur'an mein warid ho aur "Minhaaj" se murad woh umoor hain jo Sunnate Paighambar (saww) mein warid hue."
(Mufradaat e Raghib)
Iske bawajood dono word ek hi meaning mein istemaal hote hain.
Akhir mein Insaan ke man mein ye sawal uthta hai ke ye sab kiyon? Allah chahta to sab ek hi Deen par hote. Allah har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai.
Examination hall mein kiya Student ke zehen mein ye khayal paida hota hai ke kiya teacher ko nahi maloom jo ham se itne sawal poochhe ja raha hai. Teacher jan boojh kar students ko takleef mein dal raha hai taake uska Test liya jaa sake. Koi ye nahi kah sakta woh un par zulm ya na insaafi kar raha hai.
Allah ne wazeh taur par is Ayat mein bata diya ke is Duniya mein ham Exam dene aye hain. Balke Allah kah raha hai ke Nekiyon mein competition karo aur aage badh jao. Aur aise taraqqi karte karte ham Allah ke saamne hazir ho jayen ge.

Bare Ilaha hame in Imtehanat ki manzilen kamyabi se par kar lene ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Yaqeenan, balaa (musibat) zaalim ke liye Azaab hai aur Momin ke liye Imtehaan hai."_
(Jaame'ul Akhbaar p.113, Anecdotes of Reflection)
♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Momin wo hai jo balaa ko ne'mat aur aish ko musibat khayaal kare, kyun ki Duniya ki balaa Akherat ki ne'mat hai aur Duniya ka aish Akherat mein mehnat hai."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p200)

♦ _*QANOONE ILAHI SE FAISLA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (706)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَنِ احْكُمْ بَيْنَهُمْ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ وَلَا تَتَّبِعْ أَهْوَاءَهُمْ وَاحْذَرْهُمْ أَنْ يَفْتِنُوكَ عَنْ بَعْضِ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْكَ ۖ فَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَاعْلَمْ أَنَّمَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُصِيبَهُمْ بِبَعْضِ ذُنُوبِهِمْ ۗ وَإِنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنَ النَّاسِ لَفَاسِقُونَ * أَفَحُكْمَ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ يَبْغُونَ ۚ وَمَنْ أَحْسَنُ مِنَ اللَّهِ حُكْمًا لِقَوْمٍ يُوقِنُونَ*

_"Aap unke darmiyan Allah ke nazil kardah Qanoon ke mutabiq Faisla karen aur unki khwahishat ki pairavi na karen aur is baat se hoshiyar rahen ke ye log Aap ko Fitne mein dal kar is Hidayat se zarrah barabar munharif (gumrah) na karne payen jo Khuda ne tumhari taraf nazil ki hai. Phir agar ye usse moo mod len to jaan lo ke Allah ne unke kuchh gunahon ki saza ke liye unko musibat mubtila karne ka irada kar hi liya hai aur is mein koi shak nahi ke unki aksariyat Fasiq hai."_
_"Aur kiya ye Jahiliyyat ka Faisla chahte hain. Haalanki jo log Allah par yaqeen rakhte hain unke nazdeek Allah se Behtar Faisla Karne wala aur kaun ho sakta hai?"_
(Surah Maeda: 49 - 50)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ibne Abbas se iska shaane nuzool is tarah darj hai:
"Yahoodiyon ke badon ki ek Jamaat ne aapas mein saazish ki aur kaha ke Muhammad (saww) ke paas jaate hain. Shayad ise ham uske Deen se munharif kar den. Ye tai kar ke woh Paighambar e Islam ke paas aaye aur kahne lage ke ham Yahoodiyon ke Ulema aur Ashraf hain, agar ham Aap ki pairavi kar len to Musallam hai ke baqi Yahoodi hamari iqteda karenge Lekin hamare aur ek giroh ke darmiyan ek tanaza (dispute) hai (ek shakhs ke qatl ya kisi aur baat ke bare mein) agar is jhagde mein Aap hamare fayde mein faisla kar den to ham Aap par Imaan le ayenge."
Is par Paighambar e Islam (saww) ne aise (ghair aadilana, unjust) faisle se moo mod liya. Is par ye Ayat nazil hui (5:49)"
(Tafseer Al Munar, Vol 6, P-421)
Yahan ye sawal ho sakta hai ke Allah kiyon Paighambar (saww) ko tanbeeh kar raha hai ke Aap unke Khwaheshat ki pairavi na karen...?
Jawab: Tamam Anbiya wa Aimma Masoom (Infallible) hain. Aql bhi yehi kahti hai ke Rehbar, Guide ko Masoom hona chahiye. Iski detail Ismat ke Topic mein ayegi. Sirf itna bata den ke Anbiya wa Aimma Masoom jabran nahi hote, woh gunah karne ki salahiyat rakhte hue bhi gunah nahi karte. Ye inka kamal hai. Kiyonki Allah chahta to farishton ko Paighambar bana kar bhej deta jo ke woh bhi Masoom hain. Lekin jo bhi Anbiya guzre woh sab ham insaano mein se aur insaani fitrat rakhte the, kiyonki woh logon ke liye Namoona e Amal the. Nahi to log kahte woh to Masoom paida hue hain ham unki tarah kahan se ho sakte hain. Agar aisa na hota to koi unke Fazail ka qaseeda kyon padhta.

Bare Ilaha hame logon ke fitno se mehfooz rakh kahin aisa na ho ke woh hame gumrah kar den aur hamare Deen Mission mein rukawaten​ paida hon.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚖
Imam Sadiq wa Ali (as):
_"Faisle do tarah ke hote hain. Ek Allah ka Faisla hai aur doosra Jahiliyyat ka Faisla hai jo Allah ke faisle se hat kar faisla karta hai woh Jahiliyyat ka faisla karta hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

           ♦ _*AULIYA - DOST*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (707)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَتَّخِذُوا الْيَهُودَ وَالنَّصَارَىٰ أَوْلِيَاءَ ۘ بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ ۚ وَمَنْ يَتَوَلَّهُمْ مِنْكُمْ فَإِنَّهُ مِنْهُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الظَّالِمِينَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Yahoodiyon aur Nasraniyon ko apna Rafeeq (Friend) na banao, ye ek doosre ke dost hain. Agar tum mein se koi unko apna dost banata hai to unka shumar bhi unhi mein hoga. Beshak Khuda zalim logon ko rahe raast par nahi lata. (Hidayat nahi karta)"_
(Surah Maeda: 51)

📚📖 👥
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein أولياء ka word istemal hua hai aur iska root hai ولى isi se kai word bante hai aur kai meaning bhi. Iske maani dosti, rafaqat ke sath sath sarparast ke bhi maani hain. Isi se banta hai متولى yani trustee, isi se akhaz hota ha  ولاء ya ولايت jiske maani hain do cheezon ke darmiyan bahut zyada qurb, nazdeeki aur dosti hai. Nez is mein ham Paiman hone ka mafhoom bhi paya jata hai. Jis ke ham Paiman hote hain usi ki pairavi karte hain.
Allah ne yaha takeed ki hai ke Dosti apne ham maslak se karo, ghairon ko apna sarparast na banao. Balke dosti usse karo jo Allah ko dost rakhe aur Allah usko Apna dost qarar deta ho. Unhi ko Auliya kahte hain.

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Auliya ka pairokar mein rakh aur un se door rakh jo Tujhse aur Tere Auliya se dushmani rahe.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jis tarah se Yahood o Nasaara ko Sarparast banane wala unka ek fard shumar hota hai, usi tarah se jo shakhs Ale Muhammad (as) se Vila rakhe aur unhe Qarabat e Rasool (saww) ki wajah se tamam logon par muqaddam jaane, to woh bhi Ale Muhammad (as) ka fard shumar kiya jaata hai aur use apni Tawliyyat aur itteba' (Love and following) ki wajah se unhi ke fard ka rutba hasil hota hai. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala farmata hai ..(5:51)"_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Logo'n mein nek Dost 3 tarah ke tajrube se banao:_ _(1) Gaiz o gazab mein dekho ke wo haqq se khaarij to nahi hota hai,_
_(2) Daulat ke zariye se aazmao,_
_(3) Safar saath kar ke dekho."_
(Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p208)
👥
Imam Askari (as):
_"Tumhara behtareen Dost wo hai jo tumhari galtiyo'n ko bhool jaaye aur tumhare ehsaanaat ko yaad rakkhe."_
(Insaan ke Kamaal mein Akhlaaq ka Kirdaar)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (708)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَتَرَى الَّذِينَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ مَرَضٌ يُسَارِعُونَ فِيهِمْ يَقُولُونَ نَخْشَىٰ أَنْ تُصِيبَنَا دَائِرَةٌ ۚ فَعَسَى اللَّهُ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ بِالْفَتْحِ أَوْ أَمْرٍ مِنْ عِنْدِهِ فَيُصْبِحُوا عَلَىٰ مَا أَسَرُّوا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ نَادِمِينَ * وَيَقُولُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَهَٰؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ أَقْسَمُوا بِاللَّهِ جَهْدَ أَيْمَانِهِمْ ۙ إِنَّهُمْ لَمَعَكُمْ ۚ حَبِطَتْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ فَأَصْبَحُوا خَاسِرِينَ*

_"Tum dekhte ho jinke dilon mein Munafiqat hai woh unhi mein daud dhoop karte phirte hai aur kahte hain ke hame dar lagta hai ke ham kahin kisi musibat ke chakkar mein na phans jayen. Unko ye baat yaad rakhni ke anqareeb Allah Musalmano ko Fatah bakhshega ya Apni taraf se koi aur baat zahir karega to us waqt ye apne dilon mein chhupaye hue nifaq ki wajah se nidamat uthayenge."_
_"Us waqt Ahl Imaan kahenge ke kiya ye wohi log hain jo Allah ki qasmen kha kar tumhe yaqeen dilate the ke ham tumhare sath hain? Unke sab Aamaal zaye (waste) ho gaye aur Akhirkar ye nakaam o namuraad hokar rahe."_
(Surah Maeda: 52 - 53)

📚📖 👺
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke zel mein Auliya ka zikr tha. Hamara muhib woh hai jisko Khuda Dost rakhe. Aur Auliya Ahle Bait (as) hain. Ab jo apne aapko Musalman kahe aur inki baat na maane woh munafiq hi kahlaya jayega. Zel mein Ahadis mulaheza farmayen.

Bare Ilaha hame in Munafeqeen ke saye se bhi door rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Aap se koi mohabbat nahi karega siwaaye Momin ke aur koi dushmani nahi rakhega siwaaye Munafiq ke. Khuda Wande Aalam farmata hai, "Munafeqeen Jahannum ke aakhri tabqe mein honge" (Surah Nisa: 145)."_
(Manaaqib Ameerul Momeneen (as), p386)
👺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Tumhare sar par zarbat lagaayi jayegi aur Fatima (sa) par darwaza giraya jayega, Hasan (as) ki raan mein naiza mara jayega aur zeher se qatl kiya jayega aur Husain (as) ki shahadat is tarah hogi ke tamam Ahle Bait (as) us par girya karenge." Ameerul Momeneen (as) ne farmaya, "Ya Rasulallah (saww), Khuda Wande Karim ne hum Ahle Bait (as) ka imtehaan balaa aur musibat rakkha hai." Aap (saww) ne farmaya, "Aye Ali, Khuda ne mujh se ahd (waada) kiya hai ke jo tumhe dost rakhta hai wo Momin hoga aur tumhe dushman jaanne wala munafiq hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, Majlis 28, p133)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*MO'MENEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (709)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَنْ يَرْتَدَّ مِنْكُمْ عَنْ دِينِهِ فَسَوْفَ يَأْتِي اللَّهُ بِقَوْمٍ يُحِبُّهُمْ وَيُحِبُّونَهُ أَذِلَّةٍ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَعِزَّةٍ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ يُجَاهِدُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَلَا يَخَافُونَ لَوْمَةَ لَائِمٍ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ فَضْلُ اللَّهِ يُؤْتِيهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Agar tum mein se koi Allah ke Deen se phirta hai to phir jaye Allah aisi Qaum layega jin se Khuda Muhabbat rakhta hoga aur woh Khuda se Muhabbat karte honge jo Mo'meneen par narm aur Kuffar par sakht honge. Khuda ki raah mein Jihad karenge aur kisi malamat karne wale ki malamat se nahi darenge. Ye Khuda ka Fazl o Karam hai, Woh jise chahta hai ata kar deta hai. Allah wasee zarae ka Maalik aur sab kuchh jaanta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 54)

📚📖 🍁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein ye wazahat Rivayaat ke zariye ki gayi thi ke jo Ahle Bait (as) ki pairavi karega wo Momin hain aur jo unke Dushmanon ki pairavi karega woh Munafiq hoga. Is Ayat mein Mo'meneen ka zikr hua hai.
🍁
Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim mein marqoom hai ke
Is Ayat mein Rasool e Khuda (saww) ke un Ashaab se khitab kiya gaya hai jinhone Ale Muhammad (as) ka Haqq ghasb kiya aur jinhone Deen se inheraaf kiya. Allah Ta'ala ne unse farmaya ke woh unki jagah ek aisi Qaum ko layega jo Khuda se Muhabbat rakhti hogi aur Khuda unse Muhabbat rakhta hoga (Auliya e Khuda). Aur wo qaum wo hogi jo Qaem e Ale Muhammad (atfs) ka saath degi. Woh Allah ki raah mein Jihad karenge aur kisi malamat kunanda ki malamat se khauf zadah nahi honge."
(Noorus Saqlain)
🍁
Jange Jamal shuru hone se pahle Hazrat Ali (as) ne Khutba diya aur ye Ayat padhi aur farmaya:
_"Is Ayat ke misdaaq afraad aaj se pahle kisi ne koi Jang nahi ki un se Jang hogi."_
(Majmaul Bayan)

Bare Ilaha hame un Mominon ke sath shumar kar jo tere Muhib hain aur Tu bhi unhe chahta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍁
Abu Huraira se Rivayat hai ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Qayamat ke Din mere saamne mere kuchh Ashaab ayenge lekin uneh Hauz e Kausar se hata diya jayega. Us waqt mein kahuga: Parwardigar! Ye mere Ashaab hain!! Mujhse kaha jayega Aapko ilm nahi hai ke aapke baad unhone kitni tabdiliyan ki thi ye Aap ke baad ulte paon phir gaye the."_
(Tafseer e Tha'labi (Sunni)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                   *23rd Zilqad 1438*

           ♦ _*AAYAH-E-WILAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (710)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا وَلِيُّكُمُ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا الَّذِينَ يُقِيمُونَ الصَّلَاةَ وَيُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ وَهُمْ رَاكِعُونَ*

_*"Tumhara Sarparast (Wali) to sirf Allah aur Uska Rasool (saww) aur woh Momin hain jo pabandi se Namaz ada karte hai aur haalat e Ruku mein Zakat dete hain (Ali as)"*_
(Surah Maeda: 55)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat no.51 mein zikr hua tha ke kisi bhi aire ghaire ko apna Wali na maane. Yaha is Ayat mein Allah ne 3 Waliyon ka zikr kiya hai: Allah, Rasool (saww), Ali (as).
Ummat e Islamia is amr par muttafiq hai ke haalat e Ruku mein Hazrat Ali (as) ke alawa kisi ne Zakat nahi di. To sawal paida hota hai ke Allah ne do ka naam liya teesre ka sirf Ishaara hi kiyon kiya. To is wajah ye hain ke Hazrat Ali (as) ke Dushman Rasool ke zamane se hi the, ye baat Rasool (saww) ko bhi pata thi. Munafeqeen ki ta'daad zyada thi. Agar Munafeqeen ko pata chal jata to ho sakta hai aisi Ayaton ko Qur'an se kharij kar diya jata. Isi liye har Imam ne Qur'an ki tilawat ki takeed ki kiyonki is mein har Ayat Ahle Bait (as) ke Fazail ka Qaseeda hai. Lekin in Kalemat ko sirf Momin hi samajh sakte hain.

_*Shaane Nuzool:*_
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) Zuhr ki Namaz padh rahe the aur Aap (as) 2 Rakat padh chuke the aur Aap (as) Ruku ki haalat mein the. Aap ne libas ke upar ek qeemti Hullah pahen rakha tha jis ki qeemat 1000 dinar thi. Ye Hullah Najjashi badshah ne Anhazrat (saww) ki khidmat mein bataur tohfa diya tha. Anhazrat (saww) ne wohi Hullah Hazrat Ali (as) ke supurd kar diya. Aap Namaz ki haalat mein the ke ek sael (beggar) aaya aur usne kaha:
_"Allah ke Wali aur Ahle Imaan ki jaano par tasarruf rakhne wale! Aap par Salam ho! Aap Miskeen ko Sadqa karen."_
Aap ne jism se Hullah utara kar sael ki janib phenk diya aur Aap ne haath se ishaara kiya ke ye uthalo. Jis par Allah ne ye Ayat nazil farmayi.
Jis Sael ne sawal kiya tha uska talluq Bazm e Malaika se tha aur Aimma e Huda se bhi Sael sawal karte hain.

Bare Ilaha ham bhi Wali ke zariye se sawal karte hain ke ham par tere Nazre Karam ho jayen kiyon ham tere Waliyon ke naqshe qadam par chalne wale hain.

( _To be Cont'd......_)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Hamare Akheri Nabi Rasool e Akram (saww) ne farmaya:
_*"Ali (as) Namaz qaem karne wala hai aur wohi haalat e Ruku mein Zakat dene wala hai. Woh har haalat mein Allah ki Raza ko chahne wala hai. Iske mutalliq Allah ne irshaad farmaya: (5:55)"*_
(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌
*Hamare Aakhri Nabi Hazrat Mohammed Mustufa (sawa) ne Farmaya*

*"Sab se pehle jis cheez ke bare me Bande se sawal kiya jayega wo Hum Ahle Bait (as) ki Mohabbat hai."*

(Oyoono Akhbarir Reza, Vol. 2, Pg. 62)

           ♦ _*AAYAH-E-WILAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (711) *Cont'd .......*

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يَتَوَلَّ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فَإِنَّ حِزْبَ اللَّهِ هُمُ الْغَالِبُونَ*

_"Aur jisne bhi Khuda aur Uske Rasool (saww) aur un Ahle Imaan ko apna Sarparast banaya to use maloom ho ke Allah Jamat hi ghalib rahne wali hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 56)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayah e Wilayat ka bayan is Ayat mein bhi jari hai.
💍
Amali Sudooq mein Imam Mohd Baqir (as) se Rivayat hai ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Sael se sawal kiya ke use haalat e Ruku mein Ali (as) se kiya mila to usne bataya ke angoothi mili.
🕌 💍
Hazrat Umar bin Al Khattab se marvi hai ke Ayah e Vilayat, jis mein haalat e Ruku mein Angoothi dene par ek Ayat nazil hui, iske baad meine 40 Angoothiyan haalat e Ruku mein khairat ki lekin mere mutalliq koi Ayat nazil na hui.
(Noorus Saqlain)
🚩
Imam Reza (as) ne Mamoon ke Darbar mein Ummat aur Itrat mein 12 farq explain kiye, un mein se ek ye ke Allah ne Rasool e Akram (saww) ke Aqroba (family) ke liye Ghaneemat (income) mein Khums (5th part) farz kiya. Jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai.
_"Jaan lo tumhe jo bhi ghanimat (income) hasil ho us mein paanchwa (1/5th) hissa Allah, Rasool aur Rasool ke Qarabat daron ...ka hai."_ (Anfal:41)
Aur Allah ne Surah Nisa:59 mein 3 ki Ita'at wajib ki: Allah, Rasool aur Saheban e Amr. Aur Saheban e Amr Ahle Bait (as) hai."
(Uyoonul Akhbar Ar Reza (as))
🚩
Imam Zainul Abidin (as):
(Aapne ye Qur'an ki ayat padhi _"Woh Allah ki Ne'mat ko jaante hain phir woh uska inkar kar rahe hain"_ (Surah Nahl: 83) ke mutalliq farmaya:)
_"Jab Allah ne ye Ayah e Vilayat (5:55) nazil farmayi to Rasool e Khuda (saww) ke kuchh Sahabi Masjid e Nabawi mein jama hue aur unhone ek doosre se kaha ke tum is mutalliq kiya kahte ho?_
_Kuchh afraad ne kaha: Agar ham is Ayat ka inkaar karte hain to hamen baqi Qur'an Majeed ki Ayaat ka bhi inkaar karna padega aur agar ham ise maante hain to iski wajah se Ali (as) ham par musallat ho jayega aur te hamari tazleel (zillat) hai. Phir unhone kaha ke Muhammad (saww) apne tamam aqwaal mein sachche hain. Ab ham Ali (as) se Muhabbat to kar lenge lekin ham Ali (as) ke Ahkam ki ita'at nahi karenge. Us waqt Allah Ta'ala ne ye Ayat (Nahl:83) nazil farmayi aur unki aksariyat Vilayat e Ali (as) ke Munkir hain."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Vilayat e Sahebe Amr ke saye mein sabit qadam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Qayamat ke Din Rasoole Khuda (saww) ayenge, woh Khuda ke Daman se mutamassik honge aur ham Nabi e Akram (saww) ke daman e shafaqqat se mutamassik honge aur hamare pairokar hamare daman se mutamassik honge. Ham aur hamare pairokar Allah ka Giroh hain aur Allah ka Giroh hi Ghalib rahne wala hai. Khabardar Daman se murad zaheri Daman nahi. Rasoole Khuda (saww) Allah ke Deen ko tham kar ayenge aur ham apne Nabi ke Deen ko tham kar ayenge aur hamare pairokar hamare Deen ke Daman ko tham kar arsa e Mahshar mein warid honge."_
(Kitabut Tauheed e Sudooq )

         ♦ _*AAYAH-E-WILAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (712)  *Cont'd .......*

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا وَلِيُّكُمُ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا الَّذِينَ يُقِيمُونَ الصَّلَاةَ وَيُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ وَهُمْ رَاكِعُونَ*

_"Tumhara Sarparast (Wali) to sirf Allah aur Uska Rasool (saww) aur woh Momin hain jo pabandi se Namaz ada karte hai aur haalat e Ruku mein Zakat dete hain (Ali as)"_
(Surah Maeda: 55)

📚📖 💍
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein jab *إنما* Innama ka lafz aya hai yaani sirf aur sirf. Yani Wali teen ke alawa aur koi hai hi nahi. Wali yaani Sarparast. Wali Trustee hota hai. Yani Rasool (saww) ki ye qeemti property 'Islam' ke Trustee wohi hai jisko Allah ne Wali qarar diya hai.
Ulema e Ahle Sunnat ne bhi is Ayat ki yahi Tafseer bayan ki hai.
Ghayatul Maram mein 24 Ahadis Kutub e Ahle Sunnat se aur 19 Ahadis Shia Kutub se naql ki gayi hain.
Ahle Sunnat ki 30 se zyada motabar Kitaben jis mein ye maujood hai ke ye Ayat Hazrat Ali (as) ke liye nazil hui:
1. Zakhairul Uqba-Tabari
2. Tafseer Fathul Qadr-Shaukani
3. Jaame'ul Usool Vol 9,
4. Asbaabun Nuzool-Wahidi
5. Lababun Nuqool-Suyuti
6. Tazkara-Sibte Ibne Jauzi
7. Noorul Absaar- Shiblanji
8. Tafseer e Tabari
9. Al Kaafi As Shaaf-Ibne Hajr Ashqalani
10. Mafatihul Ghaeb- Raazi
11. Durrul Mansoor-Suyuti
12. Kanzul Ummal Vol 2,
13. Musnad Ibne Mardooya
14. Musnad Ibne As Shaikh
15. Sahih Nisai
16. Al Jama baenal Sihah Al Sittah.
(Refer Ahqaqul Haq, Vol 2, Al Ghadeer Vol 2, Al Murajeaat.)

Bare Ilaha hamare dilon mein Vilayat e Ali (as) qarar de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜
Ye Ayah e Vilayat zamana e Rasool (saww) ke waqt itni mashoor thi ke ma'roof Shayer Hisaan bin Sabit ne ye Ashaar Hazrat Ali (as) ke shaan mein padhe:

        *فانت الذى أعطيت إذ كنت راكعا*
         *زكاتا فدتك النفس يا خير راكع*
         *فأنزل فيك الله خير ولاية*
         *و بينها فى محكمات الشرايع*
_"Aap woh hain ke jinhone haalat e Ruku mein Zakat di. Aap par jaan fida ho, aye behtareen Ruku karne waale._
_Aur iske baad Khuda ne behtareen Vilayat Aap ke bare mein nazil ki aur Qur'an Majeed mein ise sabt kar diya."_
(Tafseer Ruhul Ma'ani-Shahabuddin Mehmood Aaloosi, Kifayatut Talib-Ganji Shafaee.)

                 ♦ _*VILAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (713)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَتَّخِذُوا الَّذِينَ اتَّخَذُوا دِينَكُمْ هُزُوًا وَلَعِبًا مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ وَالْكُفَّارَ أَوْلِيَاءَ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Jin logon ne tumhare Deen ko Mazaq aur Tafreeh ka nishana banaya hai unhe apna Dost na banao khwah unka talluq un logon se ho jinhein tum se pahle Kitab di gayi hai ya woh Kuffar hon aur Allah se Darte raho agar tum Ahle Imaan ho."_
(Surah Maeda: 57)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta kuch Ayaat mein Vilayat ka tazkara ho raha hai. Vali wa Auliya ka meaning ham pahle pata chuke hain. Vali means dost ya Sarparast, iska plural form (Jama) Auliya hai.
Yahan Allah hame takeed kar raha hai ke ham un logon se na dosti rakhen, na unko apna Sarparast maane jinhone Deen ka Mazaq udaya, chahe woh koi bhi ho. Tarikh mein ye baat mashoor hai ke Yazeed ibne Moaviya ibne Abu Sufiyan ne bhare Darbar mein jab Imam e Sajjad (as) aur Ahle Bait e athar (as) aseer kar ke laye gaye the to usne farmaya tha _"Kahan hain mere jadd jo dekhte to khush hote ke aaj mein ne kiya karnama kar dikhaya, Muhammad (as) ne Islam ka ek dhong rachaya tha balke ye sab ek khel tha."_
Us waqt Musalmano ki aksariyat usko apna Khalifatul Muslemin maan rahi thi.
Jo shakhs ye kah raha ho aisa shakhs Deen e Islam ka Sarparast ho sakta hai. Woh to khullam khulla mazaq uda raha tha. Karbala kiya thi - ye khel jo Shaqeefa se shuru hua tha Karbala mein urooj par pahuncha aur ye tha Yazeed ka radde Amal.
Ayat bilkul clear aur wazeh hai, jin logon ne Deen ko ek khel tamasha bana liya (5:58) kiya unko ham apna Auliya maan sakte hain?
Ji, agar Vali ko dosti ke maane mein lete hain to dosti usi se karenge jisko ham chahenge, aur usi dost ki nasihaten, advice maante hain jisko ham chahte hain. Lekin Aql ka taqaza ye hai hai ke usse dosti rakho jisko Allah dost rakhe. Ghaur karen Ahle Bait (as) ke siwa us zamane se lekar aaj tak kiya aur koi is layeq hai. Afzal ke hote hue mafzool ki Ita'at bewakoofi samjhi jayegi.
Vilayat ka matlab yehi hai ke ham apne tan man dhan aur apne aap ko uske hawale kar den jisko Khuda chahta hai na ke uski Vilayat qubool karen jo Deen ka mazaq uday.

Bare Ilaha hame un logon se door rakh jinone Deen ka mazaq udaya aur isko khel tamasha bana kar pamal kiya.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Ali (as)
ne Ibne Abbas se farmaya, _“Shab e Qadr har saal hoti hai aur is raat ko tamaam saal ke ahkaam naazil hote hain. Pus, Rasul ke baad *Auliya e Amr* hone chahiye.”_
Ibne Abbas ne puchha, “Wo kaun hain?”
Aap ne farmaya,
_“Main aur 11 Imam mere sulb se Muhaddas honge.”_
(Al Kaafi, v3, p175)

                  ♦ _*AZAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (714)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا نَادَيْتُمْ إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ اتَّخَذُوهَا هُزُوًا وَلَعِبًا ۚ ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ قَوْمٌ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Jab tum Namaz ke liye Nida karte ho to wo uska Mazaaq udate hain aur use khel tamasha bana lete hain aur iski wajah ye hai ke woh Aql nahi rakhte."_
(Surah Maeda: 58)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Phichhli Ayat ke zel mein is Ayat ko bhi cover kiya tha ke ham unko apna Sarparast na banayen jinhone ne Deen ka Mazaq udaya aur isko ek khel tamasha banaya. Is ki ek misal yahan ye hai ke jab Azaan hoti hai to iska bhi Mazaq udaya jata hai. Aaj bhi Azaan ki bahut Mukhalifat hoti hai, India mein Govt. se aksar demand kiya jaata hai ke loudspeaker par Azaan band ki jaye, Israel mein bhi is par pabandi lagane ka qanoon banaya gaya. Is qanoon ki khilaf warzi karte hue ek MP ne parliament mein hi Azaan deni shuru kardi. Wahi doosri taraf ye bhi dekha gaya ke ek Church ne ek Muazzin Azaan dene ke liye appoint kiya. Uski wajah ye thi ke ye Azaan itna asar rakhti hai ke har insaan is ki taraf khicha chala aata hai. Nida ka Islam mein ye ek behtareen tareeqa hai. Jabke Church ya Mandir mein ghanti baja baja kar bulaya jata hai. Azaan itna asar rakhti hai ke UK ka mashoor siyasatdan Gladstone ko kahna pada:
_"Jab tak Muhammad (saww) ka naam Azaan se buland ho raha hai, Ka'aba apni jagah qaem hai aur Qur'an Musalmano ka Rahnoma hai, us waqt tak mumkin nahi ke Islami sarzameen par hamari siyasat ki buniyad stewar (sabit) ho saken."_
Iski copy bhi gayi, Israel mein ek unche tower se ek Yahoodi Hebrew mein apne tareeqe se bula raha hai. (YouTube par available hai. https://youtu.be/IGhjlgFDfGs)

Azaan ke shuruaat kaise hui ye sawal uthta hai aur aam Musalman Kitabon mein ek jaali hadis pesh karte hai. Woh ye ke "Rasoole Khuda (saww) logon ko Namaz ki taraf bulane ka tareeqa sochne lage to Ashaab se mashwara kiya. Bahut sare suggestions aye lekin Abdulla bin Zaid aur Umar bin Khattab ne Azaan ka suggestion diya jo unhone khwab mein dekha tha. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko bahut pasand aya aur ise qubool kar liya."
(Tafseer e Qurtubi)
Is Rivayat se Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki tauheen Risaalat hai. Jaisa ke Qur'an mein hai hamara Rasool Waḥy ke alawa khitab hi nahi karta woh doosron ke suggestion par koi Ahkam lago kar raha hai. Ye is Aqeede ki manafi hai. Azaan jo ke Namaz ke liye zaroori hai, agar Namaz hukm e Khuda se amal mein ayi to Azaan bhi hukm e Khuda se hai. Imam Sadiq (as) farmate hain:
_"Azaan Paighambar e Islam ko Waḥy ke zariye Taa'leem di gayi thi. Jab Jibrael Azaan le kar aye to Paighambar e Khuda (saww) ka sar Hazrat Ali (as) ki god mein tha aur Jibrael ne Aap ko Azaan aur Aqamat batayin. Aap (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ko taaleem di. Aur phir Ali (as) ne Bilal ko Azaan sikhai."_
(Wasailus Shia, Vol 4, P-612)
Ghadeer ke Maidan mein Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Bilal ko hukm diya ke Azaan den. Bilal ne nida di:
_"Hayya Ala Khairil Amal"_
_"Neki ki taraf daudo"_
Ghadeer jahan Ali (as) ki Vilayat ka ailan hua wahin Azaan mein ye bata diya ke Vilayat hi Khair hai. Us din Rasoole Khuda (saww) Vilayat e Ali (as) ki taraf logon ko bula rahe the jo ke khair hai, Vilayat hai to Namaz hai warna woh bhi bekar hai.
(Elalus Sharaae, Vol. 2, P- 368)

Bilal Rasool (saww) ke zamane mein aisi Azaan dete the.
(Kanz al-Ummal - Muttaqi al-Hindi, vol. 8, p. 342, H- 23,174)

Azaan se Hazrat Umar ne is fiqre ko delete kar diya aur uski jagah _"Assalato khairun minan Naum"_ ko add kar diya jo ke Rasool (saww) ke zamane mein nahi tha.
(Ref: ‘Al-Mustarshid fi Imamat-e-Ali Ibn Abi Talib (a.s.) by Mohd ibne Jurair Al Tabari, on page 516)

Bare Ilaha hame aise jagah sukunat de jahan har waqt Azaan sunayi de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                  ♦ _*FAASIQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (715)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ هَلْ تَنْقِمُونَ مِنَّا إِلَّا أَنْ آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْنَا وَمَا أُنْزِلَ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَأَنَّ أَكْثَرَكُمْ فَاسِقُونَ*

_"Aap kah den, Aye Ahle Kitab! Kiya tum ham se sirf is baat par naraaz ho ke ham Allah par aur Deen ki us taleem par Imaan laye hain jo hamari taraf nazil hui hai aur jo ham se pahle nazil hui hai aur tumhare andar aksariyat Faaseqeen ki hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 59)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat Yahoodiyon ki be mahel zid, hat dharmi aur ta'assubat ke ek pahlu ki taraf ishara karti hai. Is mein is baat ka zikr hai ke agar tum khalis Tauheed aur tamam Aasmani Kitabon ke saamne tasleem kham karne par ham par eitraz karte ho to iski wajah ye hain ke tum mein se aksar Fisq aur Gunah se alooda ho chuke hain aur agar kuchh logon Pakeezgi aur Haq ka raasta apnate hain to ye tumhari nazar mein Aib hai.
Yehi wajah hai ke Munafeqeen ne bhi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke baad Haq ki adawat mein khul kar aa gaye.

Bare Ilaha hame hamesha Deen e Haq par qaem o daem rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Kabhi kabhi 2 aadmi Masjid mein daakhil hote hain aur unme se ek Aabid hota hai aur doosra Faasiq (gunah-gaar) hota hai. Magar jab Masjid se baahar aate hain to Aabid faasiq hota hai aur Faasiq Aabid hota hai, is liye ke jab Aabid Masjid mein daakhil hota hai to usko apni Ibadat par naaz hota hai aur wo isi ko sochta rehta hai aur jab Faasiq daakhil hota hai to wo apne fisq (gunah) par sharminda hota hai aur Allah uske gunaho'n ko maaf kar deta hai."_
(Elal ush Sharaye, p278)
🍁🌾
Imam Ali (as):
_"Faasiq (ayyaash / wicked) logon ki sohbat se parhez karo kyun ki burayi burayi ke saath waabasta hoti hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p213)

                  ♦ _*MAL'OON*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (716)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ هَلْ أُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِشَرٍّ مِنْ ذَٰلِكَ مَثُوبَةً عِنْدَ اللَّهِ ۚ مَنْ لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ وَغَضِبَ عَلَيْهِ وَجَعَلَ مِنْهُمُ الْقِرَدَةَ وَالْخَنَازِيرَ وَعَبَدَ الطَّاغُوتَ ۚ أُولَٰئِكَ شَرٌّ مَكَانًا وَأَضَلُّ عَنْ سَوَاءِ السَّبِيلِ*

_"Aap kah den ke kiya mein tumhe un logon ki nishaan dahi karaon jinka anjaam Khuda ke haan badtar hai? Woh jin par Khuda ki Laanat hai aur jin par Khuda ka Ghazab hua hai aur jin mein se Bandar aur Suar banaye gaye aur jinhone Taghoot ki bandagi ki aur unka darja intihai bura hai aur woh Seedhi Rah se bhatke hue hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 40)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke guzishta Ayat mein zikr hua ke Sahi o Saalim Tauheedi Aqeeda walon par eitraz karne walon ko Allah ne Fasiq qarar diya tha. Yahan is Ayat mein bhi Allah un Fasiq logon ki nishan dahi kar raha ke woh kaun log hain. Allah Yahoodiyon ki ye Sifat bata kar Munafeqeen par bhi ishaara hai. Yahan Allah Nek aur bad afraad ko compare kar ke sawal kar raha ke ham khud sochen ke kis ko sahi maanege. Kiya badtar log sahi hain ya Paak daaman log.
Allah ne Ahle Bait (as) ki Pakeezgi ka Qur'an ki Ayah e Tatheer mein Ailan kar diya. Ab jo bhi inke muqabile par aaya woh Najis hai. Taghoot ki parastish karne wala hai. Jibt o Taghoot ki tashreeh ham pahle kar chuke hai. Dua Sanam e Quraish mein Jibt o Taghoot par Laanat ki gayi hai aur is Ayat mein bhi un par Allah Laanat bhej raha hai.
Pahle ye bhi ham bata chuke hain ke Seedha Raasta wohi hai jin par Allah ki Ne'maten nazil hoti hain. Yehi Ahle Bait (as) ka raasta hai, jo is raaste se bhatak gaya uska Akherat mein badtar thikana hoga.

Bare Ilaha hame Seedhe Raaste par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗣👂🏻
*Imam Taqi (as):*
_"Jo bolne waale ki baat kaan dhar-ke sune usne (goya) uski parastish / Ibadat ki. Pus, agar bolne wala Khuda ki baat keh raha hai to usne Khuda ki ibadat ki aur agar bolne waala Shaitan ki zabaan bol raha hai to usne Shaitan ki parastish ki."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)
✊🏻
*Imam Taqi (as):*
_"4 baatein insaan ko amal par ubhaarti hai:_
_*Sehet, Maaldaari, Ilm, Taufeeq."*_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)
🕌
*Imam Taqi (as):*
_"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa le'n, yaani sargardaa'n (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumraah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar usay zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayaanat ki."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)

                  ♦ _*MUNAFIQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (717)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا جَاءُوكُمْ قَالُوا آمَنَّا وَقَدْ دَخَلُوا بِالْكُفْرِ وَهُمْ قَدْ خَرَجُوا بِهِ ۚ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْتُمُونَ*

_"Aur woh tumhare paas aate hain to kahte hain ke ham Imaan laye halaanki Kufr le kar aye the aur Kufr le kar hi wapas hue hain aur jo kuchh ye dilon mein chhupaye hue hain Allah achchi tarah se Jaanta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 61)

📚📖 👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat no. 60 mein (ghalti se jo 40 type ho gayi thi) Allah ne Fasiqon ki nishan dahi karai thi aur unki khusoosiyat bayan kiye the aur Allah ne un par Laanat bheji, Azaab nazil kiya. Is Ayat mein unki mazeed wazahat kar di gayi  aur wo ye ke ye Fasiq log Munafiq hain. Woh zahiri mein to kahte hain ham Imaan laye lekin unke dil mein Kufr hi bhara rahta hai.
Mazeed ye ke ham pichhle Messages mein kai bar ye hadis pesh kar chuke hai jo ke bahut hi maaroof hai:

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Aap se koi mohabbat nahi karega siwaye Momin ke aur koi dushmani nahi rakhega siwaye Munafiq ke. Khuda Wande Aalam farmata hai,_
_"Munafeqeen Jahannum ke aakhri tabqe mein honge"_
(Surah Nisa, Surah 4, Ayat 145, Manaaqib Ameerul Momeneen (as), p386)

Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim mein hai ke Imam Sadiq (as) ki Rivayat ke mutabiq ye Ayat Raeesul Munafeqeen Abdullah bin Abi ke mutalliq nazil hui.
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Munafiqon ke sharr se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹
Imam Ali (as):
_"Agar main Momin ki naak bhi talwaar se kaat dun ke mujhse adaawat kare to nahi karega aur agar Munafiq par saari duniya undel dun ke mujhse mohabbat kar le to nahi karega, is liye ke ye faisla Raoole Akram (saww) ki zaban se ho chuka hai ke "Aye Ali (as), Momin tumse dushmani nahi kar sakta aur Munafiq tumse mohabbat nahi kar sakta"._
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p190)
👹
Imam Taqi Al Jawad (as):
_"Jo khateeb ko sunta hai wo uska ghulam ho jata hai. Agar Khateeb Khuda ka numainda ho to woh Khuda ka Ghulam ban jata hai aur agar khateeb Shaitan ke numainda ho to woh Shaitan ka numainda ban jata hai."_
(Tuhuful Uqool)

            ♦ _*HARAAM KHORI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (719)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَتَرَىٰ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ يُسَارِعُونَ فِي الْإِثْمِ وَالْعُدْوَانِ وَأَكْلِهِمُ السُّحْتَ ۚ لَبِئْسَ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Tum unki aksariyat ko dekhoge ke woh Gunah aur Zulm o ziyadti ke kaamon aur Haram khori mein daud dhoop karte hain. Ye log bahut hi buri harkaat sar anjam de rahe hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 63)

📚📖 😈
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Munafeqeen ka tazkara kiya gaya tha aur unki khusoosiyat bayan ki gayi thi. Usika ka tazkara is Ayat mein bhi jari hai.
Jab insaan seedhi raah se bhatak jaata hai, Ahle Bait (as) ka daman chhod deta hai, ghalat mahaul, ghalat sangat, ghalat logon ko apna namoona e amal banata hai jiske natije mein woh gunahon par gunahen karta chala jata hai.

Sohot سحت literally means dar asl darakht ke chhilke utarna, shadeed bhook etc. Terminology, istelahan Najaez aur Rishwat lene ke liye use hota hai. Kiyonki Rishwat society par se Pakeezgi wa Barkat chhilke ke tarah utar deta hai. Aur Society dry ho jati hai. Society murda ho jati hai uski growth nahi ho sakti.

Is Ayat mein do Gunah ki nishandahi ki hai: Zulm o Sitam aur Haraam khori. Haram khori yani kisi ka najaez maal khana, Rishwat khori, Sood khori, Najis khana waghaira. Kitna bure ye log amal anjam dete hain. Ye ittefaqiya nahi karte balke apne in amal ko bura bhi nahi samjhte balke ye kaam nidar ho kar dat ke karte hain.

Bare Ilaha hame aise Munafiqon se door rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😈
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Apni kamaai ko paak karo taake tumhari Dua qubool ho, kyunki Ek Haraam luqma khaane se 40 din tak Dua qubool nahi hoti."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3)
♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar koi shakhs Haraam kaam ko Khauf e Khuda ki wajah se na kare to Allah (bhi) Jahannum ki aag uspar Haraam kar deta hai."_
(Tauba Aagosh e Rehmat)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*ULEMA E SOO*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (720)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَوْلَا يَنْهَاهُمُ الرَّبَّانِيُّونَ وَالْأَحْبَارُ عَنْ قَوْلِهِمُ الْإِثْمَ وَأَكْلِهِمُ السُّحْتَ ۚ لَبِئْسَ مَا كَانُوا يَصْنَعُونَ*

_*"Unke Ulema o Mashaikh (Rahbar)* unhe Gunah par zaban kholne aur Haram khori se kiyon nahi tokte. Yaqeenan woh bahut bura kar rahe hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 63)

📚📖 👳🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Munafeqeen ki ek khaslat Haraam khori ka zikr hua. Iski ek wajah ye hai ke Ulema wa qaum ke Rahbaron ne logon ko buraiyon se roka nahi.
Jab qaum ke darmiyan zahiri Nabi ya Imam na ho to ye Amr Bil Ma'roof wa Nahi Anil Munkar ki zimmedari Ulema wa Rahbaron par aan padti hai.
Ulema do tarah ke hote hai Ulema e Khair jo Khair ki dawat dete hain aur Ulema e Soo jo buraiyon ki dawat dete hain ya buraiyan dekhte hai par khamosh rahte hai.
Jahan Allah ne Ulema e Bani Israel ki ta'reef ki hai wahi is Ayat mein Ahle Kitab ke Ulema ki mazammat bhi ki hai. Lekin ye ayat Musalmano ke Ulema par bhi sadiq aati hai jo Munafeqeen ke Rahbar hote hain. Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
👳🏻
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne Khutba diya jis mein Allah Ta'ala ki Hamd o Sana ke baad Aap ne farmaya:
_"Tumse pahli Ummaten is liye halaak huin ke unhone Khuda ki nafarmani ki magar unke Ulema o Mashaikh (Chief Rahbar) ne unhe na roka. Isse logon ki jura'ate badh gayi. Phir woh sare aam gunah karne lage magar unke Ulema o Mashaikh ne phir bhi unhe mana na kiya jiski wajah se Allah ne un Ummaton par Azaab nazil kar diya. Lehaza tumhe Amr bil Ma'roof aur Nahi Anil Munkar par amal karte rahna chahiye."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
👳🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Guzishta zamane ke logon ko Allah Ta'ala ne sirf is liye apni Rehmat se door kar diya ke unhone Amr Bil Ma'roof aur Nahi Anil Munkar ko tark kar diya. Usne awam ko gunah ke irtekab aur Ulema ko Nahi Anil Munkar tark karne par apni Laa'nat ka Haqdar qarar diya aur unhe apni Rehmat se door kar diya."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Khutba Qase'ah No. 192)
👰🏻
Raavi ne Imam Baqir (as) se sawal kiya:
_"Maine suna hai ke Aap kahte hain ke jo shakhs Sunnat se hat kar apni Biwi ko Talaq de (means one time Triple Talaq de) to uski Talaq ki koi hasiyat nahi?"_
Imam Baqir (as) ne farmaya:
_"Ye sirf mera Fatwa nahi hai balke Hukm e Khuda wandi bhi yehi hai. Agar ham tumhe ghalat Fatwe dene lag jayen to ham tumse zyada bure qarar payenge. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai (5:63)"_
🙏🏻
Bare Ilaha hame itni tameez de ke ham Ulema e Soo wa Khair ke darmiyan farq kar saken.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👳🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Ye ghalat ravishen tumhe kahan liye ja rahi hain aur ye andhiyaryan tumhe kin pareshaniyon mein dal rahi hain aur ye jhooti umeeden tumhe kaheka fareb de rahi hain. Kahan se laye jaate ho aur kidhar paltaye jaate ho? Har mi'aad (terms) ka ek navishta hota hai aur har ghaeb palat kar aata hai. Apne Alim Rabbani se suno, apne dilo ko hazir karo, agar tumhe pukare to jag utho."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*FASAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (721)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا ۘ بَلْ يَدَاهُ مَبْسُوطَتَانِ يُنْفِقُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَلَيَزِيدَنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ طُغْيَانًا وَكُفْرًا ۚ وَأَلْقَيْنَا بَيْنَهُمُ الْعَدَاوَةَ وَالْبَغْضَاءَ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ ۚ *كُلَّمَا أَوْقَدُوا نَارًا لِلْحَرْبِ أَطْفَأَهَا اللَّهُ ۚ وَيَسْعَوْنَ فِي الْأَرْضِ فَسَادًا ۚ وَاللَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُفْسِدِينَ*

_"Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain. Bandhe gaye khud unke haath aur unki guftgu ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai. Allah ke Haath to Kushaadah hain, Woh jis tarah chahta hai kharch karta hai. Jo Kalam tumhare Rab ki taraf se tum par nazil kiya gaya hai wo un mein se aksar logon ki sarkashi aur batil parasti mein ulte izafe ka sabab sabit hoga. Aur (iski padash-reward mein) Hamne unke darmiyan Qayamat tak ke liye adawat aur dushmani dal di hai. Jab kabhi ye Jang ki Aag bhadkate hain Allah use bujha deta hai aur *ye Zameen mein Fasaad phailane ki koshish kar rahe hain aur Allah ko Fasaad barpa karne wale afraad na pasand hain.*"_
(Surah Maeda: 64)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein kai Topics shamil hain jo ham part by part pesh karenge.
Abhi haal mein Haryana kuchh waqeat runuma hue aur court ke faisle ke baad logon ne fasaad barpa kar diya. Hame isse koi matlab nahi ke faisla ghalat tha ya sahi. Lekin jo fasaad barpa hua wo kisi mazhab ki numaiyndgi nahi karta.
Jaisa ke kuchh din pahle hadis pesh ki thi ke jo jiska pairov hoga, jo jisko apna Peshwa maanega wo usi ke naqshe qadam par chalega. Koi bhi shaikh kisi insaan ke amal ko dekh kar ye bata sakta hai ke ye kiska pairov hai, kisko follow karta hai. Jabse Kainat khalq hui aur aaj tak kitne adyan (religions) ubhre aur unke shaidayyon ko hamne dekha. Islam ke aghaz ke pahle Yahoodi Hijaz mein powerful the. Bani Nazir aur Bani Quraiza, Bani Qeenqa ke Yahoodi apas mein Jang karte rahe kiyonki unhone apne asl Rahbaron ki nasihaton ko bhula diya tha aur kisi aur ki pairavi karne lage the. Aus o Khazraj 100 saal tak ladte rahe. Akhirkar Yahoodiyon ne Khaibar ki Islami Jang mein ghutne tek diye. Is liye jo ghalat rah par the unhone fitna o fasaad ka beej boya. Baad e wafat e Rasool (saww) phir log fasaad par utar aye. IS wa Daesh aaj ki misal hai jisne apne ham naam ki misal aaj ke daur mein pesh kar di.
Ye haqeeqat hai ke aam aadmi Allah se nazdeeki hasil karne ke liye zariye ke talaash mein rahta hai. Woh apne kisi Rahbar ki talaash mein rahta hai. Farq sirf is baat ka hai ke woh kis tarah ke Rahbar ko select karta hai. Aksar Sadhu ya Baba zaheran ziyada mutadayyan nazar aate hain. Isliye unki zaheri shakl dekh kar log mughalte mein pad jaate hain. Sadhu ya Baba inka tareeqe kar, concept same hai. Ye Riyazat (spiritual practice) karte hain jisme wo harkaat harna hai jo fitrat khilaf ho, 4 turook par amal karte hain. Jis mein se ek hain sex se door hona, shaadi na karna. Jab woh is mein mahir hota hai to chamatkar dikhata hai. Jisko dekh kar aam insaan chaunkta hai aur uska mureed ho jata hai. Lekin har insaan ko us fitrat mein paida kiya gaya, jaise insaan khilafe fitrat karta hai gunah ka murtakib hota ho jata hai. Jab Janabe Yusuf (as) bhi is manzil se guzar chuke hain jiska Quran mein bhi zikr hai. Isliye aksar Church ka Father, Sadhu ya Babaon par Rape cases paye jate hain ye aur baat hai ke in par aksar parda dala jata hai. Kiyonki inko inke followers apna Rahbar maan lete hain. Inke follower apne Rahbar mein itne ashiq ho jaate hain ke un par mar mitne par tayyar rahte hain. Unki Muhabbat mein itne doob jaate hain ke unke andar agar koi nuqs  unko dikhaya bhi jaye tab bhi uska inkar karte hain. Father ho, Sadhu ho, ya koi Baba ho unki life history ki study agar khuli aankhon se ki jaye to unke Afa'al ki pol khulti hai. Woh aise amal karte hain jo na nek hote hai ya aise amal ka irtekab karte hain jo Khuda ki doori ka sabab hon. Agar kisi bhi Rahbar ko dekhna hai to sirf uske ghar ki Ziyarat kar len. Apke liye khud sabit ho jayega ke kiya ye mera sahi Rahbar hai.
Ye silence fasaad ko tarjeeh dete hain. Haqeeqi Rahbar Fasaad barpa nahi karte, kiyonki Allah fasaad ko pasand nahi karta.

Bare Ilaha hame aise Rahbaron se door rakh jo hame Allah ki nazdeeki ke bajaye doori ka sabab banen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p130)

                ♦ _*BADA'*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (721)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا ۘ بَلْ يَدَاهُ مَبْسُوطَتَانِ يُنْفِقُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ* وَلَيَزِيدَنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ طُغْيَانًا وَكُفْرًا ۚ وَأَلْقَيْنَا بَيْنَهُمُ الْعَدَاوَةَ وَالْبَغْضَاءَ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ ۚ كُلَّمَا أَوْقَدُوا نَارًا لِلْحَرْبِ أَطْفَأَهَا اللَّهُ ۚ وَيَسْعَوْنَ فِي الْأَرْضِ فَسَادًا ۚ وَاللَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُفْسِدِينَ.

_*"Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain. Bandhe gaye khud unke haath aur unki guftgu ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai. Allah ke Haath to Kushaadah hain, Woh jis tarah chahta hai kharch karta hai.* Jo Kalam tumhare Rab ki taraf se tum par nazil kiya gaya hai wo un mein se aksar logon ki sarkashi aur batil parasti mein ulte izafe ka sabab sabit hoga. Aur (iski padash-reward mein) Hamne unke darmiyan Qayamat tak ke liye adawat aur dushmani dal di hai. Jab kabhi ye Jang ki Aag bhadkate hain Allah use bujha deta hai aur ye Zameen mein Fasaad phailane ki koshish kar rahe hain aur Allah ko Fasaad barpa karne wale afraad na pasand hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 64)

📚📖 ✊🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein jis Aqeeda *'Bada بداء'* ka concept ka zikr hai. 'Bada' ka matlab ye hai ke Allah kisi ki bhi Taqdeer ko badal sakta hai. Kisi ki bhi Taqdeer bandhi hui nahi hai. Musalmano mein sirf Ahle Bait (as) ke followers hi is Aqeede ko maante hai baqi sab inkar karte hai. Rivayat mulaheza ho:
Imam Reza (as) ne Sulaiman Mervazi se farmaya:
"Tum Bada ka inkaar karke Yahoodiyon ke nazariye ki ta'eed kar rahe ho."
Usne poochha Yahoodiyon ka Aqeeda kiya hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Yahoodiyon ke qaul ko Allah ne yun naql kiya hai:
*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ*
( _Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain._)(Ayat 5:64)
In Alfaaz se Yahoodiyon ki murad ye thi ke Allah ab tamam Umoor ke faislon se farigh ho chuka hai. Ab koi naya farman aur naya faisla jari nahi kar sakta. Unke nazrye ke ibtaal mein Allah ne farmaya:
*غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا*
_Unke apne haath bandhe hain aur unki is baat ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)
👊🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ye Ayat *وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ* ka ye mafhoom nahi ke Yahoodi ye Aqeeda rakhte the ke Allah ke zahiri Haath bandhe hue hain. Unke is qaul ka maqsad ye hai ke Allah tamam Umoor se farigh ho chuka hai aur ab na Woh Ma'melaat o Umoor mein kami kar sakta hai aur na beshi kar sakta hai. Allah Ta'ala ne unke is khayal ki tardeed ki aur farmaya:
*غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا*
Isi mafhoom ko Allah Ta'ala ne in alfaaz mein bayan kiya hai:
*يَمْحُو اللَّهُ مَا يَشَاءُ وَيُثْبِتُ ۖ وَعِنْدَهُ أُمُّ الْكِتَابِ*
_"Woh jo chahta hai mita deta hai aur jo chahta hai use sabit rakhta hai aur Asl Kitab Usi ke paas hai."_
(Surah Ra'd 39)
(Kitabut Tawheed, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Tu hamari nagahi balaon ko Rahat mein badal de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

(Roohul Hayaat)

                   ♦ _*TAQDEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (722)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا ۘ بَلْ يَدَاهُ مَبْسُوطَتَانِ يُنْفِقُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ....*
[Surat Al-Ma'idah 64]

_*"Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain. Bandhe gaye khud unke haath aur unki guftgu ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai. Allah ke Haath to Kushaadah hain, Woh jis tarah chahta hai kharch karta hai. ..."*_
(Surah Maeda: 64)

📚📖 🔏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
_*Qaza wa Qadar:*_
Hamne guzishta msg mein bataya ke is Ayat ka talluq 'Bada' بداء" se hai. Mazeed ham batana chahenge ke is ka talluq *"Qaza o Qadar , قضاء و قدر"* se hai. Means hamare Taqdeer se mutalliq hai.
Jaisa ke hamne pahle bataya ke kisi ki bhi Taqdeer bandhi hui nahi. Allah jab chahe Taqdeer ko badal bhi sakta hai. Deen mein koi Jabr nahi (Ayatul Kursi). Yahan tak ke Allah Cause & Effects (Illat o Ma'lool) ke system mein majboor nahi. Ye jo nazariya hai ke Allah ne ek bar paida / create kar diya aur phir Duniya automatic chal rahi hai, ye ghalat hai. Allah ki nazre Enayat hai to ye Duniya baqi hai. Is ki misal aap Yun samajh sakte hain ke aap apni khayalon mein ek Mahal khada karen, jab tak aapki tawajjo is Mahal par lagi hai ye Mahal baqi hai, aur kisi ne aap ko hila diya, aapki tawajjo hati, aap ka Mahal bhi Sheikh chilli ki tarah chakna choor ho gaya. Allah apni Qudrat se is poori Kainat par Tawajjo kiye hai. Lekin Uski Tawajjo insan ki tarah nahi. Isliye yahan cause and effect ka sawal nahi uthta. Cause na hote hue bhi Allah Cause  (Illat) paida kar sakta. Uski Qurat mein sab kuchh hai, kisi ko Zer kare ya Zabar kare. Isliye Khuda ke Haath nahi bandhe balke hamare Haath bandhe hain.
Allah ka is Ayat mein lahja kuchh is tarah hai:
_"O Yahoodi sun, Mere Haath nahi bandhe, bandhe honge haath tere. Mere Khule hai, (Kanjoos nahi, Khule dono Haathon se deta hun.) Kiya baat karta hai, Laanat ho tujh par."_
Jo nazarya/ Tafseer hamne pesh ki ye Ahle Bait (as) ki rivaayat ka khulasa tha. Sirf Ahle Bait (as) ke pairokar hi is Aqeedon ko qubool karte hain. Baqi Musalman mukhtalif Aqeede rakhte hain, Allah aise nazariye rakhne walon par is Ayat mein Laanat bhej raha hai.
Jo Aqeede se Muafiqat nahi rakhte woh Jabariyyah ke qael hain. Yani Deen mein Jabr (compulsion) hai. Unka kahna ye hai ke insaan ki Taqdeer mein jo likh diya hai wo badal nahi sakta. Agar aisa hota to phir Dua ka koi matlab nahi hota. Agar sab Pre-planned hai to phir Qayamat/Aakhirat bekar. Jaza wa Saza be maani ho jate. Isliye Taqdeer ka daromadar hamare Aamaal ke par hai. Ham apne hi Aamaal se apni Taqdeer badal sakte hain agar Allah chahe. Phir aap sawal karenge ke to phir Taqdeer banayi kiyon. Taqdeer yani Allah ne ek system/nizam paida to kar diya lekin hamare Aamal ke mutabiq ye badalti rahti hai. Misal ke taur par ek Software Engineer ek App ya Software computer system mein load kare, to load karke chhod nahi deta hai balki us mein requirement ke mutabiq changes karta rahta hai. Isko ham nuqs nahi kahenge. Nuqs Bug hote hain. Allah ke kaam mein koi Nuqs nahi. Jo Allah System mein changes laata hai woh insaan ke Aamal ke mutabiq ya to use develope karta hai ya saza ke taur par  past/halaak kar deta hai.
(To be Cont'd)

Bare Ilaha hame nek Aamal karne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔏
*الإمام علي (ع): القدر سر من سر الله‏، وستر من ستر الله‏ وحرز من حرز الله‏ مرفوع في حجاب الله‏، مطوي عن خلق الله‏.*

Imam Ali (as):
_"Taqdeer Allah ke Raazon mein se ek Raaz hai, Allah ka Hijab hai, Taweez hai. Allah ke Hijab utha hai jabke Allah ki Khilqat se niha (chhipa) hai."_
(At Tauheed, P-383, H-32)

*الإمام علي (ع) ـ في تحميد الله‏ سبحانه ـ: أحمده إلى نفسه كما استحمد إلى خلقه، وجعل لكل شيء قدرا، ولكل قدر أجلا، ولكل أجل كتابا.*

Imam Ali (as): Allah Subhan ki Hamd o Sana mein farmate hain:
_"Mein Uski Hamd o Sana Uske liye is tarah karta hun jaisa Woh apni Makhlooq se chahta hai. Usne har cheez ki ek miqdaar (measure) muayyan ki, aur har muayyan miqdaar ke liye Ajl (Due date) aur har Ajl ke liye ek Kitab (Record)."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Khutba 183)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (723)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا ۘ بَلْ يَدَاهُ مَبْسُوطَتَانِ يُنْفِقُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ....*
[Surat Al-Ma'idah 64]

_*"Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain. Bandhe gaye khud unke haath aur unki guftgu ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai. Allah ke Haath to Kushaadah hain, Woh jis tarah chahta hai kharch karta hai. ..."*_
(Surah Maeda: 64)

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔏
*Qaza wa Qadar:*_
*رسول الله‏ (ص): قال الله‏ جل جلاله: من لم يرض بقضائي ولم يؤمن بقدري فليلتمس إلها غيري!*

Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Allah Ta'ala ka qaul hai: "Jo shakhs Meri Qaza' se Raazi hai lekin Meri Qadar ko nahi maanta woh kisi aur khuda se maange."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar al-Reza (as), Vol 1, P-141, no. 42)
🔏
*رسول الله‏ (ص): في كل قضاء الله‏ عزوجل خيرة (خير) للمؤمن.*

Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Allah Ta'ala ki har Qaza mein Mo'meneen ke liye Khair hoti hai."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar al-Reza (as), Vol 1, P-141, no. 42)
🔏
*الإمام الصادق (ع): إن الله‏ إذا أراد شيئا قدره، فإذا قدره قضاه، فإذا قضاه أمضاه.*

Imam al-Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Allah kisi cheez ka Iraada karta hai, usko muqaddar karta hai, jab Muqaddar karta hai uski Qaza' karta hai, jab Qaza' ho jati hai to usko seal kar deta hai."_
(Bihar al-Anwar, v. 5, p. 121, no. 64)
🔏
*الإمام علي (ع) ـ وقد سأله رجل عن القدر ـ : بحر عميق فلا تلجه . قال: يا أمير المؤمنين، أخبرنا عن القدر . قال: سر الله‏ فلا تتكلفه . قال: يا أمير المؤمنين، أخبرنا عن القدر . قال: أما إذ أبيت فإنه أمر بين أمرين لا جبر ولا تفويض.*

Imam Ali (as) se Taqdeer ke bare mein sawal kiya to farmaya:
_"Ye ek gehra samandar hai, isliye is mein ghota na laga. Ye Allah ka ek Raaz hai, isliye tum isse pareshan na ho. Jaisake tum inkar karte hue dikhte ho (ya insult), to ye do amr ke beech ka amr hai - Na hi poori tarah Jabr hai aur na Tafweez (poori azaadi ya ikhtiyar)."_
(Kanz al-`Ummal, no. 1567)
(Amr bainal Amrain ke bare mein kal bayan karenge.)

   ♦ _*AMR BAINAL AMRAIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (724)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا ۘ بَلْ يَدَاهُ مَبْسُوطَتَانِ يُنْفِقُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ....*
[Surat Al-Ma'idah 64]

_*"Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain. Bandhe gaye khud unke haath aur unki guftgu ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai. Allah ke Haath to Kushaadah hain, Woh jis tarah chahta hai kharch karta hai. ..."*_
(Surah Maeda: 64)

📚📖 🔏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_.
*Amr bayn al-amrayn (Arabic: أمر بين الأمرين)*
Kuchh ahadith hamne kal bayan ki thi. Ye Eteqadaat e Ahle Bait (as) mein se hai. Imam Sadiq (as) wa Imam Ali (as), Imam Raza se bahut Rivayaat hain.
Is theory ka meaning ye hai ke Insaan ke Aamal mein na Jabr hai (Taqdeer mein bandha hai) aur na Tafweez hai (Ikhtiyar, poora Azaad hai) balke beech ka raasta hai. Na insaan poora majboor hai na poora apne Ikhtiyar mein azaad hai.
Aaamaal (Actions) ko 2 hisso mein bata jata hai.
(1) Jahan Insaan ke Ikhtiyar  mein kuchh nahi usko *Aalam-e-Takveen عالم تكوينى* kahte hain. Yahan sab sirf Allah ka Ikhtiyar hai. In Umoor mein insaan ka koi dakhal nahi hai. Jaise Paidaish, Maut o Hayat, Rizq, Qudrati Haadsaat,..... etc.
(2) Jahan Allah ne insaan ko Ikhtiyar diya hai usko *Aalam-e-Tashrii عالم تشريعى* kahte hain. Allah ne jo Shariyat bayan ki hai us par amal karne ke liye insaan ko ikhtiyar diya gaya hai. Allah insaan ke Aamaal mein dakhal nahi deta chahe achha kare ya bura kare lekin uski bhi kuchh limit hai. Kuchh had tak insaan ko chhot di jati hai. Allah ne jo Deen o Shariyat batayi hai us par amal karna, Usoole Deen, Furu-e-Deen aur Akhlaq etc sab is dayre mein aate hain.
Jahan Insaan ka ikhtiyar khatm ho jata hai, woh Allah ke saamne sar jhukata  hai, Uske saamne Dua karta hai gidgidata hai.
Isliye Insaan ko do Umoor ke beech mein rakha gaya hai na Jabr na Tafweez.
Poore explanation ki yaha gunjaish nahi isse mutalliq Kitabe refer karen. Is topic mein wo saare sawal hal ho jate hain ke insaan jab koi hadse ka shikar hota hai to Allah ki shikayat karta hai aur Allah ko Zalim samjhta hai. Un logon ko Allah ki Adalat nazar nahi aati.
Jo is theory ko nahi maante wo inko jawab nahi de sakte kiyonki unke Usoole Deen mein Adalate Ilahi nahi hai. Sirf 3 Usool par iktefa karte hain. Jabke Ahle Bait (as) ke chahne wale 5 Usool par chalte hain. Tauheed, Adl, Nubuwwat, Imamat, Qayamat.

Bare Ilaha hame Usoole Aqaaed e Ahle Bait (as) par sabit qadam rakh.
----------------------------------------------

*Amr Bayn Al-Amrayn*
http://en.wikishia.net/view/Amr_Bayn_al-Amrayn

*Aqeeda e Tafweez*
https://m.facebook.com/notes/university-of-ahlulbayt-as/aqeeda-e-tafweez/530192813742755

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔏
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ke irshaad: " La Jabr wa la tafweez bal amrun baynal amreen " ki tashrih k silsile mein Hazrat Imam Raza (as) se ye riwayet naql ki hai k Aap (as) ne farmaya: _"Jo shakhs ye etiqad rakhta hai k Khuda wand e Alam hi hamare afa'al (actions) ka Fail (Doer) hai aur phir (hamaray bure ) afa'al per hame Azaab bhi deta hai woh Jabr kr qael hain aur jo ye kahta hai k Khuda ne Paida karne , Rizq dene ka muamla apni Hujjaton (Aimma a.s) ke supurd kar diya hai to woh tafweez ka qael hain. Jabr ka qael kafir hain aur Tafweez ke qael Mushrik hain."
(Shaikh Sadooq ne Uyoonul Akhbar al Raza (page 124 , kazafi al ahtajaj page 264 )

           ♦ _*ALLAH KE HAATH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (725)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ يَدُ اللَّهِ مَغْلُولَةٌ ۚ غُلَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَلُعِنُوا بِمَا قَالُوا ۘ بَلْ يَدَاهُ مَبْسُوطَتَانِ يُنْفِقُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ.....*

_*"Yahoodi kahte hain ke Allah ke Haath bandhe hue hain. Bandhe gaye khud unke haath aur unki guftgu ki wajah se un par Laanat ki gayi hai. Allah ke Haath to Kushaadah hain, Woh jis tarah chahta hai kharch karta hai......*"_
(Surah Maeda: 64)

📚📖 👊🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat har juziyat ka tazkara jari hai. Sawal hota hai kiya Allah jism rakhta hai? Is Ayat mein Allah ke Haath ka zikr hai. Allah ne ye hamse hamari zuban baat ki hai aur ye muhavre ke taur par istemal hua hai. Allah ke Haath yani Uski Qudrat. Chunke Allah Haath nahi rakhta Woh kisi bhi bande ko Apna Haath bana sakta hai. Isliye Hazrat Ali (as) ko Allah ki taraf se Yadullah, Wajhullah, Noorullah, Janbullah, Ainullah, Uznullah nawaza gaya hai. Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
👉🏻
Raavi Abdullah bin Qais ne Imam Ali Raza (as) se sawal kiya: _"Kiya Allah ke bhi hamari tarah se do haath hain?"_
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Agar aisa hota to woh Makhlooq (creature) hota."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👉🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Kuchh log Khuda ke liyem tangon (Legs) aur Qadamon (Foots) ka Aqeeda rakhte hain aur woh kahte hain ke Baitul Muqaddas ki chattan par Allah ne apna paon (Foot) rakh the aur yahin se woh Aasmaan ki taraf buland hua tha. Aur kuchh log Khuda ke liye haath (Hands) aur ungliyon (Fingers) ka Aqeeda rakhte hain aur woh ye kahte hain ke Nabi e Akram (saww) ne farmaya the ke mein apne dil par Khuda ki Ungliyon ki thandak mahsoos ki thi. _"Jabke Khuda ki Shaan isse kahin buland o bala hai jo woh bayan kar rahe hain. Aur Khuda ki Shaan ye hai ke Woh kisi ke Mushabeh (Similar) nahi hai. Aur Uska Wasf (Attributes) bayan nahi kiya ja sakta aur Use Khayaal o Wahm (Imagination & thoughts) ke dayre mein nahi laya ja sakta. Uski Shaan Buland hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👉🏻
Ibne Athir ulema e Ahle Sunnat ki motabar Kitabon se likhta hai ke ek bar Tawaf ke darmiyan ek Aadmi ek aurat par ghalat nigah kiye hue tha. Hazrat Ali (as) ki nazr us par padi to usko ek thappad raseed kar diya. Usne Umar se shikayat ki. Umar ne usse kaha: _"Allah ki Aankhon mein se ek Aankh ne tumko sahi mein mara."_
Ibne Athir ka kahna hai iska matlab ye hua ke woh Allah ke muntakhab shuda bande the, Makhlooqat ke liye Rehmat o Maghfirat, aur Paak Qudrat e Ilahi the. Woh Janbu Allah, Makhlooqat mein sab se qareeb the.

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Makhsoos Aankh ki Ma'arefat ata farma.
--------------------------------------------
*For more details on thi Topic click on the link and read:*
https://www.al-islam.org/hayat-al-qulub-vol3-allamah-muhammad-baqir-al-majlisi/part-39-side-allah-face-allah-and-hands-allah
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👊🏻
Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Mein Khuda ka woh Haath hun jo bandon par Maghfirat o Rehmat ke liye khula hua hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👊🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne hame paida kiya aur Usne hame achchhi takhleeq se nawaza aur Usne hamari tasveer kashi ki aur hamari behtareen Tasveer Kashi ki. Usne hame apne bandon mein Apni Aankh banaya aur Apni Makhlooq mein Apni Natiq Zuban banaya aur Apne bandon par Rehmat o Maghfirat ke liye Kushaadah Haath banaya."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

                  ♦ _*ASL DEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (726)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ أَنَّ أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ آمَنُوا وَاتَّقَوْا لَكَفَّرْنَا عَنْهُمْ سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ وَلَأَدْخَلْنَاهُمْ جَنَّاتِ النَّعِيمِ*

_"Agar Ahle Kitab Imaan le aate aur Taqwa ikhtiyar karte to Ham unki buraiyan unse door kar dete aur unko Jannatun Naeem mein dakhil karte."_
(Surah Maeda: 65)

📚📖 🚩
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Yahan Ahle Kitab se mukhatib karke Allah ek General Usool bata raha hai. Yaani ek Insaan ke liye sab se pahle zaroori hai ke Asl Deen e Islam par Imaan laye aur Taqwa ikhtiyar kare to Allah usko Jannatun Naeem ki basharat de raha hai. Guzishta Anbiya ka Deen bhi yahi Islam tha lekin unke jaane ke baad Deen mein tahreef kar di gayi. In Tahreefon ko hata kar hamare Nabi ne Asli Deen e Islam pesh kiya. Lekin jaise ke hota chala aya tha, baad e rehlate Rasool (saww) phir wohi hua. Islam ke itne tukde hue ke Asl Islam ko pahchanna mushkil ho gaya. Isliye Hamare Akheri Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Akhiri Hajj ke mauqe Ailan e Vilayat e Ali (as) bata diya ke Asl Islam kahan se milega. Lekin Musalman 73 firqo mein bat gaya.
🚩
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Hazrat Moosa (as) ki Ummat ke 71 giroh hue the. Un mein se ek giroh Jannat mein jayega aur 70 Giroh Dozakh mein jayenge aur Hazrat Esa (as) ki Ummat ke 72 Giroh hue the jin mein ek Giroh Jannat mein jayega aur 71 Giroh Dozakh mein jayenge aur anqareeb meri Ummat ke 73 Giroh ban jayege jin mein se ek Giroh Jannat aur 72 Giroh Dozakh mein jayenge."_
Rasoole Khuda (saww) se poochha gaya ke Dozakh mein jaane wale kaun honge?
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Woh Jamaten hongi, woh Jamaten hongi, woh Jamaten hongi."_
Hazrat Ali (as) jab ye hadis bayan karte to ye Ayat ki tilawat karte (5:65) aur kahte ke _"Haq ki Hidayat deni wali Ummat, Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ki Ummat hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame us Giroh mein rakhna jahan Haq hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
*Hamare Aakhri Nabi, Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saws) ne farmaya:*

_*"Tamam aulad e Adam (as) ko chhod dena, magar Ali (as) ka saath na chhodna kyon ke Ali (as) tum logon ko gumrah nahin hone denge."*_
(Kanz al ummal, page 7)

                 ♦ _*NE'MAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (727)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ أَنَّهُمْ أَقَامُوا التَّوْرَاةَ وَالْإِنْجِيلَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْهِمْ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ لَأَكَلُوا مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ وَمِنْ تَحْتِ أَرْجُلِهِمْ ۚ مِنْهُمْ أُمَّةٌ مُقْتَصِدَةٌ ۖ وَكَثِيرٌ مِنْهُمْ سَاءَ مَا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Kaash unhone Torah aur Injeel aur doosri Kitabon ko qaem kiya hota, jo unke Rab ki taraf se unke paas bheji gaye thi, aisa karte to unke liye upar se Rizq barasta aur neeche se ubalta agarche in mein kuchh log raast roo bhi hain lekin unki aksariyat sakht bad amal hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 66)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke guzishta Ayat mein bataya Yahoodi hon, ya Munafeqeen unhone Asl Deen ko chhod diya. Iska natija ye hua ke woh Allah ki Ne'maton se mehroom ho gaye. Lekin jo Samajhdar the woh Raahe Raast par aa gaye.
Yahan is baat par zor diya gaya hai ke agar Sahi Deen par amal hota, uske qawaneen o Ahkam par sahi taur amal hota to Allah ki Rahmaton ki barish hoti, paidawar mein barkaten hotin.
Ek Nuqta ye bhi hai ke jisne Ahle Bait (as) ka daman chhod diya woh Allah ki sabhi Ne'maton se Mehroom ho jata hai. Har Musalman Darood ya Salwat bhejta hai to yehi kahta hai "Muhammad wa Ale Muhammad (as) par Rehmat nazil farma." Is fiqre se saaf zahir hai ke jo Ne'maton ki barsat ham par hogi to woh unhi ke tufail mein hogi, direct ham par ek bhi Ne'mat nazil nahi hogi. Ek zinda misal aaj bhi baqi hai Hazrat Ismael ki pao tale jo chashma jari hua tha aaj tak jari hai. (Abe Zam Zam).

Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim mein hai
*مِنْهُمْ أُمَّةٌ مُقْتَصِدَةٌ ۖ*
se Yahoodiyon ke woh afraad mard hain jinhone Islam qubool kiya tha, Allah ne unhe "Etedal pasand (Moderates) Ummat" ka laqab diya hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Ahle Bait (as) ke naqshe qadam par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma taake woh ham se Raazi rahen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
*Hamare Aakhri Nabi Hazrat Mohammed Mustufa (sawa) ne Farmaya:*

_*"(Ya Ali) Tum mere tarike pe qayam rahoge. Aur meri sunnat par qatl kiye jaaoge. Joh tumse mohabbat karta hai woh mujhse mohabbat karta hai. Aur joh tumse bugz rakhta hai woh mujhse bugz rakhta hai."*_

(Kanzul Ummal, Vol 6, Hadees No. 31562.)
