                  ♦ _*GHADEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (728)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الرَّسُولُ بَلِّغْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۖ وَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلْ فَمَا بَلَّغْتَ رِسَالَتَهُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَعْصِمُكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْكَافِرِينَ*

_*"Aye Rasool (saww)! Tumhare Rab ki taraf se jo kuchh nazil kiya gaya hai woh logon tak pahuncha do. Aur agar tumne aisa na kiya to uski Risaalat ki Tableegh na ki. Allah tumko logon ke shar se bachayega. Yaqeenan Allah Kafiron ko hidayat nahi karta."*_
(Surah Maeda: 67)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye maslahet e Khuda wandi hai ke Ghadeer ke mauqe par Ayaat ki series mein yehi Ayat ayi.
Ayat ko ghaur se padhe aur ghaur karen ke Khuda ka Rasool (saww) se itne sakht lahje mein hukm dena Allah ke is Message ki ahmiyat bata raha hai, yahi ye Paigham e Ilahi aisa Paigham hai, agar logon tak nahi pahunchaya to Rasoole Akram (saww) ki Risaalat bhi ja sakti hai.
Ab Maslah ye tha ke kahi ye Message sunkar log bigad na jayen aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne khatra bhi mehsoos kiya. Lekin Allah is Ayat mein is baat ki bhi surety de raha hai ke Woh Rasool (saww) ko har shar se bachayega.
🍁
Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):
_"Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (saww) farmate the ke us waqt meine dil hi dil mein apne Khuda se arz kiya ke Bare Ilaha! Meri Ummat taza Musalman hui hai aur jab meine unhe apne chacha ke farzand ke mutalliq ye khabar di to log mukhtalif qism ki chemigoiyyan karenge. Iske baad Allah ki taraf se mujh par ye takeedi hukm nazil kiya ke agar meine is Masleh ki Tableegh na ki to Khuda mujhe Azaab dega aur ya Ayat nazil hui (5:67)."_
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🍁
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Allah ne ye Ayat nazil farmayi (5:55) (Ruku mein Zakat), and (3:59) (Ayat Oolil Amr), lekin logon ko ye nahi pata chal saka ke ke Ruku mein Zakat dene wala aur Oolil Amr kaun hai? Jab Anhazrat (saww) ko ye Hukm mila to Aapko seene mein tangi ka ehsaas hua aur Aapko andesha hua ke kahin log Deen se hi munharif (bhatak) na ho jayen aur Aap (saww) ki takzeeb na karen (jhutlayen). Chunanche Aap (saww) se Khuda ne rabta kiya aur Aap par ye Ayat nazil farmayi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜 *Khutba e Ghadeer:*
Hamare Akheri Rasool (saww) ne apni Akheri Hajj ke baad Ghadeer ke maidan mein ye Khutba diya:

_"Logon! Meri baten achchhi tarah se suno aur unhe khoob samjho kiyonki mein nahi samajhta ke ainda saal mein tum logon se mil sakunga."_
_"Logon! Kiya tum jaante ho ke kaun sa Din zyada hurmat wala hai? (Logon ne kaha aaj ka Din). Ye batao ke kaunsa Mahina zyada hurmat wala hai? (Logon ne kaha yahi Mahina). Kaunsa Shaher zyada Hurmat wala hai? (Logo ne kaha ye Shaher)"_
_"Tumhare Khoon, tumhare Maal aur tumhari Namoos tum par usi tarah se Haram hai jaisa ye Din, ye Mahina, ye Shaher Haram hai. Tumko Khuda ke saamne hazir hona hai. Woh tumse tumhare Aamaal ke mutalliq poochhega. Kiya meine tum tak Khuda ka Paigham diya hai? (Logon ne kaha ji haan.)"_
Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Khudaya Gawah rahna."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

(Khutba to be Cont'd....)

                  ♦ _*GHADEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (728) (Cont'd ......)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الرَّسُولُ بَلِّغْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۖ وَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلْ فَمَا بَلَّغْتَ رِسَالَتَهُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَعْصِمُكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْكَافِرِينَ*

_*"Aye Rasool (saww)! Tumhare Rab ki taraf se jo kuchh nazil kiya gaya hai woh logon tak pahuncha do. Aur agar tumne aisa na kiya to uski Risaalat ki Tableegh na ki. Allah tumko logon ke shar se bachayega. Yaqeenan Allah Kafiron ko hidayat nahi karta."*_
(Surah Maeda: 67)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Akheri Hajj kiya aur farigh hone ke baad Anhazrat (saww) aur baqi Hajiyon ke sath wapas Medina ki taraf rawana hue ke.
🕋 🍁
Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):
"Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Johfah se 3 Mile pahle Ghadeer e Khum ke maqam par pahunche to Jibrael e Ameen (as) Aap (saww) par nazil hue. Us waqt Din ke 5 ghante guzar chuke the unhone ye Ayat padhi: (5:67). Us waqt Aap ke qafle ke afraad maqam e Johfah pahunch chuke the. Unhe wapas bulaya gaya aur jo peechhe the, unka intezar kiya gaya. Iske baad Aap (saww) ne *الصلاة جامعة* (Salatul Jame) ki nida karai aur Aap (saww) ne farmaya ke Khuda ne mujhe ek Paigham pahunchane ka Hukm diya hai aur uske sath ye takeed ki hai ke agar meine is Paigham Ko na pahunchaya to meri tamam Tableegh e Risalat bekar ho jayegi aur iske sath Khuda ne mujh se ye wada bhi kiya hai ke Woh mujhe logon ke shar se mehfooz rakhega....."
(Ehtejaaj e Tabarasi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜 *Khutba e Ghadeer:*
Hamare Akheri Rasool (saww) ne apni Akheri Hajj ke baad Ghadeer ke maidan mein ye Khutba diya:

(Cont'd.....)
_"Zamana Jahiliyyat ke tamam ehteram aur bida'at aur Khoon o Maal wo mere qadmon ke niche hai. kisi ko kisi par bartari nahi hai siwai Taqwa ke. Logon! Kiya meine tum tak paigham pahuncha diya hai?"_
(Logon ne kaha ji haan). Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Khudaya! Gawah rahna."_
Phir Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Zamane Jahiliyyat ka har Sood ma'af hai aur sab se pahle mein Abbas bin Abdul  Muttalib ka Sood ma'af karta hun. Zamana Jahiliyyat ke tamam Khoon ma'af hain. Sab se pahle Rabia ka Khoon ma'af karta hun. Logo! Kiya meine Paigham pahuncha diya?"_
(Logon ne kaha: Ji haan)
Aap (saww): _"Khudaya! Gawah rahna!"_
Phir Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Shaitan tumhari sar zameen mein apni Ibadat kiye jaane se mayus ho chuka hai. Ab woh un Aamaal par bhi raazi hai jinhen tum mamooli noiyyat ke gunah samajh kar sar anjam dete ho. Yad rakho! Jab iski ita'at ki jaati hai to woh dar asl uski Ibaadat shumar hoti hai."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

(Khutba to be Cont'd....)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (728) (Cont'd ......)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الرَّسُولُ بَلِّغْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۖ وَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلْ فَمَا بَلَّغْتَ رِسَالَتَهُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَعْصِمُكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْكَافِرِينَ*

_*"Aye Rasool (saww)! Tumhare Rab ki taraf se jo kuchh nazil kiya gaya hai woh logon tak pahuncha do. Aur agar tumne aisa na kiya to uski Risaalat ki Tableegh na ki. Allah tumko logon ke shar se bachayega. Yaqeenan Allah Kafiron ko hidayat nahi karta."*_
(Surah Maeda: 67)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasool e khuda (saww) ka ye Akheri Hajj tha. Paighambar Akram (saww) ke sath logon ki ta'daad kuchh ne 90 hazaar, kuchh ne1,14000, to kuchh ne 1,20,000 ya 1,24,000 likhi hai. Sirf Medina ke hi nahi balke sabhi jagah ke log the. Jaisa ke pahle bataya Aap (saww) Khuda ke Hukm se Ghadeer e Khum ke maidan mein ruk gaye. Tez dhoop thi, na koi saya tha, roohaniyat urooj par thi, tapti hui zameen par logon ko baithaya gaya. Zawal ka waqt tha. Woh kanton bhari zameen ko Sahaba se saaf karaya gaya.
Ghadeer e Khum Hajiyon ke liye ek Junction tha jahan se sab raste alag alag hote the. Ab tak jo sab sath-sath chal rahe the juda ho jate. Jumerat (Thursday) ka Din tha, 10th AH. Azaan hui, Zuhr ki Namaz ba Jamat hui. Fiza garam thi, itni garam ke kuchh ne majbooran apne aba' ka kuchh hissa apne paon ke niche daba rakha tha aur baqi sar par. Is bayaban mein garm ret paon ko jala Rahi thi.
Namaz e Zuhr ke baad Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne sab ko wohi baithe rahne ko kaha taake ye Important Message logon tak pahunchaya ja sake. Oont ke kajawon ka Mimbar banaya gaya. Jo aaj Masjidon mein Mimbar nazar aate hain iski shurua'at us hi Din hui. Ye bhi ek Ghadeer ki Yadgaar hai.
Phir Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Khutba shuru kiya.
Agar Is surat e haal mein agar kisi ko kuchh sunaya jaye to woh kabhi nahi bhoolega. Kam se kam waqea to yaad rahega. Rasool e Akram (saww) is Message ko Hajj ke dauran bhi de sakte the. Ya phir Ghadeer mein koi Tent ya sae ka intezaam karwa sakte the. Lekin aisa na karna aur Allah ka ye sakht Hukm logon ko sakht taur par pahuchana is Paigham ki ahmiyat bata raha hai.

Bare Ilaha hame us taraf rakh jahan Allah ka Wali rahe.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜 *Khutba e Ghadeer:*
Hamare Akheri Rasool (saww) ne apni Akheri Hajj ke baad Ghadeer ke maidan mein ye Khutba diya:

(Cont'd.....)
_"Logo! Yad rakho! Musalman Musalman ka haqeeqi bhai hai. Kisi bhi Musalman ke liye doosre Musalman ka khoon bahana Halaal nahi hai aur kisi Musalman ke liye doosre Musalman ka Maal Halaal nahi hai. Haan agar koi apni raza wa khwahish se kisi ko kuchh Maal de de to aur baat hai. Aur Khuda ki taraf se mujhe ye Hukm mila hai ke mein logon se jang karun yahan tak ke woh 'La Ilaha illallah' ka iqraar karen aur jab woh 'La Ilaha illallah' kah den to meri taraf se unka Khoon aur unka Maal mehfooz hai siwai Haq ke. Unka hisaab Allah ke zimme hai."_
_"Logo! Kiya meine Paigham pahuncha diya?"_
(Logon ne kaha: Ji haan)
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Khudaya! Gawah Rehna!"_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

(Khutba to be Cont'd....)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (729) (Cont'd ......)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الرَّسُولُ بَلِّغْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۖ وَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلْ فَمَا بَلَّغْتَ رِسَالَتَهُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَعْصِمُكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْكَافِرِينَ*

_*"Aye Rasool (saww)! Tumhare Rab ki taraf se jo kuchh nazil kiya gaya hai woh logon tak pahuncha do. Aur agar tumne aisa na kiya to uski Risaalat ki Tableegh na ki. Allah tumko logon ke shar se bachayega. Yaqeenan Allah Kafiron ko hidayat nahi karta."*_
(Surah Maeda: 67)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Akhirkar Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Allah ke Hukm ki ta'meel ki. Aur Allah ye Important Hukm Vilayat e Ali (as) tha.
Rasool e Akram (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ka haath pakda aur unhe itna buland kiya ke dono ki baghlon ke niche ki safedi nazar aane lagi aur sab logon ne unhe dekh kar pahchan liya ke ye Islam ka wohi sipeh salar hai jisne kabhi shikast ka moo nahi dekha.
Phir Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
*ایها الناس من اولی الناس بالمؤمنین من انفسهم.*
_"Aye Logo! Batao woh Kaun hai jo tamam logon ki nisbat Mo'meneen par khud unse zyada Awwaliyat rakhta hai?"_
Sab hazerin ne ba yek awaz jawab diya:
_"Khuda aur Uska Paighambar behtar jaante hain."_
Paighambar Akram (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Khuda mera Maula aur Rehbar hai, aur mein Mo'meneen ka Maula aur Rehbar hun aur unke upar unki nisbat khud unse zyada Haq rakhta hun."_
Phir farmaya:
*فمن کنت مولاه فعلی مولاه.*
_*"Jis jis ka mein Maula hun Ali (as) bhi us us ka Maula aur Rehbar hain."*_
Paighambar (saww) ne is jumle ko 3 bar repeat kiya aur kuchh Rivayaat ke mutabiq 4 martaba aur iske baad Dua ki.
*اللهم وال من والاه و عاد من عاداه و أحب من أحبه و إبغض من أبغضه و إنصر من نصر و إخذل من خذله و إدر الحق معه حيث دار.*
_*"Bare Ilaha jo unko dost  rakhe Tu usko dost rakh aur jo unse Dushmani kare Tu usse Dushmani rakh. Jo unse Muhabbat kare Tu usse Muhabbat kar aur unse bughz rakhe Tu usse Bughz rakh. Jo unki madad kare Tu uski madad kar, jo unko chhod de Tu use chhod de aur Haq ko udhar pher jidhar woh rukh kare."*_
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜 *Khutba e Ghadeer:*
Hamare Akheri Rasool (saww) ne apni Akheri Hajj ke baad Ghadeer ke maidan mein ye Khutba diya:

(Cont'd.....)
_"Logon! Meri baat yaad rakho mere baad tum isse nafa hasil karoge use achhi tarah samjho fayde mein rahoge. Khabardar! Mere baad Kafir na ho jana aur Duniya ke liye Talwar se ek doosre ko gardane na marne lag jana. Agar tum ne Aisa Kiya aur tum zaroor aisa karoge, tum mujhe Jibrael o Mikaeel ke darmiyan Malaika ke ek giroh mein paoge. Khuda ne chaha to mein Talwar le kar tumhare chehron par marunga."_
(Phir Aap (saww) kuchh der tak khamosh rahe aur phir farmaya:
_"Mein marunga ya Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) marenge."_
_*"Logon! Mein tum mein do Amr chhor kar ja raha hun. Agar tumne inka daman tham liya to tum hargiz gumrah nahi honge aur woh hain Allah ki Kitab aur Meri Itrat Ahle Bait (as). Lateef o Khabeer Khuda ne mujhe khabar di hai ke woh ek doosre se juda na honge yahan tak ke woh mere paas Hauze Kausar par warid honge. Jisne in dono ka daman thama to usne Nijaat payi aur jisne unki Mukhalifat ki to woh halaat hua.*"_
_"Logon! Kiya meine Paigham pahucha diya hai?"_
(Logon ne kaha: Ji haan)
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Khudaya! Gawah rahna."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

(Khutba to be Cont'd....)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (731) (Cont'd ......)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*سَأَلَ سَائِلٌ بِعَذَابٍ وَاقِعٍ * لِلْكَافِرِينَ لَيْسَ لَهُ دَافِعٌ * مِنَ اللَّهِ ذِي الْمَعَارِجِ*

_*"Mangne wale ne Azaab manga, jo ke waqae mein waqe hoga, Kafiron ke liye jise koi hata nahi sakta, Us Khuda ki taraf se jo Urooj ke Zeeno ka Malik hai."*_
(Surah Ma'arij: 1 - 3)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jab Ghadeere Khum mein Ailan e Vilayat e Ali (as) ho gaya to jis baat ka Rasool e Akram (saww) ko andesha tha wohi hua. Ikhtilaf khul kar saamne aa gaya. Yani Khilafat ka Ikhtilaf Rasool (saww) ke saamne se shuru ho gaya tha. Isiliye Allah ne Rasool (saww) ki safety ki guarantee li thi. Khair Rasoole Akram (saww) ne Ailan kar diya, Ayah e Takmeel e Deen bhi nazil ho gayi. To hazereen mein kuchh ne sawal kiya ke kiya ye Hukm Allah ki taraf se tha? Un mein se ek Haris bin Noman tha.

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Qasam hai us Khuda ki jiske siwa aur koi Khuda nahi, ye baat Khuda ki taraf se hai."_
Noman ne moo pher liya aur ye kahta jata tha:
_"Khuda wanda! Agar ye baat Haq hai aur Teri taraf se hai to Aasmaan se ham par Patthar barsa."_
Usi waqt ek patthar Aasmaan se uske sar par gira aur use mar dala, usi mauqe par ya Ayat (Ma'arij: 1-3) nazil hui.
(Rivayat Imam Sadiq (as): Majmaul Bayan Vol 10, P-352), Raavi Abul Qasim Haskani)
Is waqae se Ghadeer ke Ailan ki Haqeeqat sabit hoti hai. Hamne Qur'an ki 3 Ayaten pesh ki jo Ghadeer se mutalliq hain.

Bare Ilaha hame us taraf rakhna jahan Ali (as) rahen aur jahan Ali (as) wahin Haq hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜 *Khutba e Ghadeer:*
Hamare Akheri Rasool (saww) ne apni Akheri Hajj ke baad Ghadeer ke maidan mein ye Khutba diya:

(Cont'd.....)
Hazrat Umar ne arz kiya: Kiya ye Hukm e Khuda aur uske Rasool (saww) ki taraf se tha?
Aanhazrat (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Ji haan, Khuda aur uske Rasool (saww) ki taraf se ye Ailan kiya jata hai ke Ali (as) Ahle Imaan ke Ameer aur Mutaqiyon ke Imam aur Qayamat ke Din jin ke chehre Roshan honge, unke Rehbar hai. Allah Qayamat ke Roz Siraat par bithaiga. Woh apne doston ko Jannat aur apne Dushmanon ko Dozakh mein dakhil karega."_
Woh log jo baad mein munharif ho gaye the unhone ek doosre se kaha: Muhammad (saww) ne Masjid mein jo kuchh kaha tha woh tumhe maloom hai aur aaj jo kuchh unhone kaha hai woh bhi tumhari saamne hai aur jab ye Medina jayenge to hamko Ali (as) ki Bayat e Imamat ka hukm dega.
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (733)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لَسْتُمْ عَلَىٰ شَيْءٍ حَتَّىٰ تُقِيمُوا التَّوْرَاةَ وَالْإِنْجِيلَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكُمْ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ ۗ وَلَيَزِيدَنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ طُغْيَانًا وَكُفْرًا ۖ فَلَا تَأْسَ عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الْكَافِرِينَ*

_"Aap kah den ke aye Ahle Kitab! Tumhari kuchh bhi haqeeqat nahi hai jab tak Taurat o Injeel aur un doosri Kitabon ko qaem na karo jo tumhare Rab ki taraf se tumhari taraf nazil ki gayi hain aur jo Farman Aap (saww) ki taraf se utara gaya hai woh yaqeenan un mein se aksar ki sarkashi aur inkaar ko aur zyada badha dega. Aap Kafir logon ke haal par kuchh bhi taras na khayen."_
(Surah Maeda: 68)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ghadeer ke Maidan mein Vilayat-e-Ali (as) ka Ailan ke Allah ne Ayat nazil karke Takmeel e Deen ka Ailan kiya aur Deen e Islam se Raazi hua. Jabke Deen e Islam to Hazrat Adam ke zamane se hai aur har Rasool wa Anbiya ne Deen e Islam ki hi Tableegh ki, lekin logon ne kisi Aasmani Kitabon par amal nahi kiya asl Deen se munharif ho gaye. Munharif Ahle Kitab yehi sochte rahe ke ham apni Deen par qaem hain lekin unki ye soch Allah ne is ayat mein ghalat sabit ki. Agar woh sahi Deen par amal karte hote to baad na koi nayi Kitab aati na agle Rasool ko apni nayi shariyat pesh karni padti. Allah ka Usool abad se Qayamat tak na badla hai na badlega, lekin log isko badal dete hain. Jab koi Hadi usi ko pesh karta hai to woh logon ko naya Deen lagta hai. Yahi haal Islam ke saath hua. Musalmano mein bhi Munafeqeen Rasool ke hi zamane mein paida hue aur unhone shararat karna shuru ki. Isliye Ghadeer ke jo Ailan hua wahan Usi Original Islam ki tajdeed hui. Is liye Allah is Islam se Raazi hua aur apni Ne'maten tamam kardi.

Bare Ilaha hame Allah ki Kitab ka Pairokar bana kiyonki yehi Ghadeeri Islam hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚
Imam Sadiq (as):
_*"Jis tarah Ahle Kitab Aasmani Kitabon ko qaem na karen to unki koi hasiyat nahi hai. Usi tarah Ahle Islam agar Vilayat-e-Ali (as) ka Aqeeda na rakhen to unki bhi koi hasiyat nahi hai."*_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (734)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَالَّذِينَ هَادُوا وَالصَّابِئُونَ وَالنَّصَارَىٰ مَنْ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ وَعَمِلَ صَالِحًا فَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ*

_"Beshak woh log jo Imaan laye aur woh jinhone Yahoodiyat Ikhtiyar ki, Saabi aur Nasara un mein se jo bhi Allah aur Roze Akhirat par Imaan layega aur nek amal karega to un par na to koi khauf hoga aur na hi woh afsos karenge."_
(Surah Maeda: 69)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke zel is baat ka zikr hua ke guzishta Anbiya ka Deen bhi yehi Islam tha.
Ye Ayat aur doosri similar Ayat Qur'an mein 3 jagah ayi hai. (Baqarah:62, Hajj:17, Maeda:69)
Is mein teen Mazahib ka zikr hai, Jews, Christians aur Sabians. Sabians means Hazrat Yahya (as), Hazrat Nooh (as) aur Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke pairokar. Sabians kaun hain is link mein detail hai.
( *Sabians:*
https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sabians )
In mein se kafi logon ne Islam qubool kar liya tha, unka kahna tha ke kiya unke dada pardada (purwaj) jo unke mutabiq apne Deen par amal karte the, Ibadat karte the, wo sab bekar ho gayi. To Allah Ta'ala ne is Ayat mein Usool bataya hai: Agar woh Khuda aur Akhirat par Imaan rakhte the aur Nek Aamaal karte the unko Ajr milega. Yani us zamane mein Jews, Christians, Sabians mein bhi aise log the jo asl Deen par amal karte the, jab Islam ka aghaz nahi hua tha. Unko unke mutabiq Ajr milega.
Do tarah ke log hote hain ek apne ghalat Aqeede par hatdharmi dikhate hain. Doosre woh log jinhe koi jankari nahi hoti aur haq ki talash mein justujo karte hain. Pahle wale log apni wohi manzil par baithe rahte hain jabke doosre talaash karte karte Haq ko pa lete hain. Is Ayat mein Allah is doosre giroh ki baat kar raha hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Haq par chalne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Har maulood (paida hone wala bachcha) Fitrat (Tauheed / Islam) par hi paida hota hai aur us waqt tak uspar baaqi rehta hai jab tak ke uski zabaan bolne nahi lag jaati. Jab bolne lag jaati hai to phir uske waaledain use Yahudi, Nasara ya Majoosi bana dete hain."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p190)
🚩
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Vilayat e Ali (as) ka itteba (follow / paalan) karna aur unki Vilayat ko tasleem karna tumhare umoor (affairs) ko pareshaan na hone dega, adl o insaaf ko tumse qaaem rakhega aur aakhir tumko Jannat mein pahu’ncha dega."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p81)
🚩
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek Neki ke badle Allah 10 Nekiyaa'n deta hai, lekin Neki ke liye Vilayat e Ali (as) zaroori Hai. Jo shakhs Aqeeda e Vilayat rakh kar Neki kare to use har Neki ke badle kam az kam 10 Nekiyo'n ka ajr milta hai. Agar aqeeda e Vilayat ke bagair koi shakhs Neki karta hai to uski Nekiyo'n ki wajah se dunyavi takleef khatm kar di jaati hai lekin Akherat mein uska koi hissa nahi hota."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p313)

_*SHAHADAT TIFLANE MUSLIM BIN AQEEL (as) (MOHD & IBRAHIM)*_

             ♦ _*AHD O PAIMAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (735)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ وَأَرْسَلْنَا إِلَيْهِمْ رُسُلًا ۖ كُلَّمَا جَاءَهُمْ رَسُولٌ بِمَا لَا تَهْوَىٰ أَنْفُسُهُمْ فَرِيقًا كَذَّبُوا وَفَرِيقًا يَقْتُلُونَ*

_"Hamne Bani Israel se pukhta Ahd liya aur Hamne unki taraf bahut se Rasool bheje magar jab bhi koi Rasool unke paas unki khwaheshat e Nafs (Self Desire) ke khilaf koi Taa'leemat le kar aaya to kisi ko un logon ne ya to jhutlaya ya kisi ko qatl karne lage."_
(Surah Maeda: 70)

📚📖 🤝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat (Sura Baqarah:93) mein bhi Ahd ke same fiqre aye hain.
Hamne 8 July 2017 ke post mein Ayat 5:12 (Sura Maeda, Ayat 12) mein zikr hua tha ke Allah ne Bani Israel se Ahd liya gaya aur unke darmiyan 12 Naqeeb muayyan kiye. Aur ye Ahd liya tha ke woh 12 ki itteba' karenge. Lekin woh Paighambaron ke jaane ke baad wapas bhatak gaye.
Aur Ayat (5:1) mein bhi ye tambi ki ke apne Ahd ko poora karen. Jahan hamne Nahjul Balagha ko quote kiya tha ke _"Duniya bhar ke logon mein tamam tar ikhtalefat ke bawajood Eifae Ahd ki tarah kisi aur amr par ittefaq nahi hai."_
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs apne Ahd o Paiman ka wafadar nahi uska koi Deen nahi."_
(Bihar, Vol 16, P-144)
Bani Israel par Azaab nazil hua isi Ahd ko todne par. (5:24-26)
Pas sare logon ne is Duniya mein aane se pahle Aalam e Zar mein bhi Allah se Ahd o Paiman liya gaya tha. Lekin   insaan jab is Duniya mein aaya to us Ahd ko bhool gaya aur sarkashi karne laga.
Ghadeer mein bhi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne apne Akhiri Hajj ke mauqe par sabhi Musalmano wa Ashaab se Hazrat Ali (as) ki Vilayat par Ahd liya tha aur apne 12 Nuquba ka Ailan kiya. Lekin jaisa ke guzishta  Anbiya ke saath hua ya to jhutlaya ya qatl kiya. Hazrat Khatamul Mursalin (saww) ke is Duniya ke jaane ke baad bhi wohi hua. Paighambar e Islam (saww) ne kaha tha kuchh aur Ummat ne kiya kuchh aur. Poore halaat tarikh (Islamic History) mein darj hain refer karen.
Aaj hamne pichhle kuchh post ka khulasa bayan kiya, in Aayaat ki tafseel pahle aa chuki hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Tere is Ahd o Paiman par qaim rahne mein madad kar.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤝
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Allah ne apne Rasool mab'oos kiye aur lagatar Anbiya bheje *taake un se Fitrat ke Ahd o Paiman poore karayen. Uski bhooli hui Ne'maten yaad dilayen. Paigham e Rabbani pahunch kar Hujjat tamam karen, Aql ke dafinon ko ubharen aur unhe qudrat ko Nishaniyan dikhayen.* Ye saron par buland baam Aasmaan, unke niche bichha hua farsh e Zameen, zinda rakhne wala samaane maeeshat (Financial assets), Fana kar dene wali ujlen, boodha kar dene wali bimariyan, pai dar pai aane wale haadse, Allah apni Makhlooq ko baghair kisi irsal kardah Paighambar ya Aasmaani Kitab ya Daleel e qata'ee ya tareeqe roshan ke baghair yun hi nahi chhoda. Aise Rasool jinhe ta'daad ki kami aur jhutlane walon ki kasrat darmandah wa aajiz nahi karti thi. Un mein koi sabiq tha jis mein aane wale ka naam o nishan bataya. Koi baad mein aya jise pahla pahchanwa chuka tha. Isi tarah muddaten guzar gayin. Zamane beet gaye. Baap dadaon ki jagah unki Auladen bas gayin yahan tak ke Allah ne eefa e Ahd (fulfilment of Covenant) aur Itmam e Hujjat ke liye Muhammad (saww) ko mab'oos kiya."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
🤝
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Agar hamare Shia, Allah unko Uski ita'at ki tafeeq de, *ek dil hokar unke Ahdo  Paiman ko poora karte to hamari mulaqat mein takheer nahi hoti,* aur jald hi hamari ziyarat se sharaf yab hote, Haq ki Ma'arefat ke sath aur hamari huqooq ki tasdeeq karte hue."_
(Al Ehtejaaj, Vol 2, P-602)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                  ♦ _*FITNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (737)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَحَسِبُوا أَلَّا تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ فَعَمُوا وَصَمُّوا ثُمَّ تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ ثُمَّ عَمُوا وَصَمُّوا كَثِيرٌ مِنْهُمْ ۚ وَاللَّهُ بَصِيرٌ بِمَا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Aur unhone ye samjha ke koi Fitna runuma na hoga isi liye woh andhe aur bahre ban gaye. Phir Allah ne unki Tauba qabool ki to un mein se aksar afraad andhe aur bahre ban gaye aur kuchh woh karte the Allah use dekh raha tha."_
(Surah Maeda: 71)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ayat (أَلَّا تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ) ka talluq wafate Rasool ke zamane se hai. (ثُمَّ تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ) ka talluq Hazrat Ali (as) ke zamana e Khilafat se hai. (ثُمَّ عَمُوا وَصَمُّوا) is ka talluq Roze Qayamat tak hai."_
(Roza-e-Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Abhi Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne Ghadeer mein sawa lakh ke majme Vilayat e Ali (as) kiya, sab ne suna aur dekha. Rasool e khuda (saww) ki jaise hi wafat hui sab ke sab andhe aur bahre ho gaye jiske natije mein Fitne shuru hue. Islamic History pahle Fitne ki shurua'at Saqifa se shuru hui. Phir doosra, teesra aur 4th Fitno ke number diye gaye hain. Detail ke liye is link par click karen:
https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fitna_(word)

Ghadeer mein jo Ailan hua usko bhoola diya gaya aur Ummat apne aap se Khilafat ke ikhtelaf mein pad gayi.
Rivayat ke baqaul jab teesri Khilafat ke baad Ummat ne kuchh zamane se sabaq liya aur Haq ke raaste par palte, pichhli teen gumrahiyon se Tauba ki, Allah ne unki tauba qabool karte hue unke upar Haq ko masallat kar ke ek aur mauqa diya. Lekin kuchh saal tak to Ummat ne Haq ko bardasht kiya lekin phir se woh andhe aur bahre ho gaye jiske natije mein Masjid mein halate Namaz mein Haq ka qatl hua. Jabke Allah ye sab dekh raha tha.
Ab Qur'an ke akheri fiqre Qayamat tak ke liye ho gaye. Yani jo Vilayat Ali (as) ke sath baqi rahega Kamyab hoga aur jisne isse moo moda woh ta Qayamat andha aur bahra hoga.
Jaisa ke hame bataya tha ke Ghadeer mein jabke Shaitan ka khwab chakna choor ho gaya tha lekin Shaitan ne apni nayi chal chali aur us mein wo kuchh had tak kamyab hua. Rivayat mulaheza farmayen.

Bare Ilaha hame us taraf rakhna jis taraf Haq ho, aur Shaitan chaalon se hame bachaye rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹👺💩
*“Ghadeer Me Shaitan Ki Sazesh ”*
Yaom-e-Ghadeer Jab Amirul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki Vilayat Ka Ailan hua to Shaitan ne kaha aaj ka Din Esa (as) ki Duniya mein aamad jaisa hai. Khuda ki qasam mein logon ko Ali (as) ke bare mein gumrah karunga. Us Waqt Ayat (Surah Saba:20) nazil hui,” aur un pe Iblees ne apne gumaan ko Sach kar dikhaya to Mo'meneen ke 1 giroh ko chhor ke sab ne is ki ite’ba kar li. Uske baad Shaitan ne kaha mein un kam ta'daad Mo'meneen ko tamam logo ke sath mulhaq kar dunga, us waqt ye Ayat nazil hui: _”Tu hargiz meri khaas bandon pe musallat nahi ho sakega.”_ Shaitan ne kaha meri shikast Shiyon ki wajah se hai mein unke liye gunahoon ko sajaonga ke woh Ghazab-e-Ilahi ka nishana banen. Maula Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya _"Shahed ke gird jis tarah Makhyian baithti hain is se ziyada Shaitan Mo'meneen ke gird mandlata hai. Lekin Mo'meneen us buland Muqam pe hotr hain unhen junbish tak nai hoti."_
(Iblees Nama Vol -2 P-165, 66)

             ♦ _*CHRISTIANITY*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (738)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ كَفَرَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْمَسِيحُ ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ ۖ وَقَالَ الْمَسِيحُ يَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ رَبِّي وَرَبَّكُمْ ۖ إِنَّهُ مَنْ يُشْرِكْ بِاللَّهِ فَقَدْ حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ الْجَنَّةَ وَمَأْوَاهُ النَّارُ ۖ وَمَا لِلظَّالِمِينَ مِنْ أَنْصَارٍ*

_"Yaqeenan un logon ne Kufr kiya jinone kaha ke Allah Maseeh Ibne Maryam hi hai halaanki Maseeh ne kaha tha: Aye Bani Israel! Allah ki Bandagi karo jo mera bhi Rab hai aur tumhara Rab bhi hai. Jis ne Allah ke sath kisi ko Shirk thahraya to Allah ne us par Jannat Haram kar di aur uska thikana Dozakh hai aur Zalimo ke liye koi madadgar nahi hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 72)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasoole Khuda (sa) se Christians ke sath kafi debates hui aur jab Christians nahi mane to akhir mein Mubahela hua. Jab sare daleelen khatm ho gayi to sirf Ale Muhammad (as) ke Noor ko dekh kar Christians bhag chhute aur Jizya dene par razi ho gaye. Sirf Ahle Bait (as) ki zaat wo hai jinse Dushman ghabrata hai. Phir se repeat karna mauzoo ki ahmiyat bata raha hai.
Ab tak Yahoodiyon ke inherafat ka zikr chal raha tha, ab agli kuchh Ayaton mein phir se Nasaara ke Aqaed wa unke inherafat  ka zikr hai. Kuchh Ayaten same topic par guzar chuki hain.
Is Ayat mein Allah ne is baat ki nafi ki hai (negets) ke Maseeh Khuda hain. Jabke Allah kahta hai ke Maseeh Allah ke bande hain.
Khud Christianity Musalmano ki tarah kai firqon mein bati hui hai. Is Ayat mein baqaul kuchh Mufasserin Christians ke ek sect Yaqoobia ke Aqeede ka izhaar kiya hai (Tabari, Majmaul Bayan, Qurtabi)  lekin Tafseer e Namoona ka kahna hai ke ye Laskania aur Nastooria ke bare mein hain jo Trinity ke qael hain. Detail of Sects ko is link mein dekhen:
(1) https://simple.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Christian_denominations_by_number_of_members
(2) http://www.religioustolerance.org/chr_deno.htm

Bare Ilaha unhe Raahe Haq par aane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"7 aadmiyo'n ka Azaab sab se zyada shadeed hoga: Qaabil, Namrood, Baani e Yahoodiyat (Founder of Jewism), Baani e Nasraniyat (Founder of Christianity), Firoun aur 2 aadmi is Ummat ke."_
(Khisaal, ch7)

            ♦ _*HAZRAT ESA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (739)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ كَفَرَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ ثَالِثُ ثَلَاثَةٍ ۘ وَمَا مِنْ إِلَٰهٍ إِلَّا إِلَٰهٌ وَاحِدٌ ۚ وَإِنْ لَمْ يَنْتَهُوا عَمَّا يَقُولُونَ لَيَمَسَّنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ*
(Surah Maeda: 73)

                 ♦ _*TRINITY*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (739)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ كَفَرَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ ثَالِثُ ثَلَاثَةٍ ۘ وَمَا مِنْ إِلَٰهٍ إِلَّا إِلَٰهٌ وَاحِدٌ ۚ وَإِنْ لَمْ يَنْتَهُوا عَمَّا يَقُولُونَ لَيَمَسَّنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ * أَفَلَا يَتُوبُونَ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَيَسْتَغْفِرُونَهُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Yaqeenan un logon ne Kufr kiya jinohne kaha ke Allah Teen mein se ek hai (Trinity). Haalanki Ma'bood e Waahid  (One Deity) ke alawa koi Ma'bood nahi hai. Agar ye log apni baton se baaz na aye to un mein se Kufr karne walon ko sakht Azaab apni giraft mein le lega."_
_"Phir ye log Allah se Tauba wa Istighfar na karenge. Allah bahut Bakhshne wala aur Meherban hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 73 - 74)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Mubahela ke Pase Manzar mein Christianity ke kuchh batil Aqaed ka tazkara ho raha hai.
Christianity mein sab se Basic Aqeeda hai Trinity. Trinity ke bare mein ham Sura Nisa:171 ke zail mein discuss kar chuke hain. (3rd May 2017 ka post).
Trinity means God is One, The God, Jesus Christ, Holy Spirit. (Khuda, Hazrat Esa, Ruhul Quds). Yani Allah ek hai lekin Khuda (Father), Hazrat Esa (Khuda ke beta) aur Ruhul Qudus, ye sab Khuda ke roop hain. Yani 1=3 & 3=1. Ek bachcha bhi is Maths ko nahi samajh sakta.
Hazrat Esa (as) ne to Allah ki Wahdaniyat ke baat ki thi aur apne aap ko Khuda ka banda bataya tha aur Khuda-e-Yakta ki Ibaadat ki takeed ki thi, lekin
Christianity mein Hazrat Esa (as) ke uthay jane ke baad apni marzi muafiq kafi Tabdeeliyan ki gayin. Aur iska bani hai St. Paul, jo ke pahle Yahodi tha. Is mazhab ko bigadne wala yehi insaan hai.
Detail jaanne ke liye is links par click karen:
(1) *Islamic view of the Trinity:*
https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islamic_view_of_the_Trinity
(2) *Who invented the Trinity?:*
http://www.islamreligion.com/articles/600/viewall/who-invented-trinity/

Allah ne Teen ke maanne walon ko Condemn kiya hai aur Kafir bataya hai. Phir Allah ne do option rakhe ya to Raahe Raast par aa jayen, apne Batil Aqeeda chhod den, Tauba kar len, Allah Tauba qubool karne wala hai warna anqareeb woh Azaab mein mubtila honge.

Bare Ilaha hame 3 ke is Batil aqeedon se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✝
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Nasaara (Christianity) ne Hazrat Maseeh (as) (Christ) ke mutalliq Ghulu (Exaggeration) kar ke unki nafarmani ki aur unka Ghulu is hadd tak badha ke unhone Hazrat Maseeh (as) ko Allah, Ibnullah aur Teen mein se ek (ثلاث ثلاثة) tak kaha aur kuchh ne unhe Khuda (اله) kaha."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

♦ _*RASOOLE KHUDA: H. ESA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (740)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا الْمَسِيحُ ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ إِلَّا رَسُولٌ قَدْ خَلَتْ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ الرُّسُلُ وَأُمُّهُ صِدِّيقَةٌ ۖ كَانَا يَأْكُلَانِ الطَّعَامَ ۗ انْظُرْ كَيْفَ نُبَيِّنُ لَهُمُ الْآيَاتِ ثُمَّ انْظُرْ أَنَّىٰ يُؤْفَكُونَ*

_"Maseeh Ibne Maryam (as) iske alawa aur kuchh nahi ke woh ek Rasool hain. Is se qabl aur bhi bahut se Rasool guzar chuke hain aur unki Maa Siddiqa thi. Woh dono khana khate the. Dekho Ham kis tarah se unke saamne apni Ayaat ko wazeh karte hain. Phir dekho ke ye kis taraf ulte phire jaate hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 75)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta ayat ka topic jaari rakhte hua is baat ki takeed ki gayi hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) Khuda nahi ho sakte iski daleel ye hai ke woh khaate peete hain, jabke Khuda ko iski zaroorat nahi. Aur doosre Anbiya ki tarah ye bhi Rasool hain jo ke logon ki Hidayat karne aye. Jabke Christians doosre prophets ko maante hain lekin jab Jesus Christ ki baat aati hai to woh unko Son of God, ya yeh ke Ummat gunah mein doobi hui thi aur Hazrat Esa (as) ne unki taraf unke gunahon ke Kaffara ke taur par qurban ho gaye jisko "Atonement" kahte hain. Ab ek Christian chahe woh kitne hi gunah kare use uski fikr nahi karne chahiye balke Jesus ne advance mein is ke liye apni fidakari de di hai.
Ye sab unke Batil Aqaid hain jabke Hazrat Esa (as) aisi koi Taa'leem nahi di thi.

Woh Khuda hone ko is daleel se sabit karte hain ke woh bin baap ke hain, lekin ye Khudai koi daleel nahi ho sakti, jabke unki Waledah par bhi ilzaam lagaya gaya. Khuda ne Hazrat Maryam ko Siddiqa bataya hai.

Ahle Bait (as) ka is Ayat ki tashreeh mein qaul mulaheza farmayen:

Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Ye Khuda ki Hikmate Bahera aur Izzate Zahera ki wazeh tareen daleel hai kiyonki Khuda ko maloom tha ke Anbiya ke Karamat o Mo'jezat itne zyada hain ke inhe kuchh log Khuda maan lenge. Nasaara (Christians) ne Ibne Maryam (as) ke mutalliq Ghulu kiya isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Esa (as) aur unki Waledah ke mutalliq farmaya: (5:75)("Esa (as) aur unki Waledah dono Khana khate the"). Maqsad ye hai ke jo bhi khana khayega us Rafa Haajat (Toilet) ki zaroorat hogi aur jise Rafa Haajat ki zaroorat ho woh Khuda nahi ho sakta."_
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame apne Haqeeqi Ma'bood ki Ibaadat o Ita'at karne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✝
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"H. Isa (as) ne apne hawaariyo'n se kaha, "Aise shakhs ki hum-nashini (dosti) ikhtiyaar karo jiska deedar tumko Khuda ki yaad mein mubtela kar de, aur jiski guftaar (baatein) tumhare Ilm aur daanish (knowledge) mein izafa kare, aur jiska kirdaar tum ko Akherat ka mushtaaq (eager / utsuk) bana de."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p23)
✝
H. Isa (as):
_"Mukhlees (sincere) wo hota hai jo Allah Ta'ala hi ke liye amal karta hai aur is baat ko pasand nahi karta ke oos amal ki koi shakhs taarif kare."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3)

           ♦ _*MURTI POOJA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (742)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَتَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يَمْلِكُ لَكُمْ ضَرًّا وَلَا نَفْعًا ۚ وَاللَّهُ هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den kiya tum Khuda ko chhod kar uski Ibaadat karte ho jo tumhare liye na to nuqsan ka ikhtiyar rakhta hai aur na hi fayda ka ikhtiyar rakhta hai. Jabke Allah Sunnewala aur Ilm Rakhnewala hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 76)

📚📖 👻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala Hamri Aqlon ko jhajod kar sawal kar raha hai ke us Khuda ke pas kiyon jaate ho jis mein na tumhe nuqsan pahuchane ki taqat hai aur na koi fayda de sakta hai. Ye idol worship ki taraf bhi ishaara hai jaisa ke H. Ibrahim (as) ne bhi yehi daleel di thi. Aaj kal India mein khas kar Murti pooja ki bahut ahmiyat di jaati hai. Koi bhi ba sha'oor shakhs is baat ko pagal pan hi batayega ke aksar log ek patthar ya mitti ki murti par fida hain. Jabke ke woh khud iqraar karte hain ke na iski koi daleel hai balke ek aastha hai ya mythology hai.
Yaqeenan log Khuda ko samajh nahi paate hain, Uske baare mein sahi taur par jaante nahi hain to Uski Ma'arefat kahan se rakhenge.
Anbiya wa Aimma (as) ko isi liye to Khuda ne bheja taake bhatke hue logon ko Seedhi Raah par la saken.
Lekin Dushmanon ne kabhi nahi chaha ke ye logon ki Rahnumai karen isliye unhone sabko Shaheed kiye. Karbala isi ki ek kadi hai.
Bare Ilaha hame Seedhe Raaste par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

  ♦ _*GHULU (EXAGGERATION)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (743)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لَا تَغْلُوا فِي دِينِكُمْ غَيْرَ الْحَقِّ وَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا أَهْوَاءَ قَوْمٍ قَدْ ضَلُّوا مِنْ قَبْلُ وَأَضَلُّوا كَثِيرًا وَضَلُّوا عَنْ سَوَاءِ السَّبِيلِ*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab! Apne Deen mein nahaq Ghulu na karo aur un logon ki khwaheshat ki pairavi na karo jo pahle gumrah hui aur bahut se logon ko gumrah logon ko gumrah kiya aur Seedhi Raah se bhatak gaye."_
(Surah Maeda: 77)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kisi ke haq mein Ghulu (Exaggeration) karna jurm hai aur Taqseer karna bhi sahih nahi hai. Hazrat Esa (as) ke mutalliq Eisaiyon (Christians) ne Ghulu kiya to unhe Khuda aur Khuda ka beta tak kah diya. Isi tarah se Rasoole Khuda (saww) aur Aimma (as) ke mutalliq bhi Ghulu karna sahih nahi hai. Uyoonul Akhbar mein mein Rivayaat hain jis mein Ghulat wa Mufawweza ki sakhti se tardeed ki gayi hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)
🚩
Imam Reza (as):
_"Tanasukh (Transmigration-Purn Janam) ka Aqeeda rakhne wala Kafir hai. Allah Ta'ala Ghaliyon par La'anat kare. Ghali, Yahoodi, Nasrani, Murjiyyah aur Hurooriyyah (Khwarij) hain."_
_"Unke sath uthna baithna rakho aur un se kisi tarah ki dosti na rakho aur un se bezaari ikhtiyar karo. Khuda unse bezar hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Isliye zaroori hai ke ham Rasool wa Aimma (as) ki itteba' karen, jitna unhone bayan kiya itna hi bayan karen, na zyada na kam. Agar kisi ki Fazail badha den to Ghali aur ghata den to Muqassir ho jayenge. Misal ke taur par Ali (as) ke haath Yadullah, Kaan Uznullah, Aankh Ainullah..... Lekin phir bhi woh Khuda ki Makhlooq aur bande hain, Khuda ko Sajdah karte hai, Hazrat Esa (as) murdon ko zinda karte the Qur'an mein zikr hai, Ali (as) ne bhi yehi kaam kiya lekin Khuda ki izn (permission) se hai, ye Ghulu nahi hai. Jo kahte hain Rasoole Khuda (saww) ham jaise the, Muqassir hain, kiyonki unhone unke martabe ko ghata diya.

Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq de ke ham Tere Auliya ki zyada se zyada Ma'arefat hasil kar saken.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

                  ♦ _*LAA'NAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (750)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لُعِنَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ عَلَىٰ لِسَانِ دَاوُودَ وَعِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ بِمَا عَصَوْا وَكَانُوا يَعْتَدُونَ * كَانُوا لَا يَتَنَاهَوْنَ عَنْ مُنْكَرٍ فَعَلُوهُ ۚ لَبِئْسَ مَا كَانُوا يَفْعَلُونَ*

_"Bani Israel mein se jinhone ne Kufr ki ravish Ikhtiyar ki un par *Dawood (as) aur Esa bin Maryam (as) ki zabani La'anat ki gayi.* Kiyonki unhone sarkashi Ikhtiyar ki thi aur zyadtiyan karte the. Woh bure kaam karne par kisi ko rokte nahi the. Ye bahut bura tarze amal tha jise unhone apna liya tha."_
(Surah Maeda: 78-79)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rauza Kafi mein hai Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya ke Hazrat Dawood (as) ne aise logon ko Suwar kaha aur Hazrat Esa (as) ne Bandar kaha.
Sawabul Aamaal mein hai ke jab Bani Israel ne ghaltiyan karni shuru ki to ibteda mein to bhai bhai ko gunah se rokta tha magar gunehgar baaz na aate. Lekin iske bawajood unke saath uthna baithna khana peena jari raha. Phir Allah ne unke dilon ko ek doosre ke mushabeh kar diya. Phir ye Ayat padhi.
Tafseer e Ayyashi mein hai ke Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
"Wo log unki majalis o mahafil mein to shirkat nahi karte the albatta jab unse milte the to hans hans kar milte the aur pyar muhabbat ki baten karte the."
Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim mein hai ke Bani Israel ke badkar afraad Suwar ka gosht khate, Sharaab peete aur makhsoos ayyam mein apni biwiyon se maqarebat (sex) karte the. Magar doosre afraad unki badkariyon se mana' nahi karte the, isi liye Allah ne unki mazammat farmayi aur Ahle Imaan ki bhi sarzanish ki jo Imaan ke dawe ke bawajood Kafiron se dosti ka dam bharte the. (Albatta Taqayye ke Ahkam alag hain)
Majmaul Bayan mein hai Imam Mohd Baqir (as) ne farmaya ke jab Ahle "Ayla" ne Saturday ko ziyadti ki to Hazrat Dawood (as) ne un par La'anat ki thi aur unhone ke kaha: _"Khudaya! Jis tarah se ek chadar kisi ko lapet leti hai, Tu Ahle Ayla ko bhi La'anat ki lapet mein de de."_ Allah ne unhe maskh karke Bandar bana diya.
Hazrat Esa (as) ne logon ki farmayish par Allah Ta'ala se Dastarkhwan utarne ki darkhwast ki thi. Jin logon ne Dastarkhwan ki Ne'mat istemal karne ke baad unki na qadri ki to Hazrat Esa (as) ne un par La'anat ki thi.
Is Ayat se murad woh khushamdi afraad hain jo Zalim Salateen se Muhabbat karte the aur Duniya ke husool liye Salateen ki najaez khwaheshat ko aarasta karke unke samne pesh karte the.
Karbala is baat ka namuna hai. Ham Zalim o Jabir Yazeed aur unke Saathiya par La'anat bhejte hain. Ahle Bait (as) ke Dushman par La'anat bhejna isi Usool mein se hai.
Bare Ilaha hame unka dost bana jo Tere Dost hain, na ke jo bhatke hue hain.

*فَلَعَنَ اللّٰہُ اُمَّۃً قَتَلَتْکَ وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰہُ اُمَّۃً ظَلَمَتْکَ وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰہُ اُمَّۃً سَمِعَتْ بِذٰالِکَ فَرَضِیَتْ بِہٖ*
( _"Pas Allah ki La'anat ho us par jisne Aapko (Imam Husain as) Qatl kiya, jisne Aap par Zulm kiya, jisne suna aur uspar raazi raha."_)
(Ziyarat Warisa/Ashura)
https://youtu.be/Vn3uaVao3Yc
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                  ♦ _*DOSTI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (751)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*تَرَىٰ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ يَتَوَلَّوْنَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا ۚ لَبِئْسَ مَا قَدَّمَتْ لَهُمْ أَنْفُسُهُمْ أَنْ سَخِطَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَفِي الْعَذَابِ هُمْ خَالِدُونَ * وَلَوْ كَانُوا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالنَّبِيِّ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْهِ مَا اتَّخَذُوهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءَ وَلَٰكِنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنْهُمْ فَاسِقُونَ*

_"Aap un mein se aksar afraad ko dekhenge ke woh Kuffar se dosti rakhte hain. Yaqeenan unke Nafson ne unke liye bada zaade raah aage rawana kiya jiski wajah se Allah un par Ghazabnak ho gaya aur woh Azaab mein hamesha rahenge. Aur agar un logon ka Khuda, Paighambar aur unki Taa'leemat par Imaan hota jise Paighambar par nazil kiya gaya to woh Kuffar ko kabhi bhi apna Rafeeq (Friend) na banate. Lekin baat ye hai ke unki aksariyat Fasiq afraad par mushtamil hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 80 - 81)

📚📖 👥
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat ke zel mein kuchh Rivayaat bayan ki thi. Ye Ayaten bhi unhi logon ke bare mein hain. Ye Ayaten Ravadari ke mukhalefat mein hain. Islami Shariyat is tarah se hai jahan zyadar tar Kuffar ya jo hamare Aqaed ka mukhalif hai usse boycott ka hukm hai. Kafir se len den ya Khaane Peene se parhez ka hukm hai, ye wajah nahi ke woh gande hain jaisa ke log samajhte hain. Chunke jo hamara ham-Aqeeda nahi hai usse parhez hai bhale woh saf suthra ho. Isliye unse dosti karne se mana kiya gaya hai. (Taqayya ya aur koi majboori ho to exception hain, aur doosri bhi wujuhat hain.).
Hamare Secularism mein unse dosti nahi hai balke unse na hi ladai jhagda karna na jirah karna hai aur amno amaan qayem rakhna maqsood hai.
Kuchh log dosti ka bahana ye banate hain ke ham unko apni taraf kheench rahe hain, lekin agar aap Shariyat tod kar koi kaam karenge wo aapko Sawab ke bajai Azaab ki taraf le jayegi. Dosti ke asaraat iske bar-aks bhi hote hai ke ham Kafir ko seedhe raaste par laane ke bajaye ham hi bhatak kar unki raah Ikhtiyar kar lete hain.
Doosri Ayat mein is baat ki taraf bhi ishaara hai ke kam Aqeeda log aksar dekha gaya hai ke jab un par koi musibat aati hai to aksar Baba'on, Pandit ya aur koi gande taweez karne walon ke peechhe dodhte hain. Agar unke Aqeeda pukhta hote to Allah, Rasool (saww) aur Ahle Bait (as) ke dar par dastak dete.

Bare Ilaha hamari Tere Auliya ki dosti to dayam o qayam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                  ♦ _*NASAARA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (752)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَتَجِدَنَّ أَشَدَّ النَّاسِ عَدَاوَةً لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا الْيَهُودَ وَالَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا ۖ وَلَتَجِدَنَّ أَقْرَبَهُمْ مَوَدَّةً لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّا نَصَارَىٰ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّ مِنْهُمْ قِسِّيسِينَ وَرُهْبَانًا وَأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ*

_"Tum Ahle Imaan ki Dushmani mein Yahood wa Mushrekin ko tamam logon se zyada sakht paoge. Aur Ahle Imaan ki Dosti mein unhe qareeb paoge jinhone kaha tha ke ham Nasaara hain aur iski wajah ye hai ke un mein Ibaadat Guzar Aalim aur Tarakud Duniya Faqeer paye jaate hain aur woh Takabbur nahi karte."_
(Surah Maeda: 82)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaton ke bayan hua tha kis kis se Dosti nahi karna chahiye.
Is Ayat ka Shaane Nuzool mein woh waqea hai jab Musalmano ne pahli Hijrat Janabe Jafar e Tayyar ke Rehbari mein Habash (Ethiopia) ki taraf ki. Detail ki yahan gunjaish nahi hai. Habash ka Badshah Najashi jo Christian tha kafi mubahese ke baad usne Islam qubool kiya. Uski tamanna Rasool (saww) se mulaqat ki hui lekin uska daurane safar mein hi Inteqaal ho gaya.
--------------------------
Waqea detail mein is link mein padh sakte hain:
(1) http://www.ezsoftech.com/stories/islam.asp
(2) https://www.al-islam.org/jafar-al-tayyar-kamal-al-sayyid/jafar-al-tayyar
--------------------------
Is waqea kuchh ahm point:
👉🏻 Jafar ibne Abi Talib (Tayyar) ne is mein bahut bada roll play kiya hai. Najashi ko Convert karne mein unhone bahut ahm karnama kar dikhaya.
👉🏻 Quraish ne Yahoodiyon se mile bahut badi chal chali lekin kamyab nahi hue.
Is Ayat mein is baat ka zikr hai ke Yahoodi aur Mushrekin dono ek mad mein hain, dono chal baz, zalim aur sakht hain. Yani inse hamari koi dosti ka sawal hi nahi uthta. Mushrekin ka dayra bada hai, aap ginte chale jayen kaun kaun Mushrik hai, batane ki zaroorat nahi. Wahi Nasaara (Christians) ki madah sarai ki gayi hai. Lekin yahan Christians se murad sab Christians nahi. Balke ye ayat Najashi Badshah ke liye nazil hui.
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat mein jin logon ki madah ki gayi hai to ye woh log the jo Hazrat Esa (as) ke baad aur Muhammad Mustafa (saww) se pahle the aur woh Anhazrat (saww) ki aamad ke Muntazir the."_
Islam ke aghaz ke pahle ye log Christians the lekin Ibaadat Guzar the aur baad mein unhone Islam qubool kiya.
Yahan hame ye sabaq milta hai ke agarche Ghair-Muslim the lekin Nek o Saleh the to unki Allah ne bhi madah ki hai. Isliye Nek o Mukhlesana Amal mein ye kashish hoti hai ke agar Insaan ghalat raste bhatak bhi gaya hai to woh Seedhe Raaste par aa jata hai.
Bare Ilaha hame aisa Aamal karne ki Taufeeq ata farma jis mein Teri Raza ho.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

♦ _*JANABE JAFAR-E-TAYYAR (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (753)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا سَمِعُوا مَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَى الرَّسُولِ تَرَىٰ أَعْيُنَهُمْ تَفِيضُ مِنَ الدَّمْعِ مِمَّا عَرَفُوا مِنَ الْحَقِّ ۖ يَقُولُونَ رَبَّنَا آمَنَّا فَاكْتُبْنَا مَعَ الشَّاهِدِينَ*

_"Aur jab woh us Kalam ko sunte hain jo Rasool par utra hai to tum dekhte ho ke Haq Shanasi ki wajah se unki Ankhon se Aansu tapakne lagte hain. Woh kahte hain ke Parwardigar! Ham Imaan laye hamara naam gawahon mein shamil karle."_
(Surah Maeda: 83)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ka zikr is Ayat mein jari hai. Jaise ke Rivayat ke zariye bataya tha ye madah un Nasaara ke liye hai jo Rasool (saww) ki aamad ke Muntazir the. Janabe Jafar e Tayyar (as) ne ek taraf to Kuffar e Quraish ki sazishon ka muh tod jawab diya, doosri taraf Habash ke Badshah Najashi ka bhi dil jeet liya. Jab Jafar e Tayyar (as) Madina pahunche to Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Khaibar ko fateh kiya tha.
Rasoole Akram (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Mein nahi jaanta ke mujhe Khaibar ke Fatah hone ki zyada khushi hai ya Jafar ke palat aane ki."_
Tafseer Al Munar mein hai Najashi ne apne yaro o Ansar mein se 30 behtareen afraad ko Paighambar e Islam (saww) ke pas Medina bheja.
Kahte hain Shamiyon mein se 8 afraad jin mein ek Father (Rahib) tha jo Sura Yaseen sun kar itna mutassir hua ke rona shuru kar diya aur Musalman hue aur kahne lage ye Ayaten H. Maseeh se kitni mushabehat rakhti hain. Tab ye Ayat Nazil hui.

Bare Ilaha hame aisa amal karne ki Taufeeq ata farma ke ghair Muslim sirf hamara amal dekh kar Islam ki taraf raghbat karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*SALEHEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (754)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا لَنَا لَا نُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَمَا جَاءَنَا مِنَ الْحَقِّ وَنَطْمَعُ أَنْ يُدْخِلَنَا رَبُّنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الصَّالِحِينَ*

_"Aur ham akhir Khuda par aur Us Haq par Imaan kiyon na layen jo hamare paas aaya hai jabke ham ye ummid karte hain ke Khuda hame Saleh logon mein dakhil kar de?"_

(Surah Maeda: 84)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta bayan se jari:
Jaisa ke bataya ja chuka hai, un Christians ki madah sarai ki gayi jo Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki aamad ke muntazir the. Bhale hi Esaiyyon ki aksariyat gumrah ho chuki thi. Yahoodi aur Nasaara ki Aasmani Kitabon mein bahut si peshengoyan ki gayi thi. Lekin maaddiyat (Materialism) ne unko dhoke mein rakha. Ye Ayaten un Christians ke liye ayen jo Rasool (saww) ke zamane mein the aur apni Akherat bakhair ke khwahishmand the. Ye fitratan sawal hai ke jabke woh aa gaya hai jis ki ummid mein baithe the to phir der kis baat ki. Kiyonki Haq aa gaya.
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Haq Ali (as) ke saath. Bare Ilaha Tu Haq ko us taraf mod jis taraf Ali (as) hon."_

Bare Ilaha hame us taraf mod jis taraf Haq ho.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

     ♦ _*CONVERSION to ISLAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (755)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَأَثَابَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِمَا قَالُوا جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا ۚ وَذَٰلِكَ جَزَاءُ الْمُحْسِنِينَ * وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَكَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا أُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ الْجَحِيمِ*

_"Unki is guftgu ki wajah se Khuda ne unhe aise bagh ata kiye jinke neeche Nehren jaari hain. Woh un mein hamesha rahenge aur ye bhalai karne walon ki jaza hai. Aur woh log jinhone Kufr kiya aur hamari Ayaat ki takzeeb ki woh log Dozakhi hain."_
(Surah Maeda: 85 - 86)

📚📖 ✝☪ 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta bayan ko jari rakhte hue, jisne Haq ko qubool kiya uske liye Allah ne Jannat ki basharat di aur jisne inkar kiya uska thikana Dozakh hai.
Hazrat Esa (as) jo Deen laye unke pairokar us Deen ko badal diya aur aane wali naslen confused ho gayi. Lekin jo sahi raaste par aana chahte the unhe jaise hi raasta mila unhone Haq ke raaste ko apna liya.
Aajkal West mein Christianity chhod kar log jok dar jok Islam mein dakhil ho rahe hain. Uski wajah yehi hai jaise jaise unko jaankari ho rahi hai woh sahi raaste par aa rahe hain. Niche link diye Article mein padhen uska khulasa ye hai Eisaiyon ne kiyon Islam qubool kiya uski wajah bayan ki hai. Sabse badi cheez jo unhone ne Islam mein dekhi ke ye saaf suthra mazhab hai. Yahan Priesthood nahi hai. (Christians mein Priest ko ek tarah ka zalim aur dictator tasawwur karte the). Ek Christian ko Father ke saamne apne Gunahon ka iqraar karna hota hai phir woh maaf karta hai jabke Islam mein Tauba sirf Allah se hai. Yahan Insaan Azaadi mehsoos karta hai. Islam mein Equality, barabari aur Dicipline Nazm o zabt hai. Yeh asl wajah conversions ki batayi gayi hai.
___________________________
Detail is link mein padhen aur logon ke comment par bhi ghaur karen:
*Why are So Many Westerners Converting to Islam?*
http://www1.cbn.com/spirituallife/why-are-so-many-westerners-converting-to-islam
___________________________

Bare Ilaha hame aise Amal ki Taufeeq ata farma jise dekh kar Ghair Muslim khusi khusi Islam apnayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*KHAANA-PEENA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (756)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُحَرِّمُوا طَيِّبَاتِ مَا أَحَلَّ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ وَلَا تَعْتَدُوا ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُعْتَدِينَ*

_"Ay Imaanwalo! Jo Pakeezah cheezen Allah ne tumhare liye Halal ki hain unhe Haram na kar lo aur hadd se tajawuz na karo."_
(Surah Maeda: 87)

📚📖 🍪🥃🍵🥛
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Islam Deen e Fitrat hai, woh Tark e Duniya aur Rohbaniyat (رهبانیت) par Imaan nahi rakhta aur woh apne Pairokaro ko Tark e Lazzat ki hargiz Ta'aleem nahi deta. Albatta is mein sirf ek shart ka izaafa karta hai ke cheez ka Halal o Tayyab hona zaroori hai.
Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke Hazrat Habeeb e Khuda (saww) Murgh aur Falooda khaya karte the aur Aap (saww) ko Sheerani (Sweet) aur Shahed se khusoosi uns tha aur Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Momin khud meetha hota hai isi liye woh meethe ko pasand karta hai."_
_"Momin ke shikam (stomach) mein ek zawiya aisa hota jise Mithai ke alawa aur koi cheez pur nahi kar sakti."_
Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim mein hai Ameerul Mo'meneen (as) ne qasam thi ke raat ko kabhi nahi soyenge. Bilal ne qasam khai ke woh hamesha Din mein Roza rakhenge aur Usman bin Maz'oon ne Qasam khai ke woh biwi se maqarebat nahi karenge. Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko bataya gaya to unhone ne mimbar se farmaya:
_"Logon apne upar Paak Cheezon ko kiyon Haram kar rahe ho? Agah raho! Mein raat ko sota hun aur biwi se maqarebat bhi karta hun aur Din ke waqt khata bhi hun. Jisne meri Sunnat se rogardani (don't care) ki woh mujh se nahi hai.'_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Tayyabo Tahir Khana Khaane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

           ♦ _*KHAANA-PEENA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (757)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكُلُوا مِمَّا رَزَقَكُمُ اللَّهُ حَلَالًا طَيِّبًا ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ الَّذِي أَنْتُمْ بِهِ مُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Yaqeenan Allah Ziyadti karne walon ko pasand nahi karta."_
_"Aur jo Halal o Pakeezah Rizq Khuda ne tumko diya hai use khao aur Us Khuda ki nafarmani se bachte raho jis par Imaan rakhte ho."_
(Surah Maeda: 88)

📚📖 🍪🥃🍵🥛
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat se jari bayan mein ye hai ke Jo cheez Shariyat ne jaez qarar di use karna hai, hame kiya achha lag raha usse koi sarokar nahi. Allah ki Razamandi is mein hai ke Shariyat ki pabandi ki jaye, na ke ham Rohbaniyat ikhtiyar karen, yani hame na koi Baba, na Koi Peer banne ke liye kaha gaya hai, na koi Sadhu. Yani hamare mazhab mein Deen ke saath saath Duniya dari bhi nibhani hai. Na koi Riyazat, na koi chilla ka hukm hai. Haan jo hukm hua hai woh hai Zuhd o Taqwa. Ye woh Ibaadat hai jo Shariyat ke dayre mein rahkar hoti hai. Kuchh Limit rakh di hain, us Limits ko paar nahi karna hai.
Kal jo hadis hamne bayan ki thi jo ke 3 logon ne Qasam khai thi, us mein Usman bin Maz'oon ne jo Qasam khai thi usse Biwi ke huqooq pamal ho rahe the isliye wo Qasam jaez nahi thi. Lekin Hazrat Ali (as) ne jo Qasam khai thi raat mein na sone ki aur phir Rasool (saww) ke kahne par tark kiya to ye qasam ek amr e mubah ke liye thi, means qasam khaen ya na khaen koi farq nahi padta. Isliye ye koi gunah nahi hua. Aur Hazrat Ali (as) Masoom hain.
Qur'an mein ek aur Ayat mein bhi hai:
*يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ لِمَ تُحَرِّمُ مَا أَحَلَّ اللَّهُ لَكَ ۖ تَبْتَغِي مَرْضَاتَ أَزْوَاجِكَ ۚ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*
_"Aye Paighambar! (Mor) jo Aapke liye Allah ne Halal qarar diye hain apni biwiyon ko khush karne ke liye apne upar kiyon Haram karte ho."_
(Surah Tahrim: 1)
Is Ayat se pata chala ke Allah Rasool (saww) ko tanbih kar raha hai, jabke Rasool (saww) bhi Masoom hain aur Khuda ki nafarmani nahi kar sakte. Lekin isi tarah ki Rivayaat wa Ayaat logon ki Hidayat Maqsood hoti hain na ke Allah apne Rehbaran ki islah kar raha hai.
(Tafseer e Namoona)

Bare Ilaha hame Taqwa Ilahi Ikhtiyar karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                  ♦ _*QASAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (758)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا يُؤَاخِذُكُمُ اللَّهُ بِاللَّغْوِ فِي أَيْمَانِكُمْ وَلَٰكِنْ يُؤَاخِذُكُمْ بِمَا عَقَّدْتُمُ الْأَيْمَانَ ۖ فَكَفَّارَتُهُ إِطْعَامُ عَشَرَةِ مَسَاكِينَ مِنْ أَوْسَطِ مَا تُطْعِمُونَ أَهْلِيكُمْ أَوْ كِسْوَتُهُمْ أَوْ تَحْرِيرُ رَقَبَةٍ ۖ فَمَنْ لَمْ يَجِدْ فَصِيَامُ ثَلَاثَةِ أَيَّامٍ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ كَفَّارَةُ أَيْمَانِكُمْ إِذَا حَلَفْتُمْ ۚ وَاحْفَظُوا أَيْمَانَكُمْ ۚ كَذَٰلِكَ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ آيَاتِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ*

_"Allah tumhari mohmil (meaningless) Qasamon par tumhara mu'akheza nahi karega (nahi pakdega), magar jo qasamen tum jaanboojh kar khaate ho un par woh tum se zaroor mu'akheza (pakdega) karega. (Aisi Qasam todne ka) Kaffara ye hai ke 10 Miskeenon ko is ausat darje ka Khaana khilao jo tum apne gharwalon ko khilate ho ya unhe kapda pahnao ya ek ghulam azad karo aur jise iski sakat na ho (not able to do) to woh 3 Din ke Roze rakhe. Ye tumhari Qasamon ka Kaffara hai jab tum Qasam kha kar tod do. Aur apni Qasamon ki hifazat karte raho. Is tarah se Allah apni Ayaat tumhare liye wazeh karta (explain) hai taake tum Shukr ada karo."_
(Surah Maeda: 89)
🍂
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kal hamne kuchh Qasam ke bare mein wazahat ki thi. Qasam ke topic par pahle bhi tazkara ho chuka hai.
🍃
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Qasamen 3 tarah ki hain._
_(1) Jis mein Kaffara nahi hai._
_(2) Jis mein Kaffara hai._
_(3) Jhooti Qasam jiska iraada kisi ko nuqsan pahuchane ka ho, aisi Qasam Dozakh ki mojib hai._
_Wo Qasam jis mein Kaffara nahi hai woh aisi hai ke Insaan kisi Neki ke na karne ki Qasam kha le. Iska Kaffara yahi hai ke woh apni Qasam ki parwa na kare._
_Woh Qasam jis mein Kaffara hai jaise koi shakhs Qasam khaye ke woh falan burai nahi karega magar Qasam ke bawajood bhi burai kare to us par Kaffara Wajib ho jata hai aur Dozakh ka sabab banne wali Qasam wo hai ke koi shakhs kisi Musalman ke Maal ko rok lene ki Qasam khaye."_
(Al Kafi)
🌿
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) se poochha gaya ke wo Mohmil Qasamen kaunsi hain jin par Khuda hame nahi pakdega?
Imam (as):
_"Jab koi shakhs aam rivaj ke tahet لاوالله, بلی و الله (Khuda ki Qasam, Qasam Allah ki..) kahta hai to wo Mohmil Qasam hai. Haan agar is Qasam ke saath dil ka iraada shamil ho to aur baat hai."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Al Kafi)
Saeedul Haraj ne poochh ke _"ek shakhs kisi kaam ke liye Halaf uthata hai (Affedevit). Phir use maloom hota hai ke us kaam ka na karna behtar hai aur agar woh tark na kare to use apne gunahgar hone ka andesha hota hai to kiya woh use tark kar sakta?"_
Imam Sadiq (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Kiya Rasoole Akram (saww) ka farman nahi suna. Aap (saww) ne farmaya:_
_"Jab tujhe apni Qasam se koi behtar kaam nazar aye to Qasam chhod de."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌱
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs apne aap se zulm door karne ke liye Taqayya ke taur par Qasam khaye to us par koi Kaffara nahi hai aur Qasam Shikni ka koi Gunah nahi hai."_
(Kitabul Khisaal)
☘
Ameerul Mo'meneen (as):
_"Walid ke saath bete ki koi Qasam nahi aur Shauhar ke saath Biwi ki koi Qasam nahi hai."_
(Khisaal)
🍀
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"4 qism ke Kaffare hain:_
_(1) Ghulam Azad karna._
_(2) 10 Miskeenon ko medium khana khilana._
_Medium (ausat darja) se murad Sirka aur Zaitoon se khana khilana aur Aala darje mein Roti Gosht hai aur_
_(3) Sadqa har Miskeen ke liye ek Muddat Gehun (Wheat) hai. Aur koi Kapda pahenna chahe to 2 kapda pahnao._
_(4) Jo ye 3 ki sakat na rakhta ho woh 3 Din Roze rakhe."_
_"Qur'an mein lafz او 'ya' istemal hua yani do teen mein se ek chun sakta hai."_
_"Baqi Rozon mein waqfa (gap) jaez hai lekin Qasam ke Kaffara ke Roze mein waqfa (gap) jaez nahi aur ye Roze musalsal rakhe jayen."_
(Al Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🌾
Isliye WhatsApp par jo Qasam de kar Message aate rahte hain unki parwa nahi karni chahiye. Qur'an wa Ahadis wazeh ho gaya hoga.
Bare Ilaha ham Ahle Bait (as) ka wasta dete hai ke Tu hamare Gunah ko ma'af kar de kiyonki ye hamari barkaton ke khatme ka sabab hain.

  ♦ _*SHARAAB (INTOXICATION)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (759)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِنَّمَا الْخَمْرُ وَالْمَيْسِرُ وَالْأَنْصَابُ وَالْأَزْلَامُ رِجْسٌ مِنْ عَمَلِ الشَّيْطَانِ فَاجْتَنِبُوهُ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Imaanwalo! Sharab, Juwa, But aur Panse na paak hain aur Shaitani Amal hain. unse parhez karo taake tum kamyab ho jao."_
(Surah Maeda: 90)

📚📖 🍷
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as) se is Ayat ke terms ke baare mein poochha gaya to farmaya:
_" "Mayser (ميسر) means jis cheez se Juwa khela jaye (Game of chance) yahan tak ke Akhrot (Walnut) se bhi khela jaye to wo bhi shamil hai._
_" "Ansaab" (انصاب) means woh Qurbani no Mushrikeen ke Khuda le liye zabah ki jaye (Devi devtao ko Bali chadhana)"_
_" "Azlaam" (ازلام) means Panse ke Teer jis se woh taqseem karte the."_
(Al Kaafi)
Sharaab tadreejan Haram hui means step by step Haram hui.
Iska pahla marhala (Sura Baqarah:219)  mein hai. Is Ayat mein pahle bataya ke isse fayde ke bajaye Nuqsan zyada hai.
Doosra marhala (Sura Nisa: 43) mein hai yani Nashe ki halat mein Namaz nahi ho sakti.
Teesra marhala aaj ki Ayat hai (5:90) yani ye ek Shaitani amal hai.
Imam Baqir (as):
_Khamr "خمر" se sirf Sharaab hi murad nahi hai. Har woh nasha jo insaan mein khumar paida kar de "Khamr" hai aur Haram hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka farman hai: "Jis cheez ki zyada miqdar nasha paida karti ho to uski kam miqdar bhi Haram hai."_
Jab Sharaab ki hurmat ki Ayat nazil hui to us waqt Ahle Madina ke gharon mein khajoor ki Sharaab ke matke bhare hue the. Logon ne matke gharon se bahar nikale aur darwazon par matke tod kar Sharaab baha di. Us din Madine ki galiyon mein Sharaab ka sailab dikhai dene laga tha. Us din kisi ke ghar mein Angoor ke sheere ki Sharaab maujood nahi thi.
🍷
Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs Sharaab piye use kode maro. Agar woh dubara piye phir bhi kode maro. Agar woh teesri bar Sharaab noshi kare to bhi use kode maro. Agar woh chauthi bar Sharaab piye to use qatl kardo."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame aise aise Nashon se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍷
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Sharaab peene wale ko Dozakh mein woh Najis Paani pilaya jayega jo Zaniya Aurat ki Sharamgahon se baramad hoga aur uske saath use Peep aur Ghaleez Khoon pilaya jayega jiski badboo se Ahle Dozakh ko aziyyat mahsoos hogi."_
_"Jisne Sharaab pee to Chalis Din tak Namaz qubool nahi ki jayegi aur agar dubara Sharaab piye to mazeed 40 Din tak uski Namaz qubool nahi ki jayegi. Agar woh 40 Dino ke andar Tauba kiye baghair mar jaye to Allah Ta'ala Qayamat ke Din use mohlik zeher ka Sharbat pilayega."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                *13th ZilHajj 1439*
       *3rd November 2017, Friday,*

             ♦ _*GHAMBLING*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (760)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِنَّمَا الْخَمْرُ وَالْمَيْسِرُ وَالْأَنْصَابُ وَالْأَزْلَامُ رِجْسٌ مِنْ عَمَلِ الشَّيْطَانِ فَاجْتَنِبُوهُ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Imaanwalo! Sharab, Juwa, But aur Panse na paak hain aur Shaitani Amal hain. unse parhez karo taake tum kamyab ho jao."_
(Surah Maeda: 90)

📚📖 🎲🎯
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
(Cont'd...)
"Maysar" mein نرد Dice aur شطرنج Chess sare fehrist hain aur Juwe bazi (Gambling) ki har shakl "Maysar" mein shamil hai. In tamam cheezon ki khareed forokht aur inse fayda hasil karna bhi Haram hai kiyonki ye sab Shaitani amal hain.
🐔🐐
"Ansab" انصاب ke bare mein bhi Ayat no. 3 ke zail mein bata Chuke hain. Ye Pattharon ke But (idol) hote hain jinki koi shakl nahi hoti.  Kuffar/Hindu unke Devi Devtao ki Bali in Pattharon ke saamne dete the aur uska Khoon us Pattharon par mal dete the, ye rivaj Arab mein tha Ka'aba ke saamne zamana Jahiliyyat mein aur India mein bhi Mandiron ke saamne hota hai.
🎯
"Azlam" ke bare mein bhi Ayat no.3 mein bayan hua tha. Ye ek Lottery System hai. Arab mein zamane Jahiliyyat mein aisa hota tha: 10 log Qurbani ke liye Janwar khareedte the aur aapas mein shart lagate the aur Teer ki 10 lakdiyan lete, 7 par Kamyab, 3 par Nakam likh dete phir sab ek thaile mein dal dete aur phir ek ek kar ke 10 log us mein se ek ek teer nikalte jiske hisse mein Kamyab Teer aate woh Gosht ka hissa us mein se le leta lekin 3 Nakam wale ko na gosht milta balke ek tihai qeemat bhi ada karni padti. Isko Panse ke teer kahte hain. Aajkal bhi Lottery ke alag system nikale hue hain. Pas jo Lottery Gambling ke maqsad se ho wo haram hai.

Bare Ilaha hame us laghu aur bekar kamon se door rakh jo Shaitan se Nazdeeki ka baes hote hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🎲
Imam Baqir (as):
_*"Maysar (ميسر) mein Shatranj (Chess) aur Nard (Dice) shamil hain. Iske alawa qumarbazi (Gambling) ki jitni bhi mumkina soorten hain wo sab ki sab isi mein shamil hain. Yahan tak ki bachche jis Akhrot (Walnut) se khelte hain wo bhi "Maysar" ke dayrekar mein shamil hai."*_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🍷🎲🎯
Imam Reza (as):
_*"Jo shakhs Sharaab aur Shatranj ko dekhkar Hazrat Imam Husain (as) ko yaad kare aur Yazid paleed aur Ibne Ziyaad bad-nihaad par La'anat kare to Haq Ta'ala uske gunaho'n ko bakhsh deta hai agar che gunah uske shumaar mein sitaaron ke barabar ho."*_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, Vol 1, P-131, Jaame'ul Akhbar, P-177)
🎲🎯
Imam Sadiq (as):
_*"Buton (Idols) aur Juwe ke Teeron (Gambling) aur Gumrah karne wale Rehbaron aur Zalim Sarbrahon (Leaders) se Izhare La talluqi (Bara'at) Wajib hai."*_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain, Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza (as)

          ♦ _*SHAITAINI AMAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (761)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا يُرِيدُ الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ يُوقِعَ بَيْنَكُمُ الْعَدَاوَةَ وَالْبَغْضَاءَ فِي الْخَمْرِ وَالْمَيْسِرِ وَيَصُدَّكُمْ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَعَنِ الصَّلَاةِ ۖ فَهَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُنْتَهُونَ)*

_*"Shaitan to bas ye chahta hai ke woh Sharaab aur Juwe ki wajah se tum mein Bughz o Adawat paida kar de aur tumhe Allah ke zikr aur Namaz se rok de, to kiya tum ruk jaoge?"*_
(Surah Maeda: 91)

📚📖  
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasoole Akram (saww):
_"Sharab ki wajah se 10 afraad par La'anat ki:_
(1) Sharaab bana ki niyat se Angoor ki kheti karne wala.
(2) Angoor ke Baugh ka nigehbaan (Mali).
(3) Use nichodne wala.
(4) Use Peene wala.
(5) Use Pilane wala.
(6) Uska uthane wala.
(7) Jiski taraf uthai jay.
(8) Uska bechne wala.
(9) Uski khareedari karne wala.
(10) Uski Qeemat khane wala."
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)
__________________________
Detail is link mein padhen:
*14th Gunahe Kabira:*
(Intoxication, Gambling, Music & Chess, Lottery)
https://www.al-islam.org/greater-sins-volume-1-ayatullah-sayyid-abdul-husayn-dastghaib-shirazi/fourteenth-greater-sin
___________________________
Beshak ye sab amal Gunahe Kabira mein se hai. Aur ye Shaitani amal hai aur inke zariye woh apni sazishen rachta hai. Bughz  o Adawat paida karta, Allah ke Zikr o Namaz se rokta hai.
😭
Yazid mein ye sab cheezen payi jaati thi, Sharab peeta, Juwa aur shatranj (chess) khelta aur bhi bahut kuchh. Imam Husain (as) isi burai mitaane Karbala pahunche. Jabke Yazeed Islam ko ek khel samjh raha tha. Jaisa ke Imam Zamana (atfs) Ziyarat e Nahiya mein farmate hain Yazeed ne Imam Husain (as) ko nahi Islam ko qatl kar raha tha.
_"La'anat ho us Fasiq giroh par, jisne Aap ko qatl karke Islam ko qatl kiya aur Namaz wa Roze ko mua'ttal kar diya, Ahkam wa Sunan e Ilahi ki nafarmani ki, Imaan ki buniyadon ko hila diya, Ayat e Qurani mein tehreef ki aur baghawat o dushmani mein dhansta chala gaya."_
(Ziyarat e Nahiya)

Ye Shaitani sazishon ka natija tha. Aur Dushmane Ahle Bait (as) ne Shaitan ke kaam ko bakhubi anjam diya.

Bare Ilaha hame koi gham na de siwae Ghame Husain (as) ke.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😭
Rasoole Khuda (saww) jab bimar hue jiski wajah unki Shahadat hui (zeher ke asar se), Imam Husain (as) ko bulaya aur apne seene lagaya jabke maut ka paseena unse zahir ho raha tha, tab farmaya:
_"Yazeed se mera kiya lena dena? Parwardigar us par rozi irsaal mat farma, Parwardigar, Yazeed par Teri La'anat ho."_
Phir ghasi tari hui aur jab hosh aya, Imam (as) ko bosa diya jabke Ankhon se Aansu jari the aur farmaya:
_*"Agah raho! Mera aur tumhare Qatil Allah ke saamne hazir hoga (Jo hamare darmiyan faisla karega.)"*_
(Raavi Ibne Abbas, Muserrul Ahzan by Jafar bin Mohd bin Nima Hilli, Nafasul Mahmoom, Sec 2, Pg: 66-67, H-37)

      ♦ _*ITAA'AT (OBEDIENCE)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (763)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ وَأَطِيعُوا الرَّسُولَ وَاحْذَرُوا ۚ فَإِنْ تَوَلَّيْتُمْ فَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّمَا عَلَىٰ رَسُولِنَا الْبَلَاغُ الْمُبِينُ*

_"Aur Allah ki Ita'at karo aur Rasool (saww) ki ita'at karo aur unki nafarmani se bach jao aur agar tumne hukm e adooli ki (amal mein phir gaye) to tumhe maloom hona chahiye ke hamare Rasool (saww) par sirf sirf hukm pahuncha dene ki zimmedari thi."_
(Surah Maeda: 92)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is ayat mein Ita'at ka Hukm diya Allah aur Rasool (saww) ki. Means Allah jo hukm Rasool (saww) par nazil karta hai Rasool (saww) woh logon ko pahuncha dete hain, ab log maane ya na maane, amal karen ya na karen. Rasool (saww) ke hukm woh sab cheezen shamil hain jo Rasool (saww) ne logon ko batayi, Islami Taa'leemat, Sharaii Ahkamat, Aqaed, Ma'arif e Islami, Rasool (saww) ka kisi ko muqarrar karna...waghaira. Kiyonki Rasoolallah (saww) jo kuchh kahenge woh hukm Khuda kahenge. Isliye ye ita'at baghair chu chara wa baghair kisi sharait ke hai. Yahan hame Rasool (saww) ke saamne tasleem hona hoga. Ghadeer mein Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ko sabka Khalifa declare kiya, Ummat ka farz hai manna. Ab nahi maana to natija Karbala ke waqea ki surat pesh ayi. Agar Rasool (saww) ki Ummat unki ita'at karti to unke baad 73 firqe na hote.

Bare Ilaha hame Teri aur Tere Rasool ki ita'at karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Shaikh Jafar bin Mohd Qawlawayh Qummi se rivayat hai ke ek Din Imam Husain (as) Imam Hasan (as) ke paas gaye. Jab Imam Husain (as) ne Imam Hasan (as) ko dekha to girya karne lage. Imam Hasan (as) ne daryaft kiya:
_"Ya Aba Abdullah! Aap ne girya kiyon kiya."_
Imam Husain (as) ne farmaya ke jo tum par Masaib padne wale hain us par.
Imam Hasan (as) ne farmaya:
_*"Mere Masaib wo ghatak /mohlik zeher hoga, lekin mera koi bhi Din tumhare kisi Din ke barabar nahi. 30 hazar hamare Nana ki tabedari ka dawa karne wali Ummat muttahid ho kar tum par hamla karegi, tumhara khoon karegi, hurmat ki khilafwarzi karegi,  Aurton aur Bachcho ko qaid karegi, tumhare kheme lootegi. Us waqt Bani Umayya par Allah ka Azaab nazil hoga, Aasmaan se khoon ki barish hogi, tamam ashuya tum par matam karegi, yahan tak ke jangli janwar, daryaon mein Machhliyan tumhare Masaeb par matam karengi."*_
(Museerul Ehzan, Nafasul Mahmoom, Sec 2, Pg: 67-68, H-39)

          ♦ _*HARAAM GHAZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (762)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَيْسَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ جُنَاحٌ فِيمَا طَعِمُوا إِذَا مَا اتَّقَوْا وَآمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ ثُمَّ اتَّقَوْا وَآمَنُوا ثُمَّ اتَّقَوْا وَأَحْسَنُوا ۗ وَاللَّهُ يُحِبُّ الْمُحْسِنِينَ*

_"Jo log Imaan laye aur Nek Amal kiye unhone pahle jo khaya piya hoga unse uski giraft nahi hogi basharteke woh Haram cheezon se bachte rahen aur Imaan par qayem rahen aur Nek Aamaal karte rahen, phir jis jis cheez se roka jaye usse ruken aur farmane Ilahi ho us maane, phir Khuda Tarsi (Khauf e khuda) ke saath Nek rawayya rakhen. Allah Nek kirdaar logon ko pasand karta hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 93)

📚📖 🕋 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasoole Akram (saww) se sawal hua ke woh jo abhi jang mein Shaheed hue aur pahle woh Kafir the, unhone jo khaya piya uska kiya?
Aap (saww) ne jawab mein ye Ayat padhi (5:93) yani unse pichhla koi hisab nahi hoga lekin ab jo bhi woh gunah karega uski saza usko milegi.
Umar ke saamne ek mulzim Qadam bin Maz'oom ko laya gaya, usne Sharaab pi thi. Umar ne Hazrat Ali (as) se poochha iski saza kiya hai. Aap (as) ne farmaya 80 kode mare jayen. Usne jirah ki aur kaha ke mera talluq is Ayat se hai (Maeda:93) kiyonki woh pahle kafir tha ab Musalman hua. Ali (as) ne kaha nahi tu is Ayat ka misdaq nahi hai, tujhe saza milegi. (Is tarah Hazrat Ali (as) faisle kiya karte the.

Bare Ilaha hame Nek Raah chalne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😭
Ibne Abbas se rivayat hai ke ek Din mein Rasoole Akram (saww) ke huzoor mein baitha ke Imam Hasan (as) tashreef laye. Jaise hi Rasool (saww) ki nigah Imam Hasan (as) par padi unhone girya karna shuru kiya farmaya:
_"Aao mere paas, aao mere paas."_
Aur apni dayen tarah baithaya. Phir Imam Husain (as) ko bayen taraf baithaya. Phir Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) tashrif layi aur Rasool (saww) ne girya karte hue saamne bhaithne ko kaha, phir Ali (as) tashreef laye aur dayen taraf baithe. Unhone kaha aap hame dekh girya kar rahe hain kiya ham mein se koi aisa nahi jo aap ko khush kar sake?
Phir Rasoole Akram (saww) ne farmaya:
_*"Mein Uski Qasam kha ke kahta hun Jisne mujhe Nabuwwat ke Asl darje par Faiz kiya poori Kainat par Fazilat ata ki. Inse pyara mere liye koi nahi. Mera girya unke upar mere baad hone wali musibat par hai. Mein dekh raha hun mere bete Husain par jo zulm hone wala hai. Ye aisa hai ke jaise mein dekh raha hun ke woh meri Qabr par pana le rahe hain ya Ka'abe mein  lekin koi unhe wahan rukne nahi deta. Phir woh us jagah ki taraf rukh karenge jo unka jae Shahadat, Musibat o Bala hai. Jabke ek giroh unki nusrat karega jo Qayamat ke Din meri Ummat ke Shohada ke sardar honge. Jaise ke mein dekh raha hun ke un par teeron ki barish ho rahi hai aur woh zameen par gire. Phir woh zalimana taur par bhed ki tarah zabah kar denge."*_
Ye sun kar sab zor zor se girya karne lage phir Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_*"Ya Allah! Mein shikwa karta hun mere baad jo meri Aal (as) par zulm o sitam honge."*_
(Nafasul Mahmoom, Sec 2, Pg-67, H-38)
