       ♦ _*SHIKAR (HUNTING)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (764)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَيَبْلُوَنَّكُمُ اللَّهُ بِشَيْءٍ مِنَ الصَّيْدِ تَنَالُهُ أَيْدِيكُمْ وَرِمَاحُكُمْ لِيَعْلَمَ اللَّهُ مَنْ يَخَافُهُ بِالْغَيْبِ ۚ فَمَنِ اعْتَدَىٰ بَعْدَ ذَٰلِكَ فَلَهُ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Allah Yaqeenan tumhe us Shikar ke zariye se azmaega jo tumhare haathon aur Nezon ki zad mein hoga taake woh ye dekhe ke tum mein se kaun Us se ghayebana darta hai. Phir jisne is tanbeeh ke baad bhi ziyadti ki to uske liye dardnaak Azaab hai."_
(Surah Maeda: 94)

📚📖 🤺
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne Musalmanon ki azmaish ke liye har jagah ka Shikar unke liye jama kar diya tha aur Shikar itna qareeb aa gaya tha jise woh apne haathon se pakad sakte the aur woh unke Nezon ke zad mein tha aur Shikar Umrah-e-Hudaibiya mein Musalmanon ke liye jama kiya gaya tha."_
(Al Kaafi)
Test ye tha ke gunah ke liye sab cheezen saamne muhayya kar di yani asaani se shikar kiya jaa sakta tha lekin Ehram ki halat mein pabandi laga di. Taake dekha jaa sake kaun Hukm ka palan karta hai. Ye usi tarah se hai ke Ramzan mein aapni saamne Khaana, Paani sab hai lekin Hukme Khuda wandi baja laate hui aap Roze se hain kuchh Khaa pi nahi rahe. Ya Haram cheezon se parhez karna. Yehi Test hai. Duniya Examination Hall hai, yaha sab ko Test dena hai. Isse koi bach nahi sakta, ab chahe woh paas ho ya fail ho.

Bare Ilaha hame is Duniya ke azmaishon mein Kamyab hone ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😭
*(Is series ki 40th aur Akheri Hadees)*
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
"Jab Rasoole Akram (saww) ko Me'raj ki Raat Aasmaano mein le jaya gaya to Allah ne unse farmaya ke _"Mein tumhara 3 tarah se Test lunga taake tumhare Sabr ki inteha maloom ho."_
Rasoole akram (saww):
_"Ya Allah! Mein Tere Hukm ke aage apne aap ko Tere hawale karta hun! Lekin mein Tere Azmaishon ko bardasht karne ki salahiyat nahi rakhta. Barae meherbani, woh 3 tareeqe kiya hai, zara muje bata?"_
Unhe bataya gaya ke is mein pahli "Bhook" hai. Apni aur apne Ayaal se zyada Miskeen ko zyada tarjeeh dena.
Aap (saww):
_"Mein qubool karta hun Ay Parwardigar! Mein raazi hun aur Tere Hukm ke saamne apna sar jhukata hun, jabke Ne'mat o Sabr sab Teri taraf se hai."_
Doosre ye hai ke Jhooti Tohmatein jo Aap (saww) par log lagayenge, Khauf o Khatarat, apni zindagi ko Mere raaste mein khairat karna aur Kafir taaqaton se hayat o maal se ladna, unke Munafeqeen ke haathon jo takleefen aur mushkilat uthaoge us par Sabr karna, Jang ke maidan ki mushkilat o Pareshaniyan aur zakhm.
Aap (saww):
_"Mein qubool karta hun Ay Parwardigar! Mein raazi hun aur Tere Hukm ke saamne apna sar jhukata hun, jabke Ne'mat o Sabr sab Teri taraf se hai."_
Teesre ye hai ke tumhare baad tumari Aal (as) par jo Masaeb wa Shahadat hogi use bardasht karna hoga. Aur tumhare chachere bhai (Ali (as)) ko galiyon, Tanqeed, Daman ka Saamna karna padega, shiddat o zulm ke alawa hataash ka saamna karna padega.
Aap (saww):
_"Mein qubool karta hun Ay Parwardigar! Mein raazi hun aur Tere Hukm ke saamne apna sar jhukata hun, jabke Ne'mat o Sabr sab Teri taraf se hai."_
Tumhari dukhtar Fatima ko bhi ye Masaeb bardasht karne honge. Phir Tumhare cousin Ali (as) se do Farzand honge jin mein se ek (Imam Hasan as) ko buzdil qatl karenge, unka maal lootenge, Nezon se zakhmi honge. Jabke ye sab kaam tumhari Ummat karegi.
Aap (saww):
_*"Mein qubool karta hun Ay Parwardigar! إِنَّا للهِ وَإِنَّـا إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعون Beshak ham Allah ke hai, aur Us hi ki taraf palatne wale hain. Mein raazi hun aur Tere Hukm ke saamne apna sar jhukata hun, jabke Ne'mat o Sabr sab Teri taraf se hai."*_
(Nafasul Mahmoom-Shaikh Abbas Qummi, Sec 2, Pg: 68-69

        ♦ _*SHIKAR (HUNTING)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (765)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَقْتُلُوا الصَّيْدَ وَأَنْتُمْ حُرُمٌ ۚ وَمَنْ قَتَلَهُ مِنْكُمْ مُتَعَمِّدًا فَجَزَاءٌ مِثْلُ مَا قَتَلَ مِنَ النَّعَمِ يَحْكُمُ بِهِ ذَوَا عَدْلٍ مِنْكُمْ هَدْيًا بَالِغَ الْكَعْبَةِ أَوْ كَفَّارَةٌ طَعَامُ مَسَاكِينَ أَوْ عَدْلُ ذَٰلِكَ صِيَامًا لِيَذُوقَ وَبَالَ أَمْرِهِ ۗ عَفَا اللَّهُ عَمَّا سَلَفَ ۚ وَمَنْ عَادَ فَيَنْتَقِمُ اللَّهُ مِنْهُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَزِيزٌ ذُو انْتِقَامٍ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Haalate Ehram mein Shikar na karo agar tum mein se jaan boojh kar koi aisa kare to woh Jaanwar usne mara ho usi ke ham palla ek Janwar use maveshiyon mein base dena hoga jiska Kaffare mein chand masakeen ko khana khilana hoga ya uske mutabiq Roze rakhne honge taake woh apne kiye ka maza chakhe. Pahle jo kuchh guzar chuka hai Allah ne use Ma'af kar diya hai lekin ab agar kisi ne isko repeat kiya to Allah usse inqaam lega, Allah Ghalib aur Badla Lenewala hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 95)

📚📖 🕋 🤺
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Ehram bandh lo to tamam jandaron ke maarne se parhez karo. Saanp (Snake), Bichhoo aur Choohe ko maarne ki ijazat hai. Chooha Mashk mein suraakh (hole) karta hai aur diye ko ulat kar ghar mein Aag lagne ka sabab banta hai. Bichhoo moozi (danger) janwar hai ke ek martaba Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne ek patthar ki haath badhaya to Bichhoo ne Aap (saww) ko dang mara. Anhazrat (saww) ne farmaya: Tujh par Khuda ki La'anat ho tu na to Aadmi ka Haya karta hai aur na kisi bure ko chhodta hai. Aur jahan tak Saanp ka maamla hai to agar woh tum par hamla karna chahe to use maar do aur agar tum par hamla awar na ho to use kuchh na kaho. Isi tarah se bawla Kutta aur darinda tujh par hamla karne lagen to unhe mar do aur agar woh tum par hamla na karen to unhe kuchh na kaho. Aur siya rang ke Saanp ko har haalat mein mar do. Kawwe aur "حدٱة" (Hudaah-Chandol) ko Oont ki pusht par baith kar Patthar se uda do."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🐍, 🦂, 🐁, 🐕, 🐪

Kaffara mein ham pallah Janwar hona iske baare mein ikhtelaf hai. Aksar Ahle ilm ka nazariya hai ke mumaselat (similarity) ka khayal rakha jaye. Lehaza Shutar Murgh ke badle Oont aur Zebra ya us jaise janwar ke liye ek Gay aur Hiran aur khargosh ke liye ek Bakri Kaffare mein deni chahiye.
(Noorus Saqlain)
🐐🐇🦌🐮🐪
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hiran ke badle mein Bakri aur Zebra ke badle mein Gay aur Shutar Murgh ke badle mein Doodh dene wali Oontni Kaffara mein di jayegi."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam)

Qurbani ke barabar Roze kaise rakhe jayen?
Imam Zainul Abidin (as):
_"Qurbani ki qeemat lagayi jaye gi. Phir ye andaza kiya jayega ke is qeemat se kitna ghalla khareeda ja sakta hai, phir us ghalla ke Saa' (صاع) (3 Kg) banaye jayenge aur har aadhe Saa' ke badle use ek Roza rakhna hoga."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih)
🥗 🦊 🐍
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Ayat akhiri hisse ke bare mein)
"Ek shakhs ne Haalate Ehram mein ek Lomdi (Fox) ko pakda aur Aag uske chehre ke qareeb ki. Lomdi Aag ko dekh kar cheekhti aur chillati thi. Uske Saathiyon ne use is harkat se mana kiya. Kuchh der baad usne Lomdi ko chhod diya. Jab woh shakhs soya to achanak ek Saanp aaya aur woh uske munh mein dakhil ho gaya. Usne bhi us tarah se cheekhna  shuru kiya jis tarah se Lomdi cheekhi thi. Phir kuchh der baad Saanp uske munh se nikal kar chala gaya."
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Hajj o Umrah karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

🙇
"Zawa Adl ذواعدل" mein Alif kitabat ki ghalti se aya hai aur asl lafz "Zu Adl ذوعدل" hai. Adl se murad Rasoole Akram (saww) aur Zu Adl se murad Imam hai."
(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Al Kaafi, Roza e Kaafi, Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

       ♦ _*SHIKAR (HUNTING)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (766)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أُحِلَّ لَكُمْ صَيْدُ الْبَحْرِ وَطَعَامُهُ مَتَاعًا لَكُمْ وَلِلسَّيَّارَةِ ۖ وَحُرِّمَ عَلَيْكُمْ صَيْدُ الْبَرِّ مَا دُمْتُمْ حُرُمًا ۗ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ الَّذِي إِلَيْهِ تُحْشَرُونَ*

_"Tumhare liye samandar ka Shikar aur uska khana Halal kar diya gaya hai. Tum khud bhi us se iska istemal kar sakte ho aur Qafile ke liye zade rah (provision) bhi bana sakte ho. Albatta jab tak tum Ehram mein raho us waqt tak tum par khushki ka shikar Haram hai. Us Khuda ki nafarmani se bachte raho jiske saamne tumhe pesh kiya jayega."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 96)

📚📖 🕋 🐟🦈
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ehram ki haalat mein Machhli (Fish) ka Shikar karne mein koi harj nahi hai aur Mohram (jo Ehram mein hai) Namak lagi hui Khushk (dry) Machhli kha sakta hai aur use zade rah ke taur par apne saath le ja sakta hai."_
_"Woh Parinda jo khushki par rahta hai aur khushki (sookhi jagah) par hi Ande deta ho aur uske chooze bhi khushki par hi paida hote hon to wo parinda shumar kiya jayega aur jo Parinda khushki par rahta hi aur samandar mein Ande deta ho aur samandar mein us ke chooze nikalte hon to woh Parinda Samandari Parinda shumar kiya jayega."_
_"Har woh cheez jiski asl samandar mein ho aur woh khushki aur tari dono par rahta ho to Haalate Ehram mein use nahi maarna chahiye aur koi use maarega to use uska Kaffara dena hoga."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Halaal Ghaza khaane ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ _*KA'ABA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (767)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*جَعَلَ اللَّهُ الْكَعْبَةَ الْبَيْتَ الْحَرَامَ قِيَامًا لِلنَّاسِ وَالشَّهْرَ الْحَرَامَ وَالْهَدْيَ وَالْقَلَائِدَ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ لِتَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Allah ne Makan-e-Mohtaram Ka'aba ko logo ke liye qayam ka zariya banaya aur Mahe Haraam, Qurbani ke Janwaron aur Qalladon ko bhi hurmat di hai taake tumhe ye ilm ho sake ke Aasmaano aur Zameen mein jo kuchh bhi hai Allah ko uski Khabar hai aur Allah har cheez ka jannewala hai."_
(Surat Ma'idah: 97)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne Ka'aba Sharif ko logon ke Deen aur unki Ma'aash (Finance) ke qayem rahne ka zariya banaya."_
"Allah ne Hajj, Ka'aba ya Ka'aba ki tanseeb ko logon ki Ma'eeshat (Finance) aur karobar ke qayem rahne ka zariya banaya hai kiyonki Ka'aba Sharif mein har waqt logon ki aamad o raft ka silsila jaari rahta hai jiski wajah se logon ki Ma'eeshat qayem rahti hai kiyonki logon ki har waqt ki aamad o raft se Tijarat (Business) ko furogh milta hai jisse bahut si barakaat hasil hoti hain. Isi liye mashhoor taba'ii Saeed bin Jubair ne kaha tha ke is Ghar ki Ziyarat ke liye jo bhi ayega agar woh Duniya ka khwahishmand hoga to use Duniya milegi aur agar woh Akherat ka khwahishmand hoga to use Akherat ki Ne'mat milegi."
(Tafseer Ayyashi, Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🕋
Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya gaya:
"Akhir Hajj par jaane ki aur waha daulat kharch karne ki kiya zaroorat hai. Agar yehi daulat guraba wa masakeen mein taqseem kar di jaye to ye behtar hai?"
Imam (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Ye log jhoot kahte hain. Agar log aisa karne lag gaye to Baitullah mu'attal ho jayegi jabke Allah ne us Ghar ko logon ke qayam ka zariya banaya hai."_
(Ilalush Sharay)
🕋
Rasool e Khuda (saww) se Yahoodi ne sawal kiya:
" "Ka'aba" ko Ka'aba kiyonki kaha jaata hai?"
Aap (saww) ne jawab diya: _"kiyonki ye Duniya ke wast (Centre) mein waqe hai."_
🕋
Imam Sadiq (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Kiyonki wo Murabba مربع (Square) shakl ka hai."_
Raavi ne poochha Square shape kiyon hai?
Aap (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Wo isliye Square Shape mein hai ke wo char Kalemat par qayem hai aur wo Kalemat ye hain:_
*سُبْحَانَ اللهِ وَ الْحَمْدُ لِلّهِ وَ لاَ إلهَ إلاَّ اللهُ وَ اللهُ أكْبَرُ*"
Sawal kiya gaya "Baitullah" *بيت الله* ko *"بيت الله الحرام"* "Baitullahil Haraam" kiyon kaha jata hai?"
Aap (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Kiyonki us mein Mushrekin ka dakhila Haraam hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame bhi Hajj e Baitullah ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕋
Hazrat Ali (as)
ne logo'n ko Ka'aba ke gird tawaaf karte dekha aur farmaya, _"Ye log Jahiliyyat mein bhi isi tarah tawaaf kiya karte the. Unhe hukm diya gaya hai ke Ka'aba ka tawaaf kar ke hamare paas aayein aur apni Wilayat aur mohabbat hamare liye zaahir karein aur apni nusrat ko hum par pesh karein, TAB UNKA HAJJ QUBOOL HOGA."_ Phir aap ne ye Ayat padhi (Ibrahim (as) ne Khana e Kaaba banaate waqt Khuda se Dua ki) "Logo'n Ka Dil Meri Zurriyat Ki Taraf Jhuka Dena," yaani "unke dilo'n mein mohabbat de dena."
(Surah Ibrahim, Ayat 37)
(Al Kaafi, v2, p400)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦ _*KA'ABA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (768)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*اعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Tumhe maloom hona chahiye ke Allah Azaab dene mein bhi sakht hai aur is saath saath Woh Bakhshne wala aur Meherban hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 98)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _*Tafseer:*_ (5:97 Cont'd)
Ayat 97 mein Ka'aba ka tazkara tha.
Ka'aba ka Root word hai *"كعب"* means paon ke upar ki ubhri hui jagah. Baad mein ye lafz har bulandi aur ubhri hui cheez ke liye istemal hone laga. Ka'aba ek Aala maqam aur Khuda ka Ghar hai.
Ka'aba ke bare mein kuchh aur Ahadees:
🕋
_"Ka'aba ka veeran karna Paighambar (saww) aur Imam (as) ke qatl karne ke barabar hai. Iski taraf dekhna Ibaadat aur iske gird Tawaf karna behtareen Amal mein se hai."_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Munasib nahi hai ke koi shakhs apna ghar Ka'aba se ooncha banaye."_
(Safinatul Bihar, Vol 2, P-482)
Jabke ham dekhte hain Ka'aba ko oonchi oonchi imarton ne gher rakha hai.
🕋
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Khuda ne apne Ghar ko ek khushk (dry) jali hui aur sakht pahadon ke darmiyan wali zameen mein qarar diya hai aur hukm diya hai ke ise bahut hi saada masale se banaya jaye, aam aur mamooli Patthar se."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Khutba 92)

Beshak Allah hi Jabbar o Qahhar hai, aur Ghafoor bhi hai, Bare Ilaha hame Apne Fazl Insaaf karna na ke Adl se.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
Tafseer Ayat (5:98)
Imam Sadiq (as) ne apne Aba e Taherin Rivayat karte hai ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Jibrael (as) se ye baat suni:
_"Jo shakhs koi Gunah-e-Sagheera kare ya Gunah-e-Kabira kare aur woh ye na jaanta ho ke Mujhe ye Ikhtiyar hasil hai chahun to use Azaab dun aur chahu to Ma'af kar dun, aise shakhs ko Mein kabhi bhi Ma'af nahi karunga. Aur jo shakhs koi Sagheera ya Kabira Gunah kare aur ye jaanta ho ke Mujhe ye Ikhtiyar hasil hai chahun to use Azaab dun, chahun to use Ma'af kar dun, aise shakhs ko mein Ma'af kar dunga."_
(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

              ♦ _*HIDAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (769)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا عَلَى الرَّسُولِ إِلَّا الْبَلَاغُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مَا تُبْدُونَ وَمَا تَكْتُمُونَ*

_"Rasool par sirf Paigham pahuchane ki zimmedari hai aur Allah janta hai jo kuchh tum zahir kar rahe ho aur jo kuchh tum chhupa rahe ho."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 99)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Anbiya wa Rasool jinko Allah ne hamari hidayat ke waste bheje unki zimmedari sirf Allah ka Paigham ham tak pahuchane ki thi isliye Paighambar kahte hain. Allah ne 313 Rasool nai Shariyat ke saath bheje. Lekin iski koi guarantee nahi ke Rasool ki Shariyat par unki Ummat baqi rahe. Ye kaam Rasool ke Janashin/Khalifa ka hai ke woh Shariyat ki ijra (execute) kare. Imam ya Janashin bhi Hidayat karte hain aur logon ke mushkilat ko door karte hain. Ummat ko Deen se jode rakhna Imam ka kaam hai. Lekin agar Ummat Rasool ya Imam ki baat na maane, Shariyat par amal na kare to Ummat Zimmedar hai na ke Hadi wa Rahbar. Deen mein koi Jabr nahi hai. Jo Shakhs Gunah ka murtakib hoga woh uska zimmedar hoga. Allah har shakhs ke amal ko dekh raha hai chahe woh zahir mein kare ya chhup kar. Allah usko saza ya jaza dega.
Ab jo log sawal karte hain ke Imam Husain (as) ko Yazid ke moo nahi lagna tha, kiyon Karbala gaye, kiyon Yazeed se muqabela kiya? Yazeed Imam Husain (as) ke qatl ka zimmedar nahi hai, woh to Umar e Saad ya Shimr ne aisa kiya.
Iska jawab bhi same hai, Imam Husain (as) ka kam tha Hidayat karna aur Deen o Shariyat ko bachana. Imam Husain (as) ne Shariyat ki hifazat mein apni qurbani di. Yazeed Islami Shariyat ko khatm karna chahta tha. Jo jo bhi Imam Husain (as) ke qatl mein shamil the sab zimmedar hain. Yazeed ke hi hukm se ye sab hua. Kiya ek Qaatil ko Allah Ma'af kar sakta hai? Hargiz nahi. Ye sawalat sirf Yazeedi hamnawa karte hain jinhen Imam Husain (as) balke Ahle Bait e Athaar (as)  se koi lagao nahi hai. Allah unke dilon ko janta hai jo woh chhupate hain.

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Mukhlis bandon mein shumar kar.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Husain (as):
_"(Mere Allah!) Usne kya paaya jisne Tujhe khoya aur usne kuchh na khoya, jisne Tujh ko paa liya. Wo yaqeenan na-kaam huwa jo Tere bajaaye kisi aur ko pasand karne laga aur wo ghaatee mein padaa jo sarkashi ke saath Tujh se phir gaya. Kyun kar Tere gair se ummeed rakhte hain jab ke Tera ehsaan o karam rukta hi nahi aur kyun kar Tere gair se maangte hain, jab ke Tere fazl o ehsaan karne ki aadat mein tabdili nahi aati."_
(Dua e Arafa)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*FAASIQ RAHNUMA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (770)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ لَا يَسْتَوِي الْخَبِيثُ وَالطَّيِّبُ وَلَوْ أَعْجَبَكَ كَثْرَةُ الْخَبِيثِ ۚ فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ يَا أُولِي الْأَلْبَابِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Aap kah dijiye ke Khabees (Napaak) aur Paak barabar nahi hai khwah Napaak logon ki kasrat tumhe kitni hi bhali kiyon na lagti ho. Aye Aqalmand logo! Allah se darte raho taake tum kamyab ho sako."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 100)

📚📖 🖐🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Khabees (Napaak) aur Paak kabhi barabar nahi ho sakte ye Usool Allah ne is Ayat mein bata diya. Allah ne Qur'an mein hi Ahle Bait (as) ki Ismat o Taharat ka Ailan kar diya hai (33:33). Ab jo inko follow karega Paak ho jayega aur Paak afraad hi in hastiyon ko follow kar sakte hai. Paak hastiyon ke muqabile mein Khabees afraad hain, to unke followers bhi Napaak honge. Ab koi chahe ke dono ko follow kare to ye aqlan o usoolan mahaal hai. Paak aur Napaak ek jagah jama nahi ho sakte. Allah ne ye bhi bataya ke Napaak logon ki majority zyada hai, iska matlab ye nahi ke woh sab haq par hain. Kabhi kabhi koi burai itni aam ho jaati hai ke woh sab ko achhi lagne lagti hai. Misal ke taur aksariyat khaane peene mein Najis Paak ka khayal nahi karti, jaise Kafir ke haath ka khaana, agar koi ek shakhs kahta hai ke mein nahi khaata to khud Musalman tajjub karte hain. Music sarihan Haraam hai lekin itni common ho gayi hai ke log usko justify karte hain.
Iski wajah yehi hai ke log Allah ko bhool jate hai, Allah ka khauf bilkul khatm ho jata hai. Yahan is ayat mein Allah Aqalmando se khitab kar raha hai. Sirf Aqalmand log hi is Usool ko qubool kar sakte hain. Jisne Khabeeson ki pairavi ki woh Fasiq o Munafiq kahlay aur jisne Paak o Tahir ki pairavi ki woh Momin kahlaye aur Qur'an mein hi Allah Ta'ala farmata hai Momin aur Fasiq kabhi barabar nahi ho sakte. (32:18)

Imam Askari (as)
ne Surah Ankaboot, Ayat 56 ke zimn mein farmaya: _"Faasiq (paapi / ayyash) hukum-raan ki ita'at mat karo. Aur agar tumhe ye khauf hai ke wo tumhe apne muqaddas Deen se munharif (deviate) kar denge to Hijrat karo, kyun ki Hamari zameen bahut wasee (vast) aur kushaada (spacious) hai."_
(Zindagi Akhlaaq Ke Saaye Mein, p34)

Bare Ilaha hame Paak o Paakiza ke saath Qayamat ke Din mahshoor farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹
Imam Ali (as)
_"Khabardaar! Faasiqo'n (wicked / bad-kaaro'n) ki sohbat ikhtiyaar na karna kyun ki jo shakhs kisi qaum ke feyl (amal) se raazi hota hai, wo unhi mein shumaar hota hai."_
(Gorar ul Hakam, v1, p47)
🤓
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Faasiqo'n ki sohbat se bacho, is liye ke buraai buraai se mil hi jaati hai._"
(Adaab e Islami, v1, p262)
😎
Imam Ali (as)
_"Faasiq (ayyaash / wicked) logo'n ki sohbat se parhez karo kyun ki burayi burayi ke saath waabasta hoti hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p213)

                  *28th Safar 1439*
     *18th November 2017, Saturday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran:

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا مُحَمَّدٌ إِلَّا رَسُولٌ قَدْ خَلَتْ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ الرُّسُلُ ۚ أَفَإِنْ مَاتَ أَوْ قُتِلَ انْقَلَبْتُمْ عَلَىٰ أَعْقَابِكُمْ ۚ وَمَنْ يَنْقَلِبْ عَلَىٰ عَقِبَيْهِ فَلَنْ يَضُرَّ اللَّهَ شَيْئًا ۗ وَسَيَجْزِي اللَّهُ الشَّاكِرِينَ*

_"Muhammad (saww) iske siwa kuchh nahi ke bas ek Rasool hain, unse pahle aur Rasool bhi guzar chuke hain, phir agar woh guzar jayen ya qatl kar diye jayen to tum log ulte paon phir jaoge? Yaad rakho! Jo ulta phirega woh Allah ka kuchh nuqsaan nahi karega, Albatta jo Allah ka shukr guzar bande ban kar rahenge unhe Woh uski jaza dega."_
(Surah Aal-e-imran: 144)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj Shahadat e Rasoole Khuda (saww) Hai. Rasool (saww) ka gharana ranj o ghamzada hai. Ahle Bait (as) girya kuna hain. Aaj Anbiya wa Rasool ka Akheri fard is Duniya se rukhsat hua. Deen e Islam jo Rasoole Akram laye the us par khatre ke badal chhane lage. Musalman Masjide Nabawi mein jama hue. Lekin jahan Dafn o Kafan ki tayyari ho rahi thi to doosri taraf Saqeefa mein meeting ho rahi thi. Itni Musalmanon ki ta'adad hote hue Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke janaze mein kuchh hi Mo'meneen ki ta'daad thi. Rasoole Akram (saww) ke jaate hi log ulte pao phirne lage. Anhazrat (saww) ki mehnat par Paani phirne wala hi tha, lekin jiska Deen hai Usne isko baqi rakha. Unke phirne se Allah ke Deen ka koi nuqsan nahi hone wala. Kahin Islam Personal Jang ka shikar na ho isliye Hazrat Ali (as) jinhone itni bahaduri se Jange fatah ki, unhe khamoshi Ikhtiyar karni padi aur silent Hidayat ka silsilah shuru kiya. Is Ayat mein Allah ne un logon ki sataish ki jo log Haq ke saath rahe. Ye bahut bada saneha tha jahan se Islam guzra yahan tak ke Rasool (saww) ki Shahadat ki Ailan par bhi pabandi lagi, 3 Din tak Janaza rakha raha, pure Madina Shaher mein curfew jaisa mahaul tha, kuchh hi log Janaze mein shamil hue.
Balke ye silsilah aage bhi chalta raha. Aaj hi ke Din Imam Hasan (as) ki Shahadat hui. Unke Janaze par Ummat e Muslema ne Teer barsae.
Ayat Ale Imran:144 yehi ishara kar rahi hai ke Anbiya wa Rusul ko (zeher) se maut ayi ya qatl hue aur ye silsila age Aimma (as) ke liye bhi jaari raha. Lekin Deen e Islam baqi raha. Kiyonki Munafeqeen ne kitni hi sazishen ki lekin Islam ko koi nuqsan nahi pahuncha paye. Islam aaj tak zinda hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Shukr guzaron mein shamil rakh.

           ♦ _*BEJA SAWAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (771)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَسْأَلُوا عَنْ أَشْيَاءَ إِنْ تُبْدَ لَكُمْ تَسُؤْكُمْ وَإِنْ تَسْأَلُوا عَنْهَا حِينَ يُنَزَّلُ الْقُرْآنُ تُبْدَ لَكُمْ عَفَا اللَّهُ عَنْهَا ۗ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ حَلِيمٌ*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Aisi baaten mat poochho no tum par zahir kar di jayen to tumhe nagawar lagen lekin agar tum unhe aise waqt poochhoge jab Qur'an nazil ho raha ho to woh tum se bayan kar di jayengi. Allah ne pichhli baat Ma'af kar di Hai aur Allah Bakshne Wala, Burdbar hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 101)
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*
_*Shaane Nuzool:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
"Safiya binte Abdul Muttalib ka ek beta mar gaya. Woh bete ke Janaze par aa rahi thi ke ek shakhs ne us se kaha: Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki rishtedari use kuchh fayda na degi. Usne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se uski shikayat ki.
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Masjid mein farmaya:
_"Log ye guman kiyon kar rahe hain ke meri Qarabatdari fayda nahi degi. Agar Maqam e Mahmood qareeb kar diya jaye to main tumhari hajaat ke liye Shafa'at kar sakta hun. Aaj mujhse koi bhi apne Walid ke mutalliq poochhega to mein use uska haqeeqi walid bata dunga."_
Ye sun kar ek me sawal kiya ke uska Baap kaun hai. Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tu jiska beta mashhoor hai woh tera Baap nahi hai. Tera Baap falan bin falan hai."_
Iske baad ek shakhs aur utha aur usne bhi Aap (saww) se yehi sawal kiya. Aap (saww) ne farmaya tu jiski taraf mansoob hai wohi tera haqeeqi Baap hai. Phir Aap (as) ne farmaya: Woh shakhs mujhse apne Walid ke mutalliq kiyon nahi poochhta jo ye guman karta hai ke meri Qarabat kuchh fayda na degi? Ye sunkar woh shakhs utha aur kaha: "Ya Rasoolallah! Mein Allah aur uske Rasool ke ghazab se panah chata hun. Aap mukhe ma'af kar den. Us waqt ye Ayat nazil hui."
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Is Ayat mein Taqaddum o Takheer hai. Ayat ke Ma'ani ye hoga: "Aye Imaan Walo! Jin baton ko Allah ne chhod diya hai tum unke mutalliq sawal na karo."_
(Majmaul Bayan)
🎋
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Allah ne tum par kuchh faraez farz kiye hain unhe zaye na karo aur tumhare liye hudood muqarrar ki hain un se tajawuz na karo aur tumhe kuchh cheezon se mana' kiya Hai unka irtekab na karo aur kuchh cheezon se khamoshi ikhtiyar ki hai Allah ne unhe bhool kar nahi chhoda hai lehaza unke mutalliq guftugu na karo."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🍁
Imam Mahdi (atfs) ne Tauqee ke zariye Ishaaq bin Yaqoob ka Ghaibat ke mutalliq sawal ka jawab diya.
_"Jahan tak hamari Ghaibat ka ma'amla hai to Allah Ta'ala ka farman hai: (5:101) Mere Aba' e Taherin mein se har ek ki gardan mein uske Taghoot e zamana ki bayat ka qallada (phanda) raha hai, jab mein khurooj karunga to meri gardan mein kisi ki Bai'at ka qallada nahi hoga."_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Nema)

Bare Ilaha hame Mukhlis Nasirane Imam Mahdi (as) mein shamil farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

              ♦ _*BUT (IDOLS)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (772)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَدْ سَأَلَهَا قَوْمٌ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ ثُمَّ أَصْبَحُوا بِهَا كَافِرِينَ * مَا جَعَلَ اللَّهُ مِنْ بَحِيرَةٍ وَلَا سَائِبَةٍ وَلَا وَصِيلَةٍ وَلَا حَامٍ ۙ وَلَٰكِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا يَفْتَرُونَ عَلَى اللَّهِ الْكَذِبَ ۖ وَأَكْثَرُهُمْ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Tumse pahle ek giroh be isi qism ke sawal kiye the. Phir un baton ke Munkir ban gaye the."_
_"Allah ne na koi "Bahira" muqarrar kiya hai aur na "Sayba" na "Wasila" aur na "Haam". Lekin Kafiron ka ye watira hai ke woh Khuda par jhooti baatein taraashten hain aur unki aksariyat be Aql hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 102 - 103)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat no.102 Guzishta Ayat ke Sawal ke mauzoo par hai.
Zamana Jahiliyyat mein But parasti aam thi aur Buton ke alag naam se yaad kiya jata tha. India mein ye aaj tak jaari hai. Arab mein jin Buton ke bahut sare naam the, un mein se kuchh naam is Ayat mein diye hain.
🐪
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Zamana Jahiliyyat mein jab koi Oontni yake baad deegar do Nar (male) paida karti to woh kahte the ke usne _"Naron ka Wasaal"_ kiya hai. Use zabah karna Halaal nahi samajhte the aur use khaana jaez nahi jaante the. Jab koi Oontni 10 bachche janti to use "Sayba" ka naam dete the. Us par sawari karne aur uske gosht khane ko Haraam samajhte the. Aur "Haam" Oontni ke saand ko kahte the. Woh uska gosht khaana bhi jaez na samajhte the. Allah Ta'ala ne Ailan kiya ke Usne is tarah ka koi hukm nazil nahi kiya."
(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar)
🐪
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Amr bin Yahya bin Qama' bin Khandaf ki Makkah par Hukomat qayem hui thi. Deen e Islam ko sab se pahle usi ne tabdeel kiya tha. Usi ne But aur Moortiyan nasb ki thi aur usi ne "Bahira", "Sayba", "Wasila" aur "Haam" ka tasawwur diya tha. Meine dekha ke woh Dozakh mein jal raha tha aur uski badboo se Ahle Dozakh ko aziyyat mahsoos ho rahi thi."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamare andar jo but nasb hain unhe nikal phek.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Ali (as)
_"Wallah! Na mere baap ne buto'n ki parastish (idol-worship) ki, na mere dada Abdul Muttalib ne, na mere jadd e buzurg Janabe Hashim ne, na Abde Munaaf ne. Balke wo log Ka'abe ki jaanib rukh kar ke Namaz padhte the aur Deen e Ibrahim (as) par qaayam the aur Rasule Khuda (saww) ke Deen se mutamassik rahe."_
Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67

♦ _*RASOOL (SAW) KI NAFARMANI*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (773)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَوْا إِلَىٰ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ وَإِلَى الرَّسُولِ قَالُوا حَسْبُنَا مَا وَجَدْنَا عَلَيْهِ آبَاءَنَا ۚ أَوَلَوْ كَانَ آبَاؤُهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ شَيْئًا وَلَا يَهْتَدُونَ*

_"Aur jab unse kaha jata hai ke us Qanoon ki taraf aao jise Allah ne nazil kiya hai aur Rasool ke taraf aao, to woh jawab mein kahte hain ke hamare liye to bas wohi tareeqa kafi hai jis par hamne apne Baap Dada ko paya hai. Kiya unke Baap Dada hi ki Taqleed kiye chale jayenge khwah woh kuchh na jaante hon aur Sahih Raasta ki unhe khabar hi na ho?"_
(Surah Ma'idah: 104)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat mein Jahil Arbon ka rawayya Rasool (saww) ke saath kiya tha ye bataya gaya hai. Aap (saww) ne kitni hi hidayat ki lekin woh apni ravish par chalte rahe. Unhone yehi kaha ke unke Aba' o ajdad ki ravish unke liye kaafi hai.
Jab Rasool Akram (saww) ka Aakhri waqt aaya aur Aap (saww) ne qalam o kagaz manga ke mein Ummat ke liye Akhiri Wasiyat likh dun to ye kah diya gaya ke Qur'an hamare liye Kaafi hai. (Yani Ahle Bait (as) ki ab koi zaroorat nahi.) Ye bada saneha Rasool e Akram (saww) ki Shahadat ke pahle yani Jumerat ko hua aur Monday 28 Safar ko Aap (saww) is Duniya se rukhsat ho gaye. Aap (saww) ke jaate hi Aapki beti Janabe Fatema (saww) par zulm ke pahad toot pade. Aaj yani 1st Rabi ul Awwal Janabe Mohsin bin Ali (as) ki shahadat jo ke unke ghar par aag lagane aur Janabe Zehra (as) ke upar Darwaza girane ke natije mein hui.
Rasool (saww) ki wapas Jahiliyyat ke daur mein chali gayi jiske maani yehi nikle ke ham apne Aba' o Ajdad ko nahi bhoole hain aur unhi ki ravish par chalte rahenge. Sawal yeh hain ke unke Aba' o Ajdad ko to Ma'arefat thi hi nahi lekin Ummate Muslema ko to Rasoole Akram (saww) ne itni hidayat ki phir bhi woh Sahih Raaste se bhatak gayi. Faqat aaj tak Musalman yehi Dua manga raha hai Ya Allah mujhe Seedhe Raaste par chala, lekin use abhi tak Seedha Raasta mila nahi. Ahle Bait (as) ke dar ko chhod de to idhar udhar raahen bhatakte phirenge lekin Sahih Raasta nahi milega.
Ye mukhtasar khulasa tha, detail Tareekhi Kitabon mein refer kar sakte hain.
Kuchh detail is link mein refer karen.
👉🏻📖
_*Hadith of the pen and paper:*_
https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hadith_of_the_pen_and_paper

*اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ * صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ*
(Surah Fatihah: 6 - 7)

✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙄
Narrated Ibn 'Abbas:
_"When Allah's Apostle (may peace be upon him) was on his death-bed and in the house there were some people among whom was 'Umar bin Al-Khattab, The Prophet (may peace be upon him) said, "Come, let me write for you a statement after which you will not go astray." 'Umar said, *"The Prophet (may peace be upon him) is seriously ill and you have the Qur'an; so the Book of Allah is enough for us."* The people present in the house differed and quarrelled. Some said "Go near so that The Prophet (may peace be upon him) may write for you a statement after which you will not go astray," while the others said as Umar said. When they caused a hue and cry before The Prophet (may peace be upon him), Allah's Apostle (may peace be upon him) said, *"Go away!"* Narrated 'Ubaidullah: Ibn 'Abbas used to say, "It was very unfortunate that Allah's Apostle (may peace be upon him) was prevented from writing that statement for them because of their disagreement and noise."_
(Sahih Bukhari, Vol 7, Book 70, Hadith 573)
(Copied from Mobile App of Shahih Bukhari)

               ♦ _*AIB JOEE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (774)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا عَلَيْكُمْ أَنْفُسَكُمْ ۖ لَا يَضُرُّكُمْ مَنْ ضَلَّ إِذَا اهْتَدَيْتُمْ ۚ إِلَى اللَّهِ مَرْجِعُكُمْ جَمِيعًا فَيُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Tum bas apni fikr karo. Agar tum Sahih Raaste par hue to kisi ki gumrahi tumhe koi nuqsan nahi pahuncha sakti. Tum sab Ko Allah ke huzoor palat kar jana hai. Woh tumhe tumhare Aamaal ke mutalliq batla dega."_
(Surat Al-Ma'idah 105)
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Tum "Maroof" par amal karo aur "Munkir" se Parhez karo jab jab dekho ke log Duniya ko tarjeeh de rahe hain aur Bukhl ke taqazon par amal kiya ja raha hai aur khwahishat ki pairavi ki jaa rahi hai aur har shakhs apni apni ray par mar mitta hai to tujhe apne Nafs ki Islah ki taraf mutawajjah rahna chahiye. Logon ki khwaheshat ki parwa na karo."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Logon! Apni Islah karo aur logon ke oyoob ki talash mein mat raho aur logon ke shikwe na karo agar tum khud Nek hue to kisi ki gumrahi tumhe koi nuqsan na pahuchaygi."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
🎋
Imam Ali (as)
_"Kisi ke Aibo'n ke baare mein sochna bhi Aib hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)
🍃
Imam Ali (as)
_"Sab se bada aib ye hai ke tum oon baato'n ko doosro'n ke liye aib qaraar do jo tum mein khud maujood ho."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Aib)
🍂
Imam Ali (as)
_"Agar tum ek doosre ke Aibo'n (defects / buraaiyo'n) ko zaahir karne lag jaaoge to ek doosre ko Dafn karna chhor doge."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)
🍁
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Jo kisi Musalman ke Aib ko zaahir karega to Allah uske Aibo'n ko zaahir karega hatta usay khud apne ghar mein  be-izzat kar dega."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)

Bare Ilaha hame apne Amaal ki Islah karne ki taufeeq ata farma.

                 ♦ _*WASIYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (775)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا شَهَادَةُ بَيْنِكُمْ إِذَا حَضَرَ أَحَدَكُمُ الْمَوْتُ حِينَ الْوَصِيَّةِ اثْنَانِ ذَوَا عَدْلٍ مِنْكُمْ أَوْ آخَرَانِ مِنْ غَيْرِكُمْ إِنْ أَنْتُمْ ضَرَبْتُمْ فِي الْأَرْضِ فَأَصَابَتْكُمْ مُصِيبَةُ الْمَوْتِ ۚ تَحْبِسُونَهُمَا مِنْ بَعْدِ الصَّلَاةِ فَيُقْسِمَانِ بِاللَّهِ إِنِ ارْتَبْتُمْ لَا نَشْتَرِي بِهِ ثَمَنًا وَلَوْ كَانَ ذَا قُرْبَىٰ ۙ وَلَا نَكْتُمُ شَهَادَةَ اللَّهِ إِنَّا إِذًا لَمِنَ الْآثِمِينَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Jab tum mein se kisi ki Maut ka waqt aa jaye aur woh Wasiyat kar raha ho to uske liye Shahadat ka nisaab ye hai ke tum mein se do Sahibe Adl afraad gawah banaye jayen ya agar tum safar ki haalat mein ho aur wahan Maut ki musibat pesh aye to ghair logon mein se hi do gawah le liye jayen. Phir agar koi shak mein pad jaye to Namaz ke baad dono gawahon ko rok liya jaye aur woh Khuda ki Qasam kha kar kahen ke ham kisi zaati mafad ke tahet gawahi nahi bechenge khwah koi hamara rishtedar bhi kiyon na ho. Phir bhi ham sachchi gawahi denge aur ham Khuda Waaste ki gawahi ko nahi chhupayenge, aur agar hamne aisa kiya to ham Gunahgaron mein shumar kiye jayenge."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 106)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ke shaane nuzool mein ye waqea marqoom hai:
3 Afraad ne Madine se Shaam ka safar kiya: Tameem bin Aus Al Dari aur uska bhai Adi aur Amr bin Al Aas Al Sahmi ka Ghulam Ibne Abi Marya. Dono bhai Christians the. Lekin Ibne Abi Marya Muslim tha. Ibne Abi Marya bimar hua to usne apna sara samaan apne Saathiyon ko diya aur wasiyat ki ke uske waris ko pahucha den aur inteqal ho gaya. Saathiyon ne uske samaan mein se qeemti cheezen nikali aur baqi uske waris ko de diya. Lekin jab us qeemti cheez ke bare poochha to inkar kar diya. Rasool (saww) ke saamne pesh kiye to wahan bhi jhoota halaf naama diya. Lekin jab unke ghar ki talaashi li to wo qeemti cheezen bhi mil gayi. Phir ye 3 Ayaten nazil hui.
(Majmaul Bayan, Tafseer e Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Imaandari se chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏼
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Talaaq aur Royat e Hilaal (Moonsight) ke liye Aurton ki gawahi kaafi nahi hai kiyonki woh Royat (sight) se zaeef hain aur Talaaq ke liye woh Aurton ki najaez himayat karti hain. Albatta jahan sirf Aurat hi gawah ban sakti ho to uski gawahi qubool ki jayegi jaisa ke Dayi ki gawahi bachche ki paidaish ke liye qabile qubool hai aur tamam woh umoor jise Mard nahi dekh sakte aur Aurten dekh sakti hain un mein Aurton ki gawahi ko qubool kiya jayega. Isi tarah se jahan Musalman maujood na hon to wahan Ahle Kitab ko bhi gawah banana jaez hai jaisa  ke farmane Ilahi: (Ayat 5:106)"_
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

               ♦ _*GAWAAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (776)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَإِنْ عُثِرَ عَلَىٰ أَنَّهُمَا اسْتَحَقَّا إِثْمًا فَآخَرَانِ يَقُومَانِ مَقَامَهُمَا مِنَ الَّذِينَ اسْتَحَقَّ عَلَيْهِمُ الْأَوْلَيَانِ فَيُقْسِمَانِ بِاللَّهِ لَشَهَادَتُنَا أَحَقُّ مِنْ شَهَادَتِهِمَا وَمَا اعْتَدَيْنَا إِنَّا إِذًا لَمِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ*

_"Lekin agar pata chal jaye ke in dono ne apne aap ko gunah mein mubtila kiya hai to phir unki bajai do aur shakhs jo unki be nisbat shahadat (gawahi) dene ke zyada Ahl hon un logo mein se khade hon jinki haq talfee hui ho aur woh Khuda ki Qasam kha kar kahen ke hamari gawahi unki gawahi unki se zyada sachchi hai aur ham ne koi ziyadti nahi ki hai. Agar hamne aisa kiya to phir ham Zalimon mein shumar kiye jayenge."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 107)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke zel mein hamne Tameem Al Dari ka waqea pesh kiya tha, jisme bataya tha ke gawah Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saamne Mayyat ki amanat mein khayanat karta hai. Ye Ayat yahi tambih kar rahi hai ke ham gawah ko achhi tarah janch parakh len.
🌿
Imam Sadiq (as) is Ayat zel mein farmaya:
_"Is Ayat se Do Aadil Musalman gawah murad  Mard hain aur gair se Ahle Kitab murad hain. Agar Ahle Kitab maujood na ho to phir do Majoosi ko bhi gawah bana sakte hain. Jab koi Musalman musaferat mein marne lage aur use gawahi ke liye do Musalman gawah na mile to woh Ahle Kitab ko apni Wasiyat ka gawah bana le aur unse ye Ahd le ke woh apni gawahi mein kisi qism ka her pher nahi karenge. Phir agar Mayyat ke wirsa ko shak ho jaye ke unhone ghalat gawahi do hai to woh iske mutabadil (replace) do gawah pesh karen aur woh halafi bayan den ke hamari gawahi unki gawahi se zyada sahih hai. Is tarah se Qazi ko chahiye ke pahli do gawahiyon ko kar de aur doosri do gawahiyon ke mutabiq faisla saadir kare."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq de ke ham sab se Imaandari se pesh ayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚰
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Jis shakhs ke Janaze mein 40 Momin gawaahi de denge ke *'Hum iske baare mein sirf Khair jaante hain',* to Parwardigar awaaz dega ke tumhari wajah se Maine un gunahon ko bhi Ma'af kar diya jisko tum nahi jaante the lekin Main jaanta hun."_
(Khisaal, Chapter40)

                ♦ _*GAWAAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (777)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ذَٰلِكَ أَدْنَىٰ أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِالشَّهَادَةِ عَلَىٰ وَجْهِهَا أَوْ يَخَافُوا أَنْ تُرَدَّ أَيْمَانٌ بَعْدَ أَيْمَانِهِمْ ۗ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاسْمَعُوا ۗ وَاللَّهُ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْفَاسِقِينَ*

_"Is tareeqe se zyada Ummid ki ja sakti hai ke log sahih gawahi denge ya kam az kam is baat hi ka khauf karenge ke unki Qasamon ke baad doosri Qasamon se kahin unki tardeed (radd) na ho jaye aur tum Allah se Darte raho aur Hukme Khuda wandi ko sunte raho. Allah nafarman afraad ko hidayat nahi deta."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 108)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta mauzoo jaari hai:
🍃
Imam Baqir (as)
_"Bani Israil mein ek Ibadat-guzaar rehta tha jiski Ibadat J. Dawood (as) ko bahut pasand aayi. Khuda ne unko Wahi farmayi ke, "Aye Dawood (as)! Iski koi cheez tumhe pasand nahi aani chahiye kyun ki ye riya-kaar (amal mein dikawa / show-off karta) hai". Pus, jab oos Aabid ki wafaat huwi to J. Dawood (as) ne logo'n se farmaya, "Apne saathi ko dafn kar do", aur khud tashreef na le gaye. Jab usay gusl diya gaya to 50 aadmiyo'n ne khade ho kar (Janaze mein) gawaahi di ke wo siwaaye iski khair-khoobi ke aur kuchh nahi jaante. Jab wo Namaz e Janaza padhh chuke to aur 50 aadmiyo'n ne khade ho kar yehi shahadat (gawaahi) di aur jab usay dafn kar chuke to mazeed 50 aadmiyo'n ne aisi hi gawaahi di! Khuda ne J. Dawood (as) ko Wahi farmayi ke, "Tumhe oos shakhs ke Janaze mein shirkat karne se kis cheez ne manaa kiya?" Arz kiya, "Ya Allah! Tu hi ne mujhe muttale' (inform) kiya tha ke wo riya-kaar hai". Khuda ne jawaab mein Wahi farmayai ke, "Haa'n, aisa hi tha. Magar jab Ulema aur biradar ki jamaat (kaseera / bahut zyada logo'n) ne gawaahi di ke uski khair o khoobi ke siwaa kuchh nahi jaante to Maine unki shahadat (gawaahi) ko qubool kar ke usay baksh diya hai, bawajood ye ke Mujhe oos (riya-kaari) ka Ilm tha."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v2, p315)

Bare Ilaha hame jaise Tu ne apne bandon ki satarposhi (hide) ki usi tarah ham par marhamat farma, Beshak Tu Ghafoor aur Rahim hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

🙇 💰
Imam Ali (as)
_*"Behtareen Imaan amaanat-daari hai."*_
(Gorar ul Hakam, v1, p115)
💰
Imam Ali (as)
_"Jhoot se doori ikhtiyaar karo kyun ki jhoot Imaan ke saath saazgaar (compatible) nahi hai."_
(Zindagi Akhlaaq Ke Saaye Mein, p80)

♦ _*UMMAT-E-RASOOL KA SULOOK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (778)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَوْمَ يَجْمَعُ اللَّهُ الرُّسُلَ فَيَقُولُ مَاذَا أُجِبْتُمْ ۖ قَالُوا لَا عِلْمَ لَنَا ۖ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ عَلَّامُ الْغُيُوبِ*

_"Jis Din Allah sab Rasoolon ko jama karke unse poochhega ke tumhe kiya jawab diya gaya tha? Woh kahenge hame koi ilm nahi. Tu hi poshida baton ka Jannewala hai."_
(Surat Ma'idah: 109)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as) ne is Ayat ki wazahat mein farmaya:
_"Khuda ke Sawal ke jawab mein Anbiya yahi kahenge ke ham to Tere Mushaheda e Jalal o Jamal mein itne mustaghraq (gharq) the ke hamen Tere alaawa kisi ka Ilm nahi hai."_
(Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Allah Qayamat ke Din Anbiya (as) se poochhega ke tumhari Ummaton ne tumhare muqarrar kardah Ausiya (as) se kiya sulook kiya tha? Woh kahenge ke Khudaya! Hamen koi ilm nahi hai ke hamare baad hamari Ummaton ne unse kiya sulook kiya tha."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Bare Ilaha Tu bhi unke saath bhi aisa hi sulook kar jinhone Ale Rasool (saww) ke saath bura sulook kiya aur jinhone suna aur unke kartooton par raazi rahe.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌿
Ek martaba Quraish ke afraad Rasool e Akram (saww) ke paas aye aur unhone kaha: "Agar Aap (saww) Nabi hain to Aap (saww) murdon ko zinda karen. Nabi e Akram (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ko unke saath rawana kiya aur farmaya: "Tum unke saath Qabrastan mein chale jao aur jin logon ka ye naam len tum unhe pukaro aur unka naam lekar ye sada do ke Allah ka Rasool Muhammad (saww) tumse kahta hai ke Allah ke Hukm se utho.
Hazrat Ali (as) gaye aur Aap (as) ne unke naam lekar unhe pukara to Qabren phat gayi aur woh apne saron se mitti jharte hue uthe. Quraish ne unse unke umoor ke mutalliq sawalat kiye aur unhe bataya ke Muhammad (saww) mab'oos ho chuke hain."
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*KARAMAT E ESA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (779)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ قَالَ اللَّهُ يَا عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ اذْكُرْ نِعْمَتِي عَلَيْكَ وَعَلَىٰ وَالِدَتِكَ إِذْ أَيَّدْتُكَ بِرُوحِ الْقُدُسِ تُكَلِّمُ النَّاسَ فِي الْمَهْدِ وَكَهْلًا ۖ وَإِذْ عَلَّمْتُكَ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَالتَّوْرَاةَ وَالْإِنْجِيلَ ۖ وَإِذْ تَخْلُقُ مِنَ الطِّينِ كَهَيْئَةِ الطَّيْرِ بِإِذْنِي فَتَنْفُخُ فِيهَا فَتَكُونُ طَيْرًا بِإِذْنِي ۖ وَتُبْرِئُ الْأَكْمَهَ وَالْأَبْرَصَ بِإِذْنِي ۖ وَإِذْ تُخْرِجُ الْمَوْتَىٰ بِإِذْنِي ۖ وَإِذْ كَفَفْتُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ عَنْكَ إِذْ جِئْتَهُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ فَقَالَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ إِنْ هَٰذَا إِلَّا سِحْرٌ مُبِينٌ.*

_"Aur jab Allah ne kaha: Aye Esa bin Maryam! Meri us Ne'mat ko yaad karo jo Meine tum par aur tumhari Waledah par ki hai. Jab Meine Roohul Qudus ke zariye se tumhe taqat faraham ki thi to gahware mein bhi logon se kalam karte the aur pukhta umr bhi kalam karte the aur Meine tumko Kitab o Hikmat aur Taurat o Injeel ki taa'leem di. Aur tum Mere Hukm se mitti ka putla parinde ki shakl ka banate aur us mein phoonkte the aur woh Mere Hukm se parinda ban jata the aur tum paidaish andhe aur Mabroos (Leper) ko Mere Hukm se tandrusti dete the aur tum Murdon ko Mere Hukm se nikal (zinda karte) the. Phir jab tum Bani Israel ke paas wazeh Nishaniyan lekar pahuncha to un mein se jo log Munkire Haq the unhone kaha tha ke ye Jadugari ke alawa kuchh nahi hai, to Meine hi tumhe Bani Ke shar se bachaya tha."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 110)

📚📖 🍁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah ne apne Nabi Esa (as) ko jo Ne'maton se nawaza usko ginaya hai.
(1) Roohul Qudus ki taeed.
(2) Gahware (cradle) mein kalam karna.
(3) Kitab o Hikmat ki taa'leem.
(4) Mitti ke Parinde ko zinda karna.
(5) Andhon aur kodhi logo shifa dena.
(6) Murdon zinda karna.
Ye Hukm e Khuda se tha. Allah apne mehboob bande ko jab jo inayat karta hai to banda hue woh ilahi kaam kar deta hai. Hazrat Ali (as) bhi Murdon ko zinda karte the. Hadis pahle pesh kar chuke hain. Allah kisi ko agar koi khudai taqat de to hame shak nahi karna chahiye. Nusairi, Alavi yeh nahi samajh paye aur Ali (as) ko Khuda manne lage, unhone ye nahi dekha ke woh Khuda ko Sajda bhi karte the. Kiyonki woh jo bhi karte woh be izne Khuda hota. Agar Khuda in Ne'maton se na nawazta to ye nahi kar paate.

Bare Ilaha hamare Imaan ko qaem o dayem aur sabit rarkh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
*Imam Hasan Askari (as):*
_"Mere baad mera beta Qaim hoga jiski taweel umr aur ghaibat ke zariye Sunan e Ambiya (as) (practice of the Prophets (as)) jaari hongi. Uski ghaibat itni taweel hogi ke logo'n ke dil sakht ho jayenge aur koi Deen par saabit qadam (steadfast) na rahega siwaaye unke jinke quloob (hearts) par Allah ne Imaan likh diya aur jinke Roohul Qudus (ke zariye) se madad ki gayi hai."_
(Kamaluddin, v2, p496)

               ♦ _*HAWARIYON*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (780)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ أَوْحَيْتُ إِلَى الْحَوَارِيِّينَ أَنْ آمِنُوا بِي وَبِرَسُولِي قَالُوا آمَنَّا وَاشْهَدْ بِأَنَّنَا مُسْلِمُونَ*

_"Aur jab Maine Hawariyon ko Waḥy ki ke mujh par aur Mere Rasool par Imaan lao.unhone kaha: ham Imaan laye aur gawah rahna ke ham farmabardar hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 111)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as) is Ayat ke mein وحى Waḥy ko " الهام" Ilham (inspiration) ke ma'ani mein hai. Waḥy sirf Nabi aur Rasool par nazil hoti hai jabke "Ilham" kisi par bhi ho sakta hai. Jaise Moosa (as) ki Maa ko Ilham hua tha. Aur aam logon par bhi kabhi kabhi khwab mein bhi Ilham ho sakta hai.
✝
Imam Reza (as):
_"Hazrat Esa (as) ke Hawariyon ki ta'daad 12 thi. Un mein "Aluqa" (Luke) sabe Afzal aur sabse bada Aalim tha. Ulema e Nasara 3 the: Youhanna (John) Akbarbaj, Youhanna Qarsiyya, Youhanna Daylami Zajar. Uske paas hamare Nabi aur unke Ahle Bait (as) aur Ummat ka zikr mehfooz tha. Aur usi ne Ummat e Esa (as) ko Rasool e Akram (saww) ki aamad ki basharat di thi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✝
Imam Reza (as) se sawal kiya gaya: "Hawariyon ko Hawari kiyon kahte hain?
Imam (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Public mein iski wajah ye hai ke woh Dhobi the aur logon ke kapdon ka mail utara karte the aur Safai karne wale ko "Hawari حوارى" kaha jata hai. Jabke hamari nazar mein unki wajhe tasmiyah ye hai ke woh apni zaat ke Mukhlis the aur apne alawa doosron ke bhi Mukhlis the aur Wa'az o Nasihat ki wajah se Gunahon ki Mael Kuchail utara karte the."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame bhi Nek Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✝
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Ya Ali! Tumhari misaal Isa bin Maryam (as) ki tarah hai, jis se Isaiyo'n ne hadd se zyada pyaar kiya to kaafir ho gaye aur Yahudiyo'n ne bugz kiya to kaafir ho gaye."_
Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p129
✝
Rasule Khuda (saww)
Siddiq (sachche dil se waqt ke Nabi ki tasdeeq karne wale) 3 hain:
_(1) H. Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as),_
_(2) Habib e Najjar (H. Isa (as) ke Hawaari (sahabi)),_
_(3) Momin e Aal e Firoun."_
(H. Musa (as) ki nisbat se).
Khisaal, p103

           ♦ _*DASTARKHWAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (781)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ قَالَ الْحَوَارِيُّونَ يَا عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ هَلْ يَسْتَطِيعُ رَبُّكَ أَنْ يُنَزِّلَ عَلَيْنَا مَائِدَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ ۖ قَالَ اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ * قَالُوا نُرِيدُ أَنْ نَأْكُلَ مِنْهَا وَتَطْمَئِنَّ قُلُوبُنَا وَنَعْلَمَ أَنْ قَدْ صَدَقْتَنَا وَنَكُونَ عَلَيْهَا مِنَ الشَّاهِدِينَ.*

_"Jab Hawariyon ne kaha: Aye Esa bin Maryam! Kiya Aap ka Rab ham par Aasmaan se khaane ka ek khwan utar sakta hai? Esa (as) ne kaha tha ke Allah se darte raho agar tum Momin ho. Unhone kaha: Ham ye chahte hain ke us se khana khayen aur hamare dilon ko Itminaan ho jaye aur hame maloom ho jaye ke Aap ne ham se sach kaha hai aur ham us par gawah bane."_
(Surat Ma'idah 112 - 113)

📚📖 🍪🥣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ibne Abbas ka bayan hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) ne Bani Israel se kaha tha ke tum 30 Roze rakho, uske baad tum Khuda se jo bhi sawal karoge Allah tumhara sawal poora karega. Chunanche unhone 30 Roze rakhe aur jab Roze mukammal ho gaye to unhone kaha ke agar hamne kisi insaan ka kaam kiya hota to woh hame khaana zaroor khilaata. Hamne 30 Din tak  Roze rakhe hain aur bhook bardasht ki hai. Ab Aap Allah se Dua maange ke Woh hamare liye Aasman se Khaana utaare. Hazrat Esa (as) ne Dua maange. Malaika Aasmani le kar nazil hue. Is Khwan mein 7 Rotiyan thin aur 7 Machhliyan thin jise sab ne mil kar khaya.
Rasoole Akram (saww) se marvi hai ke Aasmani Khwan mein Gosht aur Rotiyan thin.
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamare Dastarkhwanon mein barkat ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🥣🍪
Imam Ali (as)
_"Dastarkhwan pe gira huwa kha lo; Allah ke hukm se oos khaane mein har dard se shifa hai, khaas uski jo uske zariye Shifa chaahe."_
(Tehzeebul Islam)
🍪🥣
Riwayat
(Raawi ka bayaan hai ke jab Khaane ka) Dastarkhwaan uthha liya gaya to hum mein se ek shakhsh uthha taaki dastarkhwaan ki giri padi gizao'n ko chunn le to Imam Kazim (as) ne farmaya, _"Ye kaam chhato'n (roof) ke niche (makaano'n) mein kiya jaata hai. Aisi jagah jaise baagh, waghaira (garden, open places etc) mein to chidiyo'n ke liye aur jaanwaro'n ke liye chhor diya jaata hai."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v7, p140)

🌹 *MARG-E-YAZEED MUBARAK* 🌹

          *14th Rabiul Awwal 1439*
     *4th December 2017, Monday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
         🌹 *HAFTA-E-BARA'AT* 🌹
***********************************
          ♦ _*EID MUBARAK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (782)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ اللَّهُمَّ رَبَّنَا أَنْزِلْ عَلَيْنَا مَائِدَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ تَكُونُ لَنَا عِيدًا لِأَوَّلِنَا وَآخِرِنَا وَآيَةً مِنْكَ ۖ وَارْزُقْنَا وَأَنْتَ خَيْرُ الرَّازِقِينَ*

_"Esa bin Maryam (as) ne farmaya: Aye Khuda, Aye hamare Rab! Ham par Aasmaan se ek Khwan nazil kar jo hamare liye agle pichhlon ke liye khushi *(Eid)* ka mauqa qarar paye aur Teri taraf se ek Nishani (Ayat) ho, hamko rizq de aur Tu behtar Rizq Denewala hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 114)

📚📖 🍪🥣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj Muhibbane Ahle Bait (as) ke liye Eid ka Din hai kiyonki aaj Yazeed Paleed is Duniya se wasil e Jahannum hua. Aaj Hawariyon e Ale Yaseen (saww) Ke liye khushi ka Din hai.
Hawariyon ne jo darkhwast ki thi unka irada Nek tha jaisa ke Ayat se zahir ho raha hai, taak itminaan e qalb ho jaye. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne bhi is tarah ki darkhwast ki thi. Isiliye unki Dua qubool bhi kar li gayi. Ye bhi Hazrat Esa (as) ka ek Mojeza tha unki darkhwast par Aasman se Dastarkhwan nazil ho gaya. Lekin Janabe Hasnain (as) ne Eid ke Din sirf apni maadare garami se kapdon ka sawal kiya to Rizwan e Jannat Jannat se Kapde le kar aa gaye.
Bani Israel ke liye bhi Aasman se khwan aye.
Jab bhi koi Ne'mat Allah ki taraf se hasil ho woh khusi ki baat hoti hai aur ye ham log ke liye Eid ka Din hota hai. Jis Din ye khwan aya woh Sunday ka Din tha. Ho sakta hai Christians ne is liye isko Holiday ka Din rakha.

Bare Ilaha hamari Rozi mein barkat ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍪🥣
Imam Ali (as)
_"Har wo din jis me Allah ki maasiyat (Na-farmaani) na ki jaaye wo oos shakhs ki Eid (ka din ) hai._"
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7, Eid)
🕌
Imam Ali (as)
_"Eid wo nahi ke insaan achcha libaas zeyb e tan kar le (pehen le), balke Eid ka din wo hai jisme insaan gunah na kare. Lihaza, jis din insaan gunah se bache, wo din uske liye Eid ka din hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p221)
🕌
Imam Ali (as)
_"Eid to bus uski hai jiske Roze ko Allah ne qubool kar liya hai aur jiske qayaam ki qadr ki gayi aur har wo din Eid hai jisme gunah na ho."_
(Aaina e Huqooq (Sharh Risaalatul Huqooq) , p214)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         🌹 *HAFTA-E-BARA'AT* 🌹
***********************************
           ♦ _*DASTARKHWAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (783)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ اللَّهُ إِنِّي مُنَزِّلُهَا عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ فَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بَعْدُ مِنْكُمْ فَإِنِّي أُعَذِّبُهُ عَذَابًا لَا أُعَذِّبُهُ أَحَدًا مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Allah ne kaha: Mein usko tum par nazil karne wala hun magar iske baad jo tum mein se na qadri karega use Mein aisi Saza dunga jo Meine tamam Jahano mein se kisi ko na di hogi."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 115)
📚📖 🍪🥣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Hawariyon ne Hazrat Esa (as) se darkhwast ki thi ke Khuda unhe aisa Ta'am (khana) ata kare jo khatm hone mein na aye. Chunanche Allah ne un par Khwan nazil kiya aur unse kaha gaya jab tak tum khayanat na karoge aur ise na chhupaoge ye yun tumhare paas maujood rahega. Aur agar tumne khayanat ki to tumhe Azaab diya jayega. Abhi poora Din nahi guzra tha ke logon ne is mein khayanat ki aur Khudai Azaab ke mustaheq qarar paye aur woh Suwar bana diye gaye.
(Noorus Saqlain)
🍪🍛🍲
Imam Moosa Kazim (as):
_"Aasmaani Khwan nazil hota, sab mil kar is khwan par baith jaate the aur ji bhar kar khaana khaate the. Uske baad Khwan upar uth jata tha. Is qaum ke Mutakabberin (Ghamandi Log) aur Sardaron ne kaha ke is Khwan par Ghareeb log hamare barabar baith kar khaana na khayen. Jis par Allah naraaz ho gaya aur Aasmani Khwan (Maedah) ke nuzool ka silsila munqata (stop) ho gaya. Khuda ne unhe Bandar aur Suwar bana diya."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamare Dastarkhwanon mein barkat nazil farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍪🍛🍲
Imam Ali (as)
_"Dastarkhwan pe gira huwa kha lo; Allah ke hukm se oos khaane mein har dard se shifa hai, khaas uski jo uske zariye Shifa chaahe."_
(Tehzeebul Islam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          *16th Rabiul Awwal 1439*

              ♦ _*EID-E-MILAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (784)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*(قَالَ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ اللَّهُمَّ رَبَّنَا أَنْزِلْ عَلَيْنَا مَائِدَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ تَكُونُ لَنَا عِيدًا لِأَوَّلِنَا وَآخِرِنَا وَآيَةً مِنْكَ ۖ وَارْزُقْنَا وَأَنْتَ خَيْرُ الرَّازِقِينَ*

_"Esa bin Maryam (as) ne farmaya: Aye Khuda, Aye hamare Rab! Ham par Aasmaan se ek Khwan nazil kar jo hamare liye agle pichhlon ke liye khushi (Eid) ka mauqa qarar paye aur Teri taraf se ek Nishani (Ayat) ho, hamko rizq de aur Tu behtar Rizq Denewala hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 114)
📚📖 🍪🥣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Eid To Quran Se saabit hai Jab Nuzool e Dastarkhwan ho jo Jannat se Ne'mat Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Esa (as) aur unke Hawariyon ko ata ki to wo Din EID ho jaye
to jab Kainat Ka Waali Rehmat e Aalameen Salallahu alaihe wa Aalehi Wassalam, jinke sadqe mein is Kaynat ko wujood mila, unka Nuzool aur Aamad ka Din Khushi ka Din hoga, yehi Eid-e-Milad hai. Is mein na koi Shirk hai na bidat.
Hazrat Esa (as) ne 3 Important Dino par *Salaam* bheja hai:
*(1) Birthday*
*(2) Death Day*
*(3) Be'sat Day.*
( *وَالسَّلَامُ عَلَيَّ يَوْمَ وُلِدْتُ وَيَوْمَ أَمُوتُ وَيَوْمَ أُبْعَثُ حَيًّا*)
(Surah Maryam: 33)

To sawal jo kiya jata hai ke Wiladat kis ne manai to Quran se bhi sabit hai. Ye Anbiya ki Sunnat hai. Jisko apni Birthday nahi maloom woh Salgirah nahi manata.

Hamare sab 14 Masoom ki Wiladat wa Shahadat maloom hai aur Aimma (as) in Makhsoos Dino ki yaad manate the.
Agar ham apne bachcho ki Salgirah na manayen to bachhon mein kiya tassurat paye jaayenge ye Psychologist behtar taur par bata sakta hai. Fitri baat hai har koi apne Mehboob ko yaad karta hai. Hamara Mehboob hamare liye Rasoole Akram (saww) se behtar nahi ho sakta. Isliye ham unki Yaum e Wiladat ka Jashn manayenge, Khushnood e Allah o Rasool ke khatir.

Bare Ilaha is ba barkat Din mein hamari Khushiyon mein izafa farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jisme ye 4 aadatein hongi wo Allah Ta'ala ke Noor e Azeem mein hoga:_
_(1) Allah ke Yekta (Akele) hone aur mere Allah ke Rasool hone ki gawaahi de_
_( *"Ash'hadu al La Ilaha Illallah Wa As'hadu Anna Muhammadar Rasulullah" kahe*),_
*اشهد ان لا اله الا الله و اشهد ان محمد رسول لله*
_(2) Jab musibat aur takleef ho to *"Inna Lillahi Wa Inna Ilaihi Raajioon"* kahe,_
*إِنَّا للهِ وَإِنَّـا إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعون*
_(3) Jab bhalaai miley to *"Al Hamdu Lillahi Rabbil Aalameen"* kahe,_
*الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ*
_(4) Jab gunah sar-zad ho to *"Astagfirullah Wa Atoobu Ilaihe"* kahe._
*استغفرالله و اتوب اليه*
(Khisaal, p120)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ♦ _*GHULOO (EXAGGERATION)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (785)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ قَالَ اللَّهُ يَا عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ أَأَنْتَ قُلْتَ لِلنَّاسِ اتَّخِذُونِي وَأُمِّيَ إِلَٰهَيْنِ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ ۖ قَالَ سُبْحَانَكَ مَا يَكُونُ لِي أَنْ أَقُولَ مَا لَيْسَ لِي بِحَقٍّ ۚ إِنْ كُنْتُ قُلْتُهُ فَقَدْ عَلِمْتَهُ ۚ تَعْلَمُ مَا فِي نَفْسِي وَلَا أَعْلَمُ مَا فِي نَفْسِكَ ۚ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ عَلَّامُ الْغُيُوبِ*

_"Jab Allah kahega: Aye Esa ibne Maryam! Kiya tumne logon se ye kaha tha ke Khuda ko chhod kar mujhe aur meri waledah ko Ma'bood maan lo? Woh kahenge Tu Paak o Paakiza hai. Mujhe nahaq kahni zeb nahi deti thi. Agar meine aisi baat kahi hoti to Tujhko zaroor Ilm hota. Tu jaanta hai jo kuchh mere dil mein hai aur mein nahi jaanta jo kuchh Tere Ji mein hain. Beshak Tu Ghaib ki baaton ko achhi tarah se Jannewala hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 116)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Reza (as) se rivayat hai:
Imam Ali (as):
_"Mere mutalliq do qism ke log halaak ho jayenge: (1) Muhabbat mein ifraat (Exaggeration) karne wale aur (2)  Mujhe se Bughz karne wale. Ham Khuda ke Huzoor un logon se Bara'at (bezaari) ka izhaar karte hain jo hamare mutalliq Ghuloo (غلو - Exaggeration) karte hain aur hamen hadd se badhate hain. Ham Ghaliyon se aise hi bezaar hain jaisa ke Hazrat Esa bin Maryam (as) Nasaara se bezaar the. Allah ne unke mutalliq ye Ayat bayan farmayi (5:116)"_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamare Naujawano ko Ghaliyon ke sharr se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👨‍💼
*الأمالي للطوسي: قال الصادق (ع): احذروا على شبابكم الغلاة لايفسدونهم ؛ فإن الغلاة شر خلق الله‏، يصغرون عظمة الله‏، ويدعون الربوبية لعباد الله‏، والله‏ إن الغلاة شر من اليهود والنصارى والمجوس والذين أشركوا، ثم قال: إلينا يرجع الغالي فلا نقبله، وبنا يلحق المقصر فنقبله، فقيل له: كيف ذلك يا بن رسول الله‏ ؟ قال: لأن الغالي قد اعتاد ترك الصلاة والزكاة والصيام والحج فلا يقدر على ترك عادته وعلى الرجوع إلى طاعة الله‏ عزوجل أبدا، وإن المقصر إذا عرف عمل وأطاع.*
🍁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Apne Naujawano ko Ghulat (Sifat mein hadd se badhane wale) se bachao kiyonki Ghulat Allah ke shararti makhlooq hai. Woh log Allah ki Azmat ko kam karte hain aur Allah ke bandon ko Ruboobiyat ka khitab dete hain. Allah ki Qasam Ghulat Yahudiyon, Eisaiyon, Majoosiyon aur Mushrekin se bhi badtar hain. Ghali hamari taraf palate to ham use qabool nahi karenge jabke laparwah jo hamse munsalik hai use qubool kar lenge."_ Poochha gaya ye kaise? Jawab diya: _"Kiyonki Ghali Tarke Namaz, Zakat, Roza aur Hajj ka aadi ho jaata hai aur ye aadat wo chhod bhi nahi sakta aur na Allah ki Ita'at ki taraf phir se rujoo ho sakta hai, jabke Muqassir (Laparwah) ko jab Ma'arefat hasil hoti hai to woh amal karta hai aur ita'at guzar ban jaata hai."_
(Amali al-Tusi, p. 650, no. 1349)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*TAWHEED* ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (786)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا قُلْتُ لَهُمْ إِلَّا مَا أَمَرْتَنِي بِهِ أَنِ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ رَبِّي وَرَبَّكُمْ ۚ وَكُنْتُ عَلَيْهِمْ شَهِيدًا مَا دُمْتُ فِيهِمْ ۖ فَلَمَّا تَوَفَّيْتَنِي كُنْتَ أَنْتَ الرَّقِيبَ عَلَيْهِمْ ۚ وَأَنْتَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ شَهِيدٌ * إِنْ تُعَذِّبْهُمْ فَإِنَّهُمْ عِبَادُكَ ۖ وَإِنْ تَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ فَإِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ*

_"(Hazrat Esa (as): Maine to un se bas wohi kuchh kaha hai jiska Tu ne mujhe Hukm diya hai: yehi ke Khuda ki Ibaadat karo jo mera aur tumhara Rab hai. Mein us waqt tak unka nigran tha jab tak mein un mein raha aur jab Tu ne mujhe wapas bula liya to Tu to khud hi unka Nigran tha aur Tu har cheez ka Gawah hai."_
_"Agar Tu unhe Azaab dena chahe to ye Tere Bande hain aur agar Tu inhe Ma'af kar de to Tu Ghalib aur Sahibe Hikmat hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 117 - 118)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein jo Allah ne Hazrat Esa (as) se sawal kiya tha ke unhone kis baat ki Tableegh ki, is Ayat mein Hazrat Esa (as) uska jawab de rahe hain.

Tafseer e Ayyashi mein hai ke Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Esa (as) se Fe'le Maazi (Past Tense) mein bayan kiya hai, jabke Allah unse ye sawal Qayamat ke Din karega. Allah Ta'ala jab kisi Yaqeeni Amr ki khabar deta hai to use Past Tense ke alfaz se bayan karta hai.
(Ba Rivayat e Imam Sadiq (as).

Har Nabi ne Tawheed e Khuda ki Tableegh ki lekin Nabi Ummaton ne unke jaane ke baad unke farameen ko faramosh kiya.  Hazrat Esa (as) yehi bata rahe hain ke unke uthay jaane ke baad kiya hua Allah behtar Jaanta hai. Aur Ummat ne Nabi (saww) ke jaane ke baad kiya kiya harkate ki Allah unhe sakht Azaab dega. Ye Allah par chhor diya ab chaahe woh Azaab mein mubtila kare ya Ma'af kar de. Ham ye bhi nahi kah sakte ke Yazid jaise Zalim ne itne sangeen zulm dhaye, gunah kiye aur ham is umeed par rahen ke Allah use Ma'af kar dega. Qatil ko jab koi insaan Ma'af nahi karta to Allah kaise Ma'af kar dega, Woh Adil hai Insaaf karne wala hai.

Bare Ilaha hamare Ma'arif e Ilahi mein izaafa farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Ism e Aazam (اسم اعظم) ke 73 huroof (Letters) hain. Un mein se 1 word Allah ne apne paas rakha hai. Isi liye kisi ko Ilm nahi hai ke Khuda ke ji mein kiya hai. Allah ne Hazrat Adam (as) ko 72 huroof ata kiye the jo Hazrat Esa (as) tak bataur Meeras Anbiya mein chalte aye. Isi liye Hazrat Esa (as) ne kaha: "Jo kuchh mere Dil mein hai Tu use jaanta hai." Yaani mere paas 72 huroof ka Ilm maujood hai aur Tera hi taa'leem karda hai. (Ayat 5:118) kiyonki Makhsoos Harf Tere paas hai isi liye kisi ko bhi ilm nahi hai ke Tere Ji mein kiya hai."_
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*YAUM-E-QAYAMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (787)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*
*(قَالَ اللَّهُ هَٰذَا يَوْمُ يَنْفَعُ الصَّادِقِينَ صِدْقُهُمْ ۚ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٌ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا ۚ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَرَضُوا عَنْهُ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ * لِلَّهِ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَمَا فِيهِنَّ ۚ وَهُوَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*

_"Allah farmayga: Ye wo Din hai jis mein sachcha ko unki sachchai fayda degi. Unke liye aise Baghat (Jannat) hain jinke neeche Nehren baih rahi hain jin mein woh hamesha rahenge. Khuda unse Raazi aur woh Khuda se Raazi hain. Ye bahut badi kamyabi hai. Aasmanon aur Zameen aur jo kuchh in mein maujood hai un sab ki Badshahi Allah ke liye hai aur Woh har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 119 - 120)

📚📖 🍪🥣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
"Jab Qayamat bapa hogi aur tamam log Hisaab ke liye Mehshoor honge to Roze Qayamat ke shadayd se unka guzar hoga aur Maidaan e Mahshar mein badi jaddo jahad ke baad pahunchenge. Unhe Maidan mein rok diya jayega aur Khuda Wand Jabbar apne Arsh se un par nigah karega. Tamam Makhlooqat jis Nida ko sab se pahle sunegi woh Hazrat Muhammad bin Abdullah Bani Qarashi Arabi ka naam pukara jayega."
"Rasoole Maqbool (saww) aage badhenge aur Arsh ki dayen janib ja kar khade honge. Iske baad Hazrat Ali (as) ko pukara jayega. Woh aage badhenge aur Nabi e Akram (saww) ki taraf ja kar khade ho jayenge. Iske baad tarteeb war har Nabi aur uski Ummat ko pukara jayega aur tamam Anbiya apni Ummaton sameet Arsh ke bayen jaanib jaakar khade honge."
"Silsilah Sawal ka aghaz Qalam se kiya jayega aur Qalam ko pukara jayega. Qalam insaani surat mein Khuda ke saamne jaakar khada ho jayega. Allah Ta'ala usse kahega ke Meine tujhe jo Waḥy o Ilhaam kiya tha kiya tu ne ise Lauh par likha tha? Qalam kahega: Malik! Meine Tere farman par amal kiya tha aur meine Teri Waḥy ke mutabiq Lauh par likha tha. Khuda kahega: Teri gawahi kaun dega? Qalam kahega: "Tere sarbasta Raaz ko Tere alawa aur kaun jaanta hai?" Allah kahega: "Tu ne apni Daleel bayan kar di."
"Iske baad Lauh ko bulaya jayega aur Lauh insaani surat mein pesh hogi aur Qalam ke saath khadi ho jayegi. Allah Ta'ala usse kahega: "Kiya Qalam ne Mere Ilhaam o Waḥy ko tujh par naql kiya?" Lauh kahega: "Ji haan! Meine woh paigham Israfeel ko pahuncha diya the."
"Phir Israfeel se bhi same sawal kiya jayega aur woh bhi haan mein jawab denge.   Aur kahenge ke meine wo Waḥy Jibrael tak pahuncha di thi."
"Phir Jibrael (as) se same sawal kiya jayega aur woh bhi haan mein jawab denge.  Phir kahenge meine Tera Paigham Anbiya ko pahuncha diya tha. Aur sab se Aakhir mein meine Teri Risalat, Teri Waḥy, Teri Hikmat, Tera Ilm, Teri Kitab aur Tera Kalam Muhammad bin Abdullah (saww) tak pahunchaya."
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
(To be cont'd Jaari...)

Bare Ilaha Qayamat ke Din Tu hamse Fazl se pesh aana na ke Adl se.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Qayamat ke Din Khuda Aalim aur Aabid (dono) ko uthhayega. Jab dono Khuda ke saamne khade honge to Aabid se kaha jayega Tu Jannat mein jaa', aur Aalim se kaha jayega, 'Tum thhehro. Logo'n ko behtareen Adaab sikhaane ki wajah se unki shafa'at karo'."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p161)

          *21th Rabiul Awwal 1439*
     *11th December 2017, Monday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
       ♦ _*YAUM-E-QAYAMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (788)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ اللَّهُ هَٰذَا يَوْمُ يَنْفَعُ الصَّادِقِينَ صِدْقُهُمْ ۚ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٌ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا ۚ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَرَضُوا عَنْهُ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ * لِلَّهِ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَمَا فِيهِنَّ ۚ وَهُوَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*

_"Allah farmayga: Ye wo Din hai jis mein sachcha ko unki sachchai fayda degi. Unke liye aise Baghat (Jannat) hain jinke neeche Nehren baih rahi hain jin mein woh hamesha rahenge. Khuda unse Raazi aur woh Khuda se Raazi hain. Ye bahut badi kamyabi hai. Aasmanon aur Zameen aur jo kuchh in mein maujood hai un sab ki Badshahi Allah ke liye hai aur Woh har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai."_
(Surah Ma'idah: 119 - 120)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta se pewast: Hadis Cont'd...
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
.........
"Rasoole Khuda (saww) se bhi same sawal kiya jayega, Kiya paigham pahunchaya. Rasoole Khuda (saww) jawab denge ji haan, woh paigham Ummat tak pahuncha diya. ....Phir Ummat ko bulaya jayega aur unse sawal kiya jayega aur woh unki Risalat ki gawahi degi. Allah Nabi e Karim (saww) se sawal karega: Kiya tumne apni Ummat mein se kisi ko apna Janashin bhi muqarrar kiya tha jo tumhare baad unhe Meri Ilm o Hikmat ki taa'leem deta aur Meri Kitab ki wazahat karta jo Meri taraf se Hujjat hota aur tumhara Janashin hota? Rasoole Khuda (saww) arz karenge: "Ji haan! Meine apne bhai, Vazir, Wasi aur Khair e Ummat Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ko apna Janashin muqarrar kiya tha aur meine use apni zindagi mein parcham bana kar nasab kiya tha aur meine logon ko uski ita'at ki dawat di thi. Meine use apni Ummat ka Imam muqarrar kiya tha. Baqi Aimma Qayamat tak uski iqteda karte rahe."
"Phir Ali (as) ko bulaya jayega aur woh Rasool (saww) ke jawab ki ta'eed karenge aur farmaynge: lekin jab Tu ne unhe maut di to unki Ummat ne mera inkaar kar diya tha aur mere khilaf saazishen ki gayi aur mujhe kamzor bana diya gaya aur qareeb tha ke mujhe qatl kar dete aur Tu ne jise peechhe kiya tha unhone us mere aage kiya aur jise aage kiya the unhone use peechhe kiya. Unhone meri baat nahi suni aur mere hukm ki ita'at nahi ki. Meine Teri Raah mein unse jihad kiya yahan tak ke mujhe qatl kiya gaya."
"Phir unke baad Hujjate Khuda ke baare mein sawal kiye gaye aur har Imam se sawal kiya gaya. Allah unka uzr qubool karega aur unki Hujjat ko jaez qarar dega. Phir Allah farmayega:
_"Us Din Sachchon ko unki sachchai fayda degi."_(5:119)
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

Alhamdulillah Surah Maeda tak Tafseer tamam hui.

Bare Ilaha hame Qayamat ke Din hamare Aimma (as) me saath mab'oos karna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Sidq صدق ki haqiqat Khuda se Bandagi, Pakeezgi ki mutaqazi hai jaisa ke Hazrat Esa (as) ki sachchai ki wajah se Roze Qayamat unhe Bara'at nasib hogi aur Ummate Muhammad (saww) ke kuchh afraad ko bhi sachchai ki barkat se nijaat nasib hogi. Ayat (5:119)"_
(Misbahus Shari'ah, Noorus Saqlain)
